## **188: Discovering a Hero and Additional Searching**

**AN:** It might be difficult to update on the 30th.

Please wait without getting your hopes up.

---

Because we failed to get into the gondola tour, we decided to walk around the urban area of Latis Island instead.

“Come on, Master, don’t be so depressed. Even just walking around, I think it’s a nice town, you know?”

As Mio said, there’s no doubt it’s enjoyable even on foot.

But that isn’t the best way to enjoy it.

“You did make a reservation, at least, right?”

“Yeah, but they said the wait would be at least a week…”

Apparently, we just happened to run into peak tourist season.

For me, that’s extremely rare.

“…No, rather than bad luck, it’s probably more natural to think something was going to happen. Fortunately, we can already see the troublesome issue.”

“Is that really something to call ‘fortunate’…?”

Ignoring Mio tilting her head in confusion, I think it through.

Rather than ‘we were unlucky’, it’s more likely that ‘this was still the best outcome’.

The troublesome issue is, of course, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

The abnormal situation where a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is forced into survival mode has already occurred.

“This town… no, this country, is it going to be destroyed?”

“Jin-kun, please don’t say scary things…”

“But if that thing revives, it’s over in one shot, right?”

That thing is, of course, the calamity dragon.

“That… I can’t deny it…”

Sakura understands too, the threat posed by the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’.

Just to be clear, the fact that Ashley’s unique skill as a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ was \<Flowing Water’s Thought> makes it almost certain that it is a ‘Water Calamity Dragon’.

Then let’s answer it, even if it might be a bit early.

Alta, is my guess correct?

A: Yes. Everything is exactly as Master imagines. Since you are not looking at the map, I will omit the details, but if Master does not act, the calamity dragon will revive and the Pajel Kingdom will be destroyed within a month at the latest.

…So it falls within a month.

It’s probably just a coincidence, but that’s about the same as the deadline for finding a \<Hero>.

“Of course the things you don’t want to be right are the ones that are right…”

It seems the information was shared with the others as well, and Mio said that unpleasantly.

“So, Master. Are you going to stop its revival? Or defeat it before it revives?”

“It depends on the situation. Of course, if it revives, I’ll definitely defeat it.”

《Beat it up!》

A calamity dragon spreads damage to its surroundings from the moment it revives.

If it revives, it’s crucial to defeat it as quickly as possible. And I have the power to do that.

However, if I act before its revival, things become extremely troublesome.

I have no responsibility toward the calamity dragon, so I have no obligation to do something that troublesome.

The only reason I’d move before revival is if there were something worth trading that trouble for.

Alta, is there any reason for me to act before it revives?

A: No, there is not. In fact, it may be recommended to allow it to revive.

Huh? Was the Pajel Kingdom the kind of country where I’d think it should just be destroyed?

A: Yes. The upper echelons of the country. Many of the nobles and royalty are corrupt.

Ah… that’s my most hated pattern.

Could this island be the same?

A: While the influence is not zero, this island is likely within Master’s tolerance range.

Hearing that put me at ease.

“Alright. We’ll protect this island, at least.”

We haven’t even finished sightseeing yet.

We’ll give up this time, but at least let it stay safe until we ride the gondola.

“Huh? The other towns are fine?”

“I wouldn’t say ‘fine’, but there are things I can’t do, and things I don’t want to do.”

After the calamity dragon revives, preventing damage everywhere would be extremely difficult.

You want me to work hard to protect corrupt royals and nobles?

No thanks. You can do that yourselves.

…So, basically, we’ve decided on taking no action regarding this country’s crisis.

If I end up involved for some reason, I’ll think about it then.

Now then, while we were walking around Latis Island chatting about trivial things, we weren’t wandering without a destination.

We were heading to a certain shop under Alta’s guidance.

And that would be this.

A slave trader.

Yes. Everyone’s favorite, the slave trader.

Latis Island is a tourist spot, but regardless of that, slave traders exist.

If you’re looking for a \<Hero>, you can’t skip the slave trader.

After all, at this point, two of the four were slaves purchased from slave traders.

Note that Cynthia, the human Hero, was an orphan directly bought as a slave and not purchased through a slave trader, so she doesn’t count.

“So Maria and I will go check it out. You guys wander around here.”

“Understood.”

《Have a good one!》

Only Maria and I went to the slave trader, while the others explored the surroundings.

According to Alta, this slave trader is quite large in scale, and the quality of the slaves varies widely.

In other words, they also handle bargain slaves… slaves who are not in a decent condition.

Sakura doesn’t want to see it, and I don’t want Dora to see it.

Mio and Sera don’t mind going to a slave trader itself, but they don’t want to see the poor conditions of bargain slaves. It brings back only bad memories.

Maria? She doesn’t care at all.

After entering the slave trader, we asked the receptionist to show us all the slaves.

From the slave trader’s perspective, there’s no point in showing all slaves to someone who might not buy, so they first checked our budget.

“Is this enough?”

For now, I showed them a bag filled with large gold coins (one coin equals one million gold).

I’ve always wanted to try this at least once.

“Welcome! Right this way, please!”

The receptionist rushed off to call the owner, and we were treated with extremely polite service.

I’ve always wanted to try this at least once.

Sitting on a sofa, slaves were introduced one after another.

I said I wouldn’t look at the map, but I didn’t forbid checking the status of someone directly in front of me.

I checked each person’s status, searching for a holder of the \<Hero> skill.

So far, there are no \<Hero> holders.

There were some rare skill holders, so I had Maria write down their names.

As an aside, because of our objective this time, male slaves are also included in the search.

“That concludes the introduction of all our slaves. Did you find anyone to your liking?”

The owner said that, but my eyes can’t be fooled.

“That’s not all of them, is it?”

“Huh?”

“You haven’t shown the slaves that would be sold at bargain prices.”

When I asked, the owner nodded nervously.

“Y-Yes, that’s correct. But would someone of your wealth really want to see bargain slaves?”

He asked with genuine confusion.

“Yeah. I said from the start I wanted to see them all, right?”

“Understood. Some of them are difficult to bring here, so may I trouble you to come to the rooms? …Honestly, I can’t recommend it.”

“I’m used to it. No problem.”

“Ah, I see. Understood.”

As he said that, the owner tried to guide us with a look of understanding.

Why?

A: It seems he judged that you have a sadistic hobby involving bargain slaves.

“Wait.”

I stopped the owner with a tone of voice I’d never used before.

I can’t tolerate that kind of misunderstanding.

“Is something wrong?”

“My purpose is not what you’re thinking.”

“Ugh…”

The owner’s face stiffened as his inner thoughts were seen through.

“In my experience, bargain slaves often have surprisingly good finds among them. I just think it’s a waste to discard them without even looking. …Now, please guide us.”

“…Understood.”

Guided by the embarrassed owner, we entered an isolated room a short distance away.

The owner himself did not enter the room; instead, a guide dedicated to the isolation area accompanied us.

As expected of a large-scale slave trader, there were quite a lot of bargain slaves as well.

Regardless of missing limbs, I checked slaves who had rare skills and were not steeped in malice.

Around halfway through, we found two rare skill holders.

As expected, the probability of rare skills is higher among bargain slaves.

However, unfortunately, there doesn’t seem to be any \<Hero> holders.

“Hm?”

Suddenly, one slave deeper inside caught my attention.

She was a human female slave in her early twenties, with no particularly rare skills.

Her belly was swollen, there were still fresh burn scars on her body, and her eyes were dead.

“That slave there, what’s her story?”

“She was originally the wife of a fairly large merchant house, but her husband died in a fire, leaving the child in her belly. She herself was burned like that, went bankrupt, and became a slave. A perfect fall from grace.”

The background I heard from the guide was utterly devoid of salvation.

So, what is it about that slave that bothers me…?

I carefully check her status.

Ah.

Found it. The \<Hero> skill.

Yes, the holder of the \<Hero> skill was inside the female slave’s womb.

According to the status, the child’s race is Dwarf.

In mixed-race marriages, children usually take the mother’s race, but in extremely rare cases, they take the father’s race.

In this case, the mother is human and the child is a Dwarf, so that rare case must have applied.

And that child has the \<Hero> skill…

Yeah, it’s a bargain sale of rare cases.

As an aside, the child did not have the \<Seal> skill that suppresses the \<Hero> skill.

It must be granted at the moment of birth.

After that, we purchased a total of four slaves: three rare skill holders and the Hero mother.

Completely by coincidence, the three rare skill holders were all female.

The bargain slaves were washed, dressed (they hadn’t been wearing clothes before), and brought before me. These services, by the way, cost extra.

After paying, we quickly completed the slave contracts, rented a room, and gave the slaves some food I had on hand.

It’s troublesome if they can’t move on their own to some extent.

When the owner saw the food I took out, his face went pale.

“Please! Please let me eat that food as well!”

Saying that, the owner performed a magnificent prostration.

According to him, the owner is a great gourmet with a weakness for good food.

Just by looking, he understood the quality of the food I brought out and couldn’t stay still.

…As a result, the entire amount I paid was refunded.

In other words, the food the slaves were eating was worth as much as or more than the slaves themselves. I don’t even understand anymore.

Escorted out by the regretful owner, we left the slave trader.

We were treated as a top customer without paying a single gold.

“Sorry to keep you waiting!”

After leaving the slave trader, we rejoined Sakura and the others.

The slaves were instructed to wear hoods and follow without speaking.

“Welcome back…”

“Judging by Master’s face, it seems you went to a slave trader.”

“But… I don’t see them?”

Sera said curiously, having only looked at the person’s own status.

《The tummy!》

Dora was the first to notice.

“Whoa! You’re right! …You succeeded with just darts!?”

《Big hit!》

“This goes beyond amazing… it’s a little scary…”

“I’m completely put off…”

Everyone except Dora was thoroughly put off.

This was my first experience finding a ‘person I’m looking for (unborn)’ too, so honestly, I’m surprised.

And for some reason, Maria looks proud.

Now then, finding the target \<Hero> skill holder (unborn) is good and all, but the mother’s damage is frankly severe, and making her walk for a long time would be cruel.

So, using blind spots to avoid attention, we teleported to Castal’s mansion.

Once again, only Maria came along.

At the mansion, Lucea, the head maid, personally came out to greet us and took custody of the slaves.

She said it’s been a while since Master personally purchased slaves, so she’s fired up.

“Gather those with childbirth experience and knowledge, and prepare thoroughly.”

Unfortunately, I have no specialized knowledge about childbirth.

However, among my subordinates, there are those with childbirth experience, and even doctors (slaves).

If we heal the burns while providing nutrition, she should be able to give birth somewhat safely.

“Arrangements have already been made. All the maids here possess medical knowledge.”

Saying that, Lucea looked at the dozen or so maids standing behind her.

Lucea is too capable, leaving me with nothing to do.

“Please examine her.”

“Yes.”

Prompted by Lucea, one of the doctor maid slaves stepped forward, palpated the confused pregnant slave, and asked a question or two.

“Given her condition, the birth will likely be in about a month and a half to two months.”

“Huh?”

At this point, an unexpected situation arose.

“Is something the matter?”

“I said I’d find a \<Hero> holder within a month, but…”

If it takes at least a month and a half before birth, there’s no way that makes the deadline, right?

I have found the \<Hero> skill itself, but whether an unborn person can be considered a skill holder is a difficult judgment.

Seriously?

“Shall we open her?”

“Wait.”

The doctor maid slave said it without changing her expression, so I stopped her with a phrase I’d grown slightly fond of since using it at the slave trader.

No matter what, that is not an acceptable option.

And it’s absolutely not something a doctor should say.

“I’m not trying to twist logic. It just didn’t sit right with me.”

As I said, ‘it’s a difficult judgment’. Depending on how you think about it, you could say I ‘found’ one.

What didn’t sit right with me was that, despite seriously searching, I’d end up settling on such a half-baked conclusion. That I couldn’t clearly and definitively say, ‘I found one’.

Could it be…

“Is there still another one?”

The possibility I arrived at was that ‘there is another \<Hero> skill holder on Latis Island’.

No one ever said there was only one \<Hero> holder. That was just my assumption.

“…Sorry, but let me go back to Latis Island. Can I leave things to you?”

“Understood. Leave it to us.”

Leaving things to Lucea and the others, I used ‘Portal’ to teleport back to Latis Island.

“There might be another \<Hero> skill holder. So I think we should continue searching.”

“The fact that you even think of that possibility isn’t normal…”

When I shared my idea with everyone, Sakura said something hard to respond to.

Now that she mentions it, it might not be a normal way of thinking.

“If you’re going that far, wouldn’t it be faster to just look at the map and finish it?”

“That’s rejected.”

I flatly cut off Mio’s suggestion.

There’s hardly anything more uncool than giving up on a self-imposed challenge halfway through.

“Let’s lower the priority and search casually while sightseeing.”

It’s gray, but since we found one, there’s no reason to rush (we weren’t rushing to begin with).

All that’s left is to act on the assumption that there is another.

“Isn’t that basically the same as your original plan?”

“You could say that.”

Originally, it might have been sightseeing over searching.

…No, more like sightseeing >>> searching.

For now, I just want to ride the gondola soon.

After that, we resumed sightseeing on Latis Island plus searching for the \<Hero> skill.

“Hmm. Aside from slave traders, I can’t think of any other leads at all…”

“Even so, isn’t it a bit much to comb the entire city?”

We’d gone all-in on slave traders, so we hadn’t actually thought of any other candidates.

As Mio said, we’re currently enjoying walking through Latis Island’s streets while checking the status of every passerby.

However, there’s no sign of finding a \<Hero> skill holder at all.

As an aside, since visually checking everyone’s status is exhausting, I set it so I’d receive a notification if someone I saw had the \<Hero> skill.

Barely, I’m not using the map.

“It can’t be helped if nothing comes to mind.”

“To begin with, is there really a second one?”

“It’s normal for there not to be, at this point, isn’t it?”

No matter how good my luck is, I can’t make impossible things happen.

If the only \<Hero> holder is an unborn fetus, then regardless of my satisfaction, the darts have no choice but to point here. Because that’s the best outcome.

And if there is a \<Hero> skill holder other than the fetus, it’s easy to imagine that the darts would point there instead. Because that would be the best outcome.

“That aside, there sure are a lot of people.”

As mentioned before, there are so many people that status checking is a pain.

At the gondola reception, they mentioned it was tourist season, so that’s probably why.

“I heard while checking out the street stalls that various events will be held on this island starting tomorrow. I think that’s why there are so many people.”

Here, Mio dropped a bombshell.

“Seriously!? That’s not something to miss!”

“I knew Jin-kun would say that…”

Of course, there’s no way I’d miss events in a water city that sound fun.

But I don’t see any posters around town. How are they announcing it?

“Apparently, to avoid ruining the town’s scenery, outdoor posters are prohibited. You have to get pamphlets from the operations headquarters or sponsor shops.”

“It’s decided. Let’s go get one later.”

And so, the list of things to do on this island was updated.

Objective 1: Ride the gondola.

Objective 2: Enjoy Latis Island’s events.

Objective 3: Search for the second \<Hero>.

It feels like the priority of \<Hero> searching is dropping rapidly.

After that, we continued walking and searching, but found nothing.

“We haven’t found anything, and it’s getting late. Let’s head back soon.”

The sun was starting to set, so it was probably time to end the search.

The concept was to search casually, after all.

“When we get back, it’s the long-awaited dinner.”

We made sure to book an inn during the search (we won’t repeat the gondola failure).

It’s quite expensive due to tourist season pricing, but it’s nothing to worry about now.

《Food!》

“I hear it’s an inn with delicious food, so I’m looking forward to it.”

Apparently, they’ll serve Italian-style dishes befitting a Venice-like townscape.

I’m thinking of just defaulting to spaghetti.

We start heading back the way we came.

Right now, we’re at the island’s largest harbor.

We came to a maritime nation, after all. It’s only natural to want to look at the harbor and ships.

There weren’t any ships rivaling our ‘Queen Sakuya’, but there were many impressive ships befitting a maritime nation.

From the entrance of the harbor, we heard the noise of a dispute, different from the lively bustle of a tourist spot.

“Something’s noisy.”

Since we’re under the no-map restriction, I don’t know what’s going on.

I’m curious, so as we pass by, I approach a little to observe.

Is it trouble? Can I get involved? Hopefully it’s not noble-related.

There stood a boy about my age wearing expensive-looking clothes, several elves, and some burly men who appeared to be sailors, along with what seemed to be their capable representative.

It looked like a confrontation between the boy and elves versus the sailors.

Name: Aston de Pajel

Title: Prince of the Pajel Kingdom

So the one wearing expensive clothes is a prince…

Yeah, if it’s royalty or nobility related, that’s an automatic pass.

Especially after hearing from Alta that many royals and nobles are corrupt.

“You dare refuse my order!?”

The prince raised his voice.

His attitude was extremely overbearing.

“Even if it is an order from royalty, we cannot accept such an unreasonable demand. Without even giving a reason, to mobilize all ships and personnel of the Maritime Guild to search for a single elf woman is beyond unreasonable. And at this time of all times…”

“Silence! You will just search for Ashley!”

It was hard to ignore the content of the argument, so we had no choice but to slow our pace.

“If you don’t find her, I am ruined! And this country too… ghk!”

An elf standing beside him delivered a solid punch to the prince’s stomach.

It landed well, and the prince clutched his belly, his legs trembling.

Strange. The prince and the elves seemed to be on the same side…

“Say no more. Have you forgotten why we are accompanying you?”

“Ugh…”

It seems the elves were not the prince’s allies, but rather his overseers.

And since the prince was about to say something he shouldn’t, they shut him up.

The fact that they could silence him with a punch means the elves are in a significantly higher position…

Alta, could these people be?

A: As you suspect, it concerns the situation of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ Ashley. The elves are the clan that seals the Water Calamity Dragon.

I knew it…

What the prince was about to say was probably about this country being destroyed by the calamity dragon.

Conversely, that means the royal family of this country knows about the calamity dragon’s existence.

From his statement, ‘I am ruined’, Prince Aston must have done something.

Probably to Ashley.

As a result, Ashley ended up surviving on that island.

Alta, am I right?

A: Yes. That is correct. Would you like to hear the details?

No, there’s no need.

That prince looks arrogant, and you said many royals and nobles are corrupt, right?

I have not the slightest desire to get involved.

As originally planned, we’ll pass right by.

And so, we normally passed right by Prince Aston’s group and returned to the inn to eat Italian-style dinner.

“There’s more food than I expected.”

I muttered as I looked at the many dishes lined up before us.

Even a low estimate would put it at over ten servings.

There’s no way this is the amount for one man, three women, and two young girls.

“Yeah. I ordered assuming Sera-chan and Dora-chan would be here. They always help.”

Mio eats small portions, but for culinary research, she tries to eat as many different dishes as possible.

She orders a lot and eats a little of each, and Sera and Dora finish the leftovers, so nothing ever goes to waste.

“Leave it to us.”

《I’ll eat lots!》

Probably, more than half will be eaten by these two again.

And then, we eat.

“There are many dishes you can eat elsewhere, but the seafood really is good.”

“Yes… I really liked the squid ink spaghetti…”

Sakura took a liking to squid ink spaghetti.

I liked the vongole spaghetti.

It’s nothing but spaghetti.

For Japanese people, it’s the most familiar Italian-style dish.

“Indeed. This seppie nere con polenta is exquisite as well.”

“What?”

Mio chanted some kind of mysterious spell.

It’s probably the name of a dish, but it completely passed through my ears.

“It’s apparently a traditional Venetian dish. I remember seeing it when I researched foreign cuisines long ago. I doubt the Italian dish names would match perfectly, so it’s certain that someone from another world came here.”

“Hmm. If it’s Venetian cuisine, then perhaps a transfer from somewhere other than Japan?”

Not many Japanese people are knowledgeable about Venetian cuisine.

It would be far more natural if the person transferred from Venice.

A transfer from outside Japan would actually be the first case.

As an aside, if we define ‘foreigner’, there is precedent in the form of an international student.

“That’s possible, but since the menu includes miso soup, I can’t rule out the possibility that they’re Japanese.”

“Ah…”

On the menu, as if it were perfectly normal, was ‘Miso Soup 150G’.

Written carefully in kanji, this menu item significantly reduced the Italian vibe. It’s sufficient grounds to suspect a Japanese person.

“If you’re curious, why not ask Alta?”

“…I’ll ask after the search is over.”

Since I’m in the middle of a self-imposed challenge, I plan to avoid asking Alta as much as possible.

After it’s over, the big reveal can happen.

A: Leave it to me.

“Hm? …Master, look at that!”

Mio seemed to have found something and pointed at the inn’s wall.

There was a single poster hanging there.

‘Latis Island Cooking Competition: General Division. The winner will be invited to a luxury gondola tour.’

It must be one of the events mentioned earlier.

The competition is tomorrow. The application deadline is… just barely in time.

I see. I see.

“Mio, I’m counting on you!”

“Roger!”

Mio snapped to attention with a salute.

---

**AN:** Everyone should try searching for seppie nere con polenta too!

+++

## **188.5: The Water Princess Shrine Maiden**

**AN:** I am sorry, but this is not part of the main story. It is just a short side tale.

I think the next update (on the 10th) will also be difficult.

This is about the circumstances of the Princess Shrine Maiden.

---

Today was the academy graduation party.

The voice that rang out in what should have been my final memory of academy life carried words that were far too cruel for me.

“Ashley, I am breaking off our engagement.”

My prince said it to me with cold eyes.

Standing beside him was not me, but another woman.

What had I done wrong?

Was it because, as an offering to eternal suffering, I had wished for a fleeting happiness?

That was about ten years ago now.

“Ashley-sama, it is about time to head to Lady Angelica.”

The one who entered the room saying that was Anastasia, my guard and attendant.

“Understood. I will prepare at once.”

I placed a bookmark in the book I had been reading and set it on the desk.

Ever since I was young, my hobby had always been reading.

I read indiscriminately, but I especially loved stories, and my favorites above all were romance novels.

“You are reading that book again. Do you not get tired of it already?”

“No. This book is my favorite right now. No matter how many times I read it, I never tire of it.”

My absolute favorite was the story where the prince and princess are united. I had read it over and over again.

In truth, I had memorized the contents long ago, but reading it in a book and merely recalling it were completely different in terms of emotional immersion. Without reading it, I could not feel moved at all.

“When I am reading this book, that is when I am happiest.”

“Ashley-sama…”

Inside the book, I was a single, free girl.

Only inside the book could I be free. Free to fall in love.

“Come now, we cannot keep Lady Angelica waiting. Let us prepare.”

I wanted Lady Angelica to live as peacefully as possible.

I hurriedly prepared myself and headed to Lady Angelica.

Lady Angelica lived in a heavily guarded castle.

Only a limited number of people were allowed to enter freely, and aside from me, the successor, there were only a few.

Anyone else had to undergo extremely thorough inspections.

No one other than guards and maids ever approached Lady Angelica.

Because they spoke only the bare minimum, there was always silence around her.

Even now, the only sound was that of our footsteps.

“Oh, Ashley. Thank you for coming.”

“It has been some time, Lady Angelica.”

Lady Angelica was my mentor, my second mother, and someone to whom I owed respect and affection.

“I truly wish I could speak with you normally, Ashley, but there is something I must tell you first.”

“What is it?”

When Lady Angelica summoned me, it was usually either about duties or casual conversation.

If it was not casual conversation, then it must be about duties.

Lady Angelica remained silent for a while, shed tears, and then said this.

“…I intend to end my duty in ten years.”

“!”

Both Anastasia beside me and I ourselves gasped.

“I thought I could endure a little longer, but it seems the burden was greater than I expected. I will squeeze out the last of my strength and endure ten years. But beyond that, I cannot. I am truly sorry, Ashley.”

I had heard that there was a very long gap between Lady Angelica’s birth and my own.

Her mind was already at its limit.

“Thank you… for your consideration…”

For my sake as a child, she said she would endure ten more years.

A mixture of deep gratitude and a trace of resentment welled up, and tears spilled from my eyes as well.

Naturally, we could not have a normal conversation, and I returned to my room for the day.

“Ashley-sama, please keep your heart strong. We still have ten years. Now that you are formally the successor, most wishes can be granted. Please ask for anything you desire within those ten years.”

“…”

Anastasia encouraged me as I fell silent.

But right now, I could not bring myself to think of anything.

“I will sleep now…”

“Ashley-sama…”

I thought I had prepared myself for this eventuality, but seeing it in reality was overwhelming.

Before I sank into a bottomless swamp of thought, I decided to sleep for today.

The next day, despite just waking up, my eyes were strangely clear.

When I sat up in bed, Anastasia was sitting on a chair, watching me.

“…Good morning.”

“A-Ashley-sama, good morning. What would you like for dinner?”

I felt like I had heard something strange.

I had just woken up. Dinner?

“Do you not mean breakfast?”

“It is already evening. You rested for an entire day.”

“…”

It had been far more shocking than I realized.

Still, thanks to sleeping well, my head felt clear.

Yesterday I had been pessimistic, but it was not all bad. That is what I decided to think.

“Anastasia. Those who perform the duty are granted every possible preferential treatment, are they not?”

“Yes. Within the country, any wish may be granted. As for matters abroad, the country will make overtures, so we cannot guarantee outcomes…”

“That is enough. There is one wish I want granted.”

“Please command anything.”

And so, I picked up my beloved book from the desk and conveyed my wish to Anastasia.

A few days later, my wish was granted.

“This is His Highness Aston, the First Prince of the Kingdom of Pajel.”

“Nice to meet you. I am Ashley.”

“The pleasure is mine.”

Before me stood a prince with silky blond hair and dignified blue eyes.

“Ashley-sama will become Prince Aston’s fiancée. As the future king, please escort the princess.”

“Yes, understood. Please, your hand.”

I took the prince’s hand and smiled.

It felt as though I had stepped into a story.

Though it was my own wish, I had not expected things to go so perfectly.

My wish was, “For the remaining ten years, become a prince’s fiancée and attend academy life.”

It was a pleasant miscalculation that there happened to be a prince of my age with an ideal appearance among the royalty.

At worst, I had thought it would be fine as long as our enrollment periods overlapped to some extent.

…I understood better than anyone that it was a farce.

I simply wanted to become like a character in a story.

To love a prince, and be loved by him. I wanted to play the role of such a happy girl.

Even if we became engaged, we could not actually marry.

There was no way I could risk bearing children.

It was truly just ten years of make-believe.

Even so, I wished for it.

With my own “story” as support, I resolved myself to endure eternity. That was all.

“Aston-sama, the weather is lovely today. Shall we go for a walk together?”

“Aston-sama, I baked some sweets. Let us eat them together.”

“Aston-sama, please escort me at the party.”

From then on, the prince became the center of my actions.

By spending as much time with him as possible, I averted my eyes from the painful future.

The prince always accompanied me with a smile.

Because I had asked Anastasia to limit candidates to princes who understood the engagement was a farce and would go along with it, I believed I could spend the promised ten years happily.

According to Anastasia, the prince also received proper compensation.

Calculation was fine. I did not care about his true feelings. As long as he gave me fleeting happiness.

After entering the academy, the distance between the prince and me grew slightly.

Naturally, our classes were arranged to be the same, but because the curriculum differed between boys and girls, it could not be helped.

We spoke in class, and he escorted me at events, so I had no complaints.

However, people gradually began to gather around the prince.

In contrast, I had no one I could call a close friend.

I was clearly different from the others, so I thought that was inevitable.

Therefore, I had no dissatisfaction. This was only natural.

The situation changed about a month before the graduation party.

I was summoned by Lady Angelica and headed to the castle.

“Lady Angelica!”

“…Ashley. Th-thank you for coming…”

Lady Angelica was utterly exhausted and collapsed on the floor.

Around her lay scattered strands of her long hair, as if she had torn it out herself.

“I cannot go on anymore… I am sorry I could not endure ten years for you…”

“Please do not worry about that. I am already prepared and resolved.”

For the past nine years, while spending time with the prince, I had also been preparing for the succession.

At first, it had been terrible.

When I first accompanied Lady Angelica on her duty, I cried and screamed disgracefully, vomited, and fell into madness.

Without an exceptionally strong heart, it was impossible to endure.

As I repeated it and grew accustomed, I no longer became as unsightly as at first.

Of course, that did not mean it was easy. Pain was pain.

The only reason I endured was because of the prince’s existence.

My resolve was the resolve to become a sacrifice to protect the prince, carrying our memories in my heart.

Having come this far, all that remained was to perform the succession ritual.

If there was anything painful, it was parting with Lady Angelica.

“Thank you… Then, we will begin the transfer…”

“Yes.”

Together with Lady Angelica, who stood up while swaying slightly, we performed the succession ritual.

Just as I had heard, it seemed that supernatural power was also transferred.

Such power was useless while living in this castle.

“Well then… I will go now… I am sorry, but please wait a little while before handing over the castle…”

“Yes. Thank you for your long years of service…”

After exchanging final words, I left the castle.

For some time afterward, the castle was in turmoil, but there was nothing more I could do.

During that turbulent period, I was made to rest from the academy.

Honestly, academy credits meant nothing to me.

And it is not boasting, but I had never relinquished the top rank in grades. I more than qualified for graduation.

“Anastasia, please. Let me attend the graduation party at least.”

“Ashley-sama, that is impossible. You cannot be exposed to even the slightest danger anymore.”

I had graduation qualifications, yet I was not even allowed to attend the graduation party…

I had already had this exchange with Anastasia many times, but this time I had a trump card I thought of yesterday. With this, I should not lose.

“But only citizens of this country attend the graduation party, correct? And within the country, all wishes are granted, right? If I wish for it, my safety is assured, is it not?”

“Ugh…”

Anastasia made a face as if struck at a sore spot.

“In a country that cannot even guarantee safety for a single day, I think I would continue to feel uneasy.”

“Th-that is…”

“It seems my term may become shorter than expected…”

“I-I understand! I will make arrangements so that you can go to the academy for just one day!”

As with Lady Angelica, my peace of mind was prioritized above all.

It ended up sounding like a threat, but this was something I could not give up.

With this, it seemed I would be able to attend the graduation party, just as the prince’s letter said.

On the day of the graduation party.

Escorted by the prince, I arrived at the party venue.

Anastasia and the other guards waited outside the venue.

This, too, was something I had forced.

There were many conditions: I could only attend for one hour, I must not eat any food, and so on, but Anastasia and the others must have conceded to their limits.

Additionally, strict inspections of belongings were imposed on all attendees.

Only food that could be eaten by hand was served, and no knives or similar items were provided.

As for magic, it did not work on me, so that was not an issue.

This should have greatly reduced the danger.

I was sorry to the other participants, but please forgive me. In exchange, I would protect you.

“Ashley, shall we dance?”

“Yes, Aston-sama.”

And so, we danced our final dance.

Yes, this was the final dance.

After dancing for a while, we decided to chat in a corner of the hall.

It was a space for those who wished to spend time quietly.

It was considered bad manners to speak to anyone there.

“Ashley, there is something I wish to tell you.”

“What is it?”

The moment I asked, the prince’s expression hardened.

“I hate you.”

“Eh?”

For a moment, I did not understand what he was saying.

“Despite my being busy studying to become king, you always followed me around. You were a nuisance.”

The prince had always accompanied me with a smile.

If he had hidden his true feelings, there would have been no problem.

“I dislike sweets, yet every time you brought tasteless confections.”

The prince had said they were delicious and eaten them.

If he had hidden his true feelings, there would have been no problem.

“As children it was one thing, but now there is too much difference in our heights. It looks less like escorting and more like babysitting. Yet you asked for escort without understanding that. It was disgraceful.”

The prince had always gently taken my hand.

If he had hidden his true feelings, there would have been no problem.

“At times, you came to see me with a terribly haggard face. Frankly, it was creepy. I hated even seeing your face.”

The prince did not know about my duty.

If he had hidden his true feelings, there would have been no problem.

“Though I attend the academy without guards despite being a prince, only you were always followed by dangerous-looking guards. It was overbearing and hindered enjoying academy life. Even when I tried to keep my distance, you came close regardless.”

There were moments when the prince had briefly frowned.

There were times when his true feelings could not be fully hidden.

“If you disliked it that much, you should have refused from the start…”

The original request had been for a prince who would go along with it knowing it was a farce.

“I accepted only because I was told the position of next king would be secured. I did not think you would be such a troublesome partner. When I later asked my father to dissolve the engagement, he refused outright.”

Dissolving the engagement would have been impossible in many senses.

This was something I learned after the engagement, but the current king and first queen adored the prince, the first prince, and wished to make him the next king.

Whoever played the role of my fiancé would gain my clan as a backer.

They likely intended to use this farce as an opportunity to make the first prince the next king.

However, if the engagement were dissolved, my clan would see the first prince as an enemy.

Even royalty could not make an enemy of my clan and remain safe.

Naturally, dissolving the engagement could never be approved.

…If that was the case, I wanted him to be told to hide his true feelings until the end.

“I have endured until now, and I know that in just one more year I will be freed from you. But I cannot endure even that one year.”

Had he hated me that much?

“I have someone I truly love, not a fake like you.”

“Ugh…”

Whether from the shock of his words or not, I was struck by intense dizziness and collapsed on the spot.

Looking closely, I was not the only one who had fallen.

The people in the party hall were collapsing one after another.

In the blink of an eye, the only ones still standing were the prince and the girl who approached him.

“Am I late?”

“Aria, I have been waiting. …Now the cast is complete.”

The girl called Aria stood beside the prince and naturally linked arms with him.

She was a beautiful girl, with an oddly alluring charm.

“What is… this…?”

“This is a ritual for me to be freed from the shackles called you. How long I have awaited this day…”

With cold eyes, the prince spoke a fatal line to me.

“Ashley, I am breaking off our engagement.”

Ah, if this were a romance novel, this would be the worst bad ending.

Am I not even allowed to dream of happiness?

“So, at last, I can be with you?”

“Yes, my beloved Aria. Soon our wish will be fulfilled.”

The two embraced right before my eyes.

Please, make the bad ending stop already.

However, my bad ending still had more to come.

With eyes different from the cold ones before, eyes that looked down on me, the prince spoke.

“Now then, you have likely noticed, but only the three of us here are conscious. This phenomenon was caused by a secret magic tool Aria possessed.”

“Yes. It is a precious item that induces sleep over a wide area. Preparation is very difficult, but if it activates successfully, no one will wake for an hour. Your guards were asleep as well.”

“Naturally, we can prevent it. You were restrained only enough to keep you from moving while we talk.”

And then I realized that there was no one here to protect me.

“I am sorry. As long as you live, you are in the way.”

“We will kill you here and then pretend to be asleep. It will be a perfect plan disguised as a bandit attack.”

Saying that, the prince took a sword from the blind spot of a wall.

“Bringing weapons was forbidden, but it seems the venue inspection was lax. It was worth waiting until the last moment to lure you in.”

Had he invited me here intending to kill me from the start?

Because the prince wished it, I forced my way here to the graduation party.

Something inside me collapsed with a rattling sound.

“This is our eternal farewell. Do you have any last words? I will not pass them on, but I will listen.”

The prince, no, Aston, drew his sword and raised it.

In truth, Aston’s actions had no meaning.

If I died, this world would perish.

If I survived, Aston would be executed.

Either way, Aston’s wish would never be fulfilled.

Then, which was better for me?

To die here, or to live and fulfill my duty?

Duty? For what? For whom?

Having lost my emotional support, I had no strength left to endure the painful duty.

But if I fled here and sought help from my clan, I would be unable to escape the duty.

Regardless of my will.

Then, was it better to die here?

If I were to taste eternal suffering anyway, dying here might not be so bad.

I gave up and tried to close my eyes.

… Is it really fine to die like this?

No. Absolutely not.

It is fine if I die. It is not fine, but in this situation, I will treat it as fine.

If I do not perform the duty, I would not live very long anyway.

But I cannot tolerate dying before Aston.

I cannot stand the thought of Aston being satisfied even for a moment.

I do not want to die until Aston dies disgracefully.

Then what must be done is clear.

“I am flowing water.”

“…? What are you saying?”

Aston made a puzzled face.

“Flowing water does not remain in one place. It continues to move. Even if poison is poured into it, eventually clear water flows again. I am the same. …Do not underestimate my recovery!”

“What!?”

I stood up and immediately activated magic.

“‘Call Element’ Aqua Wind!”

What appeared was a maiden with the body of flowing water.

This was a rare spirit possessing two attributes, water and wind, inherited from Lady Angelica.

Lady Angelica had called her Aida.

I am sorry, Lady Angelica.

I will use the power I inherited from you to protect the world, for the exact opposite purpose.

“W-What is this!?”

“A spirit… To think you commanded a spirit of such power…”

Facing the astonished pair, I was enveloped by the spirit.

With the spirit’s power, I could likely repel the prince.

But the girl called Aria was unfathomable. I did not feel I could win by fighting head-on.

So, I would flee.

With all my strength, I shouted.

“…Let this country be destroyed! …Let this world be destroyed!”

“I will not let you escape!”

As I turned, Aston swung his sword, but it was blocked by Aida.

“Gh…!?”

Immediately after, something pierced the maiden of flowing water, and the pain reached me as well.

Could this be… a curse?

Looking back as I fled, Aria was in the posture of having just thrown something.

On her face was an uncontrollable look of delight.

I burst out of the party hall and ran without thinking.

No, not ran. I flew through the air.

Aida, being a spirit who governed wind as well, could continue flying as long as magic power lasted.

Fortunately, or perhaps not, Aria did not pursue me.

However, I soon realized that thought was mistaken.

There had been no need to pursue.

Because the curse I had just received had the effect of dispersing magic power.

The curse affected not only me, but Aida as well.

Rather, I was caught up in the curse Aida received.

While I could endure it, if Aida’s magic power continued to disperse, she would not be able to maintain her existence.

If Aida disappeared and my magic power ran out, I would have no means to fight.

To heal Aida, I needed to flee to somewhere rich in magic power and safe…

Was there such a convenient place?

I desperately recalled the map of this country, but could not think of one.

My clan was long-lived and had excellent memories.

But that was not a blessing. It was also a curse. Because even what one wished to forget could not be forgotten.

In particular, the pain of the duty not fading was fatal.

I had heard that all predecessors took their own lives after completing the duty.

Lady Angelica had already been summoned to heaven.

That is it. Aida was a spirit Lady Angelica had met when she was young.

Spirits originally favor places rich in magic power. If it was the place Aida had originally resided, recovery should be possible.

“Aida! Take me to the place where you were raised!”

“!”

Aida seemed to understand my intent and changed course.

According to my memory, the sea ahead was an area with many uninhabited islands.

I arrived at Aida’s birthplace.

Aida’s magic power was nearly depleted. It was truly at the limit.

It was an uninhabited island near the border, avoided by all due to lack of resources.

However, it was rich in magic power, so Aida devoted herself fully to recovery.

The curse placed on us was not permanent. Its effect gradually weakened, and as the recovery exceeded the dispersion, Aida slowly began to improve.

While not as severely affected as Aida, I had also lost a considerable amount of magic power.

For a while, even using magic would be difficult.

I was confident in my recovery ability, but that applied only to things that healed naturally.

I was ill-suited to curses that did not heal naturally.

Moreover, my magic power recovery rate was average, making it even worse.

In a sense, I might suffer longer-lasting effects than Aida, who could absorb magic power.

For the time being, I decided to hide here.

Perhaps in a month, destruction would appear. In two months, this world would end.

After witnessing Aston and the country perish, I would end my own life.

If my clan judged it truly dangerous, they would evacuate into the sky using a secret treasure, so they would not perish.

I hated the duty, but I did not wish for Anastasia and the others to die.

Now then, as for my current appearance, it would be fair to say I was half-naked.

Specifically, I wore only a single pair of silk pants.

On an uninhabited island overgrown with trees, a dress was nothing but a hindrance.

I removed it upon arrival.

Thus, a single girl lost civilization.

What would Anastasia say if she saw me?

Aside from that, setting up a living environment was not particularly difficult.

Though my magic power was greatly reduced, I could still use minimal magic, and I had knowledge of flora and fauna from illustrated books.

It was also a great help that Aida had some knowledge of this island.

There was a hut to shelter from rain and wind, and some food stockpiled.

In the first place, rain and wind were not harmful to me anyway…

If there was a problem, it was the threat of monsters.

When Aida lived on this island, there had apparently been extremely dangerous monsters.

I had not encountered any yet, and it was unclear if they still lived, but it was better not to be optimistic.

Optimistic or pessimistic, when you encounter something, you encounter it.

One week after arriving on the island, I finally encountered that monster.

By the time I noticed all signs of life had vanished from the surroundings, it was already too late.

“This is… not an opponent I can handle…”

It was a chimera-like monster, as if various monsters had been fused together.

Its most prominent feature was its tiger-like head. It also had bird wings and plant-like vines.

Its rank as a living being was clearly different. No wonder other creatures fled.

Even if Aida and I were in perfect condition, I felt we could not win.

And now I was weakened. What could I do?

It had already completely locked onto me and was approaching leisurely.

It must understand that I had no means of escape.

Or perhaps it planned to attack the moment I tried to flee.

It seemed I would not get to see Aston’s manner of death…

That alone was regrettable.

Perhaps because I had already given up on life, I did not feel like struggling.

I understood better than anyone that struggling would be meaningless.

There was no prince who would come to save me at a time like this.

The ferocious beast continued to approach leisurely.

The tiger head opened its mouth, revealing sharp fangs.

I gave up, closed my eyes…

“Gyaa!?”

The beast leaped back violently.

-Don!!!-

The next moment, something was stuck in the spot where the beast had been.

“Kyah!”

From the impact, I could not keep my footing and fell backward.

When I raised my face, what was there was…

“A slime?”

It was an unusually transparent slime.

Where had this slime come from?

“Grururu…”

However, unlike my carefree reaction, the beast was clearly frightened.

This slime did not look that strong, but…

“Guaa!”

Still frightened, the beast leaped as if in desperation.

I did not think I had looked away.

Yet when I noticed, the beast had been split cleanly in two vertically.

The beast collapsed with a thud.

“Eh…?”

I had seen nothing.

An opponent I thought I could not defeat had been killed without resistance.

Though it did not look strong, this slime was extraordinarily powerful.

Then, the slime jumped toward me.

“Kyaa!”

Even having accepted death, it was startling when something came suddenly.

However, what came to me was not death.

The slime landed on my head and swayed gently.

It was lighter than it looked and caused almost no burden.

The part touching me was soft and pleasant.

This was clearly an action without malice.

If it had intended to kill me, it could have done so without jumping.

Since it could instantly kill the beast without moving, killing me would have been even easier.

There was only one conclusion.

This slime had saved me.

“Aha, hahaha…”

A dry laugh escaped my mouth at the situation.

I had never imagined that, betrayed by a prince and facing imminent death by monsters, a knight would appear.

Taken alone, it sounded like a novel.

But if that knight was a slime, it could never become a romance novel.

In the first place, being betrayed by the prince made a romance novel impossible…

From then on, one slime joined our life.

The slime’s usual place was on my head, but sometimes it would wander off and hunt monsters or beasts.

While not as dangerous as the ferocious beast, there were quite a few monsters that could be dangerous if caught off guard.

Just having the slime there made me feel strangely at ease.

Perhaps even more so than when I was protected by my clan.

The slime did not speak, so we could not communicate through words.

But its actions spoke volumes.

“I will protect you.”

---

**AN:** This is a trendy engagement-annulment story.

It is the story of a hero who saves a girl betrayed by her prince and driven to despair about the world.

Yes, that is not wrong.

+++

## **189: The Cooking Competition and the Championship**

**AN:** A style where the result is written right into the title.

It will probably switch to 1/10 next time.

---

The Latis Island Cooking Competition.

It is an annual event held once a year on Latis Island at this time of year.

It is also one of the main attractions of the festival week that Latis Island prides itself on.

Incidentally, festival week refers to a week-long celebration during which many events, including this competition, are held.

Looking back, the liveliness throughout the town did have a pre-festival atmosphere.

The cooking competition is divided into a shop division and a general division.

The shop division is limited to those who run a shop, whether on Latis Island or elsewhere.

Apparently, only the main round is open to the public, while the preliminaries are held without spectators.

The general division is open to anyone.

However, since there is a fairly steep entry fee, it is a bit hard to participate just for fun. Basically, only those who intend to win enter.

More specifically, things like cooks looking for employment. It apparently makes for good self-promotion.

The general division is held over two days, with preliminaries and a main round.

Today is the preliminary round, with about forty teams participating. From here, they will be narrowed down to ten teams.

I glossed over it earlier, but as I said “teams”, it is a two-person team competition.

Mio could not participate alone, so she called in Nino, a cooking maid, as support.

Nino is a veteran cooking maid and Mio’s first disciple.

Because she is a hobbit, she is small, so when the two of them are together, they just look like a child helping out.

However, her actual skill is not something to underestimate.

She does not run a shop, but she is skilled enough to be summoned to the royal castle of Castal.

Now then, let me explain the content of the preliminary round.

Participants cook food at stalls and serve it to general spectators. Rankings are then decided by votes from those spectators.

In this round, the required dishes are ones that can be made in relatively large quantities, are easy to eat, and are delicious.

After deciding to participate and reading the rules, the dish Mio chose was, of course…

“Yes! Another batch of our special croquettes is done frying!”

One of Mio’s specialty dishes. Everyone’s favorite croquettes.

If you listen to the surrounding voices, you can immediately tell that everyone loves them. See?

“I’ll pay any amount! Hurry up and let me eat!”

“The smell is insane! I can’t take it anymore!”

Everyone loves them (deadpan).

Naturally, a long line has formed at the stall.

“Please don’t push, yes! There are plenty, so please, yes!”

Nino is shouting at the top of her lungs, but her voice is drowned out by the surrounding clamor.

“Please! Let me eat just one more!”

“One per person, yes! You already ate earlier, yes!”

“No way!”

Under the rules, there is no benefit to letting one person eat more than one.

Even though they announce one per person, people asking for seconds are endless.

“As always, Mio’s cooking is crazy.”

As an aside, since we are considered related parties, we are waiting near Mio’s stall.

Only the two participants are allowed to cook, but helping with things like carrying supplies is allowed.

“We are used to it, but apparently for those without resistance, it has an addictive quality.”

Sera said something I could not ignore.

What is that? First I have heard of it.

“There is no way she is using some kind of dangerous drug, right?”

“Do you think Mio would ever do something like that with cooking?”

“No, not at all. Rather, anyone who would do something like that should not even be called a cook.”

Mio is more sincere about cooking than anyone.

Otherwise, I would never entrust her with being our traveling cook.

“Of course, Mio would never do such a thing. …Unfortunately, however, it seems that some self-proclaimed cooks of the kind you mentioned have mixed in.”

“Ugh… You are right…”

Since we are under a no-map restriction, I only checked the dishes I could see, and discovered that some of them contained prohibited addictive substances.

It is shocking that someone would be stupid enough to do something like that at a famous cooking competition.

“They probably thought it would be fine if they did not get caught, but unfortunately, it does not seem to be that simple. Please look over there.”

In the direction Sera pointed were several dogs.

After sniffing the air, they began barking at customers eating the offending dishes.

“I see. A simple and easy-to-understand countermeasure.”

“Oh, they are being caught…”

Where Sakura was looking, adventurers who appeared to have been hired by the competition staff were in the middle of suppressing the self-proclaimed cooks’ stalls.

The self-proclaimed cooks were captured without resistance by the burly adventurers.

Have dogs detect prohibited substances and adventurers capture them. A simple and effective measure.

As an aside, the dogs did not react to Mio’s cooking.

…No, that is wrong. They did react. They were drooling heavily while staring at Mio’s food.

Sorry. Since you are not customers, there is no benefit to letting you eat.

While I was looking away, the big commotion had already ended.

“The problem is the customers who ate the dishes with prohibited substances.”

“How awful.”

“That is the worst…”

Sera and Sakura show their disgust openly.

After checking with a status check, the prohibited substances fed by the self-proclaimed cooks turned out to be highly addictive, and if not dealt with early, would leave lasting damage to the brain.

It was the worst possible choice, focused only on immediate victory.

“Well then…”

I watched for a while, but although the competition staff gathered the victims, it seemed they had no countermeasure prepared for the substances used this time. Even the medical staff were at a loss.

Naturally, I have no obligation to help victims of drug use.

However, after Mio worked so hard, I do not like the idea of the competition being tainted.

Mio won the cooking competition. She rode the gondola as a prize.

There are people whose lives were ruined because of the competition. There are people suffering from aftereffects.

That would leave a bad taste.

“I am going to step out for a bit. So I can enjoy sightseeing in this city in a good mood.”

“Master, should you not say it is for the sake of the victims?”

“I am going to step out for a bit. To save the pitiful victims.”

Sera’s line sounded more correct, so I immediately corrected myself.

“I will accompany you.”

Taking Maria with me, I headed for the competition headquarters.

It took longer than expected, and I was able to return to everyone about ten minutes after leaving.

“I am back.”

“Welcome back, Jin-kun…”

“So, how did you deal with it?”

As I took out pills from \<Infinite Storage>, I explained.

“First, I mixed in a secret medicine made by Midori.”

Midori the dryad can make various secret medicines.

Making a specific antidote for addictive drugs is child’s play for her.

“You fed them this…?”

“How did you explain it?”

“Explain? There is no way I would do something so troublesome. I just did this… like this.”

I flick a pill straight up with my finger and catch it in my mouth as it falls.

“You put it in their mouths without saying anything!?”

“That is forceful…”

《That, do it to Dora too!》

I take out another pill and flick it toward Dora, who opens her mouth.

It goes right in, and Dora happily munches on the pill.

“The troublesome part was that there was one person who absolutely would not open their mouth.”

Because of that one person, it took nearly ten minutes.

“In the end, I had invisible Maria pinch their nose and mouth shut. After waiting a bit, we only released the mouth.”

Unable to breathe, they had to take a big breath through their opened mouth.

Then, aiming for that open mouth, we shot the pill in.

“Is that not a bit too forceful…?”

“Master, you sometimes resort to incomprehensible acts of violence, do you not?”

The two look exasperated.

There was nothing I could do.

That was just the first thing that came to mind…

“And thus, the victims were safely freed from the curse of the drugs. All is well that ends well.”

“You really wrapped it up forcefully.”

“There is nothing more to say. More importantly, how are Mio and the others doing?”

Well, just looking at the long line, it is obvious to anyone that things are going well.

“As you can see, Mio and the others are doing well. It is practically certain they will pass the preliminaries in first place.”

《Mio is the best!》

“Since using the map is forbidden, we cannot tell the exact number of votes, but I think there is no doubt…”

Under the rules of this competition, voting can be done at any time.

The ballot boxes are already filled with a huge number of ballots.

If we used a map, we could see the exact numbers, but maps are currently forbidden.

Besides, I have no intention of peeking at the results before they are announced in this kind of competition…

After some time passed, the end of the preliminary round drew near.

“It is about time.”

“Even so, the crowd is not thinning out…”

Mio’s line still has no end.

“What happens when time is up?”

“At that point, receiving food will be prohibited, and once people finish eating, they will vote.”

“To add to that, Jin-sama, it seems you cannot vote for a dish you have not finished eating.”

Putting Sera and Maria’s explanations together, it seems important to hand out the food even at the last moment and make sure it is completely eaten.

“Nino-chan! Close the line!”

“Yes!”

As we were talking, there was movement at Mio’s stall.

Nino took out a panel reading “Sold Out” and had the last person in line hold it.

She then immediately counted the number of people in line.

“Mio-san! Eighty-nine people, yes!”

“That is more than I thought. …Well, fine. Last spurt!”

“Yes!”

It seems they intend to make enough for everyone in line.

It would be sad to line up and not get anything.

As for people who failed to line up, they should know the rules, so that is their own responsibility.

Five minutes later.

“The competition is now over. No further food may be served. Those who have finished eating, please vote promptly.”

The announcement echoed through the venue.

“Safe!”

“That was just barely, yes!”

Mio and the others handed croquettes to the final person ten seconds before the announcement.

The speed of their cooking was incredible. I could never imitate it (I cannot cook to begin with).

“Mio, Nino, good work.”

I went over to them, praised them, and helped clean up the stall.

“Man, that was pretty tiring.”

“I am exhausted, yes.”

No matter how high your status is, if you act seriously, you get tired.

It is also proof that Mio and the others were that serious about cooking.

“…So, do we not need to deal with those guys?”

What I pointed to were the people gathering in front of the stall being cleaned up.

“There is no point dealing with them. I have no intention of leaving Master.”

“Of course, yes!”

The purpose of those gathered was to recruit Mio and Nino.

In this competition, recruiting participants during the competition period (except during matches) is not prohibited.

Seeing that line and actually eating the food, it is no wonder recruitment would concentrate.

However, Mio and Nino have not the slightest intention of accepting any offers.

In place of the tired two, Sera, the most intimidating, is driving them away.

“Besides, I cannot imagine anyone preparing a better cooking environment than Master’s, though I cannot say it loudly.”

“That is true, yes. The ingredients and tools are top-class, and highly motivated cooks gather there, yes. I do not think there is often an environment better than that, yes.”

I do not really feel it, but apparently our cooking environment is high-level.

“You look surprised, but Master’s existence is the biggest reason, you know? Everyone is doing their best for Master.”

“We are doing our best, yes!”

Because I am particular about food, my subordinates give it their all.

Yes, that makes sense.

While we were talking, Sera returned after finishing driving away the recruiters.

“…Phew, there were quite a lot of persistent ones.”

There must have been many troublesome types. Sera does not look pleased.

“Ah, Sera-chan, thank you.”

“Thank you very much, yes.”

“No need to worry. …However, there may be a bit of trouble.”

According to Sera, among the recruiters was an envoy of a noble from this country.

Judging by Sera’s reaction, she did not get a good impression, and in the worst case, they might resort to forceful means.

“I see. A noble’s forceful recruitment, huh…”

“Master? Why do you look so villainous? It is scary, you know? Seriously.”

Mio is a bit scared.

It seems my emotions showed on my face. Calm down, me.

“It goes without saying, but if they come with forceful means, I will show no mercy.”

“Well, that does sound like something you would say, Master.”

“You really hate noble-related trouble.”

I hate it very much.

“If it is only somewhat forceful, using the identification we got from Tooru and the others might be an option.”

“Oh right, we had something like that… If it can be settled peacefully, that would be best…”

Sakura is kind…

“However, if they go beyond what is acceptable, I will crush them loudly.”

《Loud is better!》

“Dora-chan… You are starting to resemble Jin-kun, you know…”

Sakura: moderate faction. Dora: radical faction.

I am feeling uneasy about Dora’s education these days.

If I am told she is becoming like me, I cannot even argue.

One hour after the match ended, the tally was completed and the results announced.

Without any major upsets, just as most expected, Mio and Nino took first place.

As an aside, during the review session for the first day, the team that used drugs was publicly announced.

The team members will apparently be punished as criminals.

The only good news in this matter was that the victims were safe.

Also, though we were on guard, there was no forceful nonsense from nobles that day.

Whether they gave up honestly or are plotting something, I cannot tell while maps are forbidden.

However, Alta knows.

A: …

And so, after a night passed, the day of the main round of the cooking competition arrived.

Unlike the preliminaries, the judges in the main round are not tourists, but judges decided in advance.

Naturally, they are a group of people with discerning palates who are picky about food.

They will also serve as judges in tomorrow’s shop division.

There is a reason the order of the competition is general division first, then shop division.

To put it bluntly, the general division is a warm-up for the shop division.

The logic is that even if there are one or two skilled cooks, they cannot match dishes made by an entire shop working together. Well, I understand what they are saying.

The rules of the main round are also simple.

Ten judges each have one vote. They eat the dishes from the ten teams and vote for the one they found the most delicious. In the case of a tie, only the tied first-place teams remain, and a re-vote is held.

In the main round, all ingredients are prepared in advance, so no backstage support during cooking is needed.

Therefore, we watched the competition purely as spectators. We used the related-party tickets distributed to Mio and the others for our seats.

“So, what kind of dish will Mio and the others make?”

“Oh my, Master, did you not hear?”

“Did you hear, Sera? Mio told me to look forward to it.”

When told “look forward to it”, there is no way to press further.

“Yes, I heard normally. …But let us keep it a secret here.”

“That is fine.”

After half-listening to the competition explanation, Mio and the others began cooking.

The first thing they took out was…

《Could that be a harpy egg?》

《Yes, that is correct.》

Harpy eggs are classified as ultra-luxury ingredients.

Since it is not something to talk about openly, I confirmed with Sera via telepathy.

Then Mio and the others took out ingredients like flour and milk one after another.

《Are the other ingredients rare as well?》

《The flour, oil, and seasonings are made in the labyrinth. They are sold on the market as luxury goods. The milk is from a combat goat, and the fruit is from a spirit treant.》

《Sorry, what are the last two?》

It is a bit much to suddenly list ingredients I have never heard of…

《They are ultra-luxury ingredients known as the Five Great Demon Foods.》

According to Sera, there are rare monster-derived ingredients known as the Five Great Demon Foods in this world.

· Birdman eggs

· Combat goat milk

· Spirit treant fruit

· Rainbow fish flesh

· Feather dragon meat

A feather dragon snuck in there…

《Of these, the ones you can obtain without killing the monster are eggs, milk, and fruit.》

《Oh, I see. So they tamed them.》

At that point, I understood Mio and the others’ idea a bit.

By taming the monsters, they can continuously procure those three ingredients.

《Exactly. Mio tamed a combat goat and a spirit treant without telling you, Master. Then she began researching dishes combining those three ingredients.》

Apparently, she gave up on combining them with the remaining two ingredients.

Mio cannot see feather dragons as food, so that is out of the question.

Rainbow fish cannot be obtained continuously, and there was no dish that could combine eggs, milk, and fruit with it. At least, none that Mio knows.

《The problem was the other ingredients and seasonings. We could not find anything on the market that would not pale in comparison when combined with those three. So in the end, we had to rely on the labyrinth.》

Beyond the fiftieth floor of the labyrinth are large-scale fields.

There, after repeated trial and error in selective breeding, they succeeded in producing high-quality ingredients that do not pale in comparison even to the Five Great Demon Foods.

As always, the labyrinth is convenient.

《Today is the day to show off those results!》

Sera is unusually fired up.

She is probably involved in that area of work as well.

“Are Mio and the others making crepes, by any chance?”

Seeing Mio spreading batter in a frying pan, I realized it.

Seeing Nino making cream beside her, there is no doubt.

Incidentally, this is content we can talk about normally, so we stopped using telepathy.

“That is correct. It is a simple dish, so even if we kept it secret, you would figure it out from the cooking method.”

Sera smiles wryly at how quickly it was revealed.

“To choose a dessert for a famous cooking competition is quite a bold move.”

Looking at the other participants, there is no team making dessert.

“According to my research, no one who served dessert has ever won.”

“If they win with that, it will stand out.”

“Yes. However, when top-class ingredients are cooked by cooks with top-class skill, it would be stranger if they did not win.”

“That is quite the confidence.”

When I say that, Sera takes some out of an item box (actually \<Infinite Storage>).

“You will understand once you eat it. There is a batch prepared in advance, and I was told to distribute it to everyone at the right time.”

《Yay!》

Dora, sitting on my lap, is overjoyed.

Dora had been silent because she was staring intently at Mio’s cooking.

《Maria, could you put up a barrier that blocks smells?》

《Understood.》

At Sera’s request, Maria activated \<Barrier Art>, surrounding us with a barrier that blocked only smell.

《Why go out of your way to put up a barrier?》

《If someone not accustomed to fine cuisine smells it, there is a chance they may lose their sanity.》

《This is different from the crepes I know…》

So even without using dangerous drugs, the food itself was dangerous.

“They wanted to present it at the competition first, but they wanted you to be the very first to eat it, Master. That is why we decided to give it to you at this timing.”

“They really love you, Jin-kun… Jin-kun, please eat it first, just as Mio-chan and the others wish.”

“Then I will gratefully partake.”

And then I take a bite of the crepe Sera handed me.

“This is… dangerous… It is insanely delicious…”

The moment you take a bite, you understand its level of completion as a dish.

Just because it is a sweet does not mean it only needs to be sweet.

When ingredient quality, harmony between ingredients, and the cook’s skill are all fulfilled at the highest level, a dish is completed.

I am not even sure what I am saying anymore.

Certainly, with this level of deliciousness, ordinary people might not be able to endure it.

Since ancient times, beauty and fine cuisine are things that drive people mad.

“I-it is really delicious…”

“Mio-chan is amazing. You have truly perfected your path.”

《It is so good!!!》

“This is a moment of bliss. Especially since we were kept waiting for so long.”

The four who began eating after me are also singing its praises.

It seems Sera herself is also tasting the finished product for the first time.

“Hm? Something is strange about the venue.”

“What could it be…?”

I had been completely focused on eating, but when I looked closely, something seemed to be happening at the competition venue.

Alta, tell me.

A: It seems that the participants cooking on both sides of Mio’s team have requested to give up. After smelling Mio’s cooking, their spirits were broken.

“The ones on both sides of Mio were supposed to be top contenders according to prior information, were they not? Because they had skill, they realized they could not win…?”

Mio’s cooking (just the smell) seems to be in a realm that breaks the spirits of skilled cooks.

There was a bit of trouble, but the judging of the main round began without issue.

As an aside, the surrender of the neighboring competitors was not accepted, and they had to finish cooking.

Mio and the others, who passed the preliminaries in first place, were judged last.

Whether intentional or not, it can be said to be the perfect timing to serve a dessert.

“They definitely planned it.”

And then, at last, it was time for tasting.

There is nothing particularly noteworthy in the process, so I will just tell you the reactions of the judges after eating Mio’s dish.

“This is delicious! Too delicious!”

“What is this! I have never eaten anything this delicious in my life!”

“So good… so good…”

“… (silently devouring it)”

“… (fainted from deliciousness)”

“… (a woman in her twenties making a face that should not be shown in public)”

Out of the ten judges, who should be accustomed to fine cuisine, three made coherent comments, three lost the ability to speak, and four lost consciousness.

They won.

---

**AN:** The difference in tone compared to the previous episode (188.5) is terrible.

If anyone knows a delicious dish that combines eggs, milk, fruit, and fish, I would be grateful if you could tell me.

## **190: Gondolas and the Drifting Island**

**AN:** I apologize, but I will be making a small change to the contents of Chapter 188.

The race that possesses an unborn \<Hero> will be changed from the Oni to the Dwarves.

The Oni will be introduced at a different time.

---

“Yeah, the scenery looks different when you see it from the waterways compared to walking.”

I muttered as we proceeded through the waterways of Latis Island by gondola.

The waterways sit lower than the walkways, so the impression of the scenery changes slightly. I prefer the view from the gondola.

“Yes, it is said that the townscape is most beautiful when seen from the waterways. That building over there is a hotel designed by the renowned architect Andrew-san, and this area offers the best view.”

The one who picked up my muttering was our guide, Aqua-san.

She is a beautiful blue-haired young woman who rows the gondola while guiding us around the island.

Despite her youth, she is said to be an excellent guide, reputed to know everything about the town.

As a tournament prize, it was written as a ‘Luxury Gondola Tour’, but the gondola itself is not especially luxurious.

Rather, it is considered luxurious because it comes with a young and beautiful guide (with many reservations and high fees). Indeed, that can only be described as luxurious.

“It caught my eye when we were walking too, but it really makes a better picture from here.”

I nod in agreement as I look at the building Aqua-san indicated.

It is a hotel that is not flashy, but has a refined elegance, and I admired it even while walking past.

…It was fully booked, though, so there was no way we could stay there.

Seen from the waterways, it has a different charm and looks like a single painting.

This is it. This right here is the true joy of sightseeing.

After being shown several famous spots on the island, we headed toward a slightly run-down waterway.

At the start, I had been asked for my preferences, and I requested that we be shown as wide a range as possible, not just the bustling areas.

After proceeding for a while, a building resembling an uninhabited cathedral came into view.

“Next is the oldest building on this island. It remains as a historical structure, but there are no official records of what it was used for. One theory says it was used for some kind of ritual.”

I love that sort of thing.

…However, my intuition is telling me that there are no special events happening right now.

“General entry is prohibited, so it can only be seen from the waterways.”

“So that’s a privilege unique to the gondola tour. …Seriously, I’m grateful to Mio and Nino for winning the tournament for us.”

“Ehehe!”

“I’m honored, yes…”

When I expressed my gratitude, Mio puffed out her chest, while Nino looked utterly blissful.

At first, Nino said it was too presumptuous to ride together with us, but since it would be unreasonable to leave behind one of the key contributors, I forced the issue and had her come along.

…Though, I think it’s a bit much that she keeps looking at me instead of the scenery. Well, Maria is also looking in my direction, or rather, around me, but for a different reason…

Among the forked paths, Aqua-san glanced at one route for just a moment, then turned toward the other.

Did that glance mean something?

“Is there something ahead?”

When I asked, Aqua-san thought for just a brief moment before opening her mouth.

“No, there is nothing today.”

“If so, what could be seen, and when?”

There must be something ahead. Just not something that can be seen ‘today.’

She probably tried to dodge the question without lying.

“To be honest, it’s not commendable to talk about something I cannot guide you to…”

Aqua-san prefaced it that way.

It seems to be her professional pride, not wanting to explain sights that cannot be seen on that day’s tour.

“If you were riding the gondola two days from now, you would be able to see the Drifting Island from up ahead.”

“The Drifting Island?”

“Yes, the island that wanders around Latis Island… no, around the Kingdom of Pajel.”

According to her, it is a small island about five kilometers in diameter that periodically moves through the seas around the Kingdom of Pajel.

The waters around the Drifting Island have high waves, making landing extremely difficult, and there are no records of anyone returning safely.

There are rumors that there is an unknown treasure somewhere on the island, which has a mountain.

After listening to Aqua-san’s explanation, something caught my attention.

A moving island… It feels like I’ve heard something like that before…

《Master, could it be the island whale that Alta mentioned before?》

《That’s it!》
