During the sea voyage toward the Regalia Beastkin Nation, Alta discovered a gigantic monster.

A whale that looks like an island moving across the sea surface, an island whale.

Distance-wise, I think it’s a different one from the one Alta found before, though…

A: Yes. It is a different individual.

I can’t tell since I’m under a map ban, but if Alta has grasped it, then it must be within map range.

An unexplored region atop a fantasy creature, huh…

《Master, we’re obviously going, right?》

《Yeah, we’re going》

《I will accompany you》

I answered immediately to Mio’s perceptive question.

Maria doesn’t even ask for confirmation, since that’s her default response.

《Whale meat!》

《How exciting. …Ah, I mean going there, of course! Not eating the meat!》

《Sera-chan, why did you dig your own grave like that…?》

We have no plans to eat the island whale, obviously.

That said, following the earlier flow of events, whale meat did appear on our dining table before.

In this world, there are no restrictions on whaling.

It was delicious. The end.

Having decided to aim for the island whale, or rather the Drifting Island, I immediately began gathering information.

“Is there a reason you separated ‘landing is difficult’ and ‘no one has returned safely’?”

“Yes, those two have clearly different meanings.”

I asked Aqua-san about the point that bothered me earlier.

“In truth, it’s not that no one has ever landed there. Some managed to approach by chance, others were swallowed by storms and drifted there accidentally. However, there are definitively no cases of anyone returning from the Drifting Island. Even if one is fortunate enough to land there, it seems no one can rely on luck again to make it back.”

The goddess of fortune does not smile twice.

A one-way unexplored region is a common enough tale.

“Still, letters have made their way back before. Letters sealed in bottles occasionally drift ashore. They are from people who were swept away by storms and ended up on the Drifting Island, reporting that they are barely managing to live there.”

Those who knew there were no returnees stopped gambling on escape and chose to live on the Drifting Island instead.

“Is there plenty of food on the island?”

Sera becomes incapacitated very quickly if food is scarce, after all. Of course she’d be concerned.

“Yes. Among those who reached it were former adventurers, and they are able to hunt the monsters on the island. There are also many edible plants, so I have heard that they do not lack for food.”

“If they were former adventurers, they must be quite capable in that regard.”

Setting us aside as exceptions, normal adventurers should have a fair amount of survival knowledge.

At the very least, they probably wouldn’t struggle just to eat.

That aside, I can’t hide my astonishment that such an ecosystem exists atop an island whale.

Plants growing on a whale. What even is that?

“It’s a dangerous island in many ways, but when viewed from afar, it’s a lovely island and makes for a wonderful memory. …That is why the reservations for two days from now are truly, absolutely full.”

Aqua-san gazes into the distance slightly. Her schedule must be in trouble.

So this was the real reason behind the one-week minimum wait for gondolas.

“Doesn’t the kingdom do anything? An unexplored island within the country seems like something they’d want to investigate.”

“As a kingdom, they have consistently taken a stance of leaving it alone. It seems they have never once conducted an investigation.”

Aqua-san answers Mio’s question without hesitation.

She truly is knowledgeable.

“Does the kingdom know something? Is going there prohibited?”

“No, going there itself is not prohibited. However, locals who know how dangerous it is do not attempt it. Adventurers sometimes head there in search of treasure and go missing.”

“They even get the missing-person ending…”

“They do sometimes return, but…”

“That’s fine. I won’t ask.”

Aqua-san never said they returned alive.

“How do adventurers arrange ships?”

I asked, since I can’t imagine adventurers owning ships.

“…It’s embarrassing to admit, but there is a shop that rents out ships for going to the Drifting Island. The fee is high, but they claim that if you make it to the island and come back, they will refund ninety percent of the fee even if the ship is wrecked, and they use that to provoke adventurers.”

I see. For adventurers intending to return alive, even if the rental fee is high, a refund upon survival would make the venture worthwhile.

《Master, how do you plan to get to the Drifting Island?》

《Obviously, by ship》

I answered Mio’s telepathic question.

《Right?》

《Wouldn’t flying be more reliable…?》

《You’re really going to take a dangerous ship on purpose?》

Only Mio accepted it, while Sakura and Sera voiced sensible opinions.

I understand what they’re saying, but…

《That would lack atmosphere. It’s an unknown island, after all. Just dropping in from the sky would be boring. At least once, we have to go by sea…》

《I get it》

《I do not understand》

《Neither do I…》

Once again, only Mio understood.

Dora? She started taking a nap on my lap.

Maria? She’ll agree with me, but she won’t understand.

《By the way, Maria-chan looks surprisingly calm even though Master is doing something dangerous again. Does she have a fever?》

《That’s rather rude of you to say so casually…》

As always, Mio is observant.

Setting aside the rudeness of her comment, it is true that Maria looks calm.

I look at Maria and nod.

《Actually, I asked Jin-sama for permission, and I have been allowed to check the map》

《…Come to think of it, there’s no way Maria-chan could tolerate a map ban》

As Mio says, the map ban was beyond acceptable limits for Maria as my bodyguard.

Right after I declared the map ban, Maria pleaded with me.

《Maria-san can’t be helped》

《I suppose so…》

Sera and Sakura nod in agreement.

《In exchange, I prohibited spoilers and asked her to refrain from offering opinions about my actions. I also told her not to let it show on her face. All Maria can do is prepare herself mentally》

《She rarely voices her opinions anyway, so I didn’t even notice…》

In fact, since the map ban, Maria hasn’t left my side for even a moment.

She doesn’t show it on her face, but her alertness is at maximum.

《So, Master, what about the ship? Are we borrowing one from the shop Aqua-san mentioned?》

《No, if possible, I don’t want to use that place. It feels bad luck, and it leaves a bad taste in my mouth》

I dislike businesses that mock adventure.

If only there were another way…

“Ah, that reminds me. There is one point I need to correct.”

“?”

Aqua-san speaks as if she just remembered.

“Earlier I said that locals do not go to the Drifting Island, but that was not entirely accurate. There is one person… now two people, on this island who are trying to go to the Drifting Island.”

“Please, tell me more.”

Aqua-san’s timely assist.

Could this be our chance to piggyback on their plan?

After enjoying the gondola ride and famous spots guided by Aqua-san, we visited a beach at the edge of the island.

“We walked quite a bit.”

“There are hardly any people once you get this far…”

“I hear there will be many people here in two days. The island whale can be seen from the closest point here.”

This is the spot where the island whale comes closest to Latis Island.

Naturally, it will be overflowing with people in two days.

“That’s the shack.”

I mutter as I spot a shack matching the features I was told about.

《Lots of boats!》

“There must be around fifty of them.”

Various shapes of boats are lined up near the shack, showing the efforts of their makers.

“…Master, you’re going to support them with everything you’ve got, right?”

“Yeah. That’s the plan for now.”

We came here because Aqua-san told us there were people trying to head to the island whale.

Their family members were left behind on the island whale, and they are trying to rescue them somehow.

At this point, we have no choice but to join in.

As we approached the shack, the door opened and two men came out.

One looked to be in his fifties, very much a man of the sea, while the other was an intellectual-looking man in his thirties, wearing a lab coat and glasses.

“Damn it! Only two days left, and now we run out of funds at a time like this!”

“We’ve gone through quite a lot of prototypes so far. Those costs really add up. If only we could somehow manage the funds for the ship still under construction…”

Thank you for the explanation.

“Hm? Who the hell are you? I don’t recognize you.”

“Are you tourists? The Drifting Island won’t be here for another two days.”

The two noticed us and called out.

Sorry, but we’re not here to see the Drifting Island. We want to go there.

“No, the ones we have business with are you two.”

“With us?”

“You plan to go to the Drifting Island in two days, right? Would you let us come along?”

When I said that, the expressions of both men visibly hardened.

“Don’t say stupid shit!”

“Earth-san, please calm down.”

When the sea man called Earth yelled, the intellectual with glasses tried to calm him down.

However, the intellectual’s expression remained just as grim.

“I don’t know who told you about us, but this is not a game. Yes, we do plan to set sail for the Drifting Island in two days. But that is to reach our family who made it there. We are not going to the island to take anyone else along.”

There was clear rejection there.

…Well, that’s only natural.

There’s no way they’d agree right away when approached like this.

But, as Asai once said, negotiations truly begin after you’re rejected.

“You don’t have the funds, right? I can help with that.”

I played one of the three sacred negotiation cards: financial power.

For the record, the other two are authority and force.

“Gh… So you overheard us…”

Earth grimaces in frustration.

“Financial support, you say. That would certainly be helpful if true, but building a ship is not cheap. Forgive me, but you don’t look like you possess that level of wealth…”

In this world, ships are built with magical devices as a given.

Through magical devices, they can generate wind, turn screws, or glide over the water surface, achieving high performance in various ways.

As an aside, I heard that the ‘Queen Sakuya’ had over one hundred propulsion-type magical devices of ten different kinds installed.

Naturally, magical devices for ships are not cheap.

Including material costs, building even a single ship would be a considerable expense.

I can’t even imagine how much funding was required to build the ships here.

As another aside, I heard that building the ‘Queen Sakuya’ would require a sum comparable to the national budget of a small country. Since the magical devices and materials were prepared internally, there is apparently a large gap between that and the actual construction cost…

“Is this enough? If not, I still have plenty more.”

As I said that, I tossed several gold bars out of my item box (for disguise).

Hearing the sound of the gold bars hitting the ground, the two gulped, finally understanding that I was serious.

For the record, the gold bars are my personal assets.

Since I rarely have opportunities to use cash, I jokingly said I wanted to hold my assets in gold, and they prepared it for me.

I knew this already, but one must be careful about joking casually in front of slaves, as it has a high chance of becoming reality.

As the two stood dumbfounded, a telepathic message came from Mio.

《What a nouveau riche move》

《I agree, it does feel like I overdid it a bit》

I intended to negotiate seriously, but before I knew it, I was acting like a textbook example of a rich upstart.

At this point, I might as well push through.

“Or is it materials you want?”

Saying that, I took out rare lumber from my item box (for disguise).

This one is effectively an offering. Apparently, it’s leftover material from building the luxury passenger ship (the Queen Sakuya).

“Or manpower? I could gather about fifty people in an hour.”

That’s a lie. I can gather over a thousand in five minutes.

“”…””

I’d like some kind of reaction soon…

“…What is your goal?”

“I’ve said it from the start, haven’t I? Our goal is to go to the Drifting Island by ship.”

I answer Earth’s question when he finally opens his mouth.

“Do you want the treasure said to be on the Drifting Island?”

“Well, that does interest me too, but our primary goal is sightseeing.”

“Are you insane?”

Earth looks genuinely bewildered.

“Yeah, I’m sane. And I’m serious.”

“…It seems he truly is serious.”

“You can tell just by looking, but still…”

They seem to have understood my goal, but neither of them looks pleased.

“Honestly, your support would be greatly appreciated, and in exchange, it would be possible to take you along. However, there are two problems.”

“Are they the kind of problems that money, materials, or manpower can’t solve?”

With those three, most things should be manageable…

“Yes. They are fundamental issues separate from that.”

“Let me hear them.”

When I prompt him, the intellectual nods.

“…To begin with, while we are thinking of going to the Drifting Island, we are hardly considering returning.”

“Then what are you going there for? Your family is on the Drifting Island, right?”

“Exactly. Our purpose is to go to our family. If they are there, there is no need to return from the Drifting Island. Even if we were to find a way back, our priority would be our family, so we cannot guarantee that we could send you back.”

…Ah, I see.

Their goal was not ‘to bring their family back’, but ‘to go to their family.’

If my goal is tourism, then there is a fundamental difference between us and those who intend to settle there.

“That’s not an issue. I have my own way to get back.”

‘Portal’, ‘Warp’, wyverns, the wings of the undead, the power of the Wind Calamity Dragon, spiritization… just off the top of my head, there are this many. If I thought harder, there would probably be more.

“You can do such a thing…? Could it be some kind of magical device?”

“If you had something like that, wouldn’t it make sense to use it from the start instead of going by ship?”

Uh-oh, Earth just stepped into forbidden territory.

“It can only be used for the return. I can’t use it for the journey there.”

I have no intention of using it, so it’s ‘can’t be used.’

That’s not a lie.

“…Can it be used to bring our family back as well?”

“!?”

Sharp thinking, intellectual glasses. Earth realizes it a moment later.

Of course, that level of after-service is no problem.

“Yeah, it can. Well? Are you willing to take me along now?”

“…If what you say is true, then we would very much like to have you with us. Incidentally, the other problem is that due to the ship’s size, we can only take two or three people.”

I glance to the side and see Maria raising her hand.

Well, Maria can’t be helped.

“Is there one more volunteer?”

“Yes!”

《Me!》

Mio and Dora raise their hands.

“What about you two?”

When I ask, Sakura and Sera shake their heads.

“If there are people who want to go, they should take priority…”

“I feel the same. We’ll be waiting here.”

And thus, the showdown between Mio and Dora begins.

“I won!”

《I lost…》

The victor of the fierce battle is Mio.

I pat Dora’s head to comfort her.

“Alright, the members going are decided. Including me, that’s three people. We’re small, so it should be fine, right?”

“Yes, that won’t be a problem, but…”

“Are you sane?”

Once again, Earth questions my sanity.

Certainly, bringing along two girls around ten years old on a potentially deadly sea voyage would naturally raise doubts about one’s sanity.

“Maria, arm wrestle with him.”

I point at the muscular Earth and order Maria.

“Yes, understood.”

Two minutes later.

“I see. So you can’t judge by appearances alone. Ow…”

Earth says with understanding, his arm hanging limply.

Proof is better than argument. That’s a good saying.

“Earth-san, are you alright? That sounded awful…”

“Honestly, I might be in trouble. I’ve completely lost sensation.”

“Do you need \<Healing Magic>?”

“Sorry, but yes. It would affect the voyage in two days.”

Apparently it was more serious than expected, and Earth nods without hesitation.

His bones don’t seem broken, so I quickly fix him up with Heal.

“You can use magic too, huh. …What else can you use besides \<Healing Magic>?”

“Anything.”

At least, I can use all generally recognized magic.

“That’s quite a claim… Can you use \<Wind Magic>?”

“Of course.”

I activate \<Wind Magic> \<Chantless>, creating a gust.

Incidentally, using the power of the Wind Calamity Dragon, I could do more than \<Wind Magic>.

I doubt I’ll ever have the opportunity to use it, though…

“With this, couldn’t we revise the plan significantly?”

“Yes, it would greatly increase the success probability.”

The two speak excitedly.

Naturally, their plan was limited to what two people could do.

Conversely, with us joining, it’s only natural that the plan would be revised.

“In our plan, to cross the rough seas and reach the Drifting Island, we intended to accelerate a sailing ship using \<Wind Magic>. Originally, we planned to use my \<Wind Magic>, but yours is clearly more powerful. Would you be willing to use \<Wind Magic> in my stead?”

“Yeah, that’s an easy request. My support includes using my abilities, after all.”

As long as the condition of ‘going by ship’ is met, I won’t hold back my cooperation.

“Then don’t hold back and support us.”

“Sorry, but we appreciate it.”

“Yeah. You can think of it as being on a big ship. I won’t make you regret it.”

This is a highly advanced pun, playing on ‘big ship’ and ‘regret’ in the context of sailing to the Drifting Island.

“””””…”””””

Yep. The reaction was underwhelming!

And so, we successfully secured a means of traveling to the Drifting Island.

---

**AN:** Now then, where is the Oni Hero?

Probably twenty days from now again. Sorry about that.

+++

## **191: Festival and Mock Battles**

**AN:** A skill you see fairly often makes an appearance.

---

The day after we secured a ship for the drifting-islands route, the festival-week organizers came to the inn where we were staying.

They said they had something to discuss with Mio and Nino regarding the cooking competition.

“The overall grand prize? Us?”

When Mio asked back, the male organizer nodded.

“Yes. Normally, the winner of the restaurant division automatically becomes the overall grand champion, but this year the two of you, as winners of the general division, have been awarded the overall championship. It was a unanimous decision by the judges.”

“But there wasn’t any mention of an overall grand prize on the competition posters, was there?”

“No. When we checked with the staff in charge, they said that since no one from the general division had ever won the overall championship before, the mention gradually disappeared from the posters.”

The general division is basically an opening act.

Putting effort into something that almost never happens would be a waste, after all.

“So, what happens if you win the overall championship?”

“The overall champion is granted a certain right, but it is premised on being from the restaurant division, and is clearly not intended for individuals. That is why we came to consult you.”

For the winners of the general division, the prizes were a “Trophy” and an “Invitation to a gondola tour”.

For the winners of the restaurant division, the prize was a “Luxurious trophy”.

And for the overall champion, the right granted is the “Right to serve food to the royal family of the Kingdom of Pajel”.

Certainly, for a restaurant it would be a good opportunity to add prestige, but for an individual, even gaining such an honor would not really lead to much benefit.

There is also apparently an inside story that the “Invitation to a gondola tour” exists as a prize to balance the restaurant division and the general division.

To think that we would get involved with royalty in this way…

A: Because of the no-spoilers rule, I refrained from speaking up.

Well, Alta already knew.

Of course, since I was the one who issued the no-spoilers order, I have no intention of complaining.

《What do we do? Decline?》

《Yeah, decline it.》

《Got it!》

I answer Mio’s telepathic message immediately.

According to Alta, the royal family and nobility of this country are basically corrupt, and they have troubles serious enough that a “Princess Shrine Maiden” ran away.

It is obvious that getting involved would lead to noble-related hassles, so I absolutely do not want anything to do with them.

“Sorry, but that right doesn’t offer us any benefit, so we’ll have to decline.”

“I see. That is a relief…”

Unexpectedly, the expression the festival organizer showed was one of relief.

“You’re happy we declined?”

“Yes. Actually, for the past few days the royal family and nobles have been rather busy with something. We were not told the reason, but they were too occupied for us to even consult them about the overall championship right.”

…Alta, you can spoil it. Please tell me.

Is the reason there was no forceful recruitment from the nobles toward Mio and the others because of this?

A: Yes. A royal order was issued to search for a High Elf. As a result, recruiting cooks became the least of their concerns.

So if it had been peaceful, there would have been forceful recruitment.

In the end, it turned out to be the best outcome for both sides. Mainly in terms of damage to the recruiting side.

“If you were from the restaurant division, we could have arranged another date, but since you are tourists, we anticipated that scheduling would be difficult. Declining is the most peaceful resolution, so for us it is ideal. Of course, we will compensate you in another form.”

When royalty has issues, making exceptional arrangements different from usual is troublesome.

It seems the organizers were relieved that things could be settled peacefully.

“Nino, you’re fine with that too, right?”

“Of course, yes.”

With the consent of both winners obtained, the festival organizer left.

As for the “Compensation in another form”, we asked for priority participation rights for festival week.

Since it is a festival, we want to enjoy more than just the cooking competition (and the gondola even more so).

However, timing-wise there is no guarantee we could join events we are interested in.

With priority participation rights, the organizers can push things through for us. Nice!

And then, we once again set foot in the festival-week venue.

Everywhere you look, it is lively.

Huh? Aren’t we helping with ship construction?

Amateurs shouldn’t be sticking their noses or hands into that, right? That is their job.

All I can do is provide money, materials, and magic.

We could have arranged skilled workers, but the two of them declined.

Construction has already entered the final stage, and adding people now would not help.

They said the hardest part was running out of money right at the final stage.

“Now then, which event should we join…”

“Jin-sama, it seems the main attractions are one per day.”

“And besides those, there are over twenty events just today…”

When I mutter, Maria and Sakura, holding pamphlets, fill me in.

Maria is skillfully watching the surroundings while reading the pamphlet.

“Mio-chan is completely satisfied with the cooking competition, so I’ll leave it up to everyone!”

“There’s an eating contest, so I would love to participate.”

《Dora wants to join too!》

Putting Mio aside, Sera and Dora are business as usual.

There are many food-related events besides the cooking competition, and the eating contest is held daily.

But is it really okay to let these two participate?

Is there even anyone who could beat them?

Incidentally, the priority participation rights are tied to Mio, so if Mio is not present, the rights do not exist.

Therefore, the usual six of us will act together.

We did invite Nino, who was a major contributor, but she declined, saying she was already more than satisfied.

She looked very content.

“Let’s start with this one.”

The first event the six of us headed to was this.

“Who Is the Strongest Warrior! Win 10 Consecutive Matches for Luxurious Prizes!”

It is an event held in the arena, a winner-stays-on match using magical tools for mock battles that cause no damage even if you are hit.

During festival week, bloody events are prohibited.

By the way, this is the type of event that does not require priority participation rights.

Those who line up fight in order, simply competing for consecutive wins.

“Gahaha! Is there no sixth opponent? Every last one of you is weak!”

On the stage, a large man who seems to have achieved five consecutive wins is taunting.

There is no one lined up right now. We could fight immediately.

His weapon is a great axe. He has \<Axe Technique> and \<Physical Enhancement>, a pure warrior.

He has scars likely from fighting monsters, showing real combat experience rather than mere brute strength. Five wins seems reasonable.

“Then, I’ll go have some fun.”

“May fortune favor you.”

《Good luuuck!》

Seeing me off, I tell the reception desk I want to participate.

“What weapon will you use?”

“The same as him. A great axe.”

Anyone perceptive would already understand what I am planning.

“Now then, the next challenger is Jin, a great-axe user who doesn’t look the part!”

I step onto the stage and get introduced by the announcer.

This time, there is no reason to hide my identity, so I registered under my real name.

“And his opponent is the formidable fighter already on a five-win streak! Dongo!”

“Gahaha! A scrawny kid like you is easy! I’ll keep this up and get ten straight wins!”

He seems to have some skill, but not much of an eye for judging opponents.

“Then, begin!”

“Take this!”

The moment the match starts, Dongo charges fiercely.

The rush of his massive body and the downward swing of his great axe, carried by momentum, are impressive.

Even knowing there is no damage, an ordinary strongman from town would freeze up.

Holding my great axe, I twist my body lightly in place.

Since it is a vertical downswing, shifting the axis makes it easy enough to dodge.

Then, riding the momentum of the rotation, I swing my great axe through…

“Gah…!”

My great axe pierces into the side of Dongo, who is still in his downswing posture.

“M-match over! Jin wins!”

– Oooooohhhh! !!-

The crowd erupts.

This time, what I focused on was a “showy fight”.

A slender man instantly defeating a big man with acrobatic movements is entertaining to watch.

On top of that, since we are using the same weapon, even amateurs can clearly see who is stronger.

There was an obviously unnecessary movement (the spin), but as a spectacle, that is no problem.

If anything, Dongo’s fights were too boring.

From what I could tell, all his previous matches ended instantly with the initial charge.

It was one-pattern and lacked excitement, so I used that against him to liven things up.

The second match opponent is Mugen, a spearman of the Tengen Muso Style.

“Take this! Tengen Muso Style secret technique, Rangetsu!”

“Rangetsu Counter!”

“Impossible! You’re catching every thrust on the spearhead!”

The third match opponent, Kuya, is an elderly swordmaster from the Izumo Wa Country.

“This flying slash I devised after years of training, take it! Hah!”

“‘Flying Sword Rapid Slash’.”

“No waaaay.”

The fourth through eighth matches were uninteresting, so I will skip them.

The ninth match. Pieri, an elven archer.

“You seem amazing with blades, but how about an archery duel?”

“Throwing!”

“Don’t just throw the arrow! At least use the bow!”

And then, the final tenth match.

“Next opponent is this ‘supe…”

“Step aside.”

A woman around twenty years old steps onto the stage, pushing aside the large man who was about to announce himself.

She is wearing something like a coat over a white bodysuit, and her purple hair is tied up on top of her head.

Her voluptuous, feminine body is emphasized by the bodysuit, and bluntly put, it is erotic.

Both her outfit and hairstyle clearly stand out from the surroundings.

“Hey, lady! Don’t cut in line! I’m next!”

“Hm, so that is the rule. Then you may offer me that right. Luna.”

“Yes.”

When the large man complains, the erotic woman calls over a woman who looks like her attendant.

“Please accept this.”

“H-hey… this…”

Handed a leather pouch stuffed with gold coins, the large man’s face stiffens.

“In exchange, I would like the right to fight him.”

“…No, I don’t need the money. I’ll give up my turn.”

With a stiff face, the large man agrees to give up his right and returns the pouch.

Judging from his reaction, he does not want to get involved with someone who would casually pay a fortune just for a match. I understand the feeling. If possible, I do not want to get involved either.

“Hm, good judgment.”

“Um… then, is it alright that the next opponent is this lady?”

“Yeah…”

As the woman speaks with satisfaction, the announcer comes to confirm the change in order.

“May I have your name?”

“My name is Sol.”

Sun and moon, huh. Simple names are nice.

“And what weapon will you use, Sol?”

“All of them. Bring out everything that is prepared.”

Sol says something strange.

As an aside, we are currently under a restriction not to check the opponent’s skills until the match ends.

“You mean you will switch weapons? There are over twenty kinds…”

“That understanding is fine. Just place them on the floor. Luna.”

“Yes.”

Following Sol’s instruction, Luna places twenty-five types of weapons on the stage.

“You have been putting on interesting fights, but this you cannot imitate, can you?”

“Yeah, that would be impossible.”

With this, using “the same weapon as the opponent” is no longer possible.

At least, not in a mock battle where magic is prohibited.

“Use the weapon you are most accustomed to.”

“I’ll do that.”

I pick up my familiar one-handed sword.

There is also a katana, but balance-wise this is closer to what I am used to.

And then, Sol and I face each other on the stage.

“Behold my martial skill.”

As Sol raises her right hand, the weapons placed on the stage float into the air.

The audience murmurs.

“Sol, the use of magic is prohibited in this event!”

“This is not magic.”

The announcer hurriedly warns her, but Sol denies that it is magic.

I do not sense any magic power, so it does not seem to be magic. It is almost certainly a skill.

“However, something like this without magic is…”

“I don’t think it’s magic either. Even if it were, it’s fine, so could you let this proceed?”

“…If Jin says so, we will allow this match. But if Sol wins, from the next match onward…”

“Rest assured. Once my bout with this one ends, regardless of the outcome, I will depart.”

“Understood…”

With both sides in agreement and no remaining concerns, the announcer has no choice but to proceed with the match.

The announcer leaves the stage, leaving only Sol, me, and the floating weapons.

“Facing an overwhelming nine-win streak is Jin! Opposing him is Sol, who floats weapons with a mysterious technique! No one can predict how this match will unfold!”

How the match will unfold is unclear, but I can roughly guess what she will do.

“Then, begin!”

At the signal, eight weapons rush at me.

“Figured.”

“Entertain me.”

A greatsword, shortsword, hand spear, long spear, hand axe, great axe, hammer, and sickle approach from all directions.

She cannot control all twenty-five at once, or perhaps this is just a test. Either way, it does not matter right now.

I dash toward Sol.

Rather than handling everything in place, it is easier to deal with them by moving and narrowing the attacks.

At this point, the weapons likely to land effective hits are the shortsword, hand spear, and hand axe.

She is probably placing smaller weapons in visible positions to secure her overall field of view.

This suggests that she may not be able to precisely control weapons she cannot see, but I do not have enough proof to assert that, so I will not build it into my tactics.

I knock aside the three weapons with my one-handed sword and close in on Sol.

“Hah!”

“Hmph!”

Sol blocks my slash with the one-handed sword she is holding.

I have the advantage in raw strength, so Sol briefly grimaces.

“A splendid strike. And to find the optimal move in that instant, you have good eyes.”

“I’m honored by the praise.”

Creating distance only disadvantages me, so if possible, I want to finish this in close combat.

Well, she is not that easy an opponent.

The shortsword and hand spear I knocked away come at me from my blind spot, so I dodge with minimal movement.

Anticipating that dodge, Sol’s sword also comes at me. Busy, busy…

On top of that, mid- and long-range attacks from a bow and whip force me to create distance.

From here on, closing in even once will be a challenge.

Now then, even in this brief exchange, I have learned something.

First, the weapons Sol controls are not simply floating and flying at me.

Their trajectories have the beauty of forms wielded by masters.

In other words, they are not merely floating, but should be thought of as being controlled by invisible masters.

Conversely, that also means it is unlikely they will take unnatural trajectories that even masters could not perform.

Second, she can control weapons she cannot see, but with reduced precision.

Earlier, the weapons that came from my blind spot, which was also Sol’s blind spot, lacked the sharpness they had before.

There is no reason to deliberately lower the precision of an attack, so this seems likely.

In other words, facing Sol with her twenty-five floating weapons is equivalent to “facing twenty-five masters who are in Sol’s sight-line.”

No, since Sol herself is also at a master level, that makes twenty-six masters…

“Focus on the duel!”

While thinking about this as I fended off the incoming weapons, Sol scolds me, having sensed it.

As an aside, it seems the reason she only used eight weapons at first was indeed a test.

All twenty-five weapons now coordinate beautifully to press their attack.

About ten come at me at once, but each leaves no opening, filling gaps seamlessly.

So far, there are no effective hits, but once distance is forced, it becomes quite tough.

“What’s wrong? Is that all? Is it already over?”

A cheap taunt. I will take the bait.

“Then, I suppose I’ll try attacking again.”

“If you can, then try.”

I change how I handle the twenty-five weapons.

Until now, I had been dodging as much as possible, only blocking or deflecting those I judged impossible to evade.

Now, I begin to deflect as much as possible.

“Hm…”

It seems Sol has an idea as well.

The likely effect of Sol’s skill is “Reproduction.”

Rather than constantly controlling all weapons, the trajectories of past techniques are probably being reproduced.

She masks it with coordination between weapons, but each weapon only used around ten types of trajectories at most, so it was not hard to notice.

And this semi-automatic control has a weakness.

While it can reproduce the trajectory of a technique, it cannot reproduce the movement after being deflected.

Weapons I dodged quickly resumed attacking, but weapons I deflected had a time lag before returning.

Perhaps deflected weapons must be manually reset.

In other words, the more weapons I deflect, the more gaps appear in the attack.

I lower my posture and attempt to close in on Sol.

“Well done…!”

The reason Sol groans, is that many of the weapons she can currently control are particularly poor at attacking low.

Weapons, in general, are bad at low attacks.

Even in martial arts, low attacks tend to have fewer variations than attacks to other parts.

There are many reasons.

The “hands” holding weapons are on the upper body, making low attacks unstable. If an attack fails, there is the risk of striking the ground. There are no immediately fatal points in the lower body.

Even with master-level movements, simply being a low attack reduces the expected precision compared to other attacks.

On top of that, trying to corner me using only large-swing weapons like great axes, greatswords, and hammers is close to impossible.

I dash through beneath the weapons that have lost balance in their stance.

This is also a move only possible because the “Invisible masters” do not actually exist. Normally, you could not run through where people are standing.

And once again, close combat.

At this distance, it is clearly advantageous for me.

“Step back!”

“No!”

Naturally, Sol tries to create distance again.

The twenty-five weapons rush at me. I was waiting for this.

I deflect the approaching shortsword with my one-handed sword and guide it toward Sol.

“Tch!”

Sol hurriedly knocks away the shortsword.

Likewise, I guide the spear coming at me toward Sol as well.

“Gah! Such skillful tricks!”

“I’m honored by the praise.”

Sol curses as she deflects the spear.

Similar exchanges to before, but now Sol has no leeway.

While deflecting the weapons, I noticed something.

The attacks from the floating weapons are light.

When people clash weapons, they instinctively adjust their strength.

Naturally, the way force is applied differs from when practicing forms.

Sol’s “Invisible masters” are performing form practice. They cannot adjust their strength, making them easy to deflect or parry.

“To see my techniques this thoroughly… I did not expect to be forced to fight seriously in a mere diversion.”

In that instant, Sol’s presence changes.

I fail to deflect a hand spear coming from behind, barely dodging it.

…The previous “lightness” is gone.

“From here on, this is my true power. It is entirely different from before, so steel yourself.”

What followed was a barrage of attacks incomparable to before.

The precision and speed of the techniques increase, the variety of trajectories expands, and the “lightness” of the weapons disappears.

“This is rough!”

Now I am barely managing to dodge.

Trying to deflect or parry throws off my balance.

My countermeasures are no longer effective against this opponent.

Moreover, astonishingly, the longer time passes, the more precise the attacks become.

…But something feels off. I should check.

I deliberately deflect a thrust from a hand spear hard, accepting the opening.

As expected, other weapons immediately rush in to exploit it.

The only direction I can move to evade is toward the “Invisible hand-spear master”.

When deflecting the spear, I intentionally created an opening that made it easy to run that way. I could not prevent an opening from appearing, but I could choose its direction.

I dash toward the “Invisible hand-spear master” and thrust with that momentum.

– Thud! –

“Gah!”

There is clearly the sound of something being pierced, and Sol cries out in agony.

Sol drops to her knees, and all the weapons fall to the ground.

Looking closer, blood is flowing from Sol’s mouth.

“…How did you realize?”

“I wasn’t certain. But the moment our weapons touched, I felt the presence of a wielder at the tip.”

As she said, the first and second stages are likely different.

In the first stage, the “Invisible masters” do not exist, and only the forms are reproduced.

But in the second stage, the “Invisible masters” themselves are reproduced, though still invisible.

If the wielders are reproduced, then attacks might connect.

Thinking that, I attacked the “Invisible master”.

I did not expect Sol to cough up blood, though…

“With such scant evidence, you launched such a high-risk attack. You are quite insane, aren’t you?”

“…I hear that a lot. More importantly, why are you coughing up blood?”

“If one is stabbed in the stomach, coughing blood is only natural.”

Does attacking the second-stage “Invisible masters” equal attacking Sol herself?

And as a bonus, the non-damaging effect of the mock-battle weapons does not activate.

“I apologize for interrupting. Now then, let us continue.”

“Huh? We’re continuing?”

“Neither of us is dead yet.”

This is supposed to be a mock battle…

She does not even care about coughing blood or the risk of death. She only thinks about fighting.

It has been a while since I met a true battle maniac.

“Do not hesitate to strike at shadows.”

No, even if you tell me not to hesitate, I will hesitate.

A mock battle where only the opponent has a risk of death has no merit whatsoever.

“Here I come.”

As Sol says that, the fallen weapons float up again.

The hand spear does not rise. Does that mean the “Invisible master” that took a decisive hit disappears?

The attack resumes.

No matter how resolved Sol is, I have no intention of killing her in a mock battle.

But Sol has forgotten this is a mock battle, and it does not look like she will stop even if one or two “Invisible masters” are defeated.

There is even the possibility she will not stop until death.

While dodging attacks, I think about how to defeat the “Invisible masters” without killing Sol.

\<Restraint>, \<Flying Sword Technique>, \<Shukuchi>… I consider various options, but none seem viable right now.

Then should I just lose?

Yeah, absolutely not.

At this point, what I can do is limited.

I am not eager to do it, but it cannot be helped.

“Sorry. I’ll end this with the next attack.”

“If you have more to show, do not hesitate to show it.”

Here, I raise my abilities by one stage.

As you know, we normally act under significant restrictions on our stats and skills.

Our abilities have reached an excessive level for operating in this world.

There are stages to these restrictions, roughly divided into: up to this point for sightseeing, up to this point for fighting enemies, up to this point for fighting strong enemies.

And now, my abilities shift from sightseeing mode to enemy-combat mode.

“Impossible!?”

As I run through all the weapons and close in instantly, Sol’s face fills with shock.

That is how different the speed was compared to before.

By the way, I am not using \<Shukuchi>.

“Gah!?”

Sol barely blocks my slash and is blown far back.

“It’s not over yet!”

Sol blocks my follow-up with all twenty-four remaining weapons.

There is not a single weapon left to attack. In fact, she is barely managing to defend even using all twenty-four.

Incidentally, the one-handed sword she is holding cannot be properly swung due to the impact of the earlier slash.

“To think you were hiding such power! But I have no intention of losing like this!”

“No, this is where it ends.”

“What?”

When I stop my hand, a sharp cracking sound echoes around us.

The sound comes from Sol’s weapons.

“My mistake. To forget the grade of my weapons… yes, this was a mock battle.”

Sol’s weapons crumble apart.

Watching, I realized that Sol’s skill puts strain on the weapons.

The more violently the weapons move, the greater the strain.

It would likely be no problem if they had artifact-level durability.

But using mock-battle weapons of low durability to block my consecutive attacks placed a strain they could not withstand.

“I concede.”

By the time Sol declares her loss, all the weapons have been reduced to fragments.

We were competing techniques, yet in the end I had to force the issue with stats.

In a sense, this is “business as usual”, but I would have liked to fight to the end at the same level of stats.

I still have a long way to go.

---

**AN:** The protagonist engages in an unusually serious battle at a festival event.

This is a rough image of status restrictions. They change depending on the situation.

Sightseeing use: Capable of destroying a country with no \<Transcendence> holders.

Combat use: Capable of defeating the Final Trial and the Demon King’s first form.

Strong-enemy combat use: Capable of defeating a Calamity Dragon.

+++

## **192: Festival Hopping and the Flea Market**

**AN:** This is a laid-back chapter.

There were a lot of weak events, so I had trouble coming up with a title. I ended up deciding on something random.

---

Having successfully achieved ten consecutive victories in the knockout tournament, I was presented with a lavish prize from the event organizers.

“What is this?”

“Discount tickets from our sponsor shops. During the festival week, all products at participating stores will be 20% off.”

Lavish… maybe?

Well, considering it is a prize from a free-to-enter event, I suppose you could call it lavish.

With discounts, profits decrease a bit, but there is no need to allocate a separate budget, so it is convenient in many ways.

“I will make good use of it.”

“No, the event was a huge success, and we are very satisfied as well. Please be sure to enjoy the festival.”

And with that, I left the event venue and rejoined the five people who were waiting outside.

“Jin-kun, congratulations…”

《Congrats!》

“Good work. Here is your drink.”

“Oh, thanks. Ah, Mio, can you hold onto this?”

I drank the beverage Maria handed me and passed the discount tickets to Mio.

“What is this? Oh! Festivals tend to be overpriced, so this really helps.”

“It truly is a great help.”

Sera, who was fully intending to eat various overpriced foods, was also pleased.

According to Mio, while we have money, she prefers to save wherever possible. Is she a housewife or something?

And then, two figures approached our cheerful group…

That was an unnecessarily dramatic way to put it, but it was Sol and Luna.

“You. Would you be willing to come to my country as one of my subordinates?”

Sol stood in front of us and suddenly said something like that.

I had guessed from the way she spoke, but it seems she really was someone important from some country.

“Your country?”

“Indeed. My name is Sol Hercules. I am the emperor of the Hercules Empire, to the east of here.”

I knew she was important, but I did not expect her to be an emperor.

Since the match was over, I took the opportunity to check her status.

Name: Sol Hercules

LV201

Gender: Female

Age: 19

Race: Human

Titles: Transcendent, Emperor of the Hercules Empire

Skills:

\<Single Inheritance LV > \<Shadow Hero Performance LV > \<Transcendence LV10>

Being under twenty years old with a level over 200 is rare, excluding our party.

And as expected, she had the “Transcendent” title…

As for skills, there were too many, so I omitted everything except the unique-class ones.

She had zero magic-type and technique-type skills, but an absurd number of martial arts and physical-type skills.

And as a bonus, almost all of them were at high levels.

Once I understood the source of her strength, it all made sense.

\<Single Inheritance>

Allows the retention of martial-arts-related skills and the owner’s knowledge. Contrary to the name, the successor cannot be designated, and it transfers randomly upon the owner’s death. It retains martial arts knowledge but does not retain memories.

\<Shadow Hero Performance>

Allows weapons to be floated and controlled. By registering forms in advance, they can be freely reproduced. By registering a person instead of a form, they can be reproduced as a shadow with a temporary ego. However, if the shadow takes damage, the same damage is inflicted on the original.

By …inheriting high-level martial arts skills through \<Single Inheritance>, which has parasitic and inheritance properties, and perfectly reproducing those techniques with \<Shadow Hero Performance>, she formed an excellent skill combo.

Note that \<Shadow Hero Performance> is not among the inheritable skills, so this build is entirely unique to Sol.

Now that I understood everything and felt refreshed, it was time to politely decline Sol’s invitation.

“Sorry, but I have no intention of serving anyone.”

“As expected. I was merely asking. I did not think a warrior like you would bow your head just because of a title like emperor. Luna.”

“Yes. Please accept this.”

Called upon, Luna took an envelope from her pocket and handed it to me.

“What is this?”

“An invitation to the Hercules Empire. Sol-sama invites those she recognizes as strong to her country.”

“You may decide whether to serve me or not after seeing my country.”

“There is no specified date or restriction on companions. Please show this invitation when you arrive.”

It is like a kind of free pass.

Alta, tell me about the Hercules Empire later.

A: Understood.

“Luna. Inform him about the weapons as well.”

“Yes. Jin-sama, Sol-sama collects weapons.”

Considering Sol’s fighting style, it would be stranger if she did not collect them.

High-rarity equipment can withstand the load of \<Shadow Hero Performance>, and if they have special abilities unique to high-rarity equipment, her strategic options expand even further.

Sol cannot truly fight seriously with sparring weapons.

“If you have any fine weapons you intend to sell, we would very much like to purchase them. At present, we lack funds, so it would be when you visit the empire…”

As an aside, Luna compensated for the sparring weapons destroyed by \<Shadow Hero Performance>.

Even though they were magical tool weapons, they were surprisingly expensive. Destroying over twenty of them would certainly deal heavy damage to one’s wallet.

“I have no plans to sell at the moment.”

“Understood. I only wished to inform you. Please remember that Sol-sama has an interest in strong individuals and weapons.”

A very battle-maniac direction of interest.

“Additionally, Sol-sama sometimes goes on expeditions to search for strong individuals and weapons. Therefore, there may be times when she is absent from the Hercules Empire. Please be aware of this. They usually last about a month. Today as well, we are returning from Izumo Wa after an expedition lasting a month.”

“Strong individuals aside, the magic sword smith was absent.”

Sol said this with dissatisfaction.

The magic sword smith of Izumo Wa… that would be our Holy Magic Smith, would it not?

A: Yes.

If I recall correctly, Mimi was originally famous as a magic sword smith.

From the perspective of a weapon collector, she would certainly be someone impossible to overlook.

Saying anything unnecessary would only complicate matters, so I kept my mouth shut.

“That I was able to find a strong individual like you at a mere diversion I happened upon was truly fortunate. If you feel inclined, come to my country.”

“Then we shall take our leave.”

And with that, the two of them left after saying what they came to say.

Since I had finished the mock battle event I wanted to participate in, we decided to enjoy the festival according to everyone else’s wishes.

First were Sera’s and Dora’s wishes. The ‘eating contest’.

“Now then, only a little time remains! Will the winner be contestant Sera or contestant Dora!?”

“Apparently, the two are traveling companions. Their food expenses must be tremendous.”

The two announcers commentated on Sera and Dora’s duel.

As initially feared, no other contestant could match them, and before anyone noticed, it became a one-on-one battle between the two.

Strictly speaking, other contestants were still present, but having had their pace disrupted by the two, their hands were no longer moving.

Sera had always been a big eater, so there was no issue, but Dora had been eating extremely well recently.

When I asked Alta about it, she said Dora’s evolution required a great deal of energy, so her food intake naturally increased. Even so, it still seemed like a lot…

She said her appetite would settle down once the evolution finished, so I was not too worried for now.

In other words, this was the only time Dora could compete evenly with Sera.

As an aside, Dora had also started eating “ration balls”, so food expenses were not an issue.

“Where does contestant Dora put all of that food!? I cannot understand it at all!”

“Contestant Sera is likely sending the nutrients she consumes to her chest. Splendid.”

One of the announcers was casually making a sexual harassment remark.

“Even so, both of your tables are very clean. In eating contests, things usually get messy to some extent… I can understand contestant Sera due to her elegant eating style, but catching food before it falls from the table like contestant Dora does is something I have never seen before.”

So the sexual harassment announcer can make serious comments too.

Sera, being a former noble lady, knew proper table manners.

Even though she ate quickly, she did not eat sloppily, and apparently she still savored the food.

Dora, on the other hand, lacked the habit of eating neatly, so spilling was unavoidable, but she disliked wasting food, so she caught it before it fell.

In a sense, both of them were handicapped, yet their speed was still overwhelming.

“Now! The number of hot dogs eaten is 256 for contestant Sera and 254 for contestant Dora! Will contestant Sera win as is, or will contestant Dora catch up!? One minute remains, the final showdown!”

“Rather than hot dogs, plain sausages might have been more popular with the male audience. What a shame.”

After a serious comment, followed by a sexual harassment remark…

Can someone do something about this announcer?

Ah, someone who looked like event staff took the sexual harassment announcer away somewhere.

It must have gone too far.

During that moment, the gap between Dora and Sera shrank to just one hot dog.

Dora’s eating speed seemed to have increased compared to earlier.

However, despite Dora’s efforts, time mercilessly ran out before she could catch up.

“And that concludes the match! The winner of the eating contest is contestant Sera!”

“I did it!”

《So frustrating!》

Sera, who won, received a set of rare and high-quality ingredients, while Dora, who narrowly placed second, received a set of high-quality but not rare ingredients.

They were all ingredient sets.

“We are back.”

《We’re back!》

The two returned after the award ceremony.

Sera was carrying both ingredient sets.

“Good job.”

“Good work… As always, that was an incredible amount of food…”

If we rank the members by how much they eat, it would be Sera and Dora in the big-eater group, me and Maria in the normal group, and Sakura and Mio in the small-eater group.

Sakura eats little for her age. It does not seem to be due to malnutrition, though…

“Just watching makes you feel full, doesn’t it?”

“Yes… I think I will keep lunch light…”

“Same here.”

The small-eater group apparently eats less just by watching the eating contest.

Personally, I was starting to feel hungry…

“Did you two enjoy yourselves?”

《I lost and I’m frustrated! But it was tasty!》

“I enjoyed it as well. Still, the end was dangerous. Dora-san’s eating speed increased.”

“Was there a reason for that?”

I was curious as well, so I asked Dora.

《Um, I realized that the way to eat a lot and the way to eat fast are different.》

“I see, so you have finally entered that realm, Dora-san. Indeed. If time is running out and you still have leeway, switching your eating method is more efficient. I did not use it this time because I bound myself to a constant pace.”

《Next time I’ll eat even better, so I won’t lose to Sera!》

“I will not lose so easily. When I get serious, I have over ten other strategies.”

“…”

I mean, this is starting to sound like an eating battle manga…

“Oh right! Show us the prize ingredients!”

“Of course.”

Prompted by Mio, Sera set down the ingredient sets and opened them.

“Mm-hm, there are some pretty good items here!”

“They all appear to be high-quality ingredients. We should have Mio-san cook them.”

《Mio, please!》

“Alright! Leave it to Mio-chan!”

With Mio so enthusiastic, tonight’s dinner was bound to be extravagant.

We also had the discount tickets from sponsor shops, so we would not lack local ingredients.

Next was Sakura’s wish, the flea market.

“Alta told me that the book I was looking for is being sold…”

According to Sakura, the series had six volumes, and she was missing only the final sixth volume.

She was desperate to know how it ended.

“If you had told us, we would have prioritized Sakura’s schedule… What if it sold out?”

“Indeed. There will be other chances for eating contests.”

Neither my martial arts tournament nor Sera’s eating contest were one-time events.

There was no issue with prioritizing Sakura, whose desired item could sell out.

“It is alright… The book only started being sold around the time the cooking contest ended…”

“If that is the case, then fine… It has not been sold yet, has it?”

A: It has not been sold.

The flea market venue was a fairly large park.

Participants displayed their goods wherever they liked.

We put browsing aside and headed straight for Sakura’s target.

At the destination, there was a large quantity of books placed on a cart.

Sakura immediately picked up one book and handed it to the elderly shopkeeper.

“I will take this…”

“Alright. That will be 1,000 gold.”

It seems that a Japanese person once passed down printing technology in this world, so books are relatively widespread.

However, since it became widespread only fairly recently, books from before that time are valuable.

Printing exists, but there is no means of duplication. Recreating them for printing is also labor-intensive, so unless it is a bestseller, it is not uncommon for books to be one-of-a-kind.

If this had been a truly rare book, the price being two or three digits higher would not have been strange.

Having completed the purchase safely, Sakura let out a sigh of relief.

“I am glad I could buy it… The binding is beautiful, so it looks nice on a bookshelf…”

As an aside, the ones who have bookshelves in their private rooms at the mansion are Sakura, Mio, and Maria.

Sakura focuses on stories, Mio on recipe books, and Maria writes down information about my original world. It is interesting that two of them are writers rather than buyers.

“Maybe I should get a bookshelf too, to appeal my intellect. Or glasses.”

“Glasses equaling intellect is a pretty old image. And in the first place, Master, are you intellectual?”

Mio’s comment made me think again.

“…My grades were not bad. I got all the multiple-choice questions right.”

“Giving you multiple-choice questions was the examiner’s mistake. What about written questions?”

“I think I did reasonably well… Yeah, let’s drop the intellectual appeal.”

To begin with, my best friend was a genuine intellectual, so the bar for the word “intellectual” is high.

I have not reached what I consider “intellectual.” I should just give up quietly.

“Maria. You do not need to prepare a bookshelf.”

“…Yes.”

Maria’s response was hesitant.

She must have started preparing as soon as I mentioned it through telepathy.

A: She had.

“Ah, but I might want to see Master wearing glasses. Don’t you think so too, Sakura-sama?”

“Yes… I would like to see it a little…”

“…Maria, prepare some glasses. Do not put any prescription in them.”

“Yes!”

When girls say they want to see you in glasses, you cannot really say no.

After this, glasses were added to the main products of the Advance Trading Company, but that is another story.

With Sakura’s objective achieved, we decided to stay at the flea market.

By order, we should have gone to Maria’s desired location next, but in times like this, Maria does not assert herself. This time as well, she said she had no particular wish and that we should go wherever others wanted.

So, since it was lunchtime, we wandered around while casually buying food from stalls.

“The two of you can still eat, huh…”

Despite having eaten so much at the eating contest, Sera and Dora were each holding more than a normal portion of food. Meanwhile, Sakura and Mio were eating lightly, just as they said earlier…

“The time limit simply came. I was not full!”

《I can still eat a lot!》

“Seriously…”

Even Sakura was taken aback, and honestly, so was I.

If the contest had been decided by quantity instead of time, it would have dragged on considerably.

“I was wondering, do your stomachs even have a limit?”

“Recently, without ‘ration balls’, I almost never feel full.”

《Me too!》

“Wow…”

Mio was also taken aback by that answer.

The only one not reacting was Maria.

When it is not related to me, she rarely shows surprise or agitation…

“Thinking about it that way, having you create the magic ‘ration balls’ that can fill Sera early on was the right choice.”

“As expected of Jin-sama’s insight and Sakura-sama’s power.”

Maria immediately praised me.

“Yes, it truly helps us. However, recently, it is regrettable that we have fewer opportunities to eat Master’s ‘ration balls’.”

In the past, I, with my large MP pool, made them almost exclusively, but now my subordinates have sufficient stats, so the opportunities to make ‘ration balls’ have decreased considerably.

《Dora likes the ones Master makes the most!》

“Huh? Do ‘ration balls’ have a taste?”

I have never eaten a ‘ration ball,’ so I do not know what they taste like.

“Of course they do. They are neither delicious nor unpleasant, a mysterious taste. However, depending on the provider of the magic power, what one feels when the effect manifests differs. Master’s ones feel… comforting.”

《I like them!》

‘Ration balls’ are magic that turns magic power into nutrition.

It is not unreasonable that the resulting item is influenced by the nature of the magic before conversion.

“When you put it that way, I am curious about the taste, but eating my own ‘ration balls’ would not have any effect…”

In fact, for ‘ration balls’ to be effective, the condition is that they must be made with someone else’s magic power.

Eating ones you make yourself does not turn into nutrients.

That is why Sera does not make ‘ration balls’ with her own magic power.

“Next time, how about we have a ‘ration ball exchange’? We form a circle and eat the ‘ration ball’ made by the person next to us. Or we play music, and when it stops, we eat the one we are holding.”

“Like a Christmas gift exchange?”

Honestly, that was the image I had in mind when I said it.

“Jin-sama, please be careful to lower the nutritional value.”

“Yeah, I know.”

I did not need Maria to tell me that.

Unadjusted ‘ration balls’ are not something ordinary people should eat.

If I recall correctly, one orb provided enough nutrition for twenty adults.

Since the nutritional value can be adjusted freely, making them as low as possible should be fine.

How low would the lowest setting be?

A: At the lowest setting, it would be about the amount a small-eating woman consumes in one meal. You may consider it equivalent to one of Sakura’s meals.

Even then, it is still a light meal.

“It would not be recommended to make a meal solely out of ‘ration balls’. Eating is not just about nutrition; the act of chewing itself has meaning.”

“We also almost never finish a meal with only ‘ration balls’. Warm meals are the best.”

“Yeah. If we do it, let us limit it to once.”

‘Ration balls’ are meant to supplement deficiencies, not serve as a staple food. If I am just curious about the taste, one exchange will suffice.

At the time, I did not realize it.

There would be an opportunity to obtain a ‘ration ball’ I made, just once. What that would mean…

Later, the ‘ration ball exchange,’ with over a thousand subordinates participating, would all begin from this trivial conversation.

After lightly filling our stomachs, we properly browsed the flea market.

Most of the time when I go to flea markets, I find some kind of hidden gem, but strangely, today I found nothing at all.

With no choice, I bought a few random ornaments.

Probably something like a relative of a beckoning cat or a tanuki statue. They were small, so they could be casually displayed on a shelf.

“Master, your story has no coherence.”

“No, since we came all this way, you would want to buy something, right? If there was a hidden gem, I would buy it without hesitation, but if there is nothing, I have to buy something random, do I not?”

“Is that not a bit too random? Did you really want them?”

“…”

Since I did not really want them, I could not comment.

“Excuse me. I will take the same thing.”

While I was talking with Mio, Maria purchased the same items.

“…In a sense, Maria-chan really wanted them. Because they match Master’s.”

“Yeah…”

On the shelves in Maria’s room, many of the same items as mine can be seen.

When entering Maria’s room, I sometimes momentarily mistake it for my own.

While there are some differences, like the bookshelf mentioned earlier, the basic layout is remarkably similar.

Even so, it is rare to find no hidden gems at all…

Alta, do you know anything about this?

A: To prevent spoilers, since it was unclear whether the hidden items would involve Master, I had Nino collect them. There were many fairly valuable items, so I judged that securing them was necessary.

So it was Alta’s doing…

No wonder there were no hidden gems left after she collected them using \<Clairvoyance>.

Could it be that Nino declined to come along because of this? If so, I feel bad…

A: No. After declining to accompany you, Nino requested work, so I asked her. Originally, I planned to call someone else.

Is Nino becoming a workaholic? Is she okay?

A: Maid vacations are mandatory, so there is no issue. I reminded the head maid, Lucea, that resting is also part of the job.

Oh, a white workplace.

Though the fact that she needs to be reminded, and that it is still work in the end, is concerning…

…Wait? Now that I think about it, I do not see Maria resting very often…

“Jin-sama, I use \<Ultra Rest> and \<Deep Sleep Quick Wake> in combination to rest efficiently in a short time, so there is absolutely no problem. More importantly, being by Jin-sama’s side is what matters.”

Oh, a black workplace.

She is even using what sound like unique-class skills to rest.

So the true workaholic was Maria…

“Relying on skills to rest seems questionable…”

“…If I try to rest for long, I worry about Jin-sama and cannot sleep.”

“That is serious… Do not overdo it.”

“Yes.”

With Maria, perhaps it is best to let her do as she likes, in many senses.

After thoroughly enjoying the flea market and rampaging through events with priority participation rights, we went to the beach at the edge of the island.

According to the plan, we would head to the drifting island first thing tomorrow morning, so this was like a final inspection.

There was a sailing ship there, more impressive than I had expected.

Its size was similar to the many ships around it, but its fundamental construction and equipment were entirely different.

A: The one here is a prototype. The main one was built elsewhere.

No wonder I had not seen it until now.

“Does everything look good for tomorrow?”

“Hm? Oh, it is you guys. As you can see, there are no problems.”

When I asked a sea man who was working, he gave a reassuring answer.

Though he was working, it seemed that preparations were already complete, and he was just repeating inspections.

“Oh, you were here as well.”

The other intellectual-looking man with glasses also noticed us.

His name was… Isle, I believe.

“I came to check if there were any changes to tomorrow’s plans.”

“Thanks to you, the ship was completed safely. It turned out better than planned, but it feels a bit wasteful to discard it after a single voyage.”

The two of them had no intention of returning from the drifting island.

Naturally, the ship did not include any functions for returning.

“It is a bit late to say that. You decided to go to that island even if it meant throwing everything away, did you not?”

“Of course. It is merely self-praise that something so good came out.”

No matter how good it was, to them it was only a means, not the objective.

“Hey, once everything is done, if you do not need it, could you give me that ship?”

“Huh? What are you saying?”

“Even if you return with your family, you will not need that ship anymore, right? If it is not completely destroyed, give it to me as a keepsake.”

It would be a waste to leave such a well-made ship on the drifting island.

If so, it would be better for me to take it home.

“I do not mind, but… are you sane?”

I am sane.

“You have provided financial support, so I do not mind either. I am curious how you plan to bring it back, though…”

“That will be for you to see.”

And thus, I ended up acquiring both the ship for the outbound journey and a ship for the return.

---

**AN:** I will not go to the Hercules Empire (I state this clearly).

+++

## **193: Landing and an Unknown Threat**

**AN:** Updates will be on a 20-day interval for a while.

I probably will not make it for April Fools either…

Since the main story is behind, I am not going to divert resources to April Fools.

---

Early in the morning, we gathered at Earth and Isle’s hut.

“Alright, just to be safe, let’s review things once more.”

Saying that, Earth explained the drifting island landing plan again.

First, our destination is the rear of the drifting island, in the direction of the Island Whale’s tail.

The head side of the Island Whale is usually like a cliff, and there is no way it could be used for landing.

In contrast, the tail side is shallow. The waves are rough, but it is possible to approach by boat.

As an aside, the reason the head side forms a cliff is to prevent seawater from flowing onto the island.

Also, on stormy days, it swims more slowly and lowers its head, so there are apparently cases where castaways end up washed onto it.

There are many mysteries surrounding the ecology of Island Whales.

The landing plan itself is simple.

The only thing attached to the boat is a magical tool that lets it glide over the water’s surface, and for the sake of weight reduction, no rotary propulsion system is mounted at all.

A normal boat would get caught in the waves and sink, so we use \<Wind Magic> to build momentum, gliding and leaping across the water’s surface as we advance.

Even if the waves are large, the theory is that a lightweight boat can ride over them without issue.

Apparently the two of them had spent a long time testing various things, but it did not sound particularly interesting, so I asked them to skip the details.

“I can leave the \<Wind Magic> to you, right?”

“Yeah. I have practiced.”

That practice involved producing wind as strong as possible, right up to the limit where it would not destroy the sails.

“Jin-san’s magic is amazing. He grasped the knack almost immediately, and the output is more than sufficient.”

“If Isle says so, then it should be fine. To be honest, relying on just Isle’s \<Wind Magic> made me a bit uneasy.”

“Yes. Even being generous, the success rate was only around thirty percent. Thanks to Jin-san, the probability has gone up significantly. Thank you very much.”

According to them, even at its best, the success rate was only about thirty percent.

Including their lack of funds, it was an extremely tight plan.

“Do not worry about it. Our own objective will be fulfilled too.”

“Yeah, that insane objective of drifting island tourism, huh…”

Earth says something rude. I will not deny it.

“Continuing on. The drifting island’s route is basically the same every year. When there is a storm, it seems to speed up to make up for lost time. That is not the case right now, so we do not need to worry about sudden course changes or acceleration. …Well, I cannot say it is absolutely certain since I have not exactly asked the drifting island itself.”

Based on the positional relationship with the Island Whale, the plan is to overtake it once, then make a U-turn and approach from behind.

Ideally, noon would put us closer and eliminate unnecessary movement, but by then tourists would be swarming the area, so they decided to execute the plan early in the morning, even knowing it would involve extra effort.

“Closest view of the Island Whale equals easiest place to board”, so there was no helping it.

“If nothing goes wrong, this should let us land on the drifting island…”

At that point, Earth’s expression darkened.

“Is there something you are worried about?”

I had asked before, but it did not seem like a plan with any obvious problems.

Of course, abnormal situations are common, but still…

“…There is.”

“To be honest, there is a concern we simply cannot verify, and we have not told Jin-san about it.”

Isle picked up where Earth left off.

“To be frank, with a plan at this level, it would not be impossible for adventurers to come up with it. There are \<Wind Magic> users, and boats that glide across the water are not particularly rare.”

“We did what we could to raise the success rate, but at its core, it is just a product of generally available technology.”

Now that they mentioned it, the landing plan was simple enough that adventurers could probably reproduce it.

Controlling \<Wind Magic> would not be easy, but it was not impossible either.

“However, as far as we know, there are no adventurers who deliberately tried to reach the drifting island and succeeded. Even the letters that came from the drifting island make no mention of that.”

“We think that, besides the waves, there is something else on the drifting island that rejects landing.”

“This is something we cannot test, so it is a complete gamble.”

“Yes, yes, question!”

At that point, Mio raised her hand.

“Why are you bringing this up now? You did not say anything about it the day before yesterday, did you?”

“”…””

Earth and Isle both looked uncomfortable.

“…Sorry. We did not say anything because we did not want to scare you off and have you withdraw your support.”

“We are truly sorry for deceiving you.”

The two of them bowed their heads apologetically.

As mentioned earlier, their plan was tight in many ways.

Even if the success rate was low, they would have departed anyway. Still, if the probability could be increased, there was no reason not to do so.

They probably could not bring themselves to mention a fact that might make me pull my funding before the boat was completed.

“The thirty percent success rate does not account for the unknown factor. To be honest, I think it is a bad gamble. So let me ask again. Will you ride our boat?”

“Sorry, but even if you do not ride, we cannot refund the money. We put our entire fortune into this plan.”

To be honest, I did not expect to be asked that at this point.

If I were the kind of person who would stop over a slight increase in danger, I would not have agreed to come along in the first place.

“My answer will not change, so there is no need to return the funds. …An unknown threat, huh. This is getting interesting.”

I could not hide my excitement, and a grin spread across my face.

Map prohibition is seriously fun.

“We are grateful, but you really are a strange person…”

“Yeah. I have never met someone this weird.”

At that point, Earth, who had been giving a wry smile, looked worriedly at Maria and Mio.

“You might be fine with it, but what about those girls? The premise has changed. Are you still taking them along?”

“I will go anywhere as long as Jin-sama is there.”

“There is no way I would not follow you to a place that sounds that interesting, even if you tried to stop me!”

Both of them answered immediately.

“Seems like they are serious. I am not too keen on it, but…”

“I will just take that sentiment.”

“We will be fine.”

“Yeah, it should not be a problem. We probably have better survival ability than you guys.”

If we really wanted to survive, there were any number of options.

Compared to Earth and Isle, who do not benefit from Special Powers, our survival capability is on an entirely different level.

“Got it. I will not say anything else.”

Perhaps giving up, Earth did not pursue the topic further and returned to discussing the plan.

After finishing the smaller details, we began preparing for departure at the beach.

The two of them had finished most of it yesterday, so it did not take long.

“Alright! Preparations complete.”

“Some impatient spectators are already arriving, so let us depart early.”

“Yeah. Let us get going before this turns into a hassle.”

As Isle said, several people had already come to claim viewing spots for the drifting island.

If I were an ordinary tourist, I probably would have been among the spectators too.

However, I am an aggressive tourist, so I chose to board the drifting island instead.

“Jin-kun, I think you will be fine, but please be careful…”

“Yeah. I will try.”

At the point where I am banning the map, one could argue that I am already cutting corners on being careful.

On the other hand, having a map might actually dull my sense of caution.

I sharpen my senses and recover my intuition without relying on the map.

That is the hidden objective of this map prohibition challenge.

“Maria-san, please take care of your master.”

“Yes, leave it to me.”

《Do not forget souvenirs!》

“I will handle Dora-chan’s souvenir, Mio-chan. I hope there is something good…”

For Earth and Isle, this was a life-risking landing operation, but our side was in a relaxed mood.

“Alright, we are departing.”

“Jin-san, please use \<Wind Magic>.”

“Leave it to me.”

After exchanging farewells, we boarded the boat and set sail, using my \<Wind Magic> as propulsion.

The boat gradually accelerated under the influence of \<Wind Magic>.

Once we reached a certain speed, I maintained it at a constant level.

“So far, so good.”

“Yes. As expected, it was the right choice to leave it to Jin-san.”

Even if you praise me, all I am doing is using \<Wind Magic>, you know?

“Ah, I can see the drifting island now!”

“You have good eyes, miss. You noticed it before me, and I am a sailor.”

“Ehehe!”

Mio puffed out her not-so-impressive chest proudly.

Our basic stats are different, after all.

Of course, both Maria and I had already noticed it. Maria with the map, though…

The drifting island, also known as the Island Whale, was moving faster than I had expected.

I knew it was fast, but since it was at sea, it was hard to gauge its speed.

A: Around 50 km per hour.

Thanks.

If a five-kilometer-wide island were moving at that speed, it would not be strange for massive waves to form.

However, the high waves were limited to the area around the Island Whale, and once you moved a certain distance away, there was almost no effect.

Just as the wind calamity dragon told me before, it seems that in this world, disasters other than calamity dragons are unlikely to occur.

From the front, all we could see was a cliff jutting out over the sea.

“Jin-san, just to be safe, please keep a bit more distance.”

“Understood.”

Our boat passed the Island Whale while maintaining a distance where the waves had no influence.

The sides of the Island Whale were also mostly cliff-like, but the cliffs gradually lowered as we moved toward the tail.

Beyond the cliffs, dense forest spread out, and we could not see deep inside.

…Why are there trees growing on top of a whale?

A: Nutrient-rich moss-like matter grows on the Island Whale’s back. Over a long period of time, the hardened moss became land, effectively forming an island.

What a ridiculous ecology.

Well, even though it is called an Island Whale, it is neither an island nor a whale, but a whale-shaped monster.

Perhaps it is wrong to think of it in terms of normal whales at all.

“Jin-san, we have passed the drifting island. Please turn left and approach from behind. We will perform maximum acceleration just before the waves become too high. Please follow Earth-san’s instructions at that point.”

“Got it. I will leave the timing to you.”

“Leave it to me! More importantly, do you have enough mana left?”

“Yeah. It has not even dropped by one percent, so I am fine.”

To be precise, natural recovery exceeds consumption, so saying it has not dropped at all would be more accurate.

“”…””

Huh? Why are they both speechless?

Well, whatever.

Following Isle’s instructions, I turned to take position behind the Island Whale.
