As I had heard, only the tail side was not a cliff but a beach, making it suitable for landing.

Of course, before that, we had to get past the raging waves.

And that was likely where the unknown threat awaited us.

Here are the stats for the unknown threat.

Basilisk

LV50

\<Petrifying Evil Eye LV5>

Title: -‘s Familiar

Notes: A giant lizard that petrifies what it sees.

…I sensed its presence and stared, which let me spot it hiding in the forest.

Once I have found something, checking its status is practically a reflex, so it cannot be helped.

\<Petrifying Evil Eye>

Inflicts the Petrification status ailment on a visually recognized target (single). Success rate varies based on skill level, distance, and resistance.

Now I understood why no one could reach the Island Whale.

The basilisk was probably petrifying anyone who approached the island. If you were petrified on a boat rocking in waves, there would be no way to survive.

And just like that, the unknown threat stopped being unknown before it even got its turn.

I went to the trouble of banning the map too…

By the way, what does this “-‘s Familiar” mean?

A: This display appears when someone without a name tames it.

So it has \<Monster Taming> but no name?

There must be someone with quite a special background out there.

《It is hiding its appearance, but it cannot fully conceal its presence.》

《That is not just presence, that is outright killing intent. Jin-sama, shall I eliminate it?》

As the two of them said, the “unknown threat (lol)” was emitting intense killing intent.

And it was clearly directed at us.

《No, let us leave it for now. At the very least, petrification will not work on us.》

《But those two would be petrified normally, would they not? Is that okay?》

Earth and Isle did not have high enough stats to resist the basilisk’s petrification.

They would definitely be petrified.

《I would not say it is okay, but if possible, I want to fight the basilisk directly. It is clearly a monster with circumstances, so it would be a waste to just eliminate it from afar, right?》

《You are treating it completely like an event…》

Exactly.

Cross the raging waves, overcome the basilisk threat, and reach the Island Whale.

Skipping pre-events would be far too wasteful.

“Hey! It is about time to accelerate!”

“Yeah! Hold on tight!”

It seemed the acceleration timing had arrived while we were communicating telepathically.

I warned everyone and increased the output of my \<Wind Magic>.

“Whoa! That is some acceleration!”

“With this acceleration, we should theoretically be able to clear the waves!”

The boat continued accelerating and finally reached the waves caused by the Island Whale.

The next moment, using the wave as a ramp, the boat soared high into the air.

It landed, glided over the water, then used another wave as a ramp to jump again, repeating the process.

We were shaken up and down like a roller coaster.

“Wooooah!”

“Aaaaaah!”

“Kyaaaaa!”

Earth, Isle, and Mio screamed.

Only Mio was smiling, clearly enjoying herself.

《If you like scream rides that much, should I set up a haunted house for you?》

《No! Stop!》

Mio’s excitement vanished, and she refused flatly with a serious face.

After that, the endurance test for our inner ears continued, and when we had crossed about half the waves, something changed.

“Hey! Isle! What is wrong?!”

“I do not… know… My… body… will not… move…”

Beside the shouting Earth, Isle’s body began to turn to stone.

The petrification spread across his entire body in an instant, completing a stone statue frozen in terror.

“S-so this is it… No wonder no bodies ever washed ashore…”

Seeing Isle turned to stone, Earth seemed to understand what had happened.

If you turned into stone and the boat capsized, you would sink straight to the bottom of the sea.

Naturally, the body would never wash up anywhere.

“Looks like this is as far as I go too…”

Sure enough, Earth’s body had also begun to petrify.

Just like Isle, the stone spread gradually.

“Maria, undo it.”

“Yes.”

At my call, Maria ran over to Earth and Isle.

Being a cat beastkin, she maintained perfect balance even on the violently shaking boat.

Maria caught the two of them, who were turning to stone and about to fall overboard, laid them down on the deck, and cast a spell.

“‘Area Anti-Stone’.”

This was an area petrification removal spell using \<Recovery Magic>.

Few enemies use petrification, and we generally do not make mistakes that get us petrified, so this was the first time I had seen it used in actual combat.

In internal training (hard mode), Tamo-san uses petrification, so sometimes you see petrified combat maids. Petrification removal spells are used then.

“I was… what…?”

“I-I turned to stone… did I not…?”

The two whose petrification had been removed were dazed and could not grasp the situation.

“The petrification status ailment has been cured. It is dangerous, so please grab onto the boat quickly.”

“O-oh.”

“Y-yes…”

After Maria explained concisely, the two followed her instructions.

“It seems it is trying to petrify us too.”

“It is panicking because it is not working.”

The basilisk was glaring at us desperately, trying to petrify us, but since nothing happened, it was clearly flustered.

Keeping your eyes open the whole time will give you dry eyes, so be careful.

Before long, we were just a short distance from the Island Whale.

Earth and Isle were positioned so that they were well hidden behind Maria to avoid being petrified.

“We are about to beach! Hold on tight!”

Almost simultaneously with Earth’s shout, the boat rode the largest wave yet and leapt high.

-GAGAGAGAGAGAGAGAGAGA!!-

With a tremendous noise, the boat landed… or rather, was flung up onto the Island Whale’s shore.

“Ow ow ow… You guys alive?”

“Y-yes… I am somehow…”

Neither of them seemed to have any serious injuries.

“Alright, looks like everyone is safe.”

“Jin-sama, good work.”

“Ah, that was fun!”

“Why are you three so unfazed…”

Earth looked at us in disbelief as we acted like nothing had happened.

The reason we are unfazed is mainly thanks to our stats. And our skills.

“Jin-sama, it is coming.”

“Yeah, I know.”

It seemed the basilisk had given up on petrification and chosen to eliminate us directly.

The massive gray lizard (one meter tall, three meters long) lumbered toward us.

“This thing is… that basilisk you hear about in rumors?”

“It matches the information in the records. To think such a monster was living on the drifting island…”

“No wonder no one could reach it.”

Just as the two correctly understood the unknown threat, the basilisk broke into a run.

“GYRUUUUUU!!!”

Moving far faster than its appearance suggested, it slashed at Maria, who was in front, with a claw attack.

The next moment, the basilisk was flipped over.

《Jin-sama, shall I kill it?》

Maria stood atop the overturned basilisk, placing her sword against its soft-looking belly.

If I said “do it”, it would be cut open nicely.

《No, before that, get information. Disable it.》

《Understood.》

After receiving my telepathic order, Maria slashed once with her sword.

The basilisk’s limbs went limp as its tendons were severed.

I touched the basilisk and activated \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7>.

Directly touching its soul, I browsed all the information it possessed.

I see, I see. Oh, so that is how it is…!

“Alright, you can kill it.”

If it is clearly an enemy and someone else’s familiar, there is no reason to keep it alive.

“Yes.”

With another slash of her sword, all strength drained from the basilisk’s body.

Since I was nearby, she avoided a method that would cause blood to spray everywhere.

“Amazing… You took down a basilisk instantly.”

“It really was the right decision to have Jin-san and the others accompany us…”

“Yeah. Absolutely.”

If they had come alone, they would have been helpless the moment petrification occurred.

From the memories I saw, the basilisk’s purpose was “to prevent landing on this island”, so the chance of the two of them reaching the drifting island was extremely low.

As an aside, it ignores castaways from storms because they do not meet its conditions.

Also, on stormy days, visibility is poor, which interferes with petrification.

In fact, attempting to land on a rainy day would slightly increase the success rate, but since people normally avoid that, no one had noticed until now.

“Alright then, shall we start exploring the island?”

“Oh, treasure! Treasure!”

Having arrived at Treasure Island (temporary), Mio and I were fired up.

Maria was just along for the ride.

“Wait! Family comes first!”

“Yes! Please let us meet them as soon as possible!”

Right, their goal was to reunite with their family. To be honest, I had forgotten.

“I am joking, joking. Of course, treasure hunting comes after searching for people.”

“…”

Mio laughed and said it was a joke, but I maintained silence.

“Huh? Master, you were joking too… right?”

“…”

When Mio asked, having noticed something, I quietly averted my gaze.

Yes. I was completely in exploration mode.

After that, we began walking toward the center of the island to search for Earth and Isle’s family.

According to letters that had washed ashore in the past, castaways lived in the central area of the island.

Unfortunately, no specific location was written, but the judgment was that heading toward the center should yield some kind of clue.

“We really cannot thank you enough…”

“Yes. We are deeply grateful…”

Earth and Isle spoke apologetically.

The reason was simple. They had no equipment suitable for moving through the forest, so we lent them ours.

Having devoted all their efforts to landing, they had not considered what came after.

I understand they planned to settle here permanently, but was that not a bit careless?

“Well, we did have an item box at first, but we sold it because we were broke…”

“We should have bought one when we received financial support…”

“These two really changed from my first impression… Are they clumsy?”

There is no demand for clumsy men (a universal truth).

All of us were equipped with the forest exploration set produced by Advance Trading Company.

For some reason, there were a lot of them inside \<Infinite Storage>.

After advancing a bit into the forest, monsters began appearing as expected. Maria killed them instantly.

They were all weak monsters, so Earth, who trained his body, and Isle, who could at least use magic, could probably have handled them. Being swarmed would have been tough, though.

“This is a hunting trace.”

As we went further, we began finding signs of human activity in the forest.

From that point on, Earth and Isle spoke less, and their eyes grew more serious.

“Why… is no one here…?”

Earth muttered this when we were just a short distance from the island’s center.

There were traces of people everywhere, yet no sign of human presence at all.

The traces increased, but none of them were recent.

An obvious unnaturalness stood out.

“Hey! There was a settlement!”

“Let us hurry!”

Spotting an open area in the forest and a human settlement, the two of them broke into a run.

“It really was a good thing we came along.”

“Yeah.”

They could not see it, but with our high stats, we could.

What had happened in the settlement ahead.

When we followed after them, just as expected, the two had collapsed inside the settlement, standing dazed.

What lay within the settlement were nothing but brutally destroyed stone statues.

Most were shattered and no longer retained their original forms, but it was clear they had once been humanoid.

Not just one or two, but over ten.

If you knew nothing, they would simply look like eerie stone statues.

However, for Earth and Isle, seeing stone statues on this island was enough to understand what had happened.

This settlement had been destroyed by the basilisk.

Next time: “Petrification Removal and the Oni Hero.” Look forward to it!

## **194: The Oni Hero and Training**

**AN:** This chapter differs from the contents announced in the previous preview.

I do have an idea for an April Fool’s joke, but whether I can write it in time is another matter. Probably impossible.

---

Now then, though it is rather late, let me talk a bit about the abnormal status known as “Petrification”.

Petrification is, as the characters literally say, an abnormal status in which the body turns to stone.

The characteristics of petrification are as follows.

– There is no consciousness.

– The subject enters a state of suspended animation.

– HP does not change.

– There is no natural recovery.

– When petrification is cured, the condition of any damage to the stone remains as-is.

Because it is a state of suspended animation and HP does not change, it means that one cannot die while petrified.

Conversely, no matter how badly damaged the stone statue may be, as long as it remains petrified, it does not die.

Strictly speaking, if the entire body melts away or otherwise completely disappears, it is treated as death.

Since there is no natural recovery, petrification must be cured by magic or medicine. However, if the stone statue is damaged, the person will revive in that exact state.

Naturally, even if you glue the pieces back together, they will fall apart again upon revival. They die.

Also, if only part of the damaged body has petrification cured, and that part happens to be a vital area that cannot be treated as a mere “loss”, then death will occur.

In other words, if someone is damaged beyond the level at which survival is possible while petrified, then at best they die. At worst, they are trapped forever in an eternal prison where they cannot even die.

The three of us, Maria, Mio, and I, approached Earth and Isle, who had collapsed to the ground.

“No way… No way…”

“Damn it… We were too late…”

The two of them muttered despairingly as they stared at the settlement.

Anyone who understands petrification would immediately realize that there is no hope left in this situation.

“Judging by the state of the settlement, this doesn’t look like something that happened just yesterday or today.”

“Yes. I believe about the same amount of time has passed as with the hunting traces.”

Looking over the settlement, we judged that the petrification was not a recent event.

“Maybe by the time the letter reached them, things were already like this.”

Even if a letter was sent floating in a bottle, it would have taken time to arrive.

As Mio said, there was a real possibility that it was already too late by the time the letter was received.

Now then, what should we do about this situation…?

“I… have a request for you…”

As I was lost in thought, Earth spoke up.

When he lifted his face, his expression was a mix of despair and resolve.

“Could you… cast a petrification cure spell on the people of this settlement…?”

That was a plea asking me to let the people of this settlement die.

“What are you saying!? Are you planning to kill them!?”

“What else can we do for them!?”

When Isle raised his voice, Earth shouted back at him.

Although petrification is not a common abnormal status, it is considered common sense that if one encounters someone who has been petrified and catastrophically damaged, then if possible, curing the petrification and letting them die is the proper courtesy.

Well, turning a shattered stone statue back into flesh results in a perfectly flawless gore scene, so there is almost no one who would willingly do it…

“That may be so… but still…!”

Isle could not accept it, yet he had no way to refute it.

Just like that, he fell silent.

…Now then, in truth, restoring petrified people is not all that difficult.

You just put the fragments of the stone statue into \<Infinite Storage> and heal them.

\<Assembly> is handled automatically by \<Infinite Storage>, and even if some fragments are missing, it is no problem as long as you use the “Revive” spell to restore lost parts.

The problem is that results related to Special Powers are, as a rule, kept secret.

If there is an alternative method, I do not mind, but I have a policy of only showing things that can only be done with Special Powers to involved parties (mainly slaves).

Put simply, I am agonizing over what to do with the two old men.

Old-man slaves would benefit absolutely no one…

As an aside, I do plan to forcibly enslave the petrified people when curing them.

It is less troublesome to secure the initiative before getting into detailed discussions.

As I was idly thinking such things, I sensed something approaching us.

“Jin-sama, please step back.”

“Maria, don’t kill her.”

“Yes.”

I left the approaching presence to Maria.

“Gyaaaaaaaaaah!!”

Charging out of the depths of the forest with a roar was a single girl.

Two horns protruded from her black hair, so her race was Oni.

She looked to be in her mid-teens, with a toned, healthy body. What should be prominent was certainly prominent.

The problem was that she was wearing nothing but a single rag, through the gaps of which all sorts of things could be seen, and that her left arm was missing.

Well then, let’s take a look at her status.

Name: Asuka

LV 30

Gender: Female

Age: 12

Race: Oni

Title: Oni Hero

Skills:

Martial Arts

\<Swordsmanship LV4>

Magic

\<Light Magic LV4>

Physical

\<Body Reinforcement LV4> \<HP Auto-Recovery LV4> \<MP Auto-Recovery LV4> \<Fighting Spirit LV4>

Other

\<Hero LV4> \<Seal LV3> \<Oni Tag: Mighty Arm LV >

Now then, here are the points worth commenting on after seeing her status.

– Why is an Oni Hero in a place like this?

– She doesn’t look 12 at all.

– Why is the \<Seal> skill only partially released?

– There is an obviously unique-looking skill here?

For now, this means we have humans, beastkin, dwarves, elves, smallfolk, and now oni. All the major races are accounted for. Good, good…?

“Don’t, near village!!!”

The girl shouted in broken speech and launched a flying kick at Maria, who was at the front.

Maria evaded with minimal movement and, as they passed each other, drove the heel of her palm into the girl’s chin.

It was a splendid counter that used the opponent’s momentum.

“Guh!?”

The girl lost her balance midair and rolled along the ground without even managing to land properly. That had to hurt.

While she was down, we took the two old men and moved away.

“Gh… guh…”

The counter to the chin seemed to have hit hard, and the girl staggered unsteadily.

Maria remained where she was, watching the girl’s condition.

“If it were Maria-chan, you could have taken her consciousness with that one hit, right?”

When Mio muttered that, Maria replied via telepathy.

《This is a good opportunity, so I intend to give her a bit of training.》

《Eh? Sorry, I don’t understand.》

Mio was bewildered by Maria’s words.

《Right now, she is trying to fight an enemy seriously. As combat experience, this is the highest grade possible. I plan to guide her properly and hammer technique into her.》

《???》

Mio’s confusion only deepened.

《Jin-sama will not ignore someone who possesses the \<Hero> skill. In other words, she will join Jin-sama’s ranks. If so, there is no loss in having her grow stronger from an early stage. She can safely accumulate valuable real combat experience. Do you not think this is a good opportunity?》

《I feel like there are some rather forceful assumptions in there, but I get what you’re saying…》

At last, Mio was convinced. I was too.

It seemed that, in Maria’s mind, it had already been decided that the girl would join my ranks.

What surprised me more was that Maria had deprioritized my protection.

At the moment, Sera, my substitute guard, was not present, so I only had Tamo-san as protection.

Whether I truly need a guard or not aside, I never thought Maria would reduce my protection.

…No, that was wrong.

Ten more Tamo-sans immediately joined the guard detail.

In a way that was not obvious at first glance, but absolutely airtight, the surroundings were secured.

Isn’t that a bit excessive?

《It is necessary. Please understand.》

I did not even use telepathy just now…

After waiting a bit, the girl finally recovered and glared at Maria with eyes filled with hostility.

After taking such a clean counter, it was impressive that her hostility had not faded.

“I won’t… lose… Defeat… enemy… Uaaaaaah!!!”

Shouting as if to psyche herself up, the girl activated her unique skill.

\<Oni Tag: Mighty Arm>

Creates and manipulates an invisible mighty arm.

From the girl’s left shoulder, where her arm was missing, a gigantic invisible arm sprouted.

It was invisible, but that did not mean it did not exist. Naturally, its presence could be sensed.

“Take this!”

Judging Maria to be the threat, the girl ignored us and charged straight at her.

She swung the invisible arm, attempting to smash Maria.

The name Mighty Arm was no exaggeration. If it landed cleanly, it might at least shave off a sliver of Maria’s HP.

It would then immediately be undone by \<HP Auto-Recovery>, but still…

There is a difference between taking no damage and taking an attack.

Without saying a word, Maria avoided the attack and swept the girl’s legs out from under her as she lost her balance.

The girl fell with all the momentum of her own attack, slamming into the ground without even managing a proper breakfall.

“Guh!!!”

Large, linear attacks almost never work against opponents who possess technique.

At the very least, one should create an opening before striking.

“Not yet…!”

The girl sprang back up and thrust at Maria again with the mighty arm.

It is easy to think that winding up increases power through centrifugal force, but in reality, it only increases the time until impact, makes the trajectory easier to read, and destabilizes one’s posture. There is almost nothing good about it.

Nothing surpasses a thrust delivered from a stable stance along the shortest path.

It is commendable that she learned that much in an instant, but her thinking is still shallow.

She is too focused on attacking and has no awareness at all of being attacked.

Did she think the earlier counter was just luck?

“Eh?”

The girl let out a dumbfounded sound, followed by a dull thunk.

A small stone Maria flicked struck the girl’s defenseless forehead. That had to hurt.

“Gh…!”

She fell onto her back but managed to take a breakfall, glaring at Maria.

“Not enough!”

The girl did not give up and launched another thrust, this time with caution.

-Thunk-

Too bad. If you only watch what’s in front of you, the stone Maria tossed upward while you were crouching will hit you.

“Ugh…”

A delayed attack from a blind spot might feel a bit mean.

However, it is also true that this attack could have been prevented simply by following the basics of “never taking your eyes off your opponent during combat”, or “not relying solely on sight and remaining aware of presence”.

“This time!!”

The girl, utterly undeterred, repeated her thrusts.

This time, even when stones hit her, she did not take her eyes off Maria, and her awareness range had broadened.

The learning ability of a local Hero is truly impressive.

That said, catching up to a diligent Hero is no easy feat.

Maria evaded the girl’s thrust to the outside.

“Ah!?”

The girl seemed to realize her mistake at that instant.

In fact, the “invisibility” of \<Oni Tag: Mighty Arm> only applies to others, the user herself can see the arm clearly.

In other words, it also blocks her own field of vision.

This is a flaw Maria knows well because she herself uses invisible weapons. …Mythical-grade equipment, though she rarely uses it outside of training.

“Gah!!!”

The price of not realizing that her own attack created a blind spot was a high roundhouse kick to the temple from Maria.

Unlike the warning stones, this was a direct strike to a vital point. The girl was sent flying and lost consciousness for a moment.

When Maria waited on the spot, the girl staggered back to her feet.

Despite being beaten this badly, her fighting spirit had not diminished at all.

After that, Maria continued to deflect the girl’s attacks without saying a word.

In every exchange, Maria always countered in a way that pointed out the girl’s specific flaws.

The girl also had \<HP Auto-Recovery>, so she would not die.

Teaching through pain. Maria is quite the strict instructor.

It was fortunate that the girl did not have the \<Martial Arts> skill.

The foundation of martial skills is efficiency of movement.

If the girl had possessed \<Martial Arts>, her movements would have been efficient from the start, and there would have been fewer points for Maria to correct.

However, that would merely be the skill producing correct answers.

It would not mean she understood ‘why’ something was wrong.

In the extreme, if one understands that, one can do the same thing as a skill even without possessing it.

After some time, once the openings in the girl’s attacks had clearly diminished, Maria began to actively go on the offensive.

Unfortunately, reducing openings in attack and becoming good at defense are not the same thing.

“Kuh! Tsu!?”

As proof of that, the girl failed to handle Maria’s attacks and was struck many times.

The issue was likely that the girl’s high learning ability was difficult to apply to defense.

She fell for Maria’s feints over and over, taking repeated hits.

She did not fall for the exact same feint twice, but even slight variations were enough to catch her again.

Her experience with defense was clearly far too shallow. Or perhaps it would be more accurate to say she lacked a foundation?

Given the sheer firepower of \<Oni Tag: Mighty Arm>, it is possible she never needed to defend before.

All we can do is patiently wait for Maria to drill defense into her.

“Hey, how long is this fight going to last? Well, calling it a fight might be wrong. It’s more like training…”

Just as I resolved to wait patiently, Earth asked a question that was rather late in coming.

A fair amount of time had already passed, but Earth and Isle had been completely absorbed in watching the two Heroes train.

If they had been calmly observing, they should have noticed much earlier.

“The girl came at us with killing intent, but Maria is clearly treating this as training. I have no idea how long it will last. Probably until the girl runs out of stamina. It’s not boring to watch, so let’s just leave it like this for now.”

Watching the girl’s growth is rather heartwarming.

“She is clearly connected to this village, so I’d like to hear her story if possible…”

“Once the training ends, we can talk. Don’t be in such a hurry.”

“Eh? Even after she attacked us with that much hostility?”

So Isle still had not noticed.

“Can’t you tell? The hostility has already left her eyes.”

“Eh?”

Indeed, at first she was brimming with hostility, and it did not seem like reason would reach her.

However, toward the latter half of her repeated attacks, she appeared to understand Maria’s intent through her fighting style and regained her composure.

And once she realized that intent, she did not stop fighting.

Instead, she continued to seriously attack Maria.

She acknowledged Maria as her superior and sought to learn her techniques.

I do not dislike girls with ambition.

After several more of Maria’s attacks, the girl’s movements clearly deteriorated.

“It looks like it’s almost over.”

“You can tell?”

“Yeah. Looks like she’s at her limit.”

There are techniques that can only be learned when one is exhausted.

For example, how to move one’s body when tired can only be learned when tired.

However, that kind of lesson cannot be fully conveyed through this sort of “wordless training”.

“Let’s end it here.”

Maria spoke for the first time in a while.

The next instant, Maria raised her gear by one level.

The girl, who had just barely begun to deflect some of Maria’s attacks, could not keep up with the sudden change in speed.

She took a restrained thrust from Maria to the chin and was blown away.

Her consciousness was completely cut off, and she lay on her back.

“Thank you for waiting, Jin-sama.”

“Good work. How was she?”

“Immature. She learns what she is told, but seems poor at thinking beyond that and sublimating it herself.”

When I asked Maria, who walked over as if nothing had happened, she gave a rather harsh evaluation.

‘Learning ten from one’ is not that easy, though.

“Mio, could you take care of her?”

“Roger.”

When I asked, Mio ran over to tend to the fallen girl.

Her HP had dropped considerably from the final blow. She had \<HP Auto-Recovery>, but even so, it would take a long time for her to regain consciousness.

As an aside, \<Oni Tag: Mighty Arm> vanished when the girl lost consciousness.

In truth, that skill has more advanced applications, but the girl had only been using it as a ‘replacement arm’. What a waste.

After a short while, the girl regained consciousness.

Since it would not be good to have many unfamiliar people around her, we left the response to Maria and Mio, while the men waited at a distance.

Naturally, I was within hearing range.

Earth and Isle were not.

“Are you okay? Can you talk?”

“I’m okay. Sorry for attacking you out of nowhere.”

Being able to apologize for something you regret is proof of being a decent person.

However, attacking out of nowhere is proof of not being a decent person.

Which is it?

“Can you tell us your name?”

“I’m Asuka. And you?”

“I’m Mio. Nice to meet you.”

“I’m Maria. Over there are, from the left, Jin-sama, Isle, and Earth.”

Maria introduced us to the girl, now properly identified as Asuka.

“Why did you attack us?”

“Women who came to this island on a clear day were enemies. I thought you were enemies too.”

On stormy days, castaways sometimes wash up on this island.

However, landing on this island on a clear day is difficult because of the basilisk.

Someone must have come here on a clear day before, and that person was an enemy. So she thought we were enemies as well.

“What are you doing on this island?”

“Earth and Isle have family on this island. So we came by ship.”

“Family… Everyone on this island turned to stone…”

Asuka’s expression clearly darkened.

“It’s my fault they turned to stone… I want to get stronger… I will take revenge for everyone.”

That must have been the reason she continued fighting Maria and sought strength.

“When did everyone turn to stone?”

“Um… About… three… years ago?”

That means the letter Earth and the others obtained was written more than three years ago.

“Have you talked to anyone during that time?”

“No.”

“I see…”

No wonder her speech was broken.

From age nine, for three years, the 12-year-old girl had not spoken to another person even once.

That is long enough for language skills to begin fading.

Mio’s questions continued.

“How did you manage food?”

“I killed monsters and ate them. There are also nuts.”

“You don’t live in the settlement?”

“It hurts to look at the stone fragments. I sleep away from there.”

“What about those tattered clothes?”

“They belonged to a girl from the settlement. My body suddenly got bigger, and I couldn’t wear them anymore. Chest is in the way…”

“I’m jealous…”

About Asuka’s life.

“What kind of people lived in the settlement?”

“About fifty people total. Thirty were descendants of castaways. About twenty were castaways.”

“Which were you?”

“A descendant.”

“Do you know about letters in bottles?”

“I know. We threw quite a lot of them. Did they arrive?”

“Yes. Apparently the letters said that the families of those two were alive.”

“Everyone who washed up here prayed that the letters would arrive.”

About the people of the settlement.

“Who were the enemies that came?”

“A pretty girl. A little older than I was back then.”

“Ah, about the same age as Maria-chan at the time…”

“Yes. That’s why I attacked. Sorry…”

“Why were the villagers turned to stone?”

“On a clear day, I found a strange girl and chased her. She noticed me and attacked. She ordered strong monsters to turn everyone to stone. Then she destroyed them… I can’t forgive her…”

About the enemy who attacked the village.

“What happened to your arm?”

“I was turned to stone by a monster. Someone protected me, so it was only my left arm. But because of that, the strongest person was turned to stone.”

“What was that invisible arm earlier?”

“When monsters attacked, everyone but me was turned to stone. I lost my arm and was dying. But when I woke up, my body moved better than before. Before I knew it, I could use that arm.”

Alta-san, explanation please.

A: A Hero’s \<Seal> disappears when the Hero dies. By entering a state of suspended animation and returning from it, the \<Seal> may have been partially released.

So that is why she did not learn anything besides Hero-related skills and her unique skill.

“Can we call those three over too? We won’t do anything cruel to you.”

“Okay. It’s fine.”

After hearing her story, we were allowed to join them.

Mio gave Earth and Isle a rough explanation.

“Hey, young lady, let me ask you…”

Earth asked about his family.

Fortunately or unfortunately, from the characteristics he described, Asuka seemed to understand who they were.

The same went for Isle’s family…

“I see… So they really did turn to stone…”

“If only we had come here sooner…”

“Ugh…”

Hearing about their families’ ends, the two broke down in tears.

Seeing them, Asuka also began to cry as memories resurfaced.

After the three had calmed down somewhat, Earth opened his mouth with difficulty.

“Young lady, do you know much about petrification?”

“Not much.”

“Yeah, I thought so…”

Earth then explained the characteristics of petrification and what it means to cure it.

That although they are technically alive, they have no consciousness and will never return.

That curing petrification and letting them die is an act of kindness.

“No! Everyone is still alive! I don’t want them to die!”

“But they will never return… Leaving them like this is cruel, isn’t it?”

“No! No! Absolutely not!”

Asuka became like a stubborn child.

Given her age and mental development, it is understandable. That said, her body has grown unnecessarily well…

Then Asuka clung to me, the one who could cure petrification.

“I’ll do anything! Anything, so please save everyone!”

Alright. “We’ll do anything”, secured.

---

**AN:** A protagonist who takes advantage of weakness. Time to show my true colors.

The naming of \<Oni Tag: Mighty Arm> was self-praise.

## **195: Releasing Petrification and the Mountain of Salt**

**AN:** It is recommended that you read the final line of Chapter 193 before reading this chapter.

---

Asuka said she would “do anything”, so I decided to test the resolve behind those words.

“Then if I told you to become my slave, would you do it?”

“Uwaa…”

For some reason, Mio recoiled.

“Slave… what?”

Asuka tilted her head and asked back.

It seemed she did not even know the word “slave” itself.

Considering there would be no opportunity to use a word like that on this island, it was not surprising that Asuka, who was born here (now 9 years old), did not know it.

“If you become my slave, you have to obey everything I say, forever. You would have no freedom, and you would keep doing ‘anything’ until the day you die.”

It was a rough explanation, but if it conveyed how miserable it was, that was enough.

“Hmm. No freedom…?”

For some reason, Mio tilted her head.

“I will! If everyone can be saved!”

Asuka answered instantly.

Local Heroes in this world really are all decisive to a fault.

“Hey, what is all this about? A slave?”

Earth called out to me with a suspicious look.

Well, if you suddenly tell a girl to become a slave, that reaction is understandable.

Next, I had to decide what to do with the two middle-aged men, something I had coincidentally been thinking about just before Asuka appeared.

Honestly, I did not need them, but after showing them what I was about to do, I could not just leave them be.

They had come this far together with us. Since it was a good opportunity, I would let them choose.

“If it were possible to save the people who were petrified and shattered, how far would you be willing to go? Could you accept becoming a slave?”

If they could accept becoming slaves, I would reunite them with their families who had been released from petrification.

If they could not, that would be the end of it. After sending them back from the island, I would come here again later and restore the petrified people. Naturally, I would not let them meet.

“Of course. If our families can be saved by us becoming slaves, that is cheap.”

“Yeah. If an old man like me will do, I will become a slave or anything else.”

Surprisingly, neither Isle nor Earth hesitated at all in their answers.

They were not even local Heroes, yet they were just as decisive.

“From the start, if our families had already died, we were prepared to end our lives here.”

“At the very least, we wanted to die in the same place.”

The two calmly spoke of their planned suicides.

If I had followed Earth’s wish and released the petrification without repairing the shattered bodies, killing the petrified people, then Earth and Isle would have killed themselves on the spot as well.

“That is the first I have heard of it.”

“It was not something we needed to tell you. Besides, we decided it quite a while ago.”

“Since we did not know the situation on this island, we thought it best to decide what to do in advance.”

“Petrification was unexpected, but… well, we can treat it the same as death.”

“We were already prepared to die. Deciding to become slaves was easy.”

I see. There was no need to test the resolve of these two men after all.

Very well. In that case, I would answer that resolve with my own.

Without a word, I activated the spell “Vacuum” from \<Infinite Storage>.

Fragments of a stone statue, exactly one person’s worth, gathered at my feet.

“Hey!? The statue fragments gathered in an instant!”

“What is this…?”

“Big sister Annie!”

Asuka could tell who it was just from the fragments…

I collected the fragments of Annie (14 years old) into \<Infinite Storage>.

“Big sister Annie!?”

“Is that the spell ‘Storage’?”

“There was no chant, was there?”

Using the synthesis function of \<Infinite Storage>, the stone statue was automatically assembled.

For parts that were missing because fragments were not present nearby, I used “Revive.”

Quietly, I activated \<Slave Arts> and made Annie (a dog beastkin) my slave without resistance.

Then, when I used “Anti-Stone” on the restored statue, the petrification was released, and Annie (small-statured), in her natural state, came out of \<Infinite Storage>.

With an unfamiliar man watching, leaving her naked would be pitiful.

After dressing her in something like a robe, I activated “Anti-Stone.”

At the same time as the petrification was released, I caught Annie (cute type) in a princess carry as she emerged from \<Infinite Storage>.

“Big sister Annie!!!???”

Asuka stared with her eyes wide open in shock.

“Ugh… I… what am I…?”

Petrification is just a normal status ailment.

If someone is petrified while conscious, once the petrification is released, they regain consciousness immediately.

“Big sister Annie!”

When I set Annie (in striped panties) down on the ground, Asuka clung to her, burying her face against her.

Asuka’s lines were starting to get repetitive.

“Eh…? Who… are you…?”

I had expected an emotional reunion, but what came back from Annie (silver semi-long hair) was that merciless question.

“You… do not remember…?”

Asuka lifted her face, her expression full of despair.

“Hey, can something like that really happen?”

“No, at least I have never heard of it.”

From the two men’s perspective, they were probably worried that their own families might end up the same way.

“Do you know where you are?”

“Um… this is the settlement where I live. Ah, who are you…?”

Ignoring the three of them, I questioned Annie (nice hips), and she gave the correct answer.

This was probably…

“My name is Jin. What is your name?”

“A-Annie.”

“Do you recognize this girl?”

I pointed at Asuka.

“No, I do not.”

“Then do you know a girl around nine years old?”

“Um… Asuka-chan and… eh…? Sniff sniff…”

Annie (flat-chested), having noticed something, sniffed Asuka, who was clinging to her.

Then she frowned. Asuka… smelled, due to living in the wild…!!!

“Ugh… but still, you really are Asuka-chan, right?”

“Big sister Annie!!!”

Asuka buried her face again. Annie frowned and muttered quietly, “Smelly…”

Yes. Annie (nearsighted) simply did not recognize Asuka because her appearance had changed too much. Also, she could not tell from the smell because it was not the smell of someone she knew.

After that, we briefly explained the situation to Annie.

“Three years… I can hardly believe it, but with the settlement in this state, it must be true…”

Annie accepted the truth surprisingly easily.

“How much do you remember from when you were petrified?”

“I remember an adventurer shouting, ‘A cockatrice is coming!’ and seeing a bird-like monster.”

“What…?”

“Eh? W-what is wrong…?”

My expression hardened, and Annie stiffened.

“Hey, what is it?”

“Is there something bothering you?”

Ignoring the two men, I covered my face with my hand.

“So much for ‘this settlement was destroyed by a basilisk’. It was a different monster entirely…”

My impression when I first saw the settlement had been completely wrong.

If you find a petrified settlement after seeing a basilisk, anyone would think the basilisk did it.

Cockatrices are also famous petrification-type monsters alongside basilisks, but expecting that was unreasonable, right!?

《Master is getting shocked over something weird again…》

《Mio-chan, what is master troubled about?》

《Well, you see…》

Mio mercilessly voiced my inner thoughts.

“”””???””””

The four people outside the telepathic link had no idea what was going on.

Putting my mistake behind me, I asked the three others besides Annie.

“Now, choose. Will you become my slave, or not?”

“Eh, slave? What do you mean?”

I had not explained the slave situation to Annie, so she asked in confusion, but explaining it would be a hassle, so I postponed it.

“After seeing something like that, there is no way we have a choice…”

“Yeah. If we become your slaves, you will save our families, right?”

“Yes, I promise. And Asuka, what will you do?”

“I become slave. Save everyone.”

As expected, Asuka did not hesitate.

“I will become a slave too. Please save my family.”

“Of course. So will I.”

Once all three agreed, I made them slaves one by one.

“By the way, what about this young lady? No, um, what will you… do… sir?”

Earth, newly enslaved, pointed at Annie and asked in clumsy polite speech.

“You do not need to force yourself to use polite speech. It just sounds strange.”

“O-oh. …Thanks.”

Earth was visibly relieved.

“I made you slaves to silence you about my abilities. Naturally, the people revived from petrification will also be made slaves for the same reason.”

“Yeah, figures…”

“Yes. We expected that… it cannot be helped, right?”

“Everyone, slave? Will you do cruel things? If you do, do it only to me.”

The three new slaves looked anxious.

“Ah, you can relax. Master does not do cruel things to slaves. He does tease them, though…”

Mio, probably the slave I tease the most, said that.

“Judging by how you talk, you young ladies… are slaves too, huh?”

“That is right.”

“Yes. It is my pride.”

She said it proudly, but was that really a good response, Maria?

“Then should not this young lady have been enslaved too?”

“Annie is already my slave. Annie, shake.”

“Yes. …Eh?”

Annie was shocked that she had shaken hands against her will.

Most beastkin dislike being treated like their base animals. More precisely, they dislike being treated like pets or livestock by strangers (family and lovers are different).

For a dog beastkin to “shake” for someone she had just met was unthinkable.

“At what point in that process did he even use \<Slave Arts>…?”

“I do not know. At this point, it is probably best to give up on thinking about the details.”

“Yes. If we are surprised every time, we will never finish.”

In a sense, “not being surprised” is the correct way to deal with me.

“Well then, I will restore the rest.”

“Please…”

“We are counting on you.”

“Please.”

“Shake… with a strange man… shake…”

Annie’s shock seemed greater than expected.

One hour later, we succeeded in releasing all the residents from petrification.

Though it was simple work, it took time because, on Maria’s suggestion, we released the petrification one person at a time.

I soon understood the meaning of her proposal.

Watching people revived from shattered stone statues right before their eyes evoked the fear that it had happened to them as well, and it carried enough pressure to make them revere the one who could undo it.

Telling them they were slaves in that state resulted in no resistance at all, only prostration.

Spending time at the beginning reduced the work afterward.

That aside, the residents were all rejoicing that everyone was safe.

Earth and Isle’s families were also revived, so they were in the middle of emotional reunions.

As an aside, everyone was shocked by the three years they had spent petrified and by Asuka’s transformation.

Once everyone had calmed down, we discussed what to do next.

“The settlement residents will decide what to do going forward. There are three main options: ‘stay on this island,’ ‘return to where you lived,’ or ‘work at a base I own’.”

The purpose of enslaving the residents was to silence them and align their stories.

If they had a place to return to, and if they wanted to stay here, I had no intention of forcing them to come with me.

“If you leave this island, the fact that you were petrified for three years will remain. However, the stone statues were not shattered. You will say that you were restored by a normal petrification-removal spell.”

If the fact that the statues had been destroyed disappeared, there would be no inconsistencies.

“Um… can you even leave this island in the first place?”

The one who raised her hand and asked was Annie.

I lifted Annie into the air using the power of the Wind Calamity Dragon.

“Hii!?”

“Do you really think you cannot leave this island even with my power?”

I spun Annie around like a juggling ball.

“We can! I think we can leave!”

Good. She understood.

“Somehow, I feel a sense of kinship…”

Mio felt a strange familiarity with Annie.

After discussion, none of the residents chose to stay on the island. They split between returning to their original homes and working at my base.

Below are some of their opinions.

“I have good memories of this island, but I still want to go back.”

“I will take the children born here and return to my parents’ home. I want them to see their grandchildren.”

“The settlement is in ruins, so we cannot live properly. Following you is the best option.”

“I grew up hearing about the outside world from my late parents. I want to see it in their place.”

“I realized this island is not safe. I am attached to the settlement, but it is not worth our lives.”

That was roughly how it went.

Some wanted to stay but gave up because with fewer residents, life would not be sustainable.

I had no intention of taking care of anyone who stayed behind.

As another aside, Earth, Isle, and their families chose to work for me.

“As promised, we will work as your slaves. Our families will come with us as well.”

“Same here. I will spend the rest of my life repaying this huge debt.”

One more aside: Asuka was not given a choice.

Sorry, but I have things I need a local Hero to do.

Even when I told her I would forcibly take her with me, Asuka did not waver at all.

“It is fine. I have no regrets. I will obey everything.”

That resolve might be a bit too firm…

Anyway.

With our future plans decided, the residents began preparing to leave.

They were allowed to take valuables and mementos, but furniture would be left behind.

Leaving furniture behind would help future castaways. Even in ruins, having buildings and furniture would improve their situation somewhat.

While the residents prepared, we would do what we needed to do on this island.

“And so, it is time for a treasure hunt.”

The four of us, me, Mio, Maria, and Asuka, headed toward the only mountain on the island.

This was following the rumor that treasures sleep in the mountains of drifting islands.

“Yay! I hope there is something good! Or rather, I hope there really is something!”

Unfortunately, it was just a rumor, so there was a higher chance of nothing being there.

Knowing that, both Mio and I were excited anyway. Maria, of course, was not.

“I saw it. This way. Soon.”

We brought Asuka because she had seen a mysterious girl heading toward the mountain.

According to Asuka, she had followed the girl but was noticed and lost her. When she found her again, the girl had cockatrices with her.

After the residents were petrified, Asuka searched the mountain area many times but found nothing.

To uncover both the rumored treasure and the truth behind the petrification, we had come all this way to the mountain.

Perhaps the two were related.

“By the way, how long are you going to keep up this no-map challenge play?”

As we walked, Mio asked as if she had just remembered.

“…Right. Once we found Asuka, there was no reason to restrict the map anymore.”

I had completely forgotten until Mio mentioned it, but the main purpose of banning the map on this adventure was to randomly encounter someone with the \<Hero> skill.

Now that we had found Asuka, an Oni Hero, that goal was achieved.

“I get that challenge play is fun, but should you not unlock the map already?”

Maria nodded vigorously with a serious expression.

“The goal is done, and it is not good to keep burdening Maria-chan.”

Maria shook her head vigorously with a serious expression.

“I do not consider it a burden. However, I wish for even a slight improvement in Jin-sama’s safety.”

“Oh, she denies the burden part…”

Maria herself does not admit it is a burden, but it clearly is.

Challenge play is fun, but there is no reason to cling to it forever.

“Alright. I will unlock the map after this exploration. Unlocking it in the middle of a treasure hunt would feel unsatisfying.”

“That sounds good. Then let us enjoy the final event of the no-map run.”

I hope it is an enjoyable event.

Guided by Asuka, we moved through the forest and reached the mountain in about ten minutes.

“Oh, I have never seen a mountain of salt before. It is quite a mystical sight.”

As Mio said, the small mountain before us was entirely made of salt.

The salt formed semi-transparent crystals like quartz, creating the shape of a mountain.

In fact, this mountain was a fumarole of an island whale.

Though it is a whale-type monster with a mysterious ecology, it shares many traits with whales, including spouting.

Rather than a volcanic eruption, it might be called a seamount geyser.

Over many years, seawater spouted repeatedly, salt accumulated around the vent, and eventually formed a mountain. A mystery of nature.

…If you think about it calmly, that logic would not produce such beautiful crystals, but let us say mysterious forces were at work and not worry about it.

“What do you think, Master?”

“It is perfect. This is exactly what makes sightseeing worthwhile.”

A natural mystery that can only be seen there.

It would not be an exaggeration to say it is an essential tourist attraction.

“Outside island, no mountain?”

Seeing our reaction, Asuka asked curiously.

“No, that is not the case.”

“Then why happy?”

“Because a mountain of salt seems like something that only exists here.”

“Outside mountains, not salt???”

Since Asuka was born on this island, the only mountain she knew was this “mountain of salt.”

If she had never seen other mountains, it was natural that this would be her standard.

Even things rare in the wider world are not rare to those who live there.

“Mio, explain it to her.”

“Okaaay. So, outside mountains are like…”

Leaving the explanation to Mio, I began investigating the mountain.

One minute passed after starting the investigation of the “mountain of salt”.

“Found it.”

“That fast!?”

While walking around the mountain, I noticed something odd. Investigating further, one section was not made of salt crystals but of real quartz.

It was cleverly disguised among the surrounding crystals, so even Asuka could not tell.

“Probably a hidden door here… yes, there it is.”

It would be difficult to open by brute force, but easy if you knew a little trick.

I am not saying it cannot be opened by brute force.

Since Mio and the others were approaching, I prepared the hidden door so it could be opened at any time.

“That was quick. You really are not using the map, right?”

Mio said something rude upon seeing the hidden door.

“Do you think I would tell such a pointless lie?”

“No. If it is you, Master, it is not that strange…”

I am Shindo Jin, a man known for finding hidden passages.

“T-there was… a door… this fast…”

Asuka was shocked that I found the hidden door she could not in less than a minute.

Even if I say it myself, she picked the wrong opponent.

“Asuka-chan, you picked the wrong opponent. Master is completely absurd.”

Mio said it for me.

“Ab… absurd…?”

“Yes. Restoring people shattered into pieces, evacuating fifty people from this island, finding a hidden door in one minute. Can a normal person do that?”

“They cannot…”

“Master can do even more amazing things. If you get shocked by something like this, you will not last as Master’s slave. I recommend getting used to it quickly.”

Was that advice?

Maria nodded proudly (she stayed unusually quiet to avoid spoilers).

“I understand. I will try to get used to it.”

“That is the spirit!”

Asuka-chan, twelve years old, very honest.

“Alright, opening it.”

Once Mio finished speaking, I opened the hidden door.

“This is…”

“Rotten smell…”

“I also smell chemicals.”

“It stinks…”

What drifted out was the smell of rotting creatures and some kind of medicine.

Fortunately, or perhaps unfortunately, there was no human smell.

This does not feel like an enjoyable event!

“Excuse us.”

Maria said that and covered us with \<Barrier Arts>.

The unpleasant smells were shut out instantly. As always, a convenient skill.

“This is…?”

“Maria-chan is also quite absurd…”

“I understand. I will get used to it.”

Once again, the adaptability of a local Hero was impressive.

With the smell gone, we entered the hidden passage and immediately found stairs leading underground.

The walls, ceiling, and stairs were all made of the same quartz as the hidden door. By cleverly using light refraction, it was made invisible from the outside. Excessively advanced technology.

“They put a lot of effort into this.”

“At this point, it does not feel like normal treasure…”

Between the hidden passage and the unpleasant smell, it felt more like a secret laboratory than a treasure room.

“Let us go down.”

At my signal, we began descending the crystal stairs.

The land we were on was moss on the back of an island whale, so the stairs should not be very deep.

As expected, the stairs ended about ten seconds after we started descending.

“Ugh…”

Asuka covered her mouth and groaned.

“Well, I kind of expected this.”

“Yeah.”

In the underground room were large numbers of monster corpses.

Some were dissected, some soaked in chemicals, some incorporated into magical devices.

No matter how you looked at it, it was a secret laboratory.

“Some seriously mad scientist was doing research here. And the monster types are unpleasantly biased…”

Mio’s disgust was understandable given the lineup.

Cockatrice (petrification), Green Mashu (paralysis), Lullaby Bye (sleep), Purple Mashu (poison), Goblin Shaman (curse), Ice Slime (freeze), Brown Mashu (confusion), and so on.

It was a parade of monsters that cause status ailments.

The cockatrice that attacked the settlement and the basilisk that blocked landing on the island whale were likely related.

“There is a lot here, but nothing pleasant. Shall we unlock the map…”

“I really do not want to manually search this place…”

Our goals were “the treasure hidden in the mountain” and “the truth behind the petrification”.

It did not look like there was treasure I wanted here, but the truth behind the petrification seemed likely.

At this point, the adventure itself had reached a stopping point, and restricting the map further did not seem like it would add any fun.

Also, there were far too many things I did not want to touch while investigating.

This felt like the perfect timing to unlock the map.

《And so, I am unlocking the map》

After notifying Sakura and the others waiting on Latis Island via telepathy, I removed the map restriction.

---

**AN:** Next time, with the map unlocked, the story will move forward rapidly.
