## **196: Report and Proposals**

**AN:** I forgot to note this earlier, but this chapter is part of the “Water Capital Arc.”

It assumes you have read Chapter 188.5.

Also, there was an inconsistency regarding Ashley’s age in Chapters 187 and 188.5. The correct age is 17.

---

Releasing the map is practically the same as stripping bare all the schemes currently in motion in that land.

By declaring the release of the map on the drifting island, and with Sakura and the others on Latis Island also using the map, we were able to grasp, in broad terms, the calamity progressing within the Pajel Kingdom.

Astonishingly, the revival of the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’ is imminent!

Now then, everyone together…

I knew it.

In reality, Alta, who is unrelated to the map restriction, had already grasped the situation, and Maria also knew through Alta. Alta had even prepared insurance for the worst-case scenario.

So, even if I did nothing, it would probably be possible to settle the situation. But once I learned a certain fact, I could no longer ignore it. Therefore, I decided to move proactively.

It is also not impossible to crush the calamity in advance.

However, as I have said before, there is no particular reason to go out of my way to protect this country, which Alta describes as a corrupted kingdom. So, I will maintain a policy of non-action regarding the revival itself.

Accordingly, the parts I will actively involve myself in are those other than the revival of the ‘Water Calamity Dragon’.

“‘Summon’.”

The first thing I did was summon Sakura and the others to the drifting island.

It would be cruel to leave them out of the loop forever.

As an aside, the only thing I place importance on is the ‘means of first landing’. After that, I freely use teleportation magic and the like.

Also, I think Mio is the only one who would sympathize with this self-imposed restriction play, so I see no problem in summoning Sakura and the others.

《Master!》

I caught Dora as she jumped at me and hoisted her onto my shoulders.

“I never imagined there would be a second Hero on this island.”

“Yes, it was surprising… But thinking back, Jin-kun was so interested that it would not be strange for there to be a Hero here, right…?”

“For Master to be satisfied with that explanation is impressive in its own way…”

Long ago, a close friend from the east once said to me, ‘Wherever Shindo walks, he runs into gold bars’.

Do not misunderstand. It does not mean ‘good things happen’. It means ‘good things happen, but they always turn into trouble’.

“So, Master, what do you plan to do now?”

What I am about to do, I have not yet explained even to Mio.

“Isn’t it obvious? My personal objectives are all finished, so I am preparing to advance the main event.”

“Game-brain… poke!”

If the pheasant does not cry, it will not be shot.

With the time limit imposed by the calamity dragon’s revival, it is necessary to assign priorities to tasks and process them in order of importance.

And the highest-priority task is to have aquatic monster subordinates, such as Maple the great sea serpent, Leila the mermaid, and the mermaid maid squad, recover those who were petrified by the basilisk and sank into the sea.

If the ‘Water Calamity Dragon’ revives, we have no idea what will happen to those lying on the seabed, so I wanted them recovered as soon as possible. Leaving them underwater forever as statues would be pitiful.

《This makes 102 people!》

《So fast… I’m still at 46…》

《The sea is my field! When it comes to swimming, I won’t lose to Leila, who’s only three years old!》

In truth, there were more basilisk victims than I initially thought.

By investigating the drifting island… specifically, the migration route of the island whale, and centering the map search there, we discovered that more than a thousand people had been petrified and sunk into the sea.

Some were damaged and scattered, so under normal circumstances recovery would be difficult.

That is where the map and aquatic monsters come in.

Both the great sea serpent and mermaids rank high among sea monsters, so they have no trouble moving underwater. Since they have been power-leveled, they also will not lose to other monsters.

With the map, we can grasp the positions of even broken fragments, so there will be no misses.

Even if some fragments have drifted out of the country, minor cases can be handled with ‘Revive’.

Thus, the recovery work proceeds at a surprising pace. It should be finished within today or tomorrow.

Naturally, those recovered, whether adventurers or others, will be enslaved before being revived.

Most of them have lost all assets, including their equipment, and have no relatives to rely on and nowhere to return to.

On top of that, socially they are already considered dead, making them wonderful human resources with absolutely no issues in enslaving and utilizing them.

Those revived from petrification will basically be treated the same as residents of the drifting island.

We will silence them regarding the petrification. Those who still have a place to return to will be sent back, while those who do not will be sent to my base. Since the eras in which they were petrified differ, they will be educated and then assigned work suited to their aptitude.

As a rule, adventurers will not be permitted to continue as such. There is a possibility that information remains in the Adventurers Guild, and those who committed the reckless act of charging directly at the drifting island have no qualifications to remain adventurers.

While we are at it, let me also talk about the residents of the drifting island.

The residents were divided into ‘those who returned to where they originally lived’ and ‘those who worked at my base’. All those whose original homes were in the Pajel Kingdom became part of the latter group.

In short, the citizens of the Pajel Kingdom do not wish to return to the Pajel Kingdom.

You cannot tell just by looking at Latis Island, but as a whole, the country must not be in good shape.

In a sense, this is fortunate.

If there had been people who wanted to return to the Pajel Kingdom, we would have had to tell them about the coming calamity and stop them, so this saved us the trouble.

As for escaping the island itself, we decided to use ‘Portal’.

It is probably the fastest method.

Given the time limit, we cannot afford to waste time on evacuation.

Honestly, I wanted to produce a grand escape drama, so it is very regrettable.

According to Alta, if left alone, the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’ will revive in four days.

Naturally, we will leave it alone.

The reason the schedule has shortened significantly compared to the original plan is due to the efforts of the ‘enemy’.

So, even if the map had not been released, Alta planned to convey this information tomorrow.

Releasing the map a day earlier than Alta’s limit had major advantages.

Specifically, maids were summoned throughout the Pajel Kingdom, and using a map-based sweep operation, we were able to collect personnel with rare skills and rare items.

In the worst case, this country may perish, so we will recover as much as possible beforehand.

If Alta’s explanation had been delayed until tomorrow, some rare items might have been missed.

With this, even if the country perishes, it will be fine.

I can now proceed with the main event without any lingering regrets.

After seeing all the tasks through, we decided to head for the island where the main event would occur.

Since we had obtained it, we would use the ship we took to reach the drifting island (Sera is using ‘Float’).

《Sniff…》

《When this country’s adventure is over, I’ll let you ride again.》

《It’s a promise!》

As an aside, when we tried to board the ship, a dragonkin somehow got wind of it and protested. It said that unless there was a sufficient reason, it wanted us to use it for transportation.

I persuaded it by explaining that this would be the last time I used the ship, and soothed it by promising a next time.

“So, we’re heading for that island, right…?”

“Yeah, the island with the half-naked little girl.”

“That is a very misleading description.”

“Does Dora take it off too?”

“Dora-chan, don’t, okay?”

Yes, the island we are heading toward is the one with the half-naked ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

Whether information about her being half-naked is necessary is left to each individual’s judgment.

“With a calamity dragon reviving, we can’t exactly proceed while ignoring the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ can we?”

“If you’re just going to beat it to death, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ doesn’t matter, though. If I recall, you beat two-thirds of them to death, right?”

“Yeah. I stomped the fire calamity dragon to death, but I punched the earth and wind ones to death. What to do this time…”

Personally, since it is a water dragon, I would like to fillet it into three pieces.

“This does not sound like a conversation one would have in a situation where a country might perish.”

Sera said with exasperation after hearing our foolish banter.

At the very least, I do not think the country will survive in the same form.

“That’s Jin-kun for you…”

《That’s right!》

That template feels oddly nostalgic.

“Oh, I can see it now.”

While chatting amicably, the island in question came into view.

Since Tamo-san, the guard for the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, was present, Alta had been checking information on this island in real time.

Needless to say, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ under Tamo-san’s protection was safe, and the hands of this country’s investigators had not reached her.

Unfortunately, there were no obstructions like those on the drifting island, so we arrived at the island without incident.

Not wanting the ship to be swept away by the waves, we used wind magic to beach it.

“Arrived!”

《Arrived!》

The two children energetically jumped off the ship.

“Sand will scatter, so Sera, don’t imitate them.”

If Sera canceled ‘Float’ and imitated them, the sand cloud would be terrible.

“I will not! It will not happen! How rude!”

“Not doing it is fine, but it would happen, right?”

“It will not! See!”

Saying so, Sera canceled ‘Float’ and jumped down.

-Boom!-

It turned out terribly.

Mainly for Mio and Dora, who had jumped down first.

“Sera-chan, think about your own weight…”

《Peh peh.》

“I’m sorry…”

To be honest, the impact was bigger than I expected. Did Sera get heavier than before?

A: Sera’s weight is…

“Do not say it!”

A: Master, what shall we do?

Let us refrain from asking.

She knows she is heavy, but it seems she does not want to hear specific numbers.

“Haah, haah… P-please wait!”

While we were engaging in a manzai-like exchange, a girl’s voice came from the forest near the beach.

The girl was running while chasing something like a liquid creature.

Needless to say, the girl was the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, and the liquid-like creature was Tamo-san.

I had asked Tamo-san to bring the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ to me.

“People… Could they be pursuers…?”

The girl emerged from the forest, noticed our presence, and muttered with clear wariness.

And ignoring all that, Tamo-san hopped up and landed on my head.

“Huh? Chevalier is… attached to you…?”

So Tamo-san is being called Chevalier, a knight-like name?

“Nice to meet you. My name is Shindo Jin. I am the one who sent this slime to you.”

I decided on the most straightforward introduction.

To convey that I am an ally, this seemed the best.

“So you are the one who sent Chevalier…”

There was no surprise in the voice of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, Ashley.

She probably did not think Tamo-san was protecting her for no reason.

She might even have realized it was acting under someone’s instructions.

“First, please allow me to thank you. Thanks to this child, I have survived until today.”

Ashley bowed her head as she said that, and Tamo-san hopped onto her head.

Since Ashley did not react, it seems this has already become his usual position.

“If you died, it would cause me all sorts of trouble. Protecting you was only natural.”

“You know my circumstances, don’t you?”

“Yes, of course. I also know that you intend to abandon maintaining the seal and meet your end here.”

“You even know that much… Then, have you come to take me back?”

Ashley showed no sign of wariness. If anything, she looked resigned.

She must understand that if I said I was taking her back, she could not resist.

“Do you want to go back?”

“No, I do not.”

An immediate answer.

“Relax. I have no intention of taking you back. I have only come to make a report and some proposals.”

“A report and proposals?”

Ashley echoed, puzzled.

“Yes. Will you hear me out?”

“I do not mind, but…”

Having obtained Ashley’s consent, I decided to make the most important proposal.

“Then here is the first proposal. Don’t you want to wear clothes that are easier to move in?”

“Ah!”

Ashley’s face turned bright red as she covered her body with her hands.

Yes. Up until this point, Ashley had been wearing only panties, her upper body bare, truly half-naked.

I think it would be unreasonable to continue a serious discussion while half-naked.

The first proposal was safely accepted by Ashley.

“I feel civilization again for the first time in a while.”

We had Ashley wear an Advanced Trading Company forest exploration set.

No matter what choice Ashley makes, there is no downside to wearing practical clothes.

“Now that the ‘clothing’ of food, clothing, and shelter, the symbol of civilization, has been satisfied, next we should satisfy food. Here you go, Mio-chan’s special pasta.”

《Yay!》

“I am looking forward to it.”

To make up for Ashley’s continued wild meals, Mio decided to serve pasta.

For some reason, Sera and Dora also seemed intent on eating together.

By the way, the wooden table and chairs for the meal were my gift.

“Thank you very much… It has been a long time since I last ate pasta.”

She ate the pasta with refined table manners, making it hard to believe she had been half-naked just moments ago.

“It is more delicious than what is served at the castle. Mio-san, you are very skilled at cooking.”

“Yes, she is our pride and joy as a cook.”

“Hmph!”

Mio puffed out her chest proudly.

For the record, all minimal self-introductions had already been completed.

Though it was a short time, I am confident we had grown quite comfortable with each other.

Once Ashley finished her meal, we continued with the ‘report and proposals’.

“First, the report. The water calamity dragon will revive in a few days.”

“Is that so? That is sooner than I expected.”

Her reaction was more subdued than I thought.

“For convenience, we will call those who desire the revival of the water calamity dragon ‘enemies’, and this is the result of their efforts.”

“‘Enemies’… Who are they?”

“To you, she went by the name Aria.”

Aria was not her real name, but I knew she used it.

Aria, together with Ashley’s fiancé, framed Ashley and tried to kill her. Although the murder attempt failed, Ashley was separated from the seal of the water calamity dragon, making its revival only a matter of time.

“So it was as I thought.”

“You had realized it?”

“I was not just living on this island without thinking about anything.”

Though she looks like a little girl, she is in fact a 17-year-old girl.

If she had mental leeway, she would naturally reflect on what had happened to her.

“I had no way to confirm it, so they were only hypotheses, but I considered several patterns. What was especially unnatural was Aria’s existence. Because of her, no matter what choice I made, the only future that awaited was the calamity dragon’s revival.”

“Correct. It seems she planned it quite thoroughly. The chimera on this island was also Aria’s doing.”

Anticipating where Ashley would flee, she had planted a dangerous monster there.

It was not a main plan, more like a light scheme where it would be lucky if Ashley died.

“That monster was also Aria’s doing… What exactly is she?”

“Aria’s true identity is an incarnation of the water calamity dragon. A calamity dragon that normally has no ego gained one for some reason, and transferred its consciousness to act in the human world. In Aria’s case, her reason for acting in the human world was the revival of the water calamity dragon.”

She is the same kind as Pes, the incarnation of the wind calamity dragon at my place.

Unlike Pes, the reason she gained an ego is unknown. As long as she does not harm me, I have no particular interest.

“An incarnation of a calamity dragon… It is hard to believe, but considering the eeriness I felt from her, it is not that strange.”

“She had been lurking in this country for quite a long time. Since she can freely adjust her apparent age to some extent, it would have been advantageous for infiltration.”

It is almost certain that the girl who came to the drifting island was also Aria.

According to Alta, rapidly changing an incarnation’s apparent age is troublesome, but changing it at the same pace as normal growth is relatively easy.

Since she appeared to be around 12 to 14 three years ago, if there was no rapid change, she would now look around 15 to 17. This matches Aria’s current appearance.

“Now that I think about it, why do you know so much? You speak as if these are obvious facts, things even I, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, do not know…”

A natural question.

“If you really want to know, I can tell you, but could you let me put it off for now? You will probably get confused.”

“…I understand. I will ask later. I am already quite confused, so any more would be too much.”

She seemed calm, but apparently she was indeed confused.

That is only natural.

“Then I will continue. Aria was talented, but she did not have the power to single-handedly break through the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ castle. So she schemed in various ways to draw the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ out. If it worked, she could kill you, and at worst she could separate you from the seal.”

“So from Aria’s perspective, even if it was not optimal, it was still a passing result.”

“Yes. Aria must be eagerly awaiting the calamity dragon’s revival.”

Though she is an ‘enemy’, it was truly a brilliant plan.

If it went well, the calamity dragon would revive on the spot, and even in the worst case, it would revive before long.

“…I am sorry to ask this right after agreeing to wait, but please allow me to ask one thing. What is your objective? Beyond this ‘report and proposals’, what do you desire?”

This, too, was a reasonable question.

From everything I had explained so far, my objective was unclear.

“My objective, huh…”

Ashley looked at me seriously, waiting for my answer.

“…None in particular.”

“Huh?”

Her serious expression collapsed.

“No, I really am not acting with a clear objective. Basically, I go with the flow and adjust things to move in a direction that seems interesting. I suppose I will end up killing the calamity dragon, but that is not an objective. It is simply that if it revives and looks like it will harm my people, I will kill it.”

In extreme terms, if the calamity dragon revives and behaves quietly, there would be no need to kill it.

“I think I will also end up punching two people, but that is not exactly a final goal either. If I wanted to, I could go punch them right now…”

“Master, Master.”

Mio tugged on my clothes.

“What is it, Mio?”

“Ashley-chan is completely frozen.”

Sure enough, Ashley’s expression was frozen in place, still collapsed.

“Why is she frozen?”

“Maybe she could not understand your behavioral principles. It is tough for people who are not used to them…”

Apparently, my principles of action place a burden on those not accustomed to them.

“Well, let me follow up. Master’s hobby is sightseeing, and wherever he goes, he gets involved in trouble. He has the power to prevent trouble beforehand, but his basic policy is to deal with it after it happens. So until then, he often does not have a clear objective.”

Mio explained my principles in an easy-to-understand way.

As expected, leaving detailed explanations to Mio is the correct choice.

“Then you have no intention of preventing the calamity dragon’s revival?”

“That is right. I do not. That is not something I must do. It is something the people of this country should do.”

I answered Ashley’s question firmly.

I have no intention of cleaning up others’ messes.

“But if the calamity dragon revives, this world will be destroyed, will it not? I have already given up, so I do not mind, but are you truly fine with that?”

“No, the world will not be destroyed. I have a way to kill the calamity dragon. If it revives and goes on a rampage, I will simply kill it.”

If the calamity dragon goes on a rampage, that means there is a possibility my people will be harmed. At that point, I will have a clear reason to act. Which means the calamity dragon dies.

“Um… I do not think the calamity dragon is an opponent that can be killed…”

“If you cannot believe it, that is fine. I have no intention of proving it.”

There is no need for Ashley to believe me here.

If Ashley were trying to prevent the calamity dragon’s revival, that would be another matter, but she has already given up. Either choice has no effect on the board.

“…At this point, doubting what you say would be meaningless. Very well. I will listen under the premise that you can defeat the calamity dragon.”

To be honest, I did not expect her to believe me.

“Good. Then here is the second proposal.”

“I am grateful for the first proposal.”

Without the first proposal, Ashley would still be half-naked.

“As a premise, the calamity dragon will revive. This country will suffer damage. But I have a policy of protecting what I like. In this country, I like Latis Island and the drifting island, so I intend to protect them.”

“You can not only kill, but also protect. If that is true, it is something extraordinary…”

“Also, Ashley, there are several reasons I do not want you to die. The details are secret.”

“Huh…?”

From Ashley’s perspective, the reasons would be incomprehensible.

Reason one: I have various connections with ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’, and if possible, I want to help those who are treated unfairly, provided their character is decent.

Reason two: Ashley is related to Lily, an elven storyteller I know. It is hard to abandon the relative of an acquaintance, again assuming decent character.

Reason three: I simply took a liking to the existence of a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ surviving half-naked.

Reason four: I already have three attribute ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’ as subordinates, so it would be troublesome for only the water one to die. Completionist spirit.

“Is there anyone you want protected from the calamity dragon’s damage? If so, I would like to protect them together with you. That is the second proposal.”

At present, Ashley has given up on everything, but if the calamity dragon dies, life will continue.

From what I can see, she does not appear so desperate as to want to commit suicide.

If someone dear to Ashley were to be harmed by the calamity dragon, she would be saddened.

Since I am protecting Ashley anyway, I might as well protect those dear to her too.

…You could also call it farming affection.

“…It is not something I should say, having abandoned everything and fled, but I want my fellow elves to remain safe. However, there is no need to worry about them. When the calamity dragon revives, they can flee to the island in the sky where the elves live.”

“Sorry, that’s impossible.”

“Pardon?”

In fact, the water ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ clan has a magical tool that allows them to flee to the land where the wind ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ clan lives, namely the Sky Castle, when the calamity dragon’s seal is broken.

What it hides is the cathedral seen during the gondola tour on Latis Island. If you bring the key item there, you can teleport to the Sky Castle.

The reason there is a teleportation device on Latis Island is that it is located in a position that will not be immediately affected even if the calamity dragon revives. This ensures safety even in unforeseen accidents.

“The place to flee is the Sky Castle where the Wind ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ resides, right?”

“Yes. At this point, questioning why you know that seems pointless. I am starting to get used to it.”

“Good to hear.”

I feel like I demand people get used to me wherever I go.

“Back to the topic. Unfortunately, the teleportation device in the Sky Castle is already broken. So even if you try to teleport, nothing will happen.”

“What!? Then my clan…!”

“Did you forget my second proposal?”

I said gently to calm the shaken Ashley.

“Ah… I see now…”

Having understood, Ashley knelt before me in a full prostration.

“Please, save my clan from the calamity dragon’s damage. I beg you.”

I did not tell her to prostrate herself… Do ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’ like prostrating?

“Understood. Leave it to me.”

I answered in a way that looked confident, while hiding my agitation.

“And now, Ashley, the third proposal. …Since we are at it, why not let yourself be saved as well?”

This is the final proposal.

---

**AN:** Like at the end of Volume 2, preparations that are hard for readers to notice will be opened up.

The next volume will be an interlude, with a rapid series of short stories focusing on side characters, buying time for writing the main story. Image-wise, it is like bonus SS included with a book.

+++

## **197: Tranquility and Destruction**

**AN:** This is the main story, told from a third-person perspective.

There are some extremely blatant reveals.

---

The Pajel Kingdom is a maritime kingdom composed of multiple islands.

There is no (royal) capital. Instead, the governing institutions are concentrated on an island called the Central Island.

On the Central Island stand two large castles. One is the Royal Castle, and the other is the residence of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

The residence of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is heavily guarded, to the point that ordinary people cannot even approach it.

However, now that the current ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ has gone missing, the significance of guarding the residence has diminished, and many of the regular guards have been dispatched to search for the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

In other words, security has grown thin.

Through the sparsely populated residence of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, three people and one beast were calmly proceeding.

The most conspicuous was the one beast. It was a basilisk, a monster. However, it was no ordinary basilisk. Various organs not found on a normal basilisk were attached all over its body, so it would be more accurate to call it a basilisk-based chimera.

Sitting atop that chimera was a girl in a dress. She wore an alluring smile, as if eagerly anticipating what was about to happen.

Walking beside the chimera was a man in a white coat. As was common for an elf, his features were well-formed, but his unhealthy appearance ruined the effect.

Lastly, bound tightly with thread atop the chimera was a boy. He was unconscious, and rather than having come along willingly, it looked as though he had simply been brought here.

After a while, the unconscious boy woke up.

“Ugh… W-where is this…? What happened to me…? I can’t move? W-what is this!?”

“Oh my, Aston-sama, you’re awake?”

The girl smiled at the confused boy.

“A-Aria!? What is the meaning of this!? And where have you been all this time!? Do you have any idea what kind of hell I went through after letting Ashley escape!?”

“Yes. I believe I know better than anyone how important she is to this country, and what it means to harm her.”

Without flinching at Aston’s furious outburst, the girl replied calmly.

About a month earlier, Aria and Aston had plotted to frame and assassinate a single girl, the current ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, at a graduation party held at an academy on the Central Island.

However, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ barely managed to escape, and has been missing ever since.

Aston and his accomplices’ sloppy plan was easily exposed by the subsequent investigation.

As the ringleader, Aston was to receive severe punishment. By this point, Aria had also vanished.

In deciding Aston’s punishment, the wishes of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ clan took precedence over the king’s intentions.

This was because the Pajel Kingdom was, in truth, ruled from the shadows by the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ clan.

Long ago, the clan had concluded that for the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ to live stably, the existence of a stable state was essential.

However, since elves are racially unsuited to governing a state, they entrusted the outward-facing politics to suitable humans. This is the secret founding story of the Pajel Kingdom.

Because of this background, not even the king could oppose the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ clan.

For Aston, who had caused the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ to flee, discussions were proceeding toward his execution, when the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ clan intervened.

Under the supervision of the clan, Aston was ordered to search for ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ Ashley.

If he found Ashley and his apology was accepted, he would not be charged with a crime.

Naturally, this was not an act of goodwill.

Put simply, he was a sacrifice to vent Ashley’s resentment.

When Ashley was found, there was no reason to think she would forgive Aston. Rather than killing him arbitrarily, it was deemed better to let Ashley decide his punishment.

That was why the condition was not “find her”, but “have your apology accepted”.

Aston had no future.

What made it laughable was that he himself believed that everything would work out once he met Ashley.

“Aria! You deceived me, didn’t you!?”

“I didn’t deceive you. It’s true that Ashley was an obstacle to both you and me, wasn’t she? I did everything I could to fulfill both of our wishes. If we had successfully killed Ashley, I even thought it would be fine to be united with you.”

“Don’t be ridiculous! You ran away the moment the assassination failed! Damn it! This binding is in the way! Hey, Aria, take this off!”

Aston raged, but being restrained, he could do nothing.

“No. Be a good boy and behave yourself for a while, won’t you?”

“…Where are you taking me?”

Realizing that he could neither free himself nor force Aria to release him, Aston glared at her resentfully as he asked.

“I’m grateful to you, Aston-sama. Thanks to you, my long-cherished wish is about to come true. As a token of my gratitude, I thought I’d let you watch the beginning of the end from a front-row seat.”

“What are you talking about! Answer me!”

At the same moment Aston shouted, two elves appeared in their path.

“A m-monster!? Who are you people!?”

“Tch, at a time like this…”

Though few, there were still guards stationed at the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ residence. The two elves were among those few survivors. Yes, survivors.

“Such a nuisance. Do it.”

“Uwaaaah!?”

“W-what is this!?”

At Aria’s command, the basilisk petrified the two elves instantly.

The speed of the petrification was incomparably faster than that of an ordinary basilisk.

Furthermore, the petrified guards crumbled into sand as they were. It was a terrifying ability that robbed them of even the possibility of revival.

“W-what did you…?”

“This child is one of the monsters I tamed, modified by Dr. Gired there. Let’s see… I suppose we can call it Basilisk Disaster. It can petrify elves of this country in an instant. If you get too noisy, shall I petrify you as well?”

“H-hii…!?”

“That’s fine. As long as you behave yourself, I’ll let you live.”

Witnessing the massacre before his eyes, Aston trembled in fear and fell silent.

Seeing this, Aria nodded in satisfaction and resumed walking.

The three people and one beast advanced deep into the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ residence, down the stairs leading underground.

“G… gh…!”

As they descended, Aston’s complexion gradually worsened.

After going a certain depth, he groaned as though he had reached his limit.

This was proof that he could no longer withstand the miasma leaking from the calamity slumbering below.

“This seems to be the limit. Is Dr. Gired all right?”

“Kihihi, I can endure a little. I am a high elf, after all. Still, it’s a bit early, but I’ll take some medicine just in case. Shall I give some to this one as well?”

“Yes, please.”

Saying so, the white-coated elf Gired took a pill from his pocket and swallowed it.

Then he forcibly pried open Aston’s mouth and shoved the same pill inside.

“Mgh!? Cough, hack! Haah, haah…”

What Gired and Aston had taken was a drug that granted resistance to miasma.

Aston did not know this, but for humans it carried extremely severe side effects.

Aria did not take the medicine. There was a reason she did not need to.

“Now then, shall we proceed?”

“Kih, yes, let’s.”

Unlike the aboveground area, there were no guards on the underground stairs.

That was because ordinary elves could not endure the miasma.

Continuing down the deserted stairs, the three people and one beast finally reached the lowest level.

At first glance, it looked like an empty cavern, but one wall surface alone appeared to be made of a different material.

In truth, that surface was not a wall. It was part of a living being’s body.

“Oh my, how unexpected. I didn’t think you would arrive before us.”

“…”

Aria spoke in genuine surprise.

A woman had already been in the cavern before they arrived.

“What’s wrong? You’ve gone quiet. This is supposed to be a touching reunion between sisters, you know.”

“I have never thought of you as my sister.”

“How odd. I’ve never thought of you as my older sister either, Aria.”

The girl called Aria called the other woman Aria as well.

Though they did not acknowledge each other as sisters, the appearances of the girl and the woman were extremely similar. If the girl were to grow a little older, she would look just like the woman.

“I currently go by Aqua. Have you decided on a name for yourself?”

“Why should I have a name like those inferior human races? …Well, as a temporary name, I do go by Aria to match yours.”

“What a hassle…”

The one whose true name was Aria currently called herself Aqua.

The one with no true name currently called herself Aria.

It was extremely confusing. From here on, unless otherwise specified, they will be referred to by their current names.

“Kihihi, Aria-san. Could you introduce her to me already?”

“Oh? Had I never told you?”

Aria tilted her head in response to Gired’s question.

“Kih, yes. If I had heard, there’s no way I would forget. She’s your kind, isn’t she?”

“That’s right. That woman is the same as me, an incarnation of the Calamity Dragon. She was born first, so she’s technically my elder sister. Although, since our originating egos are different, we don’t get along. Simply put, we’re enemies.”

“Kih! Kihihihi! How fascinating! Just the fact that a Calamity Dragon developed an ego and prepared incarnations is astonishing, but to think there are two of them! Ah! Why didn’t you tell me sooner!?”

“I didn’t want to be bombarded with questions again…”

Aria muttered softly, but her words did not reach Gired’s excited ears.

The relationship between Aria and Gired could best be described as that of accomplices.

They shared information related to their scheme, but they had not laid bare every detail of each other’s lives.

It was understandable that she would avoid bringing up something she knew would lead to relentless questioning.

“So then, what are you here for?”

“To stop your scheme… to stop the revival of the Calamity Dragon.”

When Aria asked mockingly, Aqua declared her intent with killing intent.

The Calamity Dragon is a ‘disaster’ capable of destroying the world.

It is an existence akin to a natural disaster given form, and though it is currently sealed, that seal is neither absolute nor eternal. In fact, it was about to be broken by Aria.

“Ahaha! Ahahahahaha! As expected of the ‘ego that desires tranquility’, you really do say the funniest things! To be born from a Calamity Dragon and yet refuse its revival, your very reason for existence is so nonsensical that all I can do is laugh!”

Normally, Calamity Dragons do not possess egos, but for some reason, one may arise.

When that happens, the Calamity Dragon gains the ability to create incarnations modeled after humans.

The personality and disposition of these incarnations are heavily influenced by the Calamity Dragon’s ego and emotions.

Aqua, born first, was based on the ‘ego that desires tranquility’. Aria, born later, was based on the ‘ego that desires destruction’.

Aria mocked Aqua’s words, but in truth, she was incorrect.

Even if a Calamity Dragon has an ego, it does not possess concepts like good and evil. Though its existence brings destruction, it does not do so out of preference.

In other words, the Calamity Dragon itself does not wish for its seal to be broken.

Put bluntly, Aria was born when it was irritated, and Aqua was born when it had calmed down. That was all there was to it.

“Say whatever you like. The Calamity Dragon must not be revived. And you there, elf in the white coat, why are you acting together with such a woman? If the Calamity Dragon awakens, you will be swallowed by the waves as well.”

Aqua’s anger was directed at Gired as well.

If the revival of the Calamity Dragon would destroy the world, then those who cooperated in it should naturally be destroyed too.

In Aqua’s eyes, Gired did not look like someone with a death wish.

“Kih, that’s simple. I have a way to survive even if the Water Calamity Dragon revives. More importantly, witnessing the revival up close is far more important to me.”

In truth, Gired had once had an opportunity to witness a Calamity Dragon’s revival before.

However, at that time his preparations for evacuation were insufficient, forcing him to withdraw.

This time, he had made thorough preparations and intended to be the sole survivor.

“You understand that persuasion is pointless at this stage, don’t you?”

“…Yes. I was foolish. Then I will stop you by force.”

Aqua drew a sword from her item box, unsheathed it, and took a stance.

“Hehe, I’ve found you irritating for a long time myself, so this is perfect timing. Even if you were born first, let’s see whether ‘tranquility’ can overcome ‘destruction’.”

The first to move was Aria.

“Do it.”

At that single word, the eyes of Basilisk Disaster glowed ominously, and unavoidable petrification assaulted Aqua… or so it should have.

“Oh my. You took countermeasures.”

“Of course. The plot on the drifting island… no, on the island whale, has already been exposed.”

As an incarnation of the Water Calamity Dragon, Aqua could manipulate water without using magic.

By forming a thin film of water over her body, she nullified the effect of the evil eye that petrifies those who look upon it directly.

“Now it’s my turn.”

Saying that, Aqua slashed at Aria with her sword.

Her movements were clearly not those of an amateur, conveying the sense of long years of training.

Aqua’s slash perfectly captured Aria, who was seated atop Basilisk Disaster, but Aria avoided it by leaping away at the last moment.

Twisting her body in midair, Aria then hurled several knives at Aqua.

“Poison…!”

Sensing that the knives were coated with poison, Aqua chose to evade rather than deflect them with her sword.

“Press the attack.”

At Aria’s command, Basilisk Disaster lunged at Aqua.

Though it specialized in petrification, it was still a large monster with physical strength. Even a simple charge would be devastating if it connected.

“‘Aqua Wall’!”

Aqua halted the charge with a spell activated with \<No chant>.

Both Aria and Aqua could use high-level \<Water Magic>, but \<Water Magic> had almost no effect on an incarnation of the Water Calamity Dragon.

A battle of Water Magic would amount to little more than splashing water at each other, so they were forced into physical combat instead. Precisely because they understood this, both had honed their direct combat abilities.

Of course, there was no need to hold back against Basilisk Disaster.

“‘Aqua Javelin’!”

A high-level offensive spell struck Basilisk Disaster directly.

As an aside, Aston was still bound on its back.

An ordinary basilisk would have died from that blow, but Basilisk Disaster suffered little damage, merely rearing back violently.

This too was a countermeasure Aria had prepared with her battle against Aqua in mind.

“Hah!”

Passing by Basilisk Disaster, Aqua once again slashed at Aria.

“Oh my, ignoring everyone else and focusing on me? Are you that fond of me?”

“Be quiet!”

Trading banter, Aria parried Aqua’s slash with the short daggers in both hands.

As was evident from her throwing knife skills, Aria was also well-versed in weapon handling.

From there, a fierce exchange of blades began.

The short daggers also appeared to be coated with poison, forcing Aqua to adopt a strategy of avoiding any hits at all, which in turn left her without a decisive blow.

Aqua had greater reach, making it hard for Aria to press the attack, resulting in a stalemate.

“Do it!”

“It’s useless!”

Aria periodically issued commands to Basilisk Disaster, but their coordination was poor, making it easy for Aqua to evade.

This was a drawback of modifying a monster. It lacked the intelligence to follow anything beyond simple commands.

Though it was not an overwhelming threat, it was still a two-on-one fight, which was another factor preventing a decisive outcome.

The stalemate continued for a while, until one word from Aria broke it.

“Is it about time?”

“Kihihi. Yes, that’s fine.”

The one who responded to Aria was Gired, who until now had remained uninvolved.

“What!?”

What Aqua saw was Gired touching the wall where the Calamity Dragon’s body was exposed.

“Fool. Of course reviving the Calamity Dragon takes priority over dealing with you.”

“Aren’t you the one reviving it!?”

“No. Rather, it is Dr. Gired’s research that holds the key to the Calamity Dragon’s revival.”

As an incarnation of the Calamity Dragon, Aria possessed many special powers, but she had no ability to hasten its revival. In that regard, she relied entirely on Gired’s research.

If interference arose during the revival, the plan was for Aria to buy time while Gired advanced the process.

In other words, Aria standing at the forefront had been a feint. The true mastermind behind the revival was Gired.

“Kih, kihihihihi!!!”

Laughing maniacally, Gired pressed a crystal-like object against the Calamity Dragon’s body.

The crystal flashed once, then vanished from Gired’s hand.

That alone was enough to break the seal on the Calamity Dragon that had endured for countless ages.

-Gogogogogogogogogogogo-

The Calamity Dragon began to move, and the underground chamber started collapsing with a thunderous roar.

“Kih! Kih! As I thought, my theory was correct!”

Facing a situation that could destroy a nation, or even the world, Gired shouted in ecstatic delight.

“This can’t be…”

Thus, Gired and Aria’s wishes were fulfilled, while Aqua’s wish was cut short.

The Central Island, the heart of the Pajel Kingdom, was an artificial island constructed around the Calamity Dragon’s seal.

Therefore, once the seal was broken, it was only natural that the Central Island would collapse.

The calamity governed by the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’ is, as its name suggests, ‘tsunami’.

What must not be misunderstood is that tsunamis do not occur because the Water Calamity Dragon swims through the sea. Rather, tsunamis are generated simply by its existence.

Even without a cause (like an earthquake), the result known as a tsunami manifests. That is the nature of the Water Calamity Dragon.

The Central Island was directly struck by both the collapse caused by losing its core and the tsunamis of the Water Calamity Dragon, and vanished without leaving any trace.

Tens of thousands of lives that lived on the island were swallowed into the depths.

Having escaped the underground chamber, Aria, Gired, and Aston rode atop the levitating Basilisk Disaster.

To avoid the Water Calamity Dragon’s damage and observe the situation, they were hovering about 100 meters above the sea.

This was made possible by the Flight ability Basilisk Disaster had gained through modification.

“Look. This is the result of your actions, Aston-sama.”

“A-ahh…”

Aston could only tremble at the sight below.

Seeing his birthplace, the Central Island, collapse, and the unceasing tsunamis generated by the Water Calamity Dragon heading toward the other islands, he had no mental capacity left to think.

“It was Ashley’s job to prevent this situation. Because you and I drove Ashley away, this happened.”

“N-no… I-I never wanted this…”

“This is exactly what I wanted. I truly am grateful to you.”

Only now did Aston finally understand Aria’s objective.

No matter how foolish he was, if he had known such a monster would appear, he would never have tried to kill Ashley.

Conversely, it was precisely because he was ignorant that Aria had targeted him.

“N-no… I-I had nothing to do with this…”

“Oh my, please don’t say such cruel things. Without your cooperation, my wish could never have been fulfilled. That’s why this is my thanks to you.”

“S-stop… Stop it, please…!”

Aria wore a sadistic smile, while Aston’s face was etched with despair.

Gired paid the two of them no heed, continuing to observe the Calamity Dragon’s activity.

From Aston’s perspective, the situation was already more than hopeless, but in truth, it was only the beginning.

The Water Calamity Dragon had not yet begun moving in earnest.

A Calamity Dragon that has just been unsealed cannot move very actively.

When an existence that causes destruction even without moving begins to act in full, it is not hard to imagine how vast and widespread the damage would be.

It would be fitting to call it the end of the world.

That is, if one could live to see it.

-Gogogogogogogogogogogo-

“Huh!? What!?”

A rumble similar yet different from the one that accompanied the Water Calamity Dragon’s revival was heard.

-DobaAAAAAAAAAN!!!-

In less than ten seconds, a gigantic rock wall thrust up from the sea.

Centered on the former Central Island, the rock wall appeared in a perfect circle with a radius of several kilometers, sealing it off without gaps.

As a result, all of the tsunamis caused by the Water Calamity Dragon were blocked by the rock wall.

Even as it bore the energy of the tsunamis, the rock wall did not so much as tremble.

The unceasing waves were completely sealed in.

“What is this…?”

“Kih!? Kihihi!? I don’t understand! What is happening!?”

Aria was dumbfounded, and Gired screamed like a madman.

Even the two who knew of the Calamity Dragon, a supernatural existence, could not comprehend the phenomenon unfolding before their eyes.

If they had calmly thought it through, they might have realized.

Only another supernatural existence could neutralize a supernatural existence.

However, in reality, there is no such thing as “if”.

-DON!!!!!!-

A few seconds after a shockwave that resonated to the core of one’s body, the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’ vanished without a trace.

Thus, before either of them could realize anything, Gired and Aria’s wish was cut short.

After the disappearance of the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’, Aria and Gired stood dazed for a while.

Just moments ago, a rock wall had appeared, stopping the tsunamis, and then, with a shock, the Calamity Dragon vanished.

Put into words, that was all, but there was no doubt it was a sight that defied comprehension.

For the two who had staked everything on the existence of the Calamity Dragon, the shock was immeasurable.

Especially for Aria, who believed witnessing destruction by the Calamity Dragon to be her very reason for existence, having her wish snatched away at the very moment she thought it would be fulfilled left her face devoid of expression.

-Gogogogogogogogogogogo-

As the tsunamis subsided with the disappearance of the Calamity Dragon, the rock wall sank back down with a similar rumble.

All that remained was the Central Island, destroyed by the revival of the Calamity Dragon.

“Kihihi, no way…”

Watching the scene, Gired showed signs of realizing something.

“Kih, kihihihihi!!! No way, no way! Unbelievable! Impossible! Didn’t the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’ fail to revive!? Didn’t the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ survive!? Could it be! Is there an existence capable of killing a Calamity Dragon!? Absurd! But if that’s the case, everything makes sense! No! More importantly, what about the ‘Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake’!? The ‘Fire Calamity Dragon: Volcano’!? Focusing solely on the Water Calamity Dragon after severing ties with the Sky Castle has come back to bite me!”

Ranting uncontrollably, Gired clawed at his hair.

“But even so, the timing is too perfect! How much time was there between the Wind Calamity Dragon’s revival and it causing major damage!? To surround the area with rock walls before any damage beyond the Central Island occurred, you’d have to be watching constantly just to time it! There’s no way that could happen by chance! …Don’t tell me! From the Wind Calamity Dragon onward, or even before that, my actions were being monitored!?”

They were not.

“It’s unbelievable that someone could outmaneuver a genius like me! But I can’t ignore that possibility! Still, I can’t understand why they wouldn’t act until after the Calamity Dragon revived! Without knowing their objective, it’s difficult to devise countermeasures! Ah! Where should I even begin!?”

At that moment, Gired’s best possible choice would have been to stop thinking and flee this place with all his might.

Had he done so, the moment of ruin would have been delayed just a little.

“What is this!?”

Aria, who had been dazed until now, cried out as her eyes widened in shock.

“Kih! Aria-san! What on earth is-…”

Before Gired could finish speaking, a sphere of water enveloped the three people and one beast, sealing them inside.

“Kih. Is this… magic?”

“No… This is the power of the Water Calamity Dragon. Why…?”

When Aria touched the water sphere, it felt like touching a wall.

Even when she pushed with force, her hand would not go beyond the surface of the sphere.

“Kihihi? Does that mean the Water Calamity Dragon was alive? Even if it were, there’s no reason to trap us. …Could it be possible to assimilate the Water Calamity Dragon’s power?”

Though he thought it impossible, Gired did not exclude the impossible from his options.

That flexible thinking was one of Gired’s strengths, but considering how he ignored ethics to realize such ideas, it also made him a menace in the eyes of society.

“Kih, there’s nothing left to do but run.”

Gired was, at heart, a cautious man. He also understood the danger of his own research.

Preparing for emergencies, he always kept multiple escape methods at the ready.

-Squish!-

“Kih?”

At that moment, nearly all of Gired’s prepared escape methods were pierced and rendered useless by water spears extending from the water sphere.

“Guh!?”

Next, tentacle-like appendages extended from the water sphere, entered Gired’s mouth, and destroyed the final emergency escape method inside his mouth.

“Kya!?”

“Hii!?”

“Guh!?”

The water sphere, which had not moved until now, suddenly began to move.

Naturally, the three people were carried along with Basilisk Disaster.

Ahead of the water sphere lay a single island.

---

**AN:** Still in the process of being written, but the arc should end in one or two more chapters.

Next time: “Gired Dies”.

+++

## **198: Subjugation of the Water Calamity Dragon and Retribution**

**AN:** There is some rather blatant padding in this chapter. Please forgive me.

---

There were a few slightly unexpected developments, but since the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’ revived more or less as planned, we decided to run various experiments.

“Offensive magic is reduced by ninety-nine percent, and magic that directly affects the target is nullified… Even Recovery Magic has no effect, so it seems to be indiscriminately nullifying everything…”

《Dora’s breath works though!》

“Dragon Magic appears to be an exception… Perhaps magic skills derived from abnormal individuals are treated differently…?”

“Arrows do stick, but barely get into the surface. It’s insanely tough.”

“It seems even weapon special effects are weakened. Things that inflict abnormal states are completely ineffective.”

“By stacking enhancement-type skills, including the Kusanagi Sword, we were barely able to inflict visible damage.”

The abilities of the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’ have a devastating effect on civilized society, but when considered as a single opponent, it can be said to have the lowest offensive power.

After all, if you have a way to fly, you can fight it without taking any attacks.

The other calamity dragons were dangerous even to approach, but this one is different.

Thinking this was the perfect chance to give my companions experience fighting a calamity dragon, we ended up beating it senseless together right after its revival.

“It looks like it’s about time to stop the tsunami.”

I muttered as I looked around.

At present, the tsunami caused by the Water Calamity Dragon was advancing, about to swallow the surrounding islands.

“I will accompany you.”

Taking Maria with me, I descended onto the land that had barely remained and stomped my foot several times.

-Gogogogogogo!!!-

As you can tell, I used the power of the Earth Calamity Dragon.

By creating walls of rock surrounding the Water Calamity Dragon’s body, I stopped the tsunami.

At first, I was only thinking of protecting Latis Island, but I realized that even if we saved Latis Island, life would become difficult if all the surrounding islands were wiped out, so I decided to protect the other islands as well.

Huh? The central island where the calamity dragon had been sealed? I can’t take responsibility that far.

At best, we rescued about ninety percent of the elves and thirty percent of the residents.

The elves who had been petrified and shattered were all gathered using Vacuum and revived.

As for thirty percent of the residents and ninety percent of the elves, we instead petrified them the moment they were caught in the tsunami.

Then, after they sank to the bottom of the sea, we recovered and revived them. That way, it could be handled as a miraculous survival.

Why not save everyone? Simply put, it was a karma-value issue.

Seventy percent of the humans who were on the collapsed island were not worth saving. The same applied to ten percent of the elves.

This was the island where the nobles of a rotten kingdom were most densely concentrated. I honestly can’t tell whether seventy percent is a high number or not.

Compared to the nobles, the elf clan of the Princess Shrine Maidens was more than decent, but even among them, there were some individuals who made me want to say “No.”

Naturally, those were part of the ten percent I didn’t save.

For the record, Ashley is fully aware of this. Given my past track record, it probably goes without saying, but everyone I saved was enslaved.

After being revived from petrification, Alta will apparently explain the situation to them individually.

That makes it much easier to keep the story of their ‘miraculous survival’ consistent.

…Oops, it looks like the Water Calamity Dragon is about to start moving.

As expected, rock walls alone probably won’t be enough to stop the Water Calamity Dragon itself from moving.

《Alright then, I think it’s about time to finish off the Water Calamity Dragon. Sorry, but I’ll be the one to do it, okay?》

After confirming via telepathy, I received everyone’s consent.

《Is there really anyone here who’d say no?》

Even without Mio pointing it out, I understand that. Still, following proper procedure is important.

If someone had said no, I would have persuaded them with everything I had. I had no intention of yielding.

“Ready, set!”

-Don!!!!!!-

I approached the Water Calamity Dragon and punched it with full force.

Taking the surrounding damage into account, I used a technique that transmitted only the impact internally, striking it in a way that wouldn’t blow the body away.

This is actually a technique I could use back in my original world as well.

From the earlier tests, we learned that high-powered blunt force attacks are effective against calamity dragons.

If you ignore the tough outer hide and deal damage directly to the inside, it seems to work even on calamity dragons.

In other words, my previous approach was absolutely correct.

The Water Calamity Dragon died easily, so I stored it in \<Infinite Storage>.

That makes all four calamity dragons defeated, but…

Unfortunately, my Special Power level did not increase.

Maria’s, Dora’s, and Sera’s unique skills also did not rise past level 9.

The other local Heroes had their Hero levels increase, so it seems something is missing to reach level 10.

Alright, now that skill level checks are done, it’s time to move on to the next task.

There are plenty of methods, but since we have the chance, I plan to use the power of the Water Calamity Dragon.

When I defeat a calamity dragon, I gain the ability to manipulate attributes related to the disaster that dragon governs.

This time, since it was a water calamity dragon, I can manipulate and generate \<Water>.

As a side note, the Water Calamity Dragon’s ability isn’t ‘to cause tsunamis’, but rather ‘to cause tsunamis anywhere’.

For example, if you toss the Water Calamity Dragon onto land, it generates massive amounts of water around itself, causing a tsunami. Surprisingly, the damage is greater when it’s on land than when it’s underwater.

It’s hard to notice when it’s underwater since it doesn’t generate water then, but I wanted to clarify that the Water Calamity Dragon originally has the power to generate water.

Using the power of the Water Calamity Dragon, I bound the three people responsible for the incident together inside a water-sphere cage.

Ah, sorry, but I’m going to destroy all those troublesome magical tools.

I like interesting magical tools, but the things made by that person are way too ominous, and I don’t feel like I’d enjoy them, so I have no intention of collecting them.

Next, I need to transport the water spheres containing the three prisoners to the final stage.

However, I have no intention of carrying these guys gently. So I manipulated the water spheres and launched them with great force.

The water spheres flew at incredible speed toward a certain island.

《Then let’s teleport with ‘Portal’.》

《Is that really okay?》

《As long as we catch them at the destination, it’s fine.》

We quickly used ‘Portal’ to teleport to the uninhabited island where Ashley was waiting.

The water spheres that flew through the air were re-controlled using the Water Calamity Dragon’s power and left floating in midair.

“Sorry, did I keep you waiting?”

I called out to the three women present.

The first is Ashley, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ of the Water Calamity Dragon.

The second is Asuka, the Oni hero.

The third is Ulysses, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ of the Earth Calamity Dragon.

Pretty easy to tell what kind of gathering this is, right?

The three trapped in the water spheres… Gired, Aston and Aria.

There are other spectators as well, but the main characters are these three.

Sakura and the others have gone to the spectator area (except for Maria).

“No, please don’t worry about it… More importantly, the Water Calamity Dragon has truly been eradicated. This isn’t a dream, is it?”

Ashley asked with an expression mixing surprise, joy, and confusion.

“It’s not a dream. I told you Jin-san would accomplish it, didn’t I?”

“Yes. Ulysses-san was right.”

It was Ulysses who answered Ashley’s question gently.

“You’ve gotten quite close in the time I wasn’t looking.”

“Yes. Our circumstances were similar, so we naturally bonded.”

“I haven’t suffered as terribly as Ulysses-san, but…”

Even from the perspective of a fellow ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, Ulysses’s circumstances were indeed severe.

“Are you ready yet? Hurry up!”

Asuka urged us, looking fired up.

Asuka has gotten stronger again in the time I wasn’t watching.

While we were busy with various things, she had been relentlessly training in combat with my subordinates on this island. Naturally, with a good teacher, Asuka will keep growing stronger.

Eventually, I’ll teach her common sense too, but for now, I’ll let her do as she likes.

Incidentally, I didn’t take her to the fight against the Water Calamity Dragon.

Defeating a calamity dragon raises certain skill levels, such as \<Hero> and \<Dragon Magic>.

The human Hero, the dwarf Hero, and the Sky Dragon’s were all called over right before the Water Calamity Dragon was defeated, then immediately sent back.

However, Asuka had only recently joined my subordinates and barely understood the situation.

I felt uneasy about taking her to face a calamity dragon before she was fully accustomed to my way of doing things.

Naturally, I also didn’t take the other dwarf Hero, who is still a fetus.

No matter how you look at it, calamity dragons aren’t good for a mother’s body.

“Are you both prepared?”

What I asked about was their resolve to face those they had deep grudges against.

As long as I’m here, I can guarantee their physical safety, but I can’t guarantee their emotional safety.

“”Yes.””

Hearing their firm replies, I lowered the water spheres to the ground.

Then I manipulated them further, reshaping them from spheres into restraints for the three individuals.

“Geh, cough!”

Gired had been in a semi-suffocating state inside the water sphere and was desperately gasping for air.

“Are you Ashley? Is this the island Ashley escaped to?”

At that point, Aria noticed Ashley’s presence.

Since Aria was the one who prepared the chimera on this island, she seemed to remember it.

“Ashley!! Is that really Ashley!?”

Aston, who had been dazed until now, suddenly shouted.

“Help me, Ashley! I was deceived by this woman! The one I truly love is you! Please, come back to me!”

Wow… that’s awful.

Both Ashley and Ulysses next to her were completely put off.

Anyone who knows the circumstances would think this line is utterly impossible.

As for Asuka, she doesn’t really understand the situation and is just glaring hard at Aria.

“Haa… haa… kihi, could it be that the lady over there is Ulysses-sama? It’s been a while. So the Earth Calamity Dragon was also destroyed, just like the Water Calamity Dragon… And you must be the one who defeated them.”

After catching his breath, Gired looked at Ulysses, grasped the fate of the Earth Calamity Dragon, then looked at me and understood who I was.

As expected, Gired’s intellect is quite impressive.

“A human defeating calamity dragons…? That’s impossible.”

“Kihi! But Aria-san, you saw the Water Calamity Dragon’s end with your own eyes, didn’t you? And earlier, you yourself said you felt the calamity dragon’s power in that water sphere.”

“That’s true… I do feel the same power in this water restraint.”

Looking at the water binding her, Aria accepted Gired’s argument.

Meanwhile, Aston was still groaning beside her, but he was being ignored unanimously.

“Kihi… I don’t know about that young lady over there, but with Ulysses-sama and Ashley-sama present, and this lineup on the other side, I suppose this is an execution ground?”

Gired’s use of his intellect may be despicable, but his understanding is extremely sharp.

That’s right. This is a stage for victims to punch their aggressors.

Ulysses, Asuka, and Ashley can all be said to have already been saved.

The greatest source of their misfortune has been removed.

But that doesn’t mean there’s no need to settle things.

It doesn’t justify letting the aggressors go without even punching them once.

“Correct. As you know, Ulysses was sealed in crystal by you, Gired, and forced to maintain the Earth Calamity Dragon’s seal. Asuka had her drifting-island village annihilated by Aria.”

“Kihi! Ah yes, I recall Aria-san mentioning that.”

Gired spoke as if it were someone else’s problem, but he was also involved in that cockatrice.

“Of course, you bear responsibility as well. And Ashley was framed by Aria and Aston and nearly killed.”

“Wait! That’s a misunderstanding! I was just being deceived! I never intended to kill Ashley!”

Doubtful.

At the very least, choosing to kill Ashley was Aston’s own decision.

Looking at her, Ashley’s eyes were icy cold.

“Then, were the words you spoke at that time not your true feelings?”

“Yes! Of course! I only said things I didn’t mean while suffering inside!”

Wow… (second time)

“If you insist on that, then could you please repeat what you said at that time? If you were suffering so much, you should at least remember what you said, right?”

“I-I can’t… I can’t do something so painful again.”

“Please don’t say that. If you would also convey your true feelings from that time, it would surely save my heart.”

“…”

If he claims he didn’t mean it, then he should recall and repeat what he said and explain his true feelings.

Quite a difficult challenge. Ashley has a surprisingly good personality.

“Ashley, there’s something I want to tell you.”

Since Aston wasn’t saying anything no matter how long it took, Ashley spoke up.

“I hate you. I was busy studying to become king, yet you constantly followed me around and were a nuisance. I dislike sweets, yet you brought tasteless confections every single time. When we were children it was one thing, but now the difference in our heights is so great that it looks less like escorting and more like babysitting, yet you still asked for escorts without understanding that. It was pathetic. You would sometimes come to see me with a terribly haggard look on your face. Honestly, it was creepy, and I hated even seeing your face. Though I, a prince, attended the academy without guards, only you always had dangerous-looking escorts stuck to you. It was excessive and hindered my school life. Even when I tried to distance myself, you would approach me regardless. I only accepted you because I heard the throne of the next king was assured. I never imagined you would be this troublesome. Even when I asked my father to dissolve the engagement later, he flatly refused. I endured all of this, and with just one more year, I would be free from you. I know that, but I can’t endure even that one year. I have someone I truly love, someone who is not a fake like you. Aria, I’ve been waiting for you… Now, the actors are all assembled. This is a ritual to free myself from the curse that is you. I’ve been waiting for this day so eagerly… Ashley, I am breaking off our engagement. Ah, my beloved Aria. Soon our wishes will come true. Now then, you may have noticed, but at present, only the three of us in this venue are conscious. This phenomenon was caused by a treasured magical tool Aria possessed. Naturally, we are unaffected by it. You were left just mobile enough to talk. We will kill you here, then pretend to sleep. A perfect plan disguised as the work of thieves. Weapons were forbidden, but security inspections were lax. It was worth luring you here at the last moment.”

Here, Ashley took a deep breath once.

“This is our eternal farewell. Do you have any last words? I won’t pass them on, but I’ll at least hear them.”

Judging by Ashley’s demeanor, that was the end.

“Those are the words you gave me that day. Where, and how, were you suffering? I couldn’t understand it at all. Aston-sama, won’t you please tell me?”

“No… wait… it’s a misunderstanding… I love you, Ashley…”

“Haa…”

Ashley let out a deep sigh.

“To be honest, whether it was your true feelings or not doesn’t matter at all. The engagement itself was a farce. I never sought love from the beginning.”

“Then why did you accept the engagement…?”

“I wanted emotional support. That’s all. What I asked of you was simply to behave like a proper fiancé. You should have heard that from the king…”

If she was to live while suffering as a Princess Shrine Maiden, she at least wanted emotional support, a beautiful story-like memory, even if it was a farce.

That was Ashley’s wish.

“In other words, that day, you betrayed me and tried to kill me. Your true feelings are irrelevant. For me, your actions and behavior are everything. Therefore, I will never forgive you. Never! I will never forgive you!”

To put it bluntly, it’s like the actors ad-libbed a happy-ending play into a bad ending.

From Ashley’s perspective, regardless of his true feelings, it was an unforgivable betrayal.

“You traitor!!!”

-Dogoh!-

“Gubeh!”

Ashley delivered her settling blow, smashing Aston’s jaw.

Aston flew back and lost consciousness.

“Phew, I’m satisfied.”

After saying everything she wanted to say and punching him once, Ashley showed a refreshed expression.

“Kihi! I see, victims exacting retribution upon their aggressors! Whose turn is next?”

“Aria. Shut up.”

“Kihihi!”

Next, it’s Asuka’s turn to face Aria.

Ashley does bear resentment toward Aria as well, but she has no intention of voicing grievances.

What Ashley found most unforgivable was Aston’s betrayal.

Aria was an accomplice, but given her goal of reviving the Water Calamity Dragon, she was fundamentally incompatible with Ashley.

In other words, she was a pure enemy, and since Ashley had already won, there was no point in doing anything further.

Ashley stepped back, and Asuka approached Aria.

“Why did you attack the village?”

“What are you talking about? Who are you, anyway?”

Aria didn’t remember Asuka.

Given how different Asuka looks now compared to back then, that’s understandable.

“Three years ago. The drifting-island village. You attacked with a cockatrice.”

“Oh, that. I remember. When I went to pick up monsters from Gired-sensei’s lab, a child on the island spotted me, so I had the monsters attack as a test and to silence witnesses.”

“I’m that child.”

“Oh, so there was a survivor… It’s only natural to be hated. There’s no excuse for that.”

We released everyone’s petrification, but there’s no need to mention that here.

“One punch.”

“Go ahead. With the Water Calamity Dragon gone, my life has no meaning. You can kill me if you want.”

Having lost her purpose, Aria had also lost her attachment to life.

-Gos-

A solid gut punch landed, and Aria collapsed.

“I’m satisfied.”

Asuka said only that and stepped away from Aria.

It was a very straightforward confrontation, as if settling things was her sole purpose.

With Aston and Aria unconscious, only Gired remained conscious.

“Kihihi, so that leaves only me. My opponent would be Ulysses-sama, correct?”

Even after seeing the other two get punched, he showed no agitation, maintaining a relaxed expression.

“Yes, that’s right.”

Ulysses stepped forward.

Asuka also has a grudge against Gired, but since she’s never met him, she apparently has nothing to say.

“Kihi, you resent me for sealing you in crystal as a noble sacrifice for my research, don’t you? After being bathed in calamity dragon miasma for six thousand years, your resentment must be quite deep.”

“I have no intention of complaining to you about being sealed in crystal.”

“Kihi?”

It seems Gired misunderstood the reason he was hated.

“You may have realized the sealing, but it was the entire clan that decided on it. There’s no point in hating you alone. Besides, I even gained encounters that felt like a reward for enduring six thousand years, so I can think it wasn’t all bad.”

Ulysses glanced at me.

Right. She met Sharon and Faron, two friends (Looking away).

“Kihihi? Then why did you prepare this stage? You have no other reason to resent me, do you?”

He seemed genuinely unable to understand.

“You kept boasting endlessly to me when I couldn’t move or even cover my ears, didn’t you? While I was suffering from the calamity dragon’s miasma, you gazed at the sealing crystal and basked in self-satisfaction.”

Ulysses’s resentment was toward Gired’s actions after the sealing.

Boasting and gloating in front of someone suffering naturally breeds hatred.

“Kihi? Why would that cause resentment? I merely taught you of my intellect and the brilliance of my research so you would know your sacrifice wasn’t in vain. And basking in one’s research results is perfectly natural for a researcher, isn’t it?”

Shocking. Gired’s boasting was, unbelievably, out of goodwill.

“From the sufferer’s side, whether it was in vain or not doesn’t matter at all! Hearing the aggressor boast and seeing them pleased is far more unpleasant!”

Exactly.

“Kihi? I truly don’t understand. It seems I still have much to learn.”

“This is pointless… I’ll just punch you.”

Judging words to be useless, Ulysses cut the conversation short.

“Kihi! Please go easy…”

-Mekyoh!-

“Kihbu!”

Before Gired could finish his sentence, Ulysses’s fist sank into his cheek.

This blow was filled with Ulysses’s resentment.

After being freed from the seal, she never neglected her training, all to punch Gired.

She even refused a status transfer from me because she wanted to punch him with her own strength.

It was a truly all-out strike without the slightest hint of restraint.

Teeth broke, consciousness was lost, and Gired collapsed.

He was still alive, but his HP was well below half. A clear red zone. Let’s call it the Gired Zone.

…

Thus, all three aggressors lost consciousness.

The victims had punched their aggressors and settled things, but the story doesn’t end there.

Aria and Gired are outright criminals, and Aston is still under suspended judgment.

The central island, the core of the Pajel Kingdom, collapsed, but most of the influential elf clans survived. And Ashley, the highest authority, is here.

Though not well known among commoners, the laws of this kingdom are centered around the elves.

The royal family is primarily entrusted with governance, while legal matters give priority to the elves.

If an elf with sufficient authority is present, they can freely decide the punishment of criminals caught in the act.

In other words, Ashley is allowed to decide the fate of the three here.

“We’ll proceed as planned, correct?”

“”Yes.””

“Understood.”

The punishments have already been decided.

First is Aston. His case is the simplest. Execution.

Aston’s suspended judgment meant that if he found Ashley and was forgiven, he would be acquitted. Otherwise, execution.

As you know, Ashley has declared absolute unforgiveness toward Aston. Execution is confirmed.

At Ashley’s request, Aston’s punishment will be carried out through official procedures.

In other words, not vigilante justice by Ashley’s discretion, but a death sentence under Pajel Kingdom law.

The significance is that the punishment will remain as official documentation and be announced to the citizens, stripping him of all honor and leaving him remembered as a great criminal for generations.

“He will meet a miserable end. In plays, it’s customary for evil to be punished at the end, isn’t it? Even if the script has been completely ruined and it was a farce to begin with…”

Ashley said something quite amusing.

For the record, Aston’s execution will likely take place some time later.

The collapse of an entire island has massive repercussions.

It will take considerable time to restore the kingdom’s functions.

To formally disgrace Aston, it’s preferable for the kingdom to be functioning normally.

Since Ashley desires that, Aston will spend the rest of his life trembling in fear of execution.

In contrast to Aston, Aria and Gired will not be judged through official procedures.

The collapse of the central island will be announced as an accident caused by a natural phenomenon.

Ashley has decided to conceal the calamity dragon incident. Naturally, it won’t be recorded in documents either.

That doesn’t mean the two’s crimes are forgiven. As a result, they will be dealt with secretly.

Well, dealing with them secretly is our job.

Officially, it will be framed as ‘punishment delegated by Ashley’.

In truth, ‘we are the most suitable to deliver real punishment’.

As you know, Asuka and Ulysses aren’t the only victims of Aria and Gired.

Among my subordinates, there are several other victims.

Having everyone punch them would feel too much like torture, so only representatives did the punching.

Instead, the nature of the punishment to be inflicted on the two was decided by the other victims.

I think the punishment fits their crimes quite well.

Please look forward to it!

---

**AN:** Gired did not die.

As an additional note, Gired’s stance is that ‘sacrifices are inevitable in research’ and that he is ‘grateful to the victims’.

He never spoke ill of the victims. That doesn’t mean his actions are forgivable.
