## **199: Reconstruction and Punishment**

**AN:** This chapter is effectively a chapter-result wrap-up.

There are executions, but there are no grotesque depictions. Some harsh things are done.

---

One day had passed since the revival of the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’.

Setting aside the frantic activity of those directly involved, the overall confusion across the Kingdom of Pajel had settled down to a certain extent.

This was because the majority of the elves, who were the original ruling class, had survived.

The Kingdom of Pajel had always lived with the enormous ticking bomb that was a Calamity Dragon, so its emergency response procedures were defined in meticulous detail. Naturally, only the elves knew the finer points.

Ashley going missing was unquestionably an emergency, and the elves had proceeded with their actions while keeping the possibility of the Calamity Dragon’s revival in mind.

The elite elves of the Central Island, in exchange for holding high positions, were almost guaranteed to die if the Calamity Dragon revived.

The mob elves on the other islands were supposed to immediately head to Latis Island upon the Calamity Dragon’s revival, then evacuate to the Sky Castle using teleportation magic tools.

As an aside, there is a magic tool for transmitting information to the other islands in the event that the Central Island collapses due to the Calamity Dragon’s revival.

Another aside: elves on islands far from Latis Island possess high-speed transport ships.

When we arrived at Latis Island together with Ashley, we were able to see mob elves running around in confusion because the teleportation magic tools were not activating.

Elite elves working while prepared for death, and mob elves running around in confusion due to the unexpected situation. As expected, the gap between elites and mobs is significant…

Incidentally, beneath them are the useless elves who came from the former Sky Castle.

Additionally, it was decided that the mob elves would not be informed about the Calamity Dragon’s end or our existence.

It was judged that as long as Ashley and the enslaved elite elves knew the circumstances, there was no need to inform the mob elves.

In the end, they are just mob elves…

Oh right. In order to explain various matters, Ashley has become one of my subordinates.

Not a slave, but a normal subordinate. There was no reason to make her a slave.

Recruiting Ashley was extremely difficult.

“If you become my subordinate, I’ll assign Tamo-san exclusively to you.”

“I’ll become your subordinate!”

That took about ten seconds.

Ashley loves Tamo-san far too much…

After that, the elite elves stepped forward and proceeded with public disclosure of the facts and the cleanup.

The biggest source of confusion was announcing that the true rulers of this kingdom were the elves.

With the Central Island destroyed and the royal family wiped out (excluding criminals), the elves, as the ruling class, stepped forward under the pretext that they had to govern.

The general populace may not know, but the nobles who manage each island are aware of the true rulers.

However, when they were informed of such a shocking truth alongside the destruction of an entire island, confusion among the general populace was inevitable.

In short, the general populace is confused, but the upper ranks are already rebuilding.

I sincerely hope the general populace does their best (not my problem).

We have no intention of directly involving ourselves in the kingdom’s reconstruction.

Even if we do not intervene, ships from the Advance Trading Company of the Izumo Wa Kingdom will eventually arrive carrying massive quantities of supplies needed for reconstruction…

There is no way they would miss such an obvious opportunity for expansion.

Because we did not involve ourselves in the Kingdom of Pajel’s reconstruction, some time passed.

The reason was simple: we were waiting for Aria and Gired to revive.

In fact, there was one thing that exceeded my expectations.

It seems the disciplinary punch landed too cleanly, because even after a full night had passed, neither of them woke up. They were not dead.

I did consider forcibly waking them up, but since I was the one who knocked them out, forcing them awake felt excessively cruel, so I refrained.

Thus, punishment time was postponed until they woke up naturally.

Oh right, I said yesterday that the punishment had already been decided, but based on information learned after capturing them, there were major changes.

And so, I used the free time to teleport to the Izumo Wa Kingdom.

The purpose was to return the identification papers I had received from Tooru and Kaoru.

“In the end, you never got to use them.”

“Such a shame.”

The twins spoke with genuine regret.

“I told you from the start that it’s better not to need to use them, right?”

Identification that grants treatment equivalent to a key figure of the state is better left unused.

We will set aside the fact that I ultimately added a key figure of the state to my subordinates.

“You didn’t need to go out of your way to return them.”

“That’s right. You could use them in countries around the Izumo Wa Kingdom as well.”

“No, I don’t mind receiving basic identification, but what you gave me was a rare item with limited issuance even at the national level. I can’t accept that.”

Identification granting key-figure-of-the-state treatment cannot be easily issued even by a royal family.

It was originally one of the rights the nation itself possessed.

I accepted it without much thought at first, but when I asked Alta later, I learned it was a national-level treasure.

Alta herself did not consider it a problem for me to possess it, though…

“If Jin-dono insists, then it cannot be helped…”

“It is truly regrettable…”

“If I need it again, I’ll ask.”

“”Yes (we will!) (indeed!)””

Based on my experience so far, whenever I go to a country, I inevitably become involved with authority in some form, so the secret is that I never need identification twice for the same country.

Around noon, at long last, I received word that the first person had awakened.

To cut to the chase, Aria woke up first.

It seems Gired suffered greater damage.

I gathered Aria’s victims and related parties, then teleported once more to Execution Island (the island Ashley had been on, now named), and headed for the cage holding Aria.

Naturally, Aria and Gired were restrained separately, and extensive escape countermeasures were in place.

“Oh my, I see some familiar faces. Have you come to kill me at last?”

There was no vitality in Aria’s eyes. She looked as though she had accepted her own death.

“Sorry, but I can’t kill you so easily anymore.”

“I see… torture, then?”

Death and pain would not serve as punishment for Aria.

That is precisely why an adjustment was needed.

“Yeah, but it’s mental torture.”

“I have no idea what you mean.”

“You’ll understand soon enough. Oh, and this person will be the executor.”

As I said that, a woman stepped out from a position hidden from Aria’s view.

“You are!?”

“It’s been a day. I didn’t expect to face you again.”

The person I brought was Aqua-san, a related party of Aria and the water guide of Pajel Island.

Believe it or not, Aqua-san was also an incarnation of the Water Calamity Dragon (deadpan).

The two had already confronted each other once yesterday in the underground chamber of the Central Island.

“Why are you here…!? You should have been crushed by rubble in the basement…”

“He saved me.”

Aqua-san pointed at me as she said that.

Aqua-san had no means of escaping from underground, and when she was about to be crushed by rubble, I easily rescued her using the power of the Wind Calamity Dragon.

“More importantly, I also learned about your scheme from him.”

“I see…”

Yes. That is exactly how it is.

We realized Aqua-san’s true identity when we met her during the gondola tour, naturally.

When an incarnation of a Calamity Dragon suddenly appeared right in front of me, even I was surprised.

However, since she was not doing anything malicious, I simply treated her normally.

As an aside, regarding her reputation as ‘young but highly capable guide’, it is a secret that I gave a wry smile when I saw the age field in her status.

And I was fully convinced by the reputation of ‘knows everything about the city’.

After grasping Aria’s scheme, I went to speak with her as a related party.

Here is part of that conversation from a few days ago.

“We have no intention of stopping the Calamity Dragon’s revival. What you do after hearing this is up to you.”

“I will stop the other incarnation. I will not allow the Calamity Dragon to revive.”

“Without the ‘Shrine Maiden’, revival is only a matter of time, don’t you think?”

“After stopping the incarnation, I will cooperate with the elves to search for the ‘Shrine Maiden’.”

“I think that’s pointless.”

“You know the location of the ‘Shrine Maiden’, don’t you?”

“And if I do?”

“Please tell me.”

“…What do you intend to do after finding the ‘Shrine Maiden’?”

“I will persuade her to return. If that fails, I will take over the role of the ‘Shrine Maiden’ myself.”

“Is that even possible?”

“It should be. Incarnations possess a nature extremely close to that of a ‘Shrine Maiden’.”

“Now that you mention it, Pes’s unique skill did transfer…”

“Is something wrong?”

“No, it’s nothing.”

“…May I ask you one thing?”

“What is it?”

“Why are you not trying to stop the Water Calamity Dragon’s revival? You are aware of what its revival would cause, are you not?”

“Yes, I know. There’s only one reason I won’t stop it. Because I’m not a party involved.”

“I don’t understand…”

“The revival of a Calamity Dragon is something that happens as a result of someone’s actions. I’m not one of the involved parties, so I have no intention of cleaning up after ‘someone else’, nor of bearing responsibility. However, once the Calamity Dragon revives, it becomes a crisis for the world, and then I become one of the involved parties.”

“But by the time you become involved, it will be too late!”

“It won’t be. If the Calamity Dragon revives, I’ll defeat it before the damage grows too large.”

“A Calamity Dragon is not an opponent humans can defeat.”

“I have no intention of debating that… But how about we make a bet?”

“A bet…?”

“Yes. If you succeed in preventing the Calamity Dragon’s revival, I’ll tell you the location of the ‘Shrine Maiden’.”

“Yes.”

“And if you fail and I defeat the Calamity Dragon, swear loyalty to me and become my subordinate.”

“Those are unreasonable terms… Are you telling me to become your slave?”

“No. Incarnations cannot be enslaved.”

“What? How do you know that?”

In the end, Aqua-san accepted the bet and successfully became my subordinate.

Even though she is my subordinate, I still call her Aqua-san because of her demeanor.

She somehow has an appearance that makes you want to add ‘-san’.

“So in the end, you will torture me? That is indeed humiliating.”

Being tortured and looked down upon by someone you have a grudge with would be humiliating. I am not doing that, though.

“No. I was not asked to do such a thing.”

“What do you mean?”

“I was only asked to pacify you.”

“I really don’t understand. Pacify me? I have no will to live anymore. What exactly do you intend to do?”

Without answering Aria’s question, I opened the cage holding her and entered with Aqua-san and Maria. …All their names sound similar and it’s confusing.

“You may have lost your motivation for now, but that is likely temporary due to the Calamity Dragon’s disappearance. Your essence is a ‘self that desires destruction’, and that has nothing to do with the Calamity Dragon’s life or death.”

“Indeed, my heart still desires destruction. Eventually, I will bring destruction by other means. If you’re going to kill me, now is the time.”

“That’s why I’m pacifying you. Like this…”

I grabbed Aria’s head.

“G-gyahhhhhhhhhhh!!!”

Aria screamed and struggled, but I am not lenient enough to let her escape from that.

Making its long-awaited return: the combo of \<Life and Death Control LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7>, used for ‘Contact and Manipulation of the Soul’.

Unlike normal living beings, incarnations have a weak bond between body and soul.

That is inevitable, because they are beings composed of a body modeled after humans by a Calamity Dragon and a provisional soul born from the Calamity Dragon’s ego. It is a combination that should not normally exist.

Because of that, with my ability, I can pull the soul out of the body. I can peel it away.

Even if physical torture does not work, very few can endure pain inflicted directly upon the soul.

This is the first stage of ‘mental torture’. …What? The meaning is different?

After some time, the body and soul completely separated. Aria’s body lost all strength, and Aria’s soul writhed in agony within my hand. She made no sound, though.

“All right, here we go.”

“Yes, please.”

I pushed Aria’s soul into Aqua-san.

“Guh…!?”

This time, Aqua-san let out a brief groan of pain, but quickly regained her composure.

Pushing it in is easier than pulling it out.

“How does it feel?”

“It’s hard to describe, but it doesn’t feel unpleasant. …Leave the rest to me.”

“Yeah, I’m counting on you.”

I listened to Aria’s telepathy… A voiceless voice.

《What is this!? My ‘self that desires destruction’ is fading! It’s being swallowed by a ‘self that desires peace’! Forgive me! Forgive me! Don’t come! Don’t come!!! Aaaaaaaaa!!!???》

Yes, cut.

Aria’s punishment can be summarized in one phrase: ‘overwriting the ego’.

Aria and Aqua are both incarnations of the same ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’. Aside from the type of ego they originated from, they can be said to be almost identical beings.

Ordinarily, a person can only have one soul in one body (exception: Sharon), but with these two, it was relatively easy to push the soul in and make them two minds sharing one body.

And Aria’s essence, the ‘self that desires destruction’, is crushed inside Aqua’s body by the ‘self that desires peace’ and gradually overwritten. Naturally, Aria has no control over the body.

Aria’s actions and ideology were all centered around the ‘self that desires destruction’.

Aqua-san, conversely, likely centers her actions around a ‘will that desires peace’. Otherwise, she would not have said she would stop the Calamity Dragon’s revival even if it meant becoming a ‘Shrine Maiden’.

For both of them, their originating ego holds enormous influence. The reason the two are fatally incompatible is simply because their egos are complete opposites.

The ego they value most is being overwritten by the opposite ego they despise most.

This is the most fitting punishment prepared for Aria.

As an aside, this punishment was significantly changed from the original plan after Aqua-san became my subordinate.

There were many things that could only be understood or done because Aqua-san was present.

Also, I should note that Alta’s advice was involved in the concrete implementation, so my abilities were fully utilized.

For Aria, it is a punishment equivalent to torture, but it is a trial with an end.

Once Aria becomes a complete ‘peaceful ego’, assimilation with Aqua-san will no longer be painful.

It could be called a kind of purification. Like cleansing an evil soul.

From Aqua-san’s perspective, she had felt pity that her younger sister, albeit in name, had lived her life thinking only of destruction under the influence of a ‘self that desires destruction’.

Fully aware that it was meddlesome, she decided to accept Aria’s soul with the desire to give her sister ‘peace’ as well.

More time passed, and Gired revived.

His HP had naturally recovered, and it seems he had escaped the Gired Zone.

Note that his broken teeth did not recover. I did not fix them.

This time, I gathered Gired’s victims and related parties and headed for his cage.

“Kihihi, there are many familiar faces. Ulysses-sama, Yurisus-sama, even Yulia-sama are present.”

Gired spoke with amusement upon seeing those gathered.

Ulysses and Yulia are here as victims. Yurisus is here as a related party.

“Kihi, since Princess Yuriela-sama has passed away, that means all the ‘Shrine Maidens’ of this country are assembled here. And it also means that all the Calamity Dragons have been laid to rest…”

Yuriela is actually alive, having revived despite losing her memory, but I have no intention of saying so.

Yuriela’s death was self-inflicted, so she was not called as a related party.

Yulia was called because she lost her memory due to Gired. She is happy now and has no intention of complaining about what happened before losing her memory.

“Kihihi. Well, that can be thought about later. More importantly, do you have some business with me?”

“Your punishment has been decided.”

“Kihihi, I see. So what do you want me to do?”

Gired asked calmly.

“You’re quite composed, considering you were punched by Ulysses.”

“Kihi, since Aria-san and the prince were not killed, I assumed the same would apply to me. Being punched by victims is unavoidable, but I do not wish to die. And since I am still alive now, my punishment will not involve my death, correct?”

I see. That explains Gired’s composure.

“Kihihihi, if I may say so myself, I am extremely capable. You also thought it would be a waste to kill me, didn’t you? That’s why you didn’t kill me. After losing so decisively, I have no desire to resist. I will swear loyalty to you and use this intellect for your sake.”

There was no lie in those words. The map display also showed blue (ally).

Whether I would accept that ally is a separate matter.

“Yes, your intellect is indeed a waste.”

“Kih! Right! Right!”

“But I don’t need you.”

“Kih?”

Gired’s intellect is outstanding, but it deviates greatly from what I consider ‘proper’.

Outstanding researchers tend to possess sensibilities different from ordinary people, so demanding a ‘proper personality’ may be unreasonable.

However, a researcher without a ‘proper ideal’ is not worth discussing.

Research into the ‘sealing’ of Calamity Dragons could be justified under the excuse of ‘for the sake of the world’ and could be included under ‘proper ideals’.

It could also be argued that Gired merely followed the orders of those above him.

He is undeniably despicable, but if he possessed ‘proper ideals’, it might have been enough to let the victims deliver a beating.

Even though there are victims among my subordinates, there was no harm done after I got involved.

However, research into the ‘release’ of Calamity Dragons is a different matter.

Certainly, researching ‘release’ in the process of researching ‘sealing’ is conceivable. But Gired did not hesitate to test the results of his research into ‘release’.

That was a decision Gired himself made and carried out, even if he had Aria as a collaborator.

I do not acknowledge that Gired possesses ‘proper ideals’.

A researcher without ‘proper ideals’ is not someone I want to keep close, and I even consider their mere existence harmful.

To begin with, this is a formal (albeit unofficial) punishment for attacking the ‘Shrine Maiden’ castle and reviving a Calamity Dragon. There is fundamentally no room for clemency.

Our job is to decide the punishment and carry it out.

…In theory, I could force things through Ashley and spare his life, but I do not believe Gired has that kind of value.

“Your punishment is ‘Deprivation of Knowledge’ and ‘Sealed Execution’.”

“Kih? I honestly don’t understand what that means.”

What I learned recently is that memory and knowledge are information engraved into the soul.

When reviving a living being, the longer the time since death, the more memory defects appear. This is because the soul gradually leaves the body over time, leading to memory loss.

Previously, when reviving Yuriela, the ‘Shrine Maiden’ of the Wind Calamity Dragon, there was unusually rapid memory loss. Upon investigation, it turned out this was a trait of High Elves.

High Elves are beings originally created to seal Calamity Dragons and possess special souls unlike ordinary people.

Those special souls have a weak bond with their bodies and easily leave them. This trait was one of the reasons behind Yuriela’s memory loss and Yulia’s amnesia.

And the ‘Deprivation of Knowledge’ in this punishment means erasing only academic knowledge from Gired’s soul while leaving his memories intact.

Needless to say, this is done using the combo of \<Life and Death Control LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7>.

Honestly, it’s very convenient in situations like this.

To be clear, this is not a technique that can be used on just anyone. Normally, memory and knowledge are treated as extremely important parts of the soul. In terms of ‘Individuality’, it would certainly be Rank 4 or higher.

*** See Author’s Note ‘Chapter 170.5: About the Soul’.**

However, beings with special souls like High Elves and incarnations treat memory and knowledge as having much lower importance, making them manipulable even by my ability.

Just as Aqua-san said, incarnations and ‘Shrine Maidens’… High Elves are truly very similar, for better or worse.

Naturally, this applies equally to Gired, a male High Elf who is not a ‘Shrine Maiden’.

Ironically, it means that the incarnation and the High Elf who were the masterminds of this incident ended up receiving similar punishments.

“You don’t need to understand. All you can do is regret.”

I touched Gired and activated my ability.

Separating knowledge while leaving memory intact is quite a tedious task, but with Alta’s support, it is not particularly difficult.

“Kihiiiiiiiiii!? Kihyaaaaaaa!?”

Bound in place, Gired writhed and screamed.

Apparently, having one’s soul tampered with causes indescribable discomfort and intense pain.

“K-kihi… Kihi…”

After the ‘Deprivation of Knowledge’ was complete, Gired was breathing strangely.

He likely did not yet understand what had happened to him.

“Question. How do you prevent the miasma of a Calamity Dragon?”

“Kihi… That’s simple… …Huh? Why can’t I remember!? Anything related to research! I can’t remember anything! What did you do to me!?”

“Did you forget already? I just told you.”

That should be ‘memory’, so he shouldn’t have forgotten…

“Kihi… Deprivation… Of knowledge…”

“Correct. I erased all academic knowledge from your mind.”

Memories that are completely erased from the soul never return.

“Kih!? Kih!? That’s impossible! Such a thing cannot be done! Stop saying such nonsense!”

“You’re a researcher, aren’t you? Don’t speak based on speculation. If you want to object, present evidence.”

“Kihiii!!!”

The problem is that he lacks the knowledge to produce evidence.

“Kih! It’s not over yet! If I’ve forgotten, I’ll just relearn it! I am a High Elf! I have practically infinite time!”

Truly an indomitable research spirit.

It is regrettable that he lacks ‘proper ideals’.

“Sorry, but that won’t happen. You still have one more punishment remaining.”

“Kih!? …R-right, ‘Sealed Execution’…”

“Yes. You seem to enjoy confining people. You should try being the one confined.”

As I said that, I took a crystal mass out of \<Infinite Storage>.

“Kih!? That is my creation, the ‘Sealing Crystal’…”

“Yes. The crystal that confined Ulysses. I will seal you inside it.”

“Kihihi!? You strip my knowledge, then seal me so I cannot acquire new knowledge and make me suffer indefinitely!? That is far too cruel a punishment…!?”

Even Gired turned pale and stiffened.

“Relax. Your punishment is execution. Death is guaranteed. After being sealed for 100 days, you will die. You will suffer during that time, but I will give you a clear end.”

“K-kihi…”

Gired slumped weakly.

Whether he felt relief or despair, I do not know.

I do not enjoy making someone suffer for eternity, so I give an end.

The victims did not ask for anything beyond that.

I sealed Gired inside the ‘Sealing Crystal’ and arranged for him to die after 100 days.

With the punishments of the two completed, everything that needed to be done in the Kingdom of Pajel was finished.

I returned to the mansion and organized in my mind the future of the subordinates acquired in the Kingdom of Pajel.

Since quite a few subordinates were added there, I might forget someone if I do not organize them. Supporting newcomers is important.

First are the two Heroes. As is well known, Asuka, the “Oni Hero”, completely lacks common sense, so acquiring that is the top priority. Combat training will be conducted in parallel at her request.

For the “Dwarf Hero”, the priority is being born safely. The mother seems stable as well, so I hope the child is born without issue.

According to the mother, she wants me, her benefactor and master, to decide the child’s name. …Would you say that even knowing my naming sense? No regrets?

Ashley, the ‘Water Shrine Maiden’, will remain until the Kingdom of Pajel’s functions are somewhat restored.

With the Calamity Dragon threat gone, there is no reason to remain in the kingdom. Ashley, who was originally interested in the outside world, said she would come to me after fulfilling her obligations.

Chevalier is still riding on her head. Ah, he was officially renamed (with his approval).

Aqua-san, the ‘Water Calamity Dragon’s Incarnation’, will remain on Latis Island.

Naturally so, since Aqua-san has a job on Latis Island. I cannot and will not tell her to abandon her current job and come to me when she wishes to continue it.

To be honest, I think her current profession suits her.

As previously stated, those petrified by basilisks and cockatrices will follow the policy of ‘those with a place to return go home’ and ‘those without a place to return will work for me’.

Naturally, we conducted confidentiality agreements and story alignment. Former adventurers will be assigned to non-adventurer roles. Joining the mercenary unit is permitted, so those who want to stay on the battlefield can go there.

The residents of the Central Island will receive no explanation. They will be told they survived miraculously.

Alta has explained everything to the elite elves.

It is their job to consider the future of the Kingdom of Pajel. However, I strictly ordered that it must not return to exactly the same state as before. Specifically, the corrupt noble system.

Finally, the familiar slot.

The Basilisk Disaster that was restrained together with Aria, Gired, and Aston remained idle, unmoving without orders.

Since it did not actively oppose us and merely followed orders, I fixed the negative effects of Gired’s modifications.

Then it got attached to someone. …Mio.

“Why!?”

She herself was surprised, but after fixing it, killing it now would be awkward, and releasing it would be dangerous, so Mio decided to tame it.

“Ah, it might work as a mount…”

Mio riding atop the lumbering basilisk. An odd sight.

Its dwelling will be assigned within the labyrinth. It is too dangerous to house at the mansion. Even if tamed, keeping a basilisk in the city would be problematic.

That should be everything…

I haven’t forgotten any subordinates, right?

A: No. There are none.

Then the matter of the Kingdom of Pajel is concluded. Let’s begin preparations to head to the Elven Village.

---

**AN:** Gired will die after 100 days.

He will not reappear. He will die quietly, without anyone seeing him off.

Aston’s end will also not be written.

Next time, I plan to post on 7/20 (final chapter of Volume 13).

Since I already know what to write, it should be fine. Probably. Hopefully. …If I miss the deadline, sorry.

## **200: Reunion and Summoning**

**AN:** This is the final chapter of Volume 13. A nice, round number for the main story at Chapter 200 makes me grin.

---

“Oh, you were pretty quick.”

The one who greeted us with those words was the Emperor of the Scarlet Empire, Scarlet Crimson himself.

This was the audience chamber in the Imperial castle of Guren, the Imperial capital of the Scarlet Empire.

As promised, we found the final Hero within one month and returned to the Scarlet Empire.

After enslaving Asuka, the Oni Hero, I had contacted Scarlet through the Advance Trading Company to let him know we would be heading his way ‘within a few days’, so we were able to meet smoothly.

“To think you’d really find them before a month was even up. So, where is that \<Hero>?”

“I didn’t bring her here. I’ll ‘call’ her later, so don’t worry.”

Present here were just the six of us: me, Sakura, Dora, Maria, Mio, and Sera (plus Tamo-san).

We did not bring Asuka, nor Rouge and the others.

We brought the dragonkin to the Imperial capital, but did not bring them into the castle.

On the Scarlet Empire’s side were Scarlet, Ash, and Kuroa, with not a single guard present.

I get that there are things they can’t discuss openly, but is that really okay for the emperor of a major power…?

“…Ah, one of the ‘things Jin can do’, huh. So are we heading out right away? Or should we take a break and let me entertain you?”

As always, he’s quick on the uptake.

He doesn’t ask unnecessary questions, which makes him very easy to talk to.

“If you’re going to entertain us, it’d just be a hassle, so if we can go, let’s go now. …More importantly, can an emperor really just head out so easily?”

“Yeah, no problem. I can leave things to Carmine, my successor.”

There was clear trust visible on his face.

It seems the First Princess is steadily walking the path toward becoming the next emperor.

Scarlet quickly left things to Carmine and his aides and prepared for departure.

All of that took just ten minutes. He really is a light-footed emperor.

We departed the Imperial capital of Guren on the dragonkin and headed for the Elf Village.

The Elf Village is an elven settlement centered around the World Tree, located to the northeast of the Scarlet Empire.

Within the empire, it is called an ‘Unexplored Region’, and ordinary people cannot enter due to the Forest of Bewilderment.

To enter, one needs a guide from the Elf Village.

I once again set foot in this land that could be called one of fantasy’s archetypal locations.

Incidentally, all the dragonkin except Kuroa were sent back for the time being. Thanks for the hard work.

As before, our guide through the Forest of Bewilderment was Ash, a half-elf from the Elf Village. The fact that I could reach the village without a guide is a secret.

“This time, we’ve had the World Tree’s Guardians suspend their defenses in advance.”

After receiving our contact, Ash went to report to the Elf Village, and had the World Tree’s Guardians, the village’s defense mechanism, set so they wouldn’t attack us.

I’m basically flagged as a dangerous individual to the World Tree.

“Yeah, it’d be a complete waste of resources.”

Creating the World Tree’s Guardians requires quite a lot of resources.

Making them just to be killed by me would be completely pointless.

“Yes. The chief hesitated a bit, but he didn’t oppose it because he didn’t want to be scolded by Lady Lily.”

The chief, who has a prior offense of ordering massive amounts of mannequins, seems to be behaving himself this time.

It’s not that I dislike him, but he is a troublesome opponent, so if I don’t have to deal with him, all the better.

We passed through the forest and arrived at the Elf Village.

“Welcome.”

This ethereal loli-granny is Lily, the storyteller of the Elf Village, protector of the World Tree, and also one of the first ‘Princess Shrine Maidenes’. Way too many attributes.

“Hey! You look well as ever, Granny Lily.”

“Indeed. The increase in resources seems to be having a positive effect on me as well.”

As Scarlet said, Lily’s complexion looks better than before.

Just like labyrinths, maintaining the World Tree requires resources. The current World Tree has a considerable surplus.

The reason is that we have three split Tamo-sans living in the Elf Village (with official approval).

Just that alone apparently provides more resources than the past several thousand years combined.

“I heard everything from Ash, lad. To think you really found them in such a short time…”

Scarlet already said something similar.

“I’m a man who keeps his promises.”

“Calling it a promise is a stretch. Jin just declared it himself.”

Yes. No one demanded a month from me. I just said it myself.

A promise to myself… determination, maybe? Though luck played way too big a role…

“So then, where is this \<Hero> in question?”

Lily looks around.

The people here are the same as before. A high elf with a good memory wouldn’t forget.

“I’m calling her now. ‘Summon.’”

I activated magic and summoned Asuka, who had been waiting at the mansion.

“So this is Jin’s summoning. Damn impressive…”

“W-What is this!?”

A girl appeared from thin air, and Lily was thoroughly shocked.

I had told Scarlet a bit about it, but not the elves.

“Sorry to keep you waiting.”

“Don’t worry. It’s work.”

It’s only been a short time, but I can tell Asuka is very serious and has a strong sense of responsibility.

Strong enough to blame herself for the destruction of the drifting island settlement and seek strength for revenge. I’m not saying it’s a good example.

If it’s something I formally ask of her, she’ll carry it out without complaint even if it’s not an order as a slave.

…If anything, she seems far too accustomed to ‘endurance’ and ‘self-sacrifice,’ which makes me a little worried about her future.

“Judging by the horns, is she an oni?”

“Yeah. Oni Hero, Asuka.”

“Asuka. Nice to meet you.”

She bows politely (currently studying common sense).

“Hey, nice to meet you!”

“Once again, Jin-dono’s power… From the looks of it, Lett-boy had already heard about this…”

“First time seeing it in person, though.”

Though surprised, Lily quickly understood.

“Haa… So with this power, you’ll be calling the remaining hundred as well?”

She lets out an exasperated sigh and continues.

“Yeah. I plan to finish it today.”

What the World Tree needs to grow are two things: a massive amount of ‘resources,’ and the incorporation of ‘abnormal individual’ factors that deviate from the goddess’s will.

To secure the resources, we placed Tamo-san, and to gather abnormal individual factors, we went to the Kingdom of Pajel.

The conditions for abnormal individuals were quite specific.

At least ten types of factors, at least one hundred people, and five \<Heroes>.

We will finish this incorporation today.

Ten minutes later, now in front of the World Tree.

“At my age, I never thought I’d be surprised this many times…”

“Seriously, I’m glad we made Jin our ally…”

Lily and Scarlet look at the line of people in front of the World Tree as they speak.

Lined up are about one hundred abnormal individuals under my command.

According to Lily, the ten types are divided into ‘Skills,’ ‘Race,’ and ‘Background.’

For ‘Skills,’ \<Hero> and \<Proof of the Hero> were already registered, so we brought Mimi the dwarf with \<Holy Magic Smithing> and a boy from the labyrinth orphanage (age four) with \<Branch of the System Tree>. The boy is about to turn five (when \<Branch of the System Tree> changes), so it was pretty close.

For ‘Race,’ Dragonkin were already registered, so we summoned the mermaid Leila and the angel Anju.

For ‘Background,’ reincarnators, otherworldly transmigrators besides Heroes, and labyrinth-related individuals were all already registered.

The condition of one hundred people was fulfilled by summoning a large number of Dragonkin from the Dragonkin Sanctuary.

There was some minor trouble due to one of Kuroa’s acquaintances being there, but I didn’t really care.

For the five \<Heroes>, Beastkin and Elf are already registered, so we just need Human, Hobbit, and Oni.

Gathering them is no problem, but since factor incorporation is done one person at a time, they’re currently lined up waiting their turn.

At this pace, it’ll definitely be done today.

After waiting a while, when we reached the latter half, a report came in from Alta.

A: Master, analysis of the skill \<蘚＆[[#あ](#あ)> obtained from the World Tree is complete.

Previously, when otherworlders received unique skills through the World Tree’s function, only the skill I received was garbled.

I had asked Alta to analyze it, but it required extremely complex processing and took a long time.

That it finally finished just before growing the World Tree is rather perfect timing.

So, what kind of skill was it?

A: Yes. It is a skill called \<World Tree Dominion>. Simply put, it is the World Tree version of \<Labyrinth Dominion>.

…Excuse me?

A: It seems that rather than ‘giving Master a skill’, it would be more accurate to say the World Tree ‘delegated full authority to Master’.

So, I can now modify the World Tree’s settings? Like the labyrinth?

A: Yes. Along with the analysis, corrections have been completed, granting you abilities similar to a Labyrinth Ruler. A title, ‘Master of the World Tree’, has been added. The garbling occurred because it exceeded the World Tree’s original functions. The massive resource loss was for the same reason.

The title ‘Master of the World Tree’ really has been added…

Alta’s explanation makes many things click, but first I want to ask one thing.

“Why did it willingly offer itself?”

This is less like receiving a skill and more like it offering itself up.

Honestly, I can’t quite wrap my head around it.

A: When accessing the World Tree via \<World Tree Dominion>, I discovered something like its thought history. According to that, it was ‘begging for its life.’ Judging Master’s presence as overwhelmingly powerful and impossible to resist, the World Tree decided to place itself under your protection by delegating full authority.

The World Tree was thinking in such a human-like way…

And to think the day would come when the World Tree would beg me for its life. Even I didn’t see that coming.

“Master, did something happen?”

Hearing my muttering, Mio and the others approach.

“No, the analysis of the unique skill I got earlier finished, so I was hearing the report.”

“Oh, the one you got from the World Tree! What was it!?”

《Tell us!》

“Knowing Jin-kun, it must be an amazing skill, right…?”

“Well, amazing is one way to put it…”

I explain the situation.

“So Master conquered the Elf Village without us knowing.”

“Mio, don’t put it like that. I didn’t conquer it. I just took control of its lifeline.”

“Isn’t that conquest?”

“…”

What do I do? I can’t find anything to refute that.

“World Tree skills are supposed to match the person, right?”

“Yes, the one I got was a skill related to magic that suited me…”

“And Mio-chan’s can be used for cooking!”

As Sera says, the skills from the World Tree reflect the person’s nature.

From that perspective, my skill is…

“In that sense, I think it’s a perfect fit for you, Master. You have the temperament of a ruler. Most places you go end up under your control…”

Well, that’s probably it.

“To even command the World Tree… as expected of Jin-sama.”

《Master, amazing!》

Over-the-top praise from Maria, and praise from Dora who doesn’t really understand.

I wasn’t asking for praise, you know? It’s just a skill I received…

“Conquest or control aside, does having that skill actually give you any benefits, Master?”

“Any benefits?”

I passed Mio’s question straight to Alta.

A: In terms of pure benefits, you can use resources to create World Tree-made equipment.

“World Tree equipment! In most games, that’s endgame gear!”

Mio says excitedly.

Can it surpass our current equipment?

A: No. It does not surpass equipment that has overcome the final trial and reached mythic class.

“That’s a shame…”

Mio looks disappointed.

A: Also, by using resources, you can create World Tree fruits.

“Food!”

《Food!》

“Another Mio-chan case!”

Mio’s emotions are all over the place.

Like the labyrinth, the World Tree uses resources for everything.

A: Additionally, by using a large amount of resources, you can summon people from Master’s original world.

Alta drops a massive bomb.

Now then, let’s summarize what Alta told me.

By accessing the World Tree via \<World Tree Dominion>, Alta also obtained information known only to the World Tree. I’ll ask for details later, but summoning takes priority now.

The World Tree has multiple functions related to ‘worlds’, and ‘summoning otherworlders’ is one of them.

As Lily said before, returning to the original world is difficult, but coming to this world is relatively easy.

As a supplement, only ‘people’ can be summoned. Animals or objects cannot.

This summoning differs from Hero Summoning in that no \<Blessing> is granted. It also prevents the rejection reaction of otherworldly transfer that afflicted Higashi.

The targets are limited to those connected to otherworlders. The connection serves as a marker.

So for me, that includes myself, Sakura, Mio, the dinosaur girl (a reincarnator), the Naruse mother and daughter, and the former Hero believers. Quite a lot.

Outside my subordinates, Scarlet and Sharon are also reincarnators.

Though it probably wouldn’t be meaningful to use it on Tiramisu or Scarlet, whose memories are unclear…

There are two types of summoning: ‘Forced Summoning’ and ‘Voluntary Summoning.’

‘Forced Summoning’ forcibly summons the target from another world, disregarding their will or circumstances.

‘Voluntary Summoning’ prioritizes the target’s will and will not summon those who do not wish to transfer.

‘Forced Summoning’ consumes far more resources. Consent reduces the burden.

‘Forced Summoning’ is no different from the abduction we experienced.

To make an abduction victim perform abductions themselves… I question the World Tree’s sanity.

Whether the World Tree has sanity is another matter.

‘Voluntary Summoning’ also has problems.

When summoning, the target’s intent is confirmed, but there is no option to ‘hold’. They must decide on the spot whether to accept the transfer. Normally, they’d refuse.

You’d at least want time to prepare, right? You can’t.

Even if refused, resources are still consumed. Since only a refusal result returns, you wouldn’t want to try again with the same person.

…Given all that, this function is effectively useless.

There are also ethical issues.

I don’t mean to speak ill of reincarnation, but pre- and post-reincarnation are different people. Even with ‘Voluntary Summoning’, is it right for the reincarnated person to summon their former self?

It’s even worse for someone who was unwillingly transferred to ‘Forced Summon’ people from their original world. That just increases the number of victims. It solves nothing.

“So, shelving it.”

“Wait a second!”

Just as I concluded that despite its power, it was too impractical, Mio interrupted.

“What is it? I absolutely won’t allow ‘Forced Summoning’.”

Even if Mio has someone she really wants to call, I won’t let her use ‘Forced Summoning’.

I’m basically against ‘Voluntary Summoning’ too, but depending on the reason, I might consider it. Like wanting to summon parents left behind after your death…

“I wouldn’t say that! I just want you to use ‘Voluntary Summoning’, Master!”

“Me? Who do you want me to summon?”

I don’t have anyone I actively want to call. If anything, I wanted to summon Higashi and Asai.

“Isn’t it obvious? Your little sister!”

“Oh, Jin-kun’s sister…!”

“Rin, was it? The one who hasn’t outgrown her brother…”

Sakura and Sera nod in understanding.

“Since I’m going back eventually, is there any need to call her here?”

“There is! You tell us sister stories sometimes, and she definitely hasn’t outgrown you! If you call her, she’ll definitely come! Rather, you should call her!”

We occasionally talk about our original world, and my sister comes up.

Each time, Mio and the others label her a brocon.

“I think you should call her too…”

“I agree.”

《Me too?》

Dora doesn’t seem to understand, but is going along with Sakura and the others.

A majority in favor. I can’t ignore that (though I could if I wanted).

Since it seemed like things could escalate, I decided to consult Scarlet and the others.

(Long story).

“I leave things alone for a bit and it turns into this…!”

“The World Tree desired to be ruled itself…”

Just explaining \<World Tree Dominion> shocked both Scarlet and Lily.

We haven’t even reached the summoning part yet…

(Shortened).

“Do you have enough resources to go to the ‘Goddess’s Domain’? That priority can’t change.”

“That shouldn’t be a problem. It’s being replenished even now.”

“If Jin-dono, who knows more about the World Tree than I do, says so, then it must be true…”

The ‘Master of the World Tree’ is a completely superior existence to the ‘Protectors of the World Tree’ like Lily.

After discussion with Lily, we decided not to make this public, and to continue operating the World Tree and Elf Village as before. We’ll just secretly use various functions.

By the time we finished talking, the abnormal factor incorporation was complete.

Now all that’s left is to grow the World Tree, and we’ll be able to go to the ‘Goddess’s Domain.’

Of course, I have preparations to make, and Scarlet’s abdication is also pending, so it’s not immediate, but at least the means of travel are ready.

Since that was today’s original plan, we had the nearly hundred subordinates head back first.

“I want to see the summoning too…”

“Scarlet, your presence is unnecessarily intimidating, so no. Go back and do your job.”

“Jin is so cold…”

Since summoning family isn’t something I want to show others, we sent Scarlet and the others home.

Lily said, “I’m tired in many ways, so I’ll sleep…” and went back.

I do feel like we put too much mental strain on an elderly person, but is it really okay for a ‘Protector of the World Tree’ not to watch over its use?

Well, time is of the essence, so let’s start ‘Voluntary Summoning’.

The procedure is simple: touch the World Tree, imagine the person to summon, and declare ‘Voluntary Summoning’.

If there are enough resources, resources decrease and the summoning check begins. If the target accepts, they are summoned. If not, it ends there.

“Alright, here goes. If this fails, I won’t do it again.”

“That’s fine. She’ll definitely come…”

Mio seems very confident.

“‘Voluntary Summoning.’”

When I touched the World Tree and declared it, it ‘glowed’ brightly.

And soon, a girl appeared beside me…

“Onii-chan!”

The summoned girl, Shindo Rin, clung to me.

“Rin, you really came…”

Honestly, I didn’t think she would.

Even if I plan to return someday, she doesn’t know that. From her perspective, she abandoned everything in her original world to come here.

“Of course! If I hear my Onii-chan is in another world, there’s no way I wouldn’t follow!”

“Is that really ‘of course’…?”

Let me clarify what happened to Rin.

According to Alta, Rin received a message starting with, ‘A request for transfer to another world has been received from Shindo Jin’.

After hearing the summoner and conditions, the target chooses whether to accept.

And based solely on the fact that ‘I was in another world’, Rin chose to transfer.

I’ll be blunt. I’m just her ‘brother’.

Normally, that’s not enough reason to abandon everything…

“My only family! My Onii-chan is the most important thing in the world to me!”

That’s quite a bold confession of affection…

It seems Mio was right. She hasn’t outgrown her brother.

The fact that she reverted from ‘Nii-san’ to ‘Onii-chan’ makes it obvious.

“I see. If you won’t regret it, then that’s fine by me.”

“I won’t regret it!”

“Alright. …Welcome, Rin.”

“Yes!”

Once Rin calmed down, I began explaining the situation.

“So Onii-chan, you were transferred to another world with everyone who was at school after classes.”

“…By the way, is that how you want to address me?”

“Ah! Ahem, Nii-san.”

I don’t really mind ‘Onii-chan,’ but…

“…Judging by how you are, time probably flows differently too.”

“Still sharp as ever.”

I hadn’t explained that yet, but she realized it naturally.

“That’s nothing. …But now it makes sense. No wonder I was suddenly overwhelmed by anxiety after school. I must have sensed you disappearing.”

My sister apparently sensed my otherworldly summoning.

After that, I introduced everyone present.

One reason we sent Scarlet and others away was to keep numbers down for explanations. We didn’t expect Rin to come, but just in case.

“I’m Shindo Rin. Thank you all for taking care of my brother.”

She bowed her head.

“No… we’re the ones who owe him…”

“Yeah, we’d all be dead without Master!”

“We are grateful to Jin-sama.”

“I feel the same.”

《Me too!》

Rin still can’t hear Dora’s voice.

We’ve explained that she’s a child who can’t speak.

“Slavery… does give me pause, but since it’s this world’s culture, I won’t deny it. And it was probably necessary for my brother to quickly gain allies.”

Aside from her brother complex, Rin has normal sensibilities. Slavery was just ‘a bit much’ for her…

We further explained this world and the events so far.

We also explained about where we are.

“I imagined some things since it’s another world, but it’s truly like a story or game. Brother, haven’t you been enjoying yourself?”

“No comment.”

“Master’s hobby is sightseeing, right?”

“Mio, shut up!”

“Eek!?”

We glossed over my Special Powers.

Depending on how Rin lives in this world, I plan to limit what I tell her.

Some things are better left unknown.

“By becoming your subordinate, I can establish a connection with you… Brother! Please let me join your subordinates!”

What do you think I should do when my sister asks to become my subordinate?

“Huh? Isn’t that exactly what we expected?”

“I also thought it would probably come to this…”

Seriously…?

“Please, Brother!”

Since Rin wouldn’t back down, I reluctantly decided to make her my subordinate.

“~~~♪”

Why are you so happy about becoming a subordinate, little sister?

Since she became a subordinate, I explained my Special Powers in more detail.

“How many subordinates do you have now, Brother? I’d like to greet them…”

What a diligent sister.

“I think it’s over twenty thousand.”

That’s the number of subordinates who know about my abilities.

Subordinates of subordinates sometimes know nothing.

“…That’s not a joke, is it?”

Rin’s expression stiffened.

“This will be quite a lot of greeting.”

Wait, are you seriously planning to greet all of them?

“Hehe. Still, Brother is Brother wherever he goes.”

She smiled.

“People naturally gather around you. It’s reassuring to see that hasn’t changed across worlds. …By the way, since it was a school-wide summoning, are your followers here too?”

She suddenly brings it up.

“Huh? Rin knew I had followers?”

“Of course I knew. It’s strange that you didn’t notice. Brother, you’re sensitive to hostility and malice, but far too dull to goodwill.”

For some reason, Sakura, Mio, and Sera are nodding. Dora imitates them.

We also discussed future plans.

“You’re going to return to the original world once, right? Of course, I’ll go with you. But it’s sad to hear that Higashi-san and Yoshinobu-san passed away. It’s rare to find people who can stand on equal footing with you…”

Don’t make it sound like I have no friends. Well, having few ‘friends’ is true…

“That’s the rough overview. We’ll go back to my mansion and talk in detail over tea.”

It’s better to discuss details at the mansion than in the Elf Village.

“Understood. I still have many things I want to ask. I won’t let you sleep tonight.”

“No, I will sleep. We have time now, so no need to rush, right?”

“That’s true… Then I look forward to working with you from now on, Onii-chan!”

Rin said with a beaming smile.

The contents of \<蘚＆[[#あ](#あ)> were also decided in advance. The character count matches.

After the character introductions, it’s not Volume 14 but an interlude. It’ll be short stories in a somewhat time-skipping format, with conversations between side characters and Rin’s greetings (Jin and the others will appear too). The update frequency might recover a bit.

Name: Ashley

Gender: Female

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice

Notes: A Water “Princess Shrine Maiden” who was betrayed by her fiancé and fled to a deserted island, where she survived alone. She is the youngest (actual age) High Elf currently in existence. She named one of the split Tamo-san slimes “Chevalier” and made it her personal companion. As a result of this incident, she has completely lost interest in romance. What she feels toward Chevalier is nothing more than trust and friendship. Naturally, a slime is not a romantic interest.

Name: Unknown (Pregnant Woman)

Gender: Female

Race: Human

Title: Jin’s Slave

Notes: A human woman carrying the child of a Dwarf Hero. Due to falling into slavery and living in harsh conditions, she had become quite weakened, but her condition has improved after becoming Jin’s slave. She regards Jin as her benefactor and wants him to be the one to name her child. Don’t rush it.

Name: Aqua (Real Name: Aria)

Gender: Female

Race: Human (Avatar)

Title: Avatar of the Calamity Dragon

Notes: One of the avatars of the Water Calamity Dragon, Tidal Wave. She was created based on an ego that desires peace. The reason she worked as a pilot guide on Latis Island is because she views tourism as a symbol of peace. Since she has no lifespan, she periodically changes where she lives and her name. Her real name is Aria, but she is more commonly called Aqua.

Name: Earth

Gender: Male

Title: Jin’s Slave

Notes: One of the two men who risked their lives to head for the drifting island, the “man of the sea.” Without Jin, he would certainly have died. Jin wanted to show that he would also save men.

Gender: Male

Title: Jin’s Slave

Notes: One of the two men who risked their lives to head for the drifting island, the “intellectual with glasses.” One of the few named male slaves. Jin wanted to show that he would also enslave men.

Gender: Female

Age: 12

Race: Oni

Title: Oni Hero

Notes: The only girl in the settlement on the drifting island who escaped petrification. She was the local Hero, and the fact that she was on the verge of death weakened the \<Seal>, which worked in her favor. Because she lived alone for three years starting at age nine, she has no common sense or sense of shame. She is so well-developed that she does not look like a 12-year-old and appears to be in her late teens. Serious and strong-willed, she believes the collapse of the settlement is her fault, which fuels her desire for strength. Due to the nature of being a Hero, she learns quickly, so it is thought she will grow strong quickly under Jin.

Name: Annie

Gender: Female

Age: 14

Race: Beastman (Dog)

Title: Jin’s Slave

Notes: A girl who lived on the drifting island and had been petrified for three years. Short and cute, with silver semi-long hair, a nice butt but no breasts, nearsighted, and equipped with striped panties. Despite being a minor character, Jin listed her features one after another, making her character clearly defined. She lets out a nice sound when teased. Mio feels a one-sided sense of familiarity with her. It’s a secret that she was devastated after seeing Asuka’s before-and-after (chest).

Originally highly capable and relatively flexible in thinking among elves, she went on to play an active role in the political sphere of the Kingdom of Pajel.

Gender: Female

Race: Human

A born super brother complex who loves Jin more than anything. If Jin is there, she would not hesitate at all to go to another world. Because she was summoned using the World Tree’s function, she does possess a Skill by default. Her catchphrase is “normal”, and her self-evaluation is also “normal”, but objectively speaking, she is not “normal” at all.

Name: Unknown (Residents of the Central Island)

Notes: Residents of the collapsed central island who were judged to be without issue based on a comprehensive evaluation of karma values, hostility, and other factors. They were petrified, recovered, and became Jin’s slaves. The circumstances have been explained to the elves, but the other residents are unaware of the situation. They do not understand that they are slaves, and depending on the situation, may unconsciously follow Alta’s orders. Scary.

## **Interlude 1**

**AN:** As this is an interlude, there will be some trial and error. Also, the numbering of chapters will start from 1.

Multiple short stories are compiled into a single interlude, but if there are many opinions saying it is better to separate them, I plan to repost them separately.

Basically, I will post 2 to 3 short stories at a time. This time, the following three are included.

– A Girl Named Shindou Rin

– Shindou Rin’s Interactions – Bath Edition

– Riding Dragon Blue – Jin’s Room
