Title: A Girl Named Shindou Rin

POV: None

Time: After Volume 13

Shindou Rin is the one and only younger sister of Shindou Jin, and his only family.

“Is this big mansion Brother’s?”

Rin had come to the mansion owned by her older brother, Shindou Jin.

“It is a mansion I’m proud of, located in the country’s prime area. If you want, Rin, you can live here too.”

“After hearing Brother’s story, I would like to decide after considering what I should do.”

“Yeah, got it.”

For Rin, she avoids making easy decisions until she understands what conditions suit her best.

If she says something careless and it turns out to be disadvantageous, that would be a problem.

“I heard there were maids, but aren’t there too many? …Could it be that they are also under Brother’s command?”

After entering the mansion and being guided to the reception room, Rin asked as she looked at the lined-up maids.

“Yeah, that’s right. There are other bases too, so these are just some of them.”

“At this point, nothing Brother does surprises me, but when Brother acts freely, the scale of things just keeps getting bigger. I understand why you were called a disaster in the original world.”

“I’d rather you not understand that…”

As an aside, Jin has absorbed the embodiment of disasters in this world.

If Jin so wished, this world would truly be swallowed by disaster.

When they sat down, a maid placed tea and sweets on the table.

“Alright, preparations are done, so let’s talk in detail about various things.”

“Thank you in advance.”

And so, Jin began to explain in detail about this world and everything that had happened so far.

When explaining the principles of this world, the existence of Skills and Status cannot be left out.

Strictly speaking, these are not things generally recognized in this world.

However, for Jin and the others, they are extremely familiar and very important.

“So this is my Status?”

Saying that, Rin checked her own Status.

Name: Shindou Rin

Gender: Female

Age: 13

Race: Human

Skill: \<Otherworld Standard LV >

“If I try, I can also see the details of the Skill.”

“I don’t think I explained that function yet?”

“This is normal. You said it was close to a game, Brother.”

\<Otherworld Standard>

The amount of Skill proficiency gained for Skills obtainable in another world becomes 10 times higher. The applicable other world is limited to the world where the owner was born.

“I have no recollection of obtaining such a Skill.”

“It is a Skill automatically granted when you transfer to this world. Apparently, a Skill suited to the person is chosen.”

“A Skill suited to me… Does it suit me?”

Rin asked curiously.

“Isn’t it because ‘normal’ is your catchphrase?”

“Even so, it seems like a Skill that is far from normal…”

“Yeah, it’s extremely rare and extremely powerful. I only know one other Skill that affects Skill proficiency. More importantly, 10 times is insane…”

The Skill Jin was referring to was \<Transcendence>, but its increase value is 2 times.

Ten times is clearly an abnormal value.

“Then, I will give this Skill to Brother.”

“Huh?”

“You can move Skills, right? I don’t need a Skill that isn’t normal.”

Depending on how it is used, it could become an incredibly powerful weapon, but Rin said it without the slightest hesitation. Her fixation on being “normal” is strong.

As an aside, Skills obtained from the World Tree can generally be used by others as well.

The exception is \<World Tree Domination> held by Jin. This is because it does not function without the title “Master of the World Tree.”

“Are you serious?”

“Yes. It was a good example that something suited to a person and something a person wants are different.”

Has there ever been a Unique Skill (with no drawbacks) that was so unwanted by its owner?

“I appreciate the thought, but for ‘me,’ even if I had that Skill, it would have no meaning.”

“What do you mean?”

“Do you know, Rin? No matter what you multiply by zero, it’s still zero…”

Jin gives an explanation that doesn’t really explain anything.

“I’m sorry, Onii-san. I don’t understand what you mean.”

“I’ve got a constitution where I can’t gain skill proficiency. Even if you multiply 0 by 10, it’s still just 0, right?”

It would be rare to find a skill that is this incompatible with Jin.

However, it is extremely compatible with Jin’s Special Power.

“Even if I have it, it’s meaningless, so I want you to hold that skill, Rin. Though, it would help if you could share it with others. Sharing skills means…”

Jin explains about sharing skills through \<Bond of Contract>.

“I understand. If Onii-san says so, then I’ll hold it. Of course, sharing it is no problem.”

Rin easily overturns what she had just said before.

Rin is very particular about what she considers “normal.” However, her attachment to “Jin” is even stronger.

And so, \<Otherworld Standard> ended up being owned by Rin as it was.

By the time all the discussions were finished, quite a lot of time had passed.

“So, what do you want to do from here, Rin? Of course, you don’t need to decide right away. Calling you into this world was for my own convenience. I intend to grant your wishes as much as possible.”

After Jin says that, Rin thinks for a moment before speaking.

“As an absolute condition, I want an environment where I can meet Onii-san regularly.”

“That’s the first thing you say…”

“Of course. You’re my only family.”

The fact that her request related to Jin came out before anything else shows just how unwavering Rin’s brother complex is.

“Anything else?”

“Since I will no longer have the position of being a student, I would like to work. Could you arrange something for me? I have no connections in this world, so I think it would be difficult.”

“Now that I think about it, wouldn’t a brother who makes his little sister drop out of middle school and go work be the worst…?”

Jin realized something he probably shouldn’t have.

He hurriedly shook his head.

“No, no, I’ll support at least one little sister! I’ve got enough means for that!”

In reality, with Jin’s personal assets (excluding those related to the Advance Company), he could probably support more than twelve little sisters.

“If I’m not going to school, then working is normal. Besides, I don’t want to be a burden on you, Onii-san. Please let me work.”

“My little sister is way too much of a decent human being. Would it have been better to let her live in the original world…?”

Jin seriously wondered if losing someone as decent as Rin would be a huge loss for their original world.

“Please don’t say that! If I had been summoned just a few minutes later, I’m confident I would have gone insane!”

“My little sister is way too scary. Was Rin always this emotionally unstable?”

The Rin that Jin knew was a spoiled yet reliable girl.

Recently, the amount she clung to him had decreased, so he thought she had started to grow out of depending on her brother.

“As long as Onii-san is here, I’ll be fine. If you’re not, I’ll go crazy.”

Rin says that with full confidence.

It shows that her first request, ‘to be able to meet Jin’, was truly an absolute condition for her.

“…Whatever. So, do you have any preferences for where you want to work?”

Having learned a side of his little sister he didn’t know, Jin decided to pretend he hadn’t heard it and moved the conversation along.

“As much as possible, somewhere with little influence from you, Onii-san. I want to reduce being treated specially just because I’m your sister. Since you’re the one arranging it, I understand it’s impossible to eliminate that completely.”

Rin wanted to minimize preferential treatment resulting from Jin’s influence as much as possible.

This was a stance Rin had maintained since her original world.

“I see. …Then how about a job like this?”

“I’ll take it.”

Rin agreed without properly hearing the details.

Since it’s Jin >>>>> stance, it can’t be helped.

---

**Settings**

– About sharing through \<Bond of Contract>

\<Bond of Contract> has a function for sharing skills and the like. Simply put, if there is one skill, all targets of \<Bond of Contract> can use that same skill, but this effect is only enabled for certain skills. Even if a skill is shared, only one person can generally use it at a time, so relying on sharing carries risk in operation. Only skills prepared in advance for sharing, like Rin’s \<Otherworld Standard>, which everyone can use, are set to be shared. For the former, searching “semaphore” might help you understand.

Title: Rin Shindou’s Interactions – Bath Edition

POV: None

Time: After Volume 13

The girl named Rin Shindou could objectively be called a beautiful girl.

Glossy black hair that reached her waist, fair and finely textured skin, well-balanced facial features, slender limbs, and while her chest was large for her age of 13, it was not so much as to be overly assertive.

Overall, she gave off a neat and refined impression, and there was no doubt she would stand out if seen in town.

“Little sister-chan is really beautiful…”

“Her chest… 13 years old…”

Mio muttered as she took a good, long look at Rin’s figure.

Also, Sakura (not nonexistent) muttered while looking at Rin.

Currently, excluding Jin, the party members and Rin had come to the bath in the mansion.

It was a slightly old-fashioned method proposed by Mio, to deepen bonds through naked interaction.

“Please don’t look at me too much. It’s honestly embarrassing…”

Rin, wrapped in a bath towel with her cheeks flushed, exuded an allure that made Mio swallow hard.

“This is the allure of a 13-year-old… It’s a different kind of charm compared to Sera-chan’s overwhelming allure.”

“Could you not bring me into this there?”

Sera was also around the same age, but physically more mature than Rin.

Her chest was also larger than Rin’s, but she lacked what could be called a Yamato Nadeshiko-style allure. If anything, she was overflowing with a more open kind of allure.

“Little sister-chan. Being this beautiful, you must have been really popular in your original world, right?”

Mio spoke to Rin casually.

This was because Rin had strongly requested that they not be overly formal with her.

That said, in Mio’s case, there was a high chance she would have interacted the same way even without being told.

“That wasn’t the case at all. I’ve never even been confessed to.”

“Boys have no eye for quality.”

“Is there some reason for that…?”

Since they shared the common ground of the original world, Rin, Mio, and Sakura found it easy to keep the conversation going.

“It seems to be my brother’s influence.”

“Ah…”

“That makes sense…”

The influence Jin himself was unaware of was surprisingly large.

While chatting like that, the six of them soaked in the bath.

“Still, little sister-chan really was a brocon.”

“I had expected it, but…”

“It was more than I thought.”

Based on what they had heard from Jin, Mio, Sakura, and Sera had seen through the fact that Rin was a severe brocon.

That was also why they had agreed to Rin’s summoning.

“Mio-san, you heard about me from my brother, right? May I ask how he described me?”

Rin’s eyes were extremely serious.

“What I heard from Master was mostly that his little sister had stopped being clingy lately. But here and there in his stories, I could see elements of a severe brocon.”

“Yes, the impression was that you were only pretending to have moved on from your brother.”

“But Jin-kun didn’t notice at all…”

It was a harsh evaluation, but Rin herself had been desperately trying to hide it.

“That he never noticed is a blessing in disguise…”

“But because he didn’t notice, he apparently thought there was no need to worry about the original world either.”

“Even the summoning by the World Tree wouldn’t have even come up as a candidate if Mio-san hadn’t said anything.”

Rin’s cheek twitched slightly.

“Is that so?”

“Yes… He said there was no need to call you when he’d be returning eventually…”

“Should I be glad for my brother’s obliviousness? Or lament it?”

Rin’s feelings on the matter were extremely complicated.

“Thanks to all of you, I was able to come to my brother’s side. Thank you very much.”

Saying that, Rin bowed her head.

After soaking in the bath for a while, the six of them got out of the tub to wash their bodies.

“Rin-sama, I will wash your back.”

“You don’t need to add ‘-sama,’ Maria-san.”

“That would not be appropriate. My apologies, Rin-sama, but being Jin-sama’s blood relative alone makes you a special existence.”

Rin asked her not to be so formal, but Maria could not accept that.

At this point, Rin did not know it yet, but many of the maids would tell her the same thing.

“I suppose it can’t be helped. In that case, please wash my back. After that, I will wash yours.”

“N-no! I’m quite fine…!”

“That won’t do. If we’re deepening our friendship, it’s not right for only one side to be washed.”

Maria offering to wash her back was the result of her own consideration.

Faced with such sound reasoning, Maria could not refuse.

“…Understood. Then, please.”

“Oh? Are we washing each other’s backs? Since we have the chance, why don’t we all line up and do it?”

“That sounds nice. I feel like it would deepen our bonds.”

With Rin agreeing to Mio’s slightly old-fashioned idea, they decided to line up and wash each other’s backs.

《Ei!》

“Wha!? Dora-chan, why are you bringing out your wings!?”

Just as they lined up in order of height, Dora brought out her wings and entered angel mode.

Mio, who was behind her, was bewildered.

《Wash them?》

Dora cannot wash her wings by herself.

She usually takes care of it with ‘Purification’ and when she bathes together with Jin, he washes them for her.

Since they were washing each other’s backs, it seemed she wanted the others to wash them too.

“Isn’t the difficulty level different for just one person here?”

There was no doubt it would take more effort than simply washing someone’s back.

“Such beautiful wings. You really do look like an angel.”

Rin, seeing Dora in angel mode for the first time, was captivated and moved closer.

“Of course, they’re Master’s favorite.”

“May I touch them too?”

《Sure-》

With Dora’s permission, Rin touches the wings. She strokes them.

“Even when they’re wet, they feel nice to the touch.”

《That’s the same way Master touches them-!》

“Is that so? That makes me happy. Next time, may I touch them when they’re not wet?”

《Of course, you can-！》

Dora likes having her wings stroked by those she likes.

Rin, who is Jin’s family and carries a scent similar to his, was included among those Dora liked.

The six of them washed each other’s backs, chatted idly, and soaked in the bath at leisure. It would be fair to say that they were able to deepen their bonds sufficiently, just as they had intended.

Rin is an extreme case of brother-complex and puts Jin first above all else, but when it comes to things unrelated to Jin, she has a fairly normal sensibility.

Moreover, she was originally quite sociable, does not find it difficult to talk with others, and if anything, she welcomes it when they are people who get along well with Jin.

“So then, little sister, how are you going to interact with Master from here on out?”

Just as they were about to get out of the bath, Mio asked her final question.

“What do you mean by how?”

“I mean whether you’ll keep pretending to distance yourself, or go back to being all over him.”

For now, she is pretending to have grown independent from her brother, but Jin has also heard about it and has begun to suspect the truth.

Since she hasn’t actually managed to grow independent, it’s only a matter of time before he’s found out. If that’s the case, Mio suggests that it might be better to just go back to being attached to him.

“For now, I think I’ll continue like this. It’s lonely, but if this is what people call the proper distance between siblings, then I have no choice but to try my best.”

“I won’t stop you if you insist, but Master probably doesn’t want you to force yourself either, you know? If it really becomes too hard, you should tell him properly.”

“Hijiri… you say the same kind of things as my best friend. Understood. So that I don’t make my brother worry, I’ll consult him when I get close to my limit.”

“Little sister, you’re a die-hard little sister…”

Mio doesn’t know this, but Rin’s best friend Hijiri had also described Rin as a ‘die-hard little sister’.

“That’s right. I will always be my brother’s little sister.”

And Rin never once denies that assessment.

Title: Riding Dragon Blue – Jin’s Room

Viewpoint: Blue

Time: Volume 12

“I’m back-“

“Welcome back, nano-“

“We have been waiting, no ja”

When I opened the door to Master’s room, Aya, who had been reading a book, and the Progenitor Divine Dragon El welcomed me.

At present, the three of us, including myself, are staying in Master’s room in the Castal Kingdom.

It’s not that we can’t get our own rooms, nor that we never go outside, but the three of us spend most of our time in Master’s room. Because of that, our interactions have naturally deepened.

The reason I stay in Master’s room is so that I can respond immediately whenever Master calls for me.

Even when I go out, I limit myself to facilities related to Master.

Master has told me that I don’t need to go that far, but it’s not that I’m forcing myself.

If, by some chance, I failed to respond when he called, I feel like I wouldn’t be able to forgive myself.

“Where did he go this time?”

“He said a place called the Pajel Kingdom, a country with a beautiful sea. Apparently, he is searching for someone with the \<Hero> Gift.”

“Using a map would make it instant.”

“Apparently, he is going to search without using a map.”

“As usual, I have no idea what that person is thinking…”

Understanding what our capricious Master is thinking is difficult.

Not that I am in any position to say that, considering I owe my life to that very capriciousness…

“Now that you mention it, El is staying behind this time too?”

“Mm, I was not called this time.”

El says it without seeming particularly bothered.

At the beginning, El and I competed to be of use to Master, but as we spent more time with him, we realized that such efforts were meaningless.

Master can basically do most things alone (except cooking). There is practically no situation where a familiar would be necessary. He can even fly without a riding dragon.

The reason he made El his familiar and me his riding dragon was not out of necessity, but simply because ‘it seemed more fun’.

In other words, being ‘relied upon’ by Master is extremely difficult.

Even if it is not necessary, Master likes riding on me. Of course, I am happy and enjoy being ridden as well.

That is precisely why I want to maintain a state where I can give it my all whenever I am needed.

To add one thing, El’s situation is a little different.

Because El is a being created by Master, she could disappear with a single thought from Master.

If she were deemed unnecessary, the likelihood of being erased would increase, so she had been desperately trying to be useful.

Fortunately, some time ago, Master clearly stated that she had no intention of erasing El, so she was able to settle into the same stance as me, only giving her all when asked by Master.

“More importantly, let us continue from earlier.”

“Alright. After traveling through the sky with Master, do you really think you can beat me while I am in such good form?”

“The world of competition is not so kind that you can win on mentality alone!”

We resumed the card game that had been interrupted when Master called us.

Today’s game is ‘Daifugo’, whose basic rules Master taught us.

In Master’s world, this game was apparently famous for having an enormous number of variant rules.

After hearing that, we asked people from the other world about the rules, and there were more than ten variations, with multiple combinations… or rather, everyone was playing with a different combination.

In his original world, Master used the abundance of variant rules to his advantage, playing in a style where ‘every few games, the variant rules would be switched’ (commonly called “Master Rules”).

The variant rules are listed on paper, and a coin toss determines whether each rule is active or inactive, so it is necessary to adjust your strategy depending on the rules in play.

If contradictory rules are active at the same time, both become invalid.

‘Master Rules’ were extremely useful for us, who often play cards in the room, as they helped prevent boredom, so we gratefully adopted them.

“I go out with a 3 after an ‘8 cut’.”

“Ku… you had been saving that 8 until this moment…”

“That is what happens when you get careless and play your low cards first!”

I became the ‘Daifugo’.

“Gh… pass…”

“Oh my, you cannot play a pair at all? This is my chance.”

“In that case, I will ‘lock’ that pair play.”

“Wha!? Wait!”

I became the ‘Daifumin’” I was supposed to be a ‘Commoner’, but at times like this, the ‘Downfall’ rule is in effect.

“Q.”

“Pass.”

“Pass.”

“At last, at last I’ve become a parent. Now eat this! A 6 Revolution!”

“What did you say!?”

“Ah, a 4 Counter-Revolution.”

“Why!?”

I’m still stuck as the ‘Greater Pauper’. Once you fall, it’s a rule that makes it hard to climb back up.

I was aiming solely for a Revolution…

And then the rules switch.

“A Staircase from 8 to Q.”

“It gets cleared automatically…”

“On top of that, with a Joker included, a 5 to 7 Staircase plus a two-card play!”

“Isn’t that way too skewed?”

“I’m just glad ‘Downfall’ is gone…”

If the rules hadn’t switched, Aya would have become the ‘Greater Pauper’ at this point…

Well, I beat Aya after that anyway, so she ends up as the ‘Greater Pauper’ regardless.

-Knock knock-

At that moment, there was a knock on the door.

“Come in.”

It’s not my room, but I have Master’s permission, so it’s fine.

“Excuse us.”

“Hey there~♪”

The ones who came in saying that were Megumi and Tiramisu, our fellow gaming companions.

Both of them are reincarnators, and since they’re from the same world as Master, they readily agreed when I invited them to play. That said, they both have work during the day, so they can only join in the evenings.

“You’ve come.”

“Welcome.”

These two came today, but there are actually quite a few others in our gaming group.

In particular, it’s fair to say that almost everyone from Master’s world participates. The only exceptions are the former Heroes who don’t come near the mansion.

“Playing Daifugo again today?”

“Yes, we are.”

“Nice-♪, five people is perfect☆”

Since they both have experience with these ‘Master Rules’, they checked the current rules and immediately joined the game. Anyone joining mid-game always starts as a Commoner.

“It’s a locked Eleven Back. Considering the discard pile, you can’t play anything except the Joker, right?”

“Then Tira-chan will play the Joker☆”

“So it was Tiramisu who had the Joker. Since the card I got from Aya was a King, I knew one of the Commoners had it…”

“You can’t say that!”

“I was wondering what was going on with all the passes…”

As expected, Aya continued her run as the ‘Greater Pauper’.

After three rounds, the rules switched again.

Since the number of players increased, we decided to add more types of local rules from here on.

According to Master, they’re ‘even more obscure rules’.

“Fufufu, it’s a ‘Grand Revolution’ with the Joker included.”

“Wha… what did you say…?”

“This time there’s a ‘Downfall’. El drops here.”

“I’m a ‘Peasant,’ so I’d at least like to move up to ‘Commoner’…”

“Not happening☆”

I became the ‘Grand Millionaire’. As expected, getting two cards is huge.

After several rounds of maintaining my position as the ”Grand Millionaire’, the room door opened.

The one who entered was the owner of this room, my master.

“I’m back. Oh, you’re the ‘Grand Millionaire’ today. …Maybe I’ll join in for once.”

“!?” x5

At master’s words, all five of us held our breath.

I have no intention of speaking badly of master. None at all, but if master joins, it stops being a game. The difference in strength is just too large.

At the very least, it’s certain that a ‘Downfall’ will occur next match. ‘Grand Pauper’ huh…

“Ah, there are exactly five people. In that case, it would be uneven, so I’ll pass.”

“Phew…” x5

The optimal maximum number of players for ‘Daifugo’ is five.

Master doesn’t like exceeding the proper number of players or forcing someone out to join, so he lost interest in the game right there.

I love master, but losing a game is frustrating in its own way.

Even with five allies, the chances of winning are far too slim (as a premise, when facing master, it’s many versus one).

“Master, are you sleeping here tonight?”

“No, today was the day I give Aya… bodily fluids, right? I just came back once.”

“Jin, I love you!”

Aya jumped onto master.

For Aya, master’s bodily fluids are like food.

Usually she’s limited to indirect intake, but periodically she’s allowed to lick it directly.

Of course, we’re talking about sweat.

Aya stripped off her clothes until she was down to just her underwear, and licked master’s sweat.

The next moment, Aya’s body matured.

“Fufufufu, now that it’s come to this, I won’t lose anymore.”

Only when taking it directly can Aya temporarily assume an adult form.

In this state, Aya’s abilities improve. Naturally, her thinking ability as well…

“I’m heading back, but don’t stay up playing too late.”

“Okaaay! (♪)” x5

Since master said that, we’ll probably end after about three more rounds.

I’ll finish this as the ‘Grand Millionaire’!

---

**Characters**

Name: Blue

Gender: Female

Age: 16 (at first appearance)

Race: Dragonkin (Sky Dragon)

Title: Jin’s Familiar

Notes: She was originally a candidate for clan leader in the “Dragonkin Sanctuary,” but after it was discovered that she had secretly exiled Dora, she was about to be executed when Jin saved her. She was tamed by Jin and became his riding dragon, and at that point abandoned the name Tenri. Once she swore loyalty, she became obedient (a tsundere in the original sense), and what she loves most is flying with Jin on her back. Her rivals are draft horses and the wings of the undead.

Name: El

Gender: Female

Age: None (equivalent to 0 as a pseudo-personality)

Race: None

Notes: A pseudo-personality created by Jin’s unique ability. The basis of her personality is the Progenitor Divine Dragon, the final trial that Jin defeated. She is treated as Jin’s “familiar,” but has only performed familiar-like duties a handful of times. This is because anything a familiar can do, Jin can also do, which is a fatal flaw. When danger levels are high, she may be brought along as a precaution. Basically, she does not do work outside of being a familiar.

Name: Aya

Gender: Female

Age: 0 (at first appearance)

Race: Ashen (Otherworlder)

Title: Transferred Individual

Notes: A member of the race called Ashen, whom Jin brought back from the “Gray World.” She is also a composite of 1,024 Ashen individuals. Her true identity is the surviving remnants of humanity from the “Gray World.” In order to adapt to their collapsing world, they lost intelligence and knowledge to conserve energy. By taking in the energy contained in Jin’s bodily fluids, they regain their intelligence. Each of the 1,024 individuals has their own specialty, so they help with various tasks at Jin’s mansion.

Name: Tiramisu

Gender: Female

Age: 0 (at first appearance)

Race: Tyrannosaurus (Reincarnator)

Title: Jin’s Familiar

Notes: A monster and reincarnator born from a “Dinosaur Egg” that appeared as an area annihilation bonus. She only vaguely remembers her memories from Japan. In addition to her Japanese past life, she also seems to possess some memories of the Tyrannosaurus that Jin defeated in a single blow, and out of fear, she flatters Jin with all her might. Currently, she works mainly in the Atto Confederation as a mercenary specializing in anti-monster combat.

Name: Naruse Megumi

Gender: Female

Age: 0 (before using “Rebirth,” she was 14)

Race: Human (Reincarnated Body)

Title: Jin’s Slave

Notes: A Japanese girl who was reincarnated into another world as a demon. Her name as a demon was Crownliese. She had lost her memories at the time of reincarnation, but regained them through shock therapy and became one of Jin’s subordinates. Through her unique magic “Rebirth,” she was reborn as a human, so her age is counted as 0. She currently works as a shop clerk at the Castar main branch of the Advance Trading Company.

## **Interlude 2**

**AN:** This time, there are two pieces. Basically, it will be about two per post.

– Shindo Rin’s Interactions: Younger Sister Arc

– Head Maid Lucea: Executive Meeting

---

Title: Shindo Rin’s Interactions: Younger Sister Arc

Point of View: Author

Timing: After Volume 13

That day, Sakuya, the Queen of the Kingdom of castal, was fighting the greatest tension she had ever felt.

For Sakuya, who as Queen had spoken with all manner of people, this was her first experience of being so nervous simply about ‘meeting someone’.

Put into words, it was nothing serious. ‘Meeting Jin’s younger sister’, that was all.

“To think the day would come when I would face the real younger sister… ugh…”

For Sakuya, who had been appealing herself to Jin in the role of ‘little sister’, the existence of Jin’s real younger sister (strictly speaking, his cousin) was dangerous in more ways than one.

To be honest, her little-sister appeal was meant to increase intimacy, and beyond that she was aiming for a deeper relationship. However, it would be hard to say things were going well.

If she were to lose even the little-sister position on top of that, Sakuya would have no cards left to play.

Because of this, she had decided not to show her face at Jin’s mansion until she settled on a stance toward Jin’s sister, Shindo Rin.

However, before she could decide on that stance, the person in question, Rin herself, sent a request for a meeting.

Cornered, Sakuya could not refuse, and while holding her head in her hands, waited for Rin’s visit.

_-Knock knock_–

“Your Majesty Sakuya, Lady Rin has arrived.”

One of the maids announced Rin’s arrival.

“Please have her come in.”

“Excuse me.”

Despite this being the royal castle of a kingdom, and the Queen’s office at that, Rin showed no sign of nervousness as she entered.

“I am Sakuya, Queen of Castal. Rin-san, welcome.”

Sakuya greeted Rin in her formal tone.

As an aside, Sakuya has roughly three ways of speaking.

Her official ‘noja’ tone as Queen.

Her natural tone when speaking with Jin and the others.

And a semi-private polite tone for those she is not particularly close with (a practically dead setting).

Since her stance toward Shindo Rin was not yet decided, she used the polite tone.

Incidentally, this polite tone is only confirmed to have been used in ‘Volume 2, Chapter 34.5.’

“Nice to meet you. My name is Shindo Rin. Thank you for taking the time to see me today.”

Since both of them were using polite speech, distinguishing their dialogue was troublesome.

“Not at all. If you are related by blood to Jin-san, it is only natural to welcome you.”

Even Sakuya could not bring herself to call Jin ‘big brother’ in front of his real younger sister.

When the two sat facing each other at the table, a maid laid out tea and sweets.

This maid was one of Jin’s subordinates, so she thought nothing of Rin meeting with the Queen.

“My brother is always indebted to you. I will also be living in Castal from now on, so I thought it proper to greet you first and requested this meeting.”

It felt a bit odd that the first person she greeted was the Queen.

However, it was also true that greeting the Queen first would make many things certain.

Of course, that was only possible if one had the connections.

“How very courteous. If anything, I am the one being taken care of by Jin-san…”

This was unquestionably Sakuya’s true feeling.

Not only Sakuya personally, but the entire Kingdom of Castal had benefited from Jin’s abilities and influence.

“In fact, I wish he would rely on me more.”

“Being relied upon by my brother in the truest sense is rather difficult, you know? He rarely finds himself troubled…”

“Yes, I know.”

The only thing Jin completely leaves to others is cooking.

That is precisely why he prioritized purchasing slaves to handle cooking.

“I apologize for speaking so much about my brother, but there is one thing I would like to ask. May I?”

“…Yes.”

From Sakuya’s perspective, it felt like the moment had finally come.

“Sakuya-san, what was it about my brother that you fell in love with?”

“Fwah!?”

A sharp punch came from a completely different direction than Sakuya had expected.

She had braced herself for a straight punch, only to take a body blow to the liver instead.

“W-Why would you ask such a thing!?”

“Out of pure curiosity. I have asked others as well who seem to harbor affection for my brother. In our original world, almost no one showed him ordinary romantic interest, so I was curious.”

Rin’s eyes were serious. She did not appear to be teasing.

“You have asked others as well…”

“Yes. Fortunately, many people connected to my brother gather at the mansion, so I did not lack opportunities. I had no chance to meet you, Sakuya-san, so I wanted to speak with you while also offering my greetings.”

Since Sakuya herself had been avoiding her, it was only natural they had not met.

“Of course, I do not insist. If it is inconvenient, you need not answer. But if you do not mind, I would appreciate hearing your thoughts.”

“Well…”

She had been surprised by the sudden question, but she was not hiding her feelings for Jin.

It was not a topic that troubled her to discuss, so after thinking briefly, Sakuya answered.

“I think the biggest factor is the sense of security. When Jin-san is nearby, I feel at ease, and simply being under his protection makes most things less frightening.”

For Sakuya, Jin had become a symbol of security.

He first saved her from a life-threatening situation, and afterward resolved problems that arose time and again. On the scale of a nation, he is someone who commands numerous S-rank adventurers and world-spanning merchant companies.

Whether as an individual or as a Queen, it would be no surprise for her to grow attached to him.

“As I thought, it may be a matter of sample size.”

“What do you mean?”

After hearing Sakuya’s story, Rin began to think.

“Many others also cited things akin to ‘a sense of security’. In our original world, that ‘sense of security’ was perceived as something like a ‘miracle’ and it tended to lean more toward ‘faith’ than ‘romance’.”

“Even in this world, it is not as though he lacks followers…”

In fact, even in this world, Jin has many followers. Very many.

“Yes. He has even more followers in this world than in the original one. Because the total number of people is larger, perhaps the actual number of people who leaned toward ‘romance’ rather than ‘faith’ increased. That is what I thought.”

There are many who were ‘saved by Jin’ or who ‘found a sense of security in Jin’.

Most of them lean toward ‘faith’, but a very small number lean toward ‘romance’. Because the population satisfying those conditions is larger than in the original world, those few who leaned toward ‘romance’ stood out more.

“From what I have heard, this hypothesis seems quite likely to be correct. Sakuya-san, thank you very much for your valuable opinion.”

This younger sister was seriously analyzing her brother’s love life.

“As thanks, I would like to offer one piece of advice. If you wish for my brother to see you as a romantic interest, I would not recommend pushing the little-sister angle.”

“Fwoah!?”

At that moment, the straight punch she thought would not come finally flew.

“My brother almost never deviates from categories he has decided on. If you present yourself as a little sister, you will never escape being treated as one.”

“Is it wrong to present myself as a little sister…?”

“What problem is there with that?”

For Sakuya, this was the biggest issue of all, but Rin only tilted her head in puzzlement.

“I am calling myself his little sister while he already has a real one.”

“I generally do not interfere in my brother’s personal relationships. And even if the number of his little sisters were to increase, that would not make me stop being his little sister, so it would not be a problem.”

Rin believes that, except in cases where there is a social problem, interfering in her brother’s relationships is not something a ‘normal’ little sister would do.

If there is no social issue, and it does not affect the fact that ‘Rin is Jin’s little sister’, she will not interfere.

Of course, if someone tried to destroy the relationship between Jin and Rin, she would fight them thoroughly.

“Whether you call yourself a little sister or not is up to you, Sakuya-san. However, in exchange for not interfering, I will not support any specific individual either. I have told the others that as well.”

“…”

Sakuya considered her future stance.

“I think I will continue being a little sister for a while longer. As I am now, I am lacking in what it takes to make him see me as a woman. Ultimately, I want to graduate from being a little sister and aim to become his lover or spouse.”

Normally, one does not ‘graduate’ from being a little sister.

“Honestly, being treated as a little sister is not so bad, so part of me feels it would be fine to stay like this…”

“So you have set a general direction, but there are still parts you are unsure about?”

“Yes. What frightens me most is the situation where I graduate from being a little sister, but cannot become a lover or spouse. And I cannot return to being a little sister either.”

It is similar to confessing to a childhood friend, failing, and being unable to become lovers or return to being childhood friends.

If one were to name it, perhaps it would be something like being a ‘romantic ronin’.

“If there were a blood relationship, you would not have to worry about that. I envy you, Rin-san.”

Even if things became somewhat awkward, if there is a blood relationship, it is not impossible to return to the original relationship.

“I will absolutely never graduate from being a little sister. Even if I were to become his lover for some reason, I would never abandon being his little sister.”

For Rin, the relationship of ‘little sister’ is absolute.

Even if other relationships were added, it would not be replaced.

“A hard-core little sister…”

Sakuya recalled Mio’s evaluation of Rin as a ‘hard-core little sister’.

Indeed, this was truly a ‘hard-core little sister’. Someone on a completely different level from a ‘pseudo little sister’ like herself.

Sakuya honestly accepted that fact.

“To me, that is a compliment.”

And so, the number of people whose evaluation of Rin became ‘hard-core little sister’ increased by one.

---

**Characters**

Name: Sakuya

Gender: Female

Age: 10 (at first appearance)

Race: Human

Title: Queen of the Kingdom of Castal

Notes: The Queen of the Kingdom of Castal, who was saved by Jin when she was captured by demons. The first member of Jin’s royal woman collection (tentative, Dora excluded). All of her relatives were killed by demons, putting the royal line quietly at risk. Thus, both romantically and politically, she absolutely cannot let Jin go. While she benefits from Jin’s influence, she is also regarded by the public as a highly capable ruler.

Title: Head Maid Lucea: Executive Meeting

Point of View: Lucea

Timing: Volume 13, Chapter 200

My name is Lucea. I was formerly a Queen’s Knight of the Kingdom of Castal, but now I am a believer of Master, and among Master’s subordinates, I serve as the Head Maid who oversees the maids and butlers.

Today, the regular executive meeting is being held in the conference room of the castal estate.

At first, it was a report meeting where all on-duty maids participated, but as the number of maids grew enormous and it became difficult for everyone to attend, it was reshaped into an executive meeting that gathers only those in charge.

“Then, we will begin this week’s report meeting.”

I used to act as the facilitator, but now that role has been passed to mid-level maids.

Developing the next generation is an issue every organization inevitably faces.

“The first agenda item is personnel matters. Lucea-sama, if you would.”

“Yes.”

Given my position as Head Maid, I am the highest authority regarding personnel matters.

“Recently, when Master visited the Kingdom of Pajel, over a thousand people joined his subordinates. In accordance with Master’s policy, those who have a place to return to will be sent back, and those who do not will work under Master.”

The Kingdom of Pajel is a country Master has been visiting recently.

Due to several factors overlapping, a large number of subordinates were added.

“The return group has already departed, and the remaining group is currently being trained in the labyrinth. After that, they will be assigned according to their aptitudes. Departments with personnel requests should be sure to submit applications in advance.”

While individual aptitude is prioritized, shortages in staffing will also be taken into account.

“The next agenda item concerns the Advance Trading Company. Regarding store expansion, Colette-san, please.”

“Yes.”

Colette-san, who is responsible for the expansion of Advance Trading Company’s stores, takes over.

Officially, I am still the highest authority, but direct operations have already been delegated.

Not only with Advance Trading Company, but with many other matters, I was involved from the initial stages, yet in most cases I have stepped away from being the primary person in charge.

Rather, the impression is that only the personnel-related portions remain under my purview.

“As planned, transport of supplies to the Kingdom of Pajel and preparations for stores are proceeding smoothly.”

In the Kingdom of Pajel, an extraordinary monster known as a Disaster Dragon awakened, causing the collapse of the nation’s core.

Ships are being sent from the neighboring Izumo Wa Kingdom to provide aid, and at the same time, plans are in place to expand stores there.

Until now, due to business policy reasons, opening stores in the Kingdom of Pajel had been postponed. However, now that the core of the Kingdom of Pajel has fallen under Master’s banner, this is an opportune time.

Advance Trading Company is not a profit-oriented organization, but one meant to support Master’s sightseeing.

Even so, why had we not opened stores in the Kingdom of Pajel, a land famous as a tourist destination?

Because we were convinced that the Kingdom of Pajel was what Master calls ‘a land where events occur’.

Thanks to Master’s power, we can obtain information about the lands we travel to.

While this is a convenient ability, it also deprives sightseeing of its ‘sense of surprise’.

Before heading to a new land, we investigate it in advance, and if we judge it to be a ‘land where events occur’ that Master would likely enjoy, we do not open stores there and avoid approaching it.

After investigation by the maids, it was concluded that the Kingdom of Pajel was a land where events involving elves, or possibly a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, would occur. For that reason, opening stores there had been postponed.

“At present, we are also investigating countries that are trading with the Kingdom of Pajel in parallel. At this point, there do not appear to be any Master-related cases.”

By ‘Master-related cases’, she meant ‘cases where store openings are postponed due to events’.

“If there is any hesitation in judgment, please share the information immediately.”

“Yes, we will do so.”

Even if we were to open a store ahead of time in a land where events occur, Master would not scold us, nor are there any penalties defined.

Failures can happen. That is precisely why we do not cut corners, to reduce failures as much as possible. That is our policy. Anyone who does not understand this cannot become an executive.

“The next agenda item is monster taming. Asha-san, please.”

“Yes.”

Next called was Asha-san, a specialist in taming.

While working as a high-ranking adventurer, she is also affiliated with Advance Trading Company and concurrently serves as the head of the taming unit.

Incidentally, it was I who once broke Asha-san’s spirit, so she harbors a considerable sense of discomfort toward me.

“Monster taming is going well. This week, there were quite a few material-type monsters.”

The role of the taming unit is, as the name suggests, to tame monsters and expand Master’s forces.

They gather monsters useful as straightforward combat power, as sources of materials, and as support for daily life and production.

“There were five extermination bonuses, and we obtained one new skill, but it is close to a lower-tier version of an existing skill, so we will refrain from announcing it here.”

When all monsters within a territory are exterminated, rare monsters appear. Once exterminated, they do not appear again for a while, so we make a point of exterminating them periodically.

Bonus monsters sometimes possess rare skills, making them convenient targets for us, who are collecting skills, in many respects.

“Thank you, Asha-san.”

From there, we move on to those in charge of slave acquisition and skill acquisition.

“New slaves number 212. This figure does not include the additional count from the Kingdom of Pajel. New skills number four. These include skills highly useful for production, so the skill manager will speak later. Four individuals have particularly unusual backgrounds…”

“New skills total seven. One from taming, four from slaves, and two from extermination targets. Of these, three are particularly useful: one each for production, collection, and combat. As for the details…”

These figures could be said to be roughly average.

“I am Nino from the cooking division, yes. Of the recipes collected in the Kingdom of Pajel, fourteen can be considered completely new. The others would be described as arrangements of existing dishes, yes.”

Nino-san, the head of the cooking maids, participated in the Kingdom of Pajel events at Master’s request. Since these were cooking-related events, recipe collection seems to have progressed well.

Unfortunately, due to the collapse of the core of the nation, recipe collection could not be fully carried out.

“Outside of the Kingdom of Pajel cases, we successfully recreated five old dishes for which recipes no longer exist, yes. There were ten proposals for arranged dishes, but only three were adopted, yes. Both will appear in the dining hall within a few days, yes.”

I am convinced that the dining hall of this estate is the best in the world, both in number of menu items and in quality.

With Master’s power used without restraint to gather recipes and ingredients from across the world, and high-level \<Cooking> skill holders preparing the food, this result is only natural.

As for ingredients, since we borrow a section of the labyrinth, they are unaffected by the environment, including weather, and the soil is rich in nutrients, allowing for a stable supply of high-quality produce.

Additionally, among the monsters gathered by the taming unit, there are monsters that produce foodstuffs. To clarify, we do not use tamed monsters as meat.

“If there is sufficient popularity, we will also consider expanding to dining establishments, yes.”

Advance Trading Company also operates dining establishments in various locations.

Ingredients are primarily sourced locally, and these establishments serve as training grounds for mid-level and lower cooking maids.

Their \<Cooking> skill levels are not particularly high, so compared to the estate’s cooking, they cannot help but be inferior, but even so, they do not lose in flavor to ordinary eateries.

This is not limited to \<Cooking>, but when one acts with awareness of skills, even at the same skill level, differences in results can arise.

This is because understanding the existence of skills and what actions they support allows one to learn the proper degree of ‘reliance on skills’.

Skill growth rates differ from person to person.

This is because each individual has a different skill growth rate.

Furthermore, even if skill level and understanding are the same, the effects can vary between individuals.

This is due to aptitudes that differ from growth rates.

One major factor in Master’s forces having expanded this far is that these growth rates and aptitudes are understood, and skills are operated with optimal personnel assignments.

Master’s basic policy is, ‘Have people do what they are good at, rather than what they are bad at’.

After that, we got through several more agenda items.

The management of adventurer clans, explorers, and mercenary groups was proceeding as usual.

Land reclamation in the Kingdom of Brown Wall was going smoothly.

The transfer of inferior wyverns to friendly forces was also progressing.

The orchestra’s concerts continued to have an excessively packed schedule.

The collection of magic items was so-so.

Other minor matters continued.

“That concludes the agenda. Does anyone have additional topics or urgent matters?”

With the scheduled agenda complete, I check whether anyone has unscheduled business.

Usually, meetings end without any additional matters.

…Oh? Telepathic communication at a time like this?

《…》

“Emergency situation! In the elven village, Master’s younger sister has been summoned!”

-Rustle-

The conference room erupted into commotion.

We had heard that Master had a younger sister left behind in his original world, but we never expected her to appear in this world. No preparations had been made.

By any measure, this was an emergency of extremely high importance.

“For now, we will adjourn this meeting. Please prepare the minutes excluding the emergency matter. We will immediately convene personnel regarding the emergency and continue discussions.”

While our policy is to refrain from speaking out of turn, there is no time for that in an emergency.

“Dismissed!”

It looks like things will be busy for a while.

---

**Characters**

Name: Lucea

Gender: Female

Age: 24 (at first appearance)

Race: Human

Title: Jin’s slave, former Queen’s Knight

Notes: Formerly a Queen’s Knight of Castal, she was reduced to slavery by demons and later saved by Jin, becoming a believer through Maria’s preaching. In the story, she is treated almost as a symbol of the maids. While she has no combat scenes, she is not weak. Now, as Head Maid, she handles the majority of personnel matters among Jin’s subordinates. A behind-the-scenes contributor who does not stand out.

Name: Colette

Gender: Female

Age: 20 (at first appearance)

Race: Human

Title: Jin’s slave

Notes: A subordinate of Advance Trading Company who appeared briefly in Volume 4. With high ability in management, she rose smoothly through the ranks and came to occupy a position akin to vice-representative of Advance Trading Company. The teacup Jin used at the branch she managed is her treasured possession.

Name: Asha

Gender: Female

Age: 18 (at first appearance)

Race: Human

Title: Jin’s slave

Notes: A monster tamer who worked as an A-rank adventurer in the Atto Confederation. After being defeated by a Gigant Maneater and developing ‘Berserk’, she was saved by Jin and became his slave. She has since been promoted to S-rank and concurrently serves as the representative of Advance Trading Company’s monster unit. She is outstanding when it comes to monsters and beasts, and is highly valued by Jin.

A disciple of Mio, she appears frequently in cooking-related events. When she was acting alongside Jin in Volume 13, her heart rate became extremely high.

## **Interlude 3**

**AN:**

– Rin Shindo’s Connections: Reunion Arc

– Basilisk Welcome Party

Since the first part is longer, the latter ends as a shorter story.

---

Title: Rin Shindo’s Connections: Reunion Arc

POV: None

Timing: After Volume 13

On that day, two guests were visiting the highest-class guest room in the royal castle located in Gran Leon, the royal capital of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

And the one who welcomed them was Queen Sharon, the highest authority of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

“Hey, Ulysses. It’s been a while.”

“It’s been a long time. Sharon-chan, Faron-chan, have you been well?”

One of the guests was Ulysses, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ of the Earth Calamity Dragon.

She was Sharon’s close friend, with a relationship spanning ten years.

“We have. You look well too, Ulysses.”

Naturally, she was also someone Faron, Sharon’s other personality, could call a close friend.

When Sharon and the others received word from Ulysses that she wanted to meet after a long time, they did not hesitate to reserve the highest-class guest room.

“Yes. I’ve been spending my days happily under Jin-san. I’ve finally settled down enough to visit here again.”

“That does seem to be the case. But even so, Ulysses, you didn’t really have to come all the way to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, you know? We could have gone to another country instead.”

“I couldn’t very well make the queen leave her country for such a reason. And besides, visiting occasionally isn’t a problem. There are many unpleasant memories, but it’s also the land where I was born and raised, and it’s not as if there are zero good memories.”

For Ulysses, the Regalia Beastman Kingdom held more bad memories than good.

Her decision to place herself under Jin’s protection also strongly meant leaving the Regalia Beastman Kingdom behind.

“I see. Regardless of the reason, I’m just glad that you stepped onto the land of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom again.”

“We welcome you, Ulysses.”

Knowing Ulysses’ feelings, Sharon and the others could not bring themselves to ask her to come.

They simply rejoiced, from the heart, that Ulysses had come to visit.

“So then, is that the person you wanted me to meet?”

“Yes, that’s right. If things go well, she’ll become my sister-in-law.”

The other guest was wearing a hooded robe that concealed her head.

It was not an outfit one would wear when visiting a royal castle.

“Nice to meet you, Sharon-san. …Or rather, long time no see, Shiro. Do you remember me? I heard about you from my brother and came to see you.”

The other guest, Rin, Jin’s younger sister, removed her hood.

At the sight of Rin, astonishment and delight spread across Sharon’s face.

“Could it be Rin!? Wow, this brings back memories! What, Rin came to this world too!?”

In her previous life, Sharon had been Jin’s pet white cat, so of course she knew Rin, Jin’s younger sister.

Here, there is one thing that must not be misunderstood.

The white cat was ‘Jin’s pet’, not ‘the Shindo family’s pet’.

It was not that she wasn’t fond of Rin, but for the white cat at the time, the only person she could truly call her owner was Jin alone.

“I came, rather, I was summoned by my brother recently.”

“Jin can even summon people from another world now…?”

“Yes. According to my brother, he only became able to do so recently.”

“As always, he overturns the world’s common sense so easily…”

This was a shared understanding among those who knew Jin.

The three of them sat on chairs in the guest room, talking while drinking tea.

The first topic was about what happened after Ulysses left the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

In fact, after parting ways in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, Ulysses and Sharon’s group had exchanged letters via beastmen subordinates of Jin, who had become one of the Eight Vassal Beasts.

However, since there was a possibility that these letters could be seen by third parties, they could not bring up topics related to Jin, and only wrote harmless, minimal updates.

As a result, Sharon and the others never had the opportunity to learn about the turmoil surrounding the Calamity Dragons and the ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’.

“So he wiped out the Calamity Dragons entirely…”

Sharon muttered, sounding half exasperated and half impressed after hearing Ulysses’ account.

Of course, she omitted parts that could not be shared with outsiders, but Sharon and the others, who understood Jin’s circumstances, did not press for details.

“To think that the day would come when the threat of the Calamity Dragons would vanish from the world.”

“Jin is amazing.”

Jin defeated four Calamity Dragons and protected… enslaved four ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’.

It was truly an achievement that could be called saving the world.

Needless to say, he himself was not aware of it.

“I’ve never seen these Calamity Dragons. Are they really that incredible?”

Rin was summoned after all the Calamity Dragons had already been destroyed.

She had heard stories, but since she had not heard the details specifically about the dragons, she could not quite grasp the scale.

“Of course it’s incredible. To put it in terms Rin can understand, it’s like a ‘single human wiping out a natural disaster’.”

“That would be impossible for a normal human.”

“Jin isn’t a normal human, so it wasn’t impossible.”

Sharon and Faron had been sent by Ulysses into the subspace where the Calamity Dragons resided.

Having seen that threat firsthand, even if only once, there were things they could say because of it.

“What amazes me most is that even though the Calamity Dragons revived, not a single country was destroyed.”

“Yes. I always thought that the revival of a Calamity Dragon was the same as the collapse of civilization. To think that aside from the land where the dragons were, there was almost no damage. It’s unimaginable.”

Ulysses nodded in agreement with Faron’s opinion.

Two of them, the Wind Calamity Dragon and the Water Calamity Dragon, actually had their seals broken.

Although the land itself collapsed due to their revival, they were defeated afterward with almost no further damage.

For those who knew of the Calamity Dragons’ existence, this too was an impossible situation.

“Jin can be pretty decisive. He absolutely won’t save people he dislikes…”

“With the Water Calamity Dragon, apparently he could have stopped it if he wanted to. But Jin-san seems very strict when it comes to people reaping what they sow.”

According to Jin, ‘I refuse to clean up other people’s messes’.

“Yes, that’s the kind of person my brother is. On the other hand, he also has a gentle side toward complete victims.”

“I remember that.”

“Same here.”

Both of them had been saved by Jin before, so they readily accepted it.

“By the way, the other ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’ besides the Wind one survived, right? What kind of girls are they?”

As Sharon, she was naturally curious about her close friend’s kin.

Incidentally, the Wind Calamity Dragon’s ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is also alive, but since resurrection of the dead is confidential information for Jin, Sharon and the others did not know.

“The Fire Calamity Dragon’s ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is apparently the top executive of the Adventurers Guild.”

“What!? Is it okay for a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ to be out in the open!?”

Since the revival of a Calamity Dragon was recognized as the practical end of the world, the existence of a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ should be kept secret as much as possible. At least, that was how Sharon and the others thought.

“The very founding of the Adventurers Guild was apparently for the purpose of securing combat power against the Calamity Dragons.”

“No, that’s impossible.”

“She apparently gave up on that too.”

“Right?”

No matter how many S-rank adventurers gathered, there was no vision of them defeating a Calamity Dragon.

“The Water Calamity Dragon’s ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is a girl with a slime on her head.”

“Sorry, I don’t understand what that means.”

Sharon tilted her head, but Ulysses was not joking or lying in the slightest.

“It seems she developed a mild distrust of people, and that slime has become her emotional support.”

“Do slimes have therapeutic effects?”

They do not.

“She apparently succeeded the position a few months ago, and at seventeen, she’s the youngest ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.”

“Even then, she’s older than me.”

Sharon and Faron were both fifteen years old.

“Wrong. If you add Sharon’s previous life, she’s over seventeen.”

“Does saying that even mean anything? At the very least, it wasn’t a ‘life’ in that sense.”

One must not calculate using cat years. She would end up a rather awkward middle-aged woman.

“…As for the Wind Calamity Dragon’s ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, she assisted in Gired’s inhumane research and was killed by one of the victims’ fathers. Honestly, she wasn’t a very likable person.”

“I see. I don’t like speaking ill of the dead, so I’ll refrain from commenting, but as long as Ulysses wasn’t hurt by the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ dying, that’s what matters.”

The Wind Calamity Dragon’s ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ death was undoubtedly the result of her own actions.

“You got to punch Gired over the Water Calamity Dragon incident, right?”

“Yes. It felt refreshing.”

Being able to punch Gired, a past connection, was also a major reason Ulysses could revisit the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

“I wanted to punch him too. You should have called me.”

“That would have been impossible. It’s a very distant country, you know?”

It was no exaggeration to call it far away.

If she traveled without Jin, it would interfere with governing the kingdom.

“To put it bluntly, Gired doesn’t have a direct connection to us. If Ulysses couldn’t punch him, punching him on her behalf would be fine, but punching him separately wouldn’t make sense, right?”

“I know. I was just saying.”

“Faron’s jokes are hard to understand.”

Faron likes jokes, but that does not mean they are funny.

“But after hearing the story, I understand. The reason Ulysses has calmed down enough to come to this country is because the Calamity Dragons are gone, and you got to punch Gired.”

“Yes. My past has been completely settled.”

“Ulysses, that’s good.”

With all her unpleasant past settled, Ulysses was able to prepare herself to return to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

Understanding that, Sharon and the others sincerely felt glad that they had entrusted Ulysses to Jin.

Ulysses’ story came to an end for now, and the topic shifted.

“So then, what kind of girl was Sharon-chan in the previous world?”

“She was a rather unusual white cat.”

“…Could you explain that in a bit more detail?”

For Rin, ‘normal’ or ‘not normal’ was the easiest standard to understand.

However, Ulysses had no grasp of what was ‘normal’ for cats in another world.

“It was obvious that she understood human language, and when we taught her tricks, she learned them right away.”

“Thinking back on it, it really was strange. Yeah, I do remember her being able to understand human speech.”

Although Sharon had been a mysterious white cat in her previous life, she herself did not know the reason why.

“A cat that understood human language in her previous life, and in this life, a white tiger beastman with two souls. Sharon, you’re strange enough that you can’t talk about your owner.”

“I can’t deny it, but I think it’s questionable for you to say that, Faron. At the very least, that makes you half as strange as I am, right?”

Sharon and Faron’s relationship was that of an older sister reincarnated from a cat and a younger sister who died during childbirth.

And since Faron’s soul merged into Sharon’s body, they ended up with two souls in one body.

The dominant personality is Sharon, the owner of the body, but due to Sharon’s wishes, Faron spends more time on the surface.

“I’m just Sharon’s extra. The cause lies with Sharon.”

“Isn’t it a bit cruel to push responsibility onto me there?”

Faron does not feel guilty about that fact, nor does she become self-deprecating.

She even jokes about it, as she is doing now.

“Hehe, you two are as close as ever. I don’t think you’ve ever fought, have you?”

“No, there was one time we had a huge fight.”

“What? How do you even fight?”

Rin could not imagine a fight between two personalities.

“You punch your own body, and then switch right before it hits.”

“It was a fierce battle of seizing and pushing away control.”

Although Sharon is the dominant personality, Faron is not in a one-sidedly disadvantaged position.

Sharon has a slight edge, but they are balanced enough to fight over control.

“…You both did something like that?”

“…That’s a pretty awful image to imagine.”

Ulysses and Rin recoiled after imagining the scene.

Specifically, a girl punching her own body and rolling around alone.

“Truly, a battle with no winner.”

“And after that big fight, we haven’t fought like that again.”

“At the very least, we haven’t had any fights that went beyond verbal arguments.”

They learned from that big fight that physical fights had nothing to gain.

One would want to tell them they should have realized that beforehand.

“What was the cause of that big fight?”

“Let’s see…”

“Sharon, stop!”

As Sharon was about to speak after being asked by Ulysses, Faron stopped her.

“We promised not to say that.”

“Ah, sorry. That’s right. Even you wouldn’t want people to hear about that, Faron.”

It seemed to be something embarrassing for Faron.

“If you say it, we’re cutting ties.”

“What? How do you cut ties?”

Rin could not imagine how two personalities would sever relations.

“…We’re accepting suggestions.”

Apparently, there was no specific method.

“More importantly, tell us about Sharon’s embarrassing past.”

“Hey!? What are you asking!”

Faron changed the direction of attack.

She seemed to want material to tease Sharon if possible.

“Well…”

“No, you don’t have to say it!”

Seeing Rin start to think, Sharon hurriedly tried to stop her, but Rin did not stop.

“That was…”

…

“Sharon-chan, even if you were a cat, that was just too…”

“Sharon, pervert.”

“Wait! Let me explain!”

“Is it okay to declare it’s an excuse from the start?”

For the sake of Sharon’s honor, the contents will be withheld.

After talking until they were satisfied, the gathering broke up near evening.

“Today was fun. If it’s alright, may I come again?”

“Yeah, you’re welcome anytime.”

“There is no reason to refuse a friend.”

“Of course, Rin is welcome too.”

For Sharon, Rin, who she had known since her previous life, was a welcome guest.

“I want you to tell me more about Sharon’s past.”

“Yes, I would very much like to visit again.”

“I’d rather you not talk about the embarrassing ones…”

For Faron as well, they were favorable companions since they shared common topics.

“Indeed. I can’t talk about that to others. Let’s keep it secret.”

“Please, let me hear it!”

“You’re declaring there’s more above that, right? Sharon-chan, just what did you do?”

“Don’t tell me… that… Why does Rin know about that…?”

Apparently, Sharon had something in mind.

“You didn’t know? In the Shindo household of the original world, there are hidden cameras.”

“!!!???”

Even a cat that understands human language does not necessarily understand human-made machines correctly.

Humanity’s wisdom had captured the disgrace of a beast on camera.

“Please! Don’t tell anyone!”

The queen of a nation performed a full prostration.

Rin Shindo is Jin Shindo’s younger sister.

Just like Jin Shindo, she is likely destined to have royalty prostrate themselves before her.

---

**Characters**

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice, Jin’s Slave

After her liberation, she left the Regalia Beastman Kingdom and now devotes herself to her specialty of magical tool creation under Jin. She is in love with Jin, who freed her from suffering, but her attempts to appeal have not gone well.

Name: Sharon

Gender: Female

Age: 15 (at first appearance)

Race: Beastman (White Tiger, Reincarnator)

Titles: Queen of the Regalia Kingdom, Dual Personality

Notes: The queen of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom and Faron’s twin older sister. A reincarnator whose previous life was a white cat kept by Jin. The true owner of the body she shares with Faron. She wishes to become Jin’s equal, but also wants to be spoiled as his pet cat like before. There are no plans yet, but there is a feeling that she may eventually become Jin’s subordinate.

Name: Faron

Gender: Female

Age: 15 (at first appearance)

Race: Beastman (White Tiger)

Titles: Queen of the Regalia Kingdom, Dual Personality

Notes: The queen of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom and Sharon’s twin younger sister. Her soul is lodging in Sharon’s body. She spends more time with her personality on the surface than Sharon does. Since Sharon already fully enjoyed one cat life, Sharon wants Faron to enjoy her life. Faron feels apologetic about being a lodger yet appearing more than the dominant personality. Despite how they appear in the story, they are actually very close.

Title: Basilisk Welcome Party

POV: Author

Timing: After Volume 13

This is a story from right after the Basilisk became Mio’s new familiar.

Note that in this chapter, lines have secondary voice annotations, but these do not guarantee the actual speech or tone, and exist only to convey nuance.

Even if there are differences from the tone used during actual telepathic communication, complaints will not be accepted.

“Woof! (Alright then, let’s hold a welcome party for the newcomer!)”

Potato Chip, Mio’s first familiar (Fairy Wolf, male), energetically declared.

“Meow! (Yay!)”

“Squeee! (Clap clap!)”

Myao, the second familiar (Young Divine Beast, female), and Blanc, the third familiar (Feather Dragon, female), chimed in enthusiastically.

Incidentally, Mio treats the relationships between her familiars as siblings.

In other words, Potato Chip is the eldest son, Myao is the eldest daughter, and Blanc is the second daughter.

“Ku… (Nice to meet you…)”

Unfortunately, the Basilisk who had newly joined the siblings was not good at raising his excitement.

Although healed by Jin, the Basilisk had lost all intelligence beyond following orders due to Gired’s actions, and as an aftereffect, he became poor at emotional expression.

He had originally been a bright Basilisk who aggressively attacked anyone…

“Woof! (Let’s start with introductions!)”

“Ku. (My name is Basil, a Basilisk. I was tamed by Mio-san. Mio-san has told me to become the third younger brother.)”

Mio had named the male Basilisk ‘Basil’.

Strictly speaking in terms of simple age, Basil was older, but since he had spent most of his time with low intelligence and had lost his previous memories, Mio decided to treat him as the youngest, the second son.

“Squee! (At last, there’s a sibling younger than me. I welcome you.)”

Blanc, who had been the youngest sister, honestly rejoiced at Basil’s addition.

“Kuuun… (This means big sis will stop riding me now, right? Seriously, this is a lifesaver.)”

Despite being frail, Potato Chip had been trained as a mount, and he was rejoicing in an improper way.

Although his status enhancements allowed him to carry people and run, he disliked exercise to begin with and had poor balance, so he really wanted people to stop riding him.

“Meow… (This pathetic big brother…)”

Myao looked at him as if seeing something pitiful.

Needless to say, Potato Chip had almost no dignity as the eldest son.

“W-woof! (H-hey, that’s fine! It’s about putting the right person in the right place!)”

“Squee? (What are you suited for, big brother?)”

“W-woof? (Huh?)”

“Mmph! (Pfft!)”

At Blanc’s merciless retort, Myao burst out laughing.

Blanc could not see what aptitude Potato Chip had.

“W-woof… (W-well, my fur, maybe…)”

“Meow? (Huh? Do you think you can beat me in fur?)”

“Squee. (I have no intention of losing either.)”

According to Mio, Potato Chip’s fur is coarse.

“W-woof… (F-fighting… no. Guard dog… also no.)”

“Squee. (I’m sorry. I asked something bad.)”

“Kuuun! (It’s sad when you apologize like that!)”

Blanc looked genuinely apologetic, and Potato Chip looked on the verge of tears.

“Ku… (You all get along so well…)”

Basil watched the three of them with envy.

“Woof! (Don’t act like an outsider. You’re going to get along with us from now on! Just so you know, you don’t have the right to refuse!)”

“Meow. (That’s right, this is the siblings’ cup. Once you drink it, we’re siblings.)”

“Squee! (It’s delicious, so savor it!)”

In front of the four of them was a plate filled with milk.

It was the siblings’ cup (non-alcoholic).

“…Ku? (…Is it really okay? I’m a boring guy, you know?)”

“Woof! (Don’t worry! I’m useless myself, you know?)”

“Squee. (I’m sorry about earlier.)”

“Woof! (I said don’t apologize! Come on, drink it already!)”

“Meow… (Big brother is half giving up…)”

Potato Chip was the first to start licking the milk, followed by Myao and Blanc.

Then Basil made up his mind and began to lap the milk from the plate.

“Ku. (Ah, it’s tasty.)”

“Woof? (Right?)”

It was milk from a Fighting Goat that appeared in Volume 13, so of course it was delicious.

Incidentally, the previous cup had been ordinary milk.

“What a heartwarming scene. I wonder what they’re talking about?”

Mio muttered as she passed by and saw her familiars amicably licking milk together.

---

**Characters**

Name: Potato Chip

Gender: Male

Title: Mio’s Familiar

His stats have improved thanks to an ability, but his personality remains unchanged and he is not suited for combat. He is Mio’s pet and definitely not a guard dog. His fur is coarse, so he escaped Jin’s clutches.

Name: Myao

Gender: Female

Race: Young Divine Beast

Title: Mio’s Familiar

Notes: Tamed by Mio in the Atto Confederation. She looks like a perfect pet, combining dog and cat features, but surprisingly is a bundle of ambition. She actively participates in combat training, and in a head-on fight could probably defeat Potato Chip. Having received Jin’s fluffing, both body and soul have become captivated by Jin. I’ll say it again. Her master is Mio.

Notes: Tamed by Mio in the Pajel Kingdom. He was forgotten in the Volume 13 character list, so this is his first introduction. One of Gired’s research results, a monster that lost its intelligence and specialized in petrification. As demonstrated in Volume 13, he possessed the power to bring down an entire nation. He has now returned to being a normal Basilisk. He chose Mio over Jin because he felt no threat or fear from Mio. He felt at ease.
