## **Interlude 4**

**AN:**

• The Holy-Demonic Blacksmith Mimi: The Sword That Reaches Creation

• Maximum Firepower

This is not part of the main story, but important events that also relate to the main story take place here.

---

Title: The Holy-Demonic Blacksmith Mimi: The Sword That Reaches Creation

Point of View: Mimi

Timeframe: After Volume 13

At last, this day has come.

Today, I will forge a sword that can truly be called the culmination of my life as a blacksmith.

“…Um, we have everything now, right?”

“It’s fine… I’ve confirmed it… We can’t afford to fail…”

I nod in response to the question from Knot-kun, who is both my assistant and my disciple.

I have checked the materials needed for this forging again and again.

Some of them are rare materials that can probably never be obtained again, so failure is absolutely not an option.

“If you tried to buy and gather all the materials here, a major power’s finances would just collapse normally, right?”

“The Izumo Wa Kingdom would definitely collapse.”

“Yes, we wouldn’t even be able to gather half of them.”

If Tooru-san and Kaoru-san, who are actually royalty of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, say so, there can be no mistake.

These two are not my disciples, but they are serving as assistants for this forging.

Both of them are huge sword enthusiasts, and they have more blacksmithing knowledge than ordinary people, so they came pitching themselves as assistants who would not get in the way.

Incidentally, since they became Lord Jin’s subordinates around the same time and have various connections with him, when I told them I would be forging my greatest masterpiece, they asked to be present no matter what, and that was how it started.

“It feels a little wasteful that the purpose of forging a sword with materials like this is that, but if it’s to be used by Master, it can’t be helped…”

“It’s already… been decided…”

Knot-kun says this with a hint of regret, but this has already been decided.

The maids’ power was indispensable to gathering this many materials. And if it is a weapon that will be ‘for Lord Jin’, the maids will spare no effort to help.

I cannot use that to make a weapon that will not benefit Lord Jin.

“If possible, I would like you to forge a sword for me.”

“If you can prepare… the same materials… I will make one…”

Since my \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing> has its performance directly tied to my mental state, the performance would probably be lower than a sword made for Lord Jin, but if the materials are prepared, I will not refuse.

“That’s absolutely impossible…”

Of course, I was only saying it hypothetically.

“Hmm, even if we put the Izumo Wa Kingdom up as collateral, it would be impossible.”

“Is that something royalty is allowed to declare, even as a metaphor?”

“It’s just an example, you know?”

“No, I get that, but…”

Even as a metaphor, having someone on the ruling side say something like that makes you uneasy.

…We have gotten quite off topic.

It’s good for relieving tension, but loosening up too much is not good either.

“It’s about time… to begin the work…”

Hearing my words, the three of them also tightened their expressions and nodded.

I take a deep breath myself and step into the forge once more.

For Lord Jin, weapons are not something that are absolutely necessary.

Once you reach Lord Jin’s level of existence, even myth-class weapons no longer have a major impact on the outcome of a battle.

Holding a half-baked weapon could even get in the way of fighting.

Therefore, the weapon that is easiest and most frequently used by Lord Jin is his own fists.

The reason Lord Jin uses the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’ is not because it is strong.

It is because the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’ is his favorite. I have heard this directly.

In other words, even if I were to make a weapon stronger than the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’, if he did not like it more than that blade, Lord Jin would not use it.

To be frank, the moment I heard this, I gave up on forging a blade to replace the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’.

Because within me, there was no guiding principle for ‘a blade that Lord Jin would like’.

Forging a blade without a fixed direction and betting on the chance that Lord Jin might coincidentally like it is far too risky.

After that, for some time, I repeated trial and error.

I gave up on forging a blade to replace the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’, but that does not mean I gave up on forging a weapon that would be useful to Lord Jin.

I considered making auxiliary weapons, such as daggers.

However, even the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’ itself is used infrequently.

There is no stage left for an auxiliary weapon to appear.

Even if he did use it, I do not think it would truly be useful.

Conversely, I also considered making weapons other than a blade.

Lord Jin is not incapable of using weapons other than blades. If we prepared such a weapon in advance for when he might want to use one, there is a chance he would use it.

At best, he would probably use it once.

Unfortunately, I must say that this is far removed from my true aspiration.

And finally, I arrived at a single conclusion.

This conclusion could only be reached through \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing>, and it can provide nothing but benefit to Lord Jin.

Here, let me explain the skill known as \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing>.

\<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing> is a skill that creates holy swords and demonic swords, but its essence cannot be explained by that alone.

More precisely, it is a skill that grants directed magical power to the weapons it creates.

This directionality is determined by the strong wish held at the time the weapon is forged, and it ultimately manifests as the weapon’s special effects.

If a weapon is forged with negative emotions, the directionality becomes distorted, resulting in special effects different from the original intent. This is why demonic swords are born.

If a weapon is forged with positive emotions, the desired special effects are obtained with correct directionality, and it becomes a holy sword.

In fact, the skill \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing> has no modifiers related to blacksmithing skill.

Its essence is ‘manipulation of magical power’, and blacksmithing is merely the means by which it manifests.

Now, consider the ultimate form of ‘manipulation of magical power’.

The hint already existed. Among demonic swords, there are things known as living weapons. These are demonic swords whose granted magical power became distorted, developed a self, and turned into monsters.

Living weapons came to be called ‘monsters’ because a ‘self’ resided within the vessel of a weapon.

Then, what would you call ‘magical power’ that gained a ‘self’ without having a vessel? The answer is ‘spirit’.

Though it is not widely known, living weapons and spirits share extremely similar properties, at least in part.

Just because they share similar properties does not mean spirits can be easily created.

There is an unimaginably vast difference between creating a living weapon and creating a spirit.

No matter how much effort the holder of \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing> puts in, it is a difference that can never be bridged.

…This is a bit of a tangent, but within Lord Jin’s faction, there are various kinds of people.

For example, spirits that possess Lord Jin’s magical power.

For example, users of ‘Spiritization’, who merge with spirits.

For example, users of \<Spirit Arts> who can contract with spirits.

For example, adventurers capable of gathering materials related to spirits.

And then, Lord Jin’s Special Power can do the following.

Fully disclose information on skills and items.

Use maps to ascertain the locations of rare materials.

Strengthen the skill \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing> by one stage.

By now, you should understand.

If there is a gap that cannot be bridged no matter how much effort the holder of \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing> puts in, then it is enough to use other powers to fill it.

Under Lord Jin, that becomes possible.

Several hours have passed since I began forging.

“It’s… finished…”

Saying so, I raise a single white straight blade.

Spirit Blade: Shisei

Classification: Blade, Spirit

Rarity: Myth-class

Notes: Owner Restriction, Unbreakable, Weapon Summoning, Silence, Spiritization

By strengthening \<Holy-Demonic Blacksmithing> through \<Expanded Interpretation> and consuming a massive amount of rare materials related to spirits, one blade was forged, and in doing so, one spirit was born.

“Incredible.”

“Incredible indeed.”

“Incredible…”

Unfortunately, at the moment an artificial spirit was born, the vocabulary of the three of them died.

The three stare without blinking, burning the Spirit Blade: Shisei into their eyes.

A myth-class item has that much presence.

This is probably the first myth-class weapon ever created by the hands of the human races.

If it were made public, it would be a feat worthy of going down in history, but I am not interested in such things in the slightest.

What matters is whether this blade possesses the power I desire.

“Let’s… confirm the special effects…”

“Ah, ah. Right.”

At my prompting, the three of them begin checking the special effects of the Spirit Blade: Shisei.

Owner Restriction. A special effect that makes it unusable by anyone other than Lord Jin. The original effect is that if someone else uses it, its abilities are greatly restricted, but in the case of this blade, it cannot even be touched. Right now, since the spirit has not yet awakened, even I can touch it.

Unbreakable. A special effect that prevents it from being destroyed by normal means. It can be said to be a standard special effect for myth-class equipment. Normally, spirits have HP, but this spirit has no HP and instead possesses Unbreakable. In other words, it is an immortal spirit.

Weapon Summoning. A special effect that returns the weapon to your hand when called. It is slightly different from the special effect of the same name on other weapons, in that it does not require a corresponding ring to activate. Naturally, it is an effect that only Lord Jin can use.

They are all slightly different from their original effects, but these are fairly common special effects.

Weapons created with positive emotions often receive these effects.

However, the special effects beyond this point are all things I have never seen before.

Let us check one by one whether the effects I truly wished for have been granted.

With the confirmation of the special effects complete, I promptly present it to Lord Jin.

“Lord Jin… please… accept this…”

I kneel and present the Spirit Blade: Shisei to Lord Jin.

“What is this?”

“The greatest blade… forged… for Lord Jin…”

“Hoh.”

Lord Jin gazes at the blade he received with interest.

“Myth-class… So Mimi has become a myth-class blacksmith. Well done.”

“…! I-It’s… an honor…”

That was close. I almost lost consciousness from Lord Jin’s heartfelt praise.

“It seems to be a rather unusual blade. Since we have the chance, explain it to me in your own words, Mimi.”

“Y-Yes… Leave it… to me…”

My heart is pounding so loudly it hurts, from both tension and excitement.

“This blade is… at the same time a blade… and a spirit… The goal is… to combine the advantages… of blades and spirits… It has no attack power… and cannot be touched by anyone other than Lord Jin… And then… it can ‘Spiritize’… with the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’…”

The special effect Spiritization possessed by this blade refers to ‘Spiritization’ applied to a weapon.

“When ‘Spiritization’ is used… this blade’s properties… are also granted… to the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete …”

This ‘Spiritization’ does not increase the power of the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete.

It simply grants the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete the properties of this blade, including its special effects.

“May I try it?”

“Of … course…”

As he says that, Lord Jin draws the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete and brings it into contact with the Spirit Blade: Shisei.

Then, the two blades become one. In appearance, it remains the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete.

“The presence of the weapon has diminished? Ah, so this is the effect of Silence.”

“Yes… Now… you can use it… regularly…”

“This is appreciated. The Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete has become easier to use.”

That is precisely my objective.

The Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete originally emitted a presence even greater than other myth-class equipment.

Likewise, without the special effect of the scabbard, Aura Control, which also became myth-class, it would stand out to a degree that would make even carrying it around normally something to hesitate over.

This is one of the reasons Lord Jin stopped using the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete as much.

The special effect Silence allows the presence of a weapon to be suppressed at will.

If the presence of the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete is suppressed by the effect of the Spirit Blade: Shisei, then opportunities to use the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete will increase.

In other words, it also means that the Spirit Blade: Shisei will be used.

By making the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete easier to use, the Spirit Blade: Shisei that is Spiritized with it will also be used at the same time.

This is the ultimate conclusion that benefits both Lord Jin and myself.

“You can also… summon it… with Weapon Summoning…”

When I say that, Lord Jin throws the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete without hesitation.

In the next instant, the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete returns to Lord Jin’s hand.

“This is convenient too.”

Basically, the word hesitation does not exist in Lord Jin’s dictionary.

“By the way, what kind of guy is the spirit of this blade? Did you create it, Mimi?”

“I created it… using a fragment of Rain…”

“I see. No wonder it meshes so well.”

Creating a spirit that dwells within Lord Jin’s weapon is no different from saying that Lord Jin’s contracted spirits have increased by one. I confirmed this with Rain, who is Lord Jin’s contracted spirit.

When Rain heard my story, she tore off a part of her own body and handed it to me.

That became the core material for the ‘Spirit Blade’ I created.

In other words, it was Rain’s declaration of ‘No spirits unrelated to me’.

Since she is a taciturn spirit, she probably will not speak of it.

Incidentally, since it is a part of Rain and a spirit I myself created, its favorability toward Lord Jin exceeds the maximum value from the start.

“Lastly… this blade… will not collapse… under \<Expanded Interpretation>…”

“Nande!?”

Lord Jin looks extremely surprised.

It is not a difficult explanation.

The Spirit Blade: Shisei is a weapon. Therefore, its abilities can be increased using \<Expanded Interpretation>.

The Spirit Blade: Shisei is a spirit. Therefore, it can avoid the side effect of \<Expanded Interpretation>, which is collapse.

The Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete has inherited the properties of the Spirit Blade: Shisei. Therefore, it can do the same thing as the Spirit Blade: Shisei, which is both a spirit and a weapon.

That is what it means to ‘combine the advantages of blades and spirits’.

“And then… through \<Expanded Interpretation>… it surpasses myth-class… and reaches creation-class…”

“Nani!?”

I heard this from Alta, but even if you use \<Expanded Interpretation> on a myth-class item, it does not become creation-class.

With multiplication through \<Expanded Interpretation>, the numbers are insufficient to reach creation-class.

Incidentally, this is not based on actual testing, because that would be wasteful. Naturally.

Then, what about the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete that has undergone ‘Spiritization’ with the Spirit Blade: Shisei?

This ‘Spiritization’ is, so to speak, addition.

If multiplication alone is not enough, then you simply add first and then multiply.

Add two myth-class items, and then apply \<Expanded Interpretation>.

Only by doing this can one finally reach creation-class.

“You came up with something interesting.”

As I stumble through explaining the logic, Lord Jin smiles happily.

Faced with a smile clearly directed only at me, my heart starts making noise again.

“Can you tell me the origin of the name Shisei?”

“I named it… after creation-class… ‘reaching creation’…”

Heart, please be quiet. I cannot hear Lord Jin’s words properly.

“So it’s a weapon you created by thinking through everything from one to ten, not a product of chance.”

“Yes… I created it… thinking about how it could be useful… to Lord Jin…”

“Interesting. Truly interesting. Well done, Mimi.”

Saying that, Lord Jin pats the head of me as I kneel.

“Kyu…”

“Hey!”

My heart, which had exceeded its tolerable limit, chose to calm itself by knocking me unconscious.

When I awaken from fainting and open my eyes, the ceiling of the room given to me comes into view.

In my heart, there is a sense of fulfillment from having accomplished my life’s purpose.

“I could… die now…”

“No, don’t jump to that conclusion.”

Knot-kun reacts to the heartfelt words that slipped out.

When I sit up, it seems that not only Knot-kun, but also Tooru-san and Kaoru-san are present.

Once I calm down a little, I recall what happened just before I fainted, and realize that an overwhelming sense of despair equal to my sense of fulfillment has arisen.

“Ah… what a blunder…”

Yes. Overcome by excitement, I lost consciousness in front of Lord Jin.

It is an utterly fatal blunder.

“I want to… die…”

“You die whether you’re happy or sad, you know?”

“What a troublesome person…”

I am aware that I have a rather troublesome personality.

“Why… am I here…?”

“Master carried you here. He was surprised that you fainted when he patted your head.”

“Ah…!”

On top of my blunder, I caused trouble as well!?

“He carried you princess-style and laid you on the bed.”

“P-Princess…!? Princess…? Hh… kyu…”

“She fainted again…”

Overwhelmed by embarrassment, guilt, and an overwhelming sense of happiness that surpassed them both, I lost consciousness once more.

---

**Characters**

Name: Mimi

Gender: Female

Age: 19 (at first appearance)

Race: Dwarf

Title: Former Noble Lady

Notes: A young dwarf blacksmith girl who was living in seclusion in a forest within the Izumo Wa Kingdom due to a demerit skill. She was saved by Jin when she was about to die in a forest fire, and became one of Jin’s subordinates and a believer at the same time. Though it is easy to misunderstand, she did not become a slave. She is the best blacksmith among Jin’s subordinates. Publicly, she is believed to have died in the forest fire.

Name: Knot

Gender: Male

Age: 10 (at first appearance)

Race: Dwarf

Title: Jin’s Slave

Notes: One of the adventurer slave group from Castal, and excluding the main party, he is one of the earliest slaves. Currently, in addition to his fame as an S-rank adventurer, he is also becoming well known as a blacksmith. The weapons Knot makes are provided to members of the same clan and are widely known to be overwhelmingly superior to commercially sold products.

Name: Tooru Izumo

Gender: Female

Age: 14 (at first appearance)

Race: Oni

Title: Princess of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, Jin’s Slave

Notes: One of the twin princesses of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, the older sister. She became Jin’s slave after being caught up in her younger sister’s rampage. A severe sword maniac who actually rejoices at having become a slave. She cross-dresses and is a mental masochist. As her chest has been growing, the limits of cross-dressing are approaching.

Name: Kaoru Izumo

Gender: Female

Age: 14 (at first appearance)

Race: Oni

Title: Princess of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, Jin’s Slave

Notes: One of the twin princesses of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, the younger sister. She attacked Jin and became a slave after being counterattacked. Like Tooru, she is a severe sword maniac. She frequently switches places with Tooru and is a physical masochist. Just a little, just a little bit, her chest is smaller than Tooru’s. Despite being twins.

Name: Rain

Gender: Female

Age: 0 (at first appearance)

Race: Great Spirit

Title: Jin’s Contracted Spirit, Spirit Queen

Notes: A spirit that served as the core of an Oni God sealed in the Izumo Wa Kingdom. She was revived by Jin and became his contracted spirit. She does not speak to begin with, and this time she only appears in a flashback. She is an extremely special spirit, and it would not be an exaggeration to say that her body (magical power) is an ultra-rare material.

Title: Maximum Firepower

Point of View: None

Timeframe: After Volume 13 (Immediately after ‘The Holy-Demonic Blacksmith Mimi: The Sword That Reaches Creation’)

This is another world that Shindo Jin calls the ‘Gray World’.

A world abandoned by the goddess, waiting only for annihilation by the approaching ‘Wall of Collapse’.

In the past, even Shindo Jin could not interfere with this ‘Wall of Collapse’.

The ‘Wall of Collapse’ is one of the most solid laws established at the time of creation, and laws of lower priority cannot even interfere with it.

It is only natural that laws of lower priority, such as weapons and skills, cannot interfere.

The Special Powers possessed by Shindo Jin and Kinoshita Sakura are powers that forcibly rewrite laws.

It would probably not be impossible to interfere with the ‘Wall of Collapse’.

However, at the time, Shindo Jin did not possess an Special Power that could interfere with the ‘Wall of Collapse’.

Since the ‘Gray World’ was not an important place for Shindo Jin, he likely did not even think to interfere with it.

As a result, the optimal conditions for today’s test were in place.

“Rain, Eclipse. ‘Double Spiritization’.”

“”!!!””

Saying this, Shindo Jin simultaneously ‘Spiritized’ with the two great spirits, Rain and the miasma spirit Eclipse.

Parts of his body turn black or emit light in a flurry.

“Over here as well, ‘Spiritization’.”

He brings the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete into contact with the Spirit Blade: Shisei he holds, fusing them into one blade.

“And then, \<Expanded Interpretation>.”

He uses \<Expanded Interpretation> on the Spiritized Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete.

At that moment, the rarity of the Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete, which had been myth-class, was raised to creation-class.

Shindo Jin calls this blade the ‘Divine Spirit Blade: Shisei: Complete’.

In terms of simple physical ability, the state of ‘Double Spiritization’ is the strongest.

As equipment, nothing exists that surpasses creation-class.

“Now then, will this reach it?”

Shindo Jin, who has maximized his status and undergone ‘Double Spiritization’, swings the creation-class equipment, the ‘Divine Spirit Blade: Shisei: Complete’.

On this day, the annihilation of the ‘Gray World’ was stopped.

The scar carved into the ‘Wall of Collapse’ completely destroyed that law.

---

Settings

• About creation-class equipment

At present, not a single piece of creation-class equipment exists in the world.

The ‘Divine Spirit Blade: Shisei: Complete’ was only made pseudo-creation-class through the use of Special Powers, and strictly speaking, it cannot be called true creation-class equipment.

At the level of creation-class, discussing performance as a weapon loses meaning, and it instead strongly takes on the aspect of a device for directly interfering with laws.

To begin with, the meaning of creation-class is ‘an existence that should be recorded in the Book of Creation’, which is on a completely different level from the meaning of myth-class, which is ‘equipment used in myths’.

As an aside, even without ‘Double Spiritization’, the ‘Wall of Collapse’ could have been stopped.

However, no scar would have remained.

---

**AN:** At last, ‘Incomplete’ has become ‘Complete’. It has been a long road. The concept itself has existed for quite some time.

Just to be clear, it is not an ‘Intelligent weapon’. It is a spirit with an extremely thin self-awareness.

That said, the settings may change along the way (it might suddenly start talking?).

A labor-of-love joke

“Shisei: Complete” -> “Shiseikan” -> “Shiseikan”

## **Interlude 5**

**AN:** I apologize, but this time it is only one story.

Discarded idea from last time: Iyokan’s dark-fallen form “Calamity Spirit Blade: Seven Sins: Completion”

---

Title: S-Rank Adventurer Coco – Imperial Princess Airlift

Point of View: Coco

Timing: Volume 12

That day, after Cicely and I had finished a request, we received an emergency named request from the Advance Trading Company.

To be honest, a named request from the Advance Trading Company is little more than a formality.

Viewed broadly, the Advance Trading Company and I belong to the same organization, so the movement of capital is practically nonexistent (the Adventurers Guild does take a margin).

Rather than the request itself, they place importance on going through the procedure of a named request so that it maintains the appearance of ‘carrying out a request as an adventurer’.

That said, we had already been contacted beforehand via telepathy, so we were fully aware of the details.

Escort Princess Strawberry, who is currently in the Brown Wall Kingdom, to the Crimson Empire.

That is the content of this named request, and if I put it even more simply, it is ‘escorting a lost child back to her faraway home’.

Indeed, Cicely and I are well suited for this request.

The Brown Wall Kingdom and the Crimson Empire are far apart, so using an aerial route is the best option. We were given Lesser Wind Dragons by our master, so this is possible.

The princess has one attendant with her, but it is difficult for more than three people to ride a Lesser Wind Dragon. Since I often act together with Cicely, it is easy to split into two groups.

Additionally, since the client is a noble lady, it is preferable for women to take the request.

“Keeping Her Highness waiting would be rude, so let’s go quickly.”

“Okaay.”

We immediately accepted the request and headed for the Lesser Wind Dragons.

At the Advance Trading Company, Brown Wall Kingdom Branch No. 19, there were two women dressed in riding clothes.

Even without checking their status, the refined woman with pale pink hair was undoubtedly Princess Strawberry.

Since she would be riding a Lesser Wind Dragon, her hair was tied back in a ponytail.

The other woman had chestnut-colored hair in a short bob, so there was no need for her to tie it up.

“Nice to meet you. I am Coco, an S-rank adventurer who accepted your request.”

“And I’m Cicely.”

At first it felt awkward, but I have now grown accustomed to using polite speech with clients.

“My name is Strawberry Crimson. I look forward to working with you today.”

“I am her attendant, Milfy. Please take good care of Her Highness.”

After brief introductions, we immediately discussed the request details.

“We expect to arrive in the Crimson Empire in three days. We will take at least five breaks per day, but we will adjust based on your physical condition, so please let us know immediately if anything feels wrong.”

“Milfy, you do not need to push yourself out of consideration for me.”

“Thank you for your concern.”

Princess Strawberry was sturdier than her appearance suggested.

Milfy, on the other hand, is a complete civilian, so we cannot force her to overexert herself.

For reference, if it were only Princess Strawberry, we could arrive in a day and a half with a forced march and no breaks.

“There may be times when no high-class inns are available, so please understand.”

“Yes, that is no problem. I have become quite used to sleeping outdoors or staying at cheap inns.”

Princess Strawberry gazed off into the distance.

It seems she went through quite a lot while she was lost.

Princess Strawberry rode on my Lesser Wind Dragon, while Milfy rode on Cicely’s.

“It has been a while since I traveled through the sky. The view is lovely.”

Once the Lesser Wind Dragons finished ascending and entered stable flight, Princess Strawberry murmured that.

“Have you ridden a Lesser Wind Dragon before?”

“No. Previously, I was given a ride by the mount of Sir Jean, a Dragon Knight of Castal. I did not know its exact species, but it was not a Lesser Wind Dragon.”

I see. So that is why the Advance Trading Company got involved, due to a connection with our master.

Our master and Queen’s Knight Gene are officially considered separate individuals, so I must be careful not to say anything unnecessary.

“I apologize, but compared to Sir Jean’s dragon, the ride will not be as comfortable.”

I feel bad saying this about my partner, but I do not believe a Lesser Wind Dragon can match a Sky Dragon specialized for flight in terms of comfort.

If the same standard is expected, that would be troublesome.

“Now that you mention it, you received your Lesser Wind Dragons as a gift from Sir Jean, did you not? …Fortunately, I did not ride long enough to notice the difference, so it is not an issue.”

The ‘official announcement’ regarding how we obtained our Lesser Wind Dragons is that we received them from Queen’s Knight Gene through our master’s connections.

Just to be safe, I should make sure Cicely understands the situation.

《Cicely, it seems we need to be careful about what we talk about.》

《Coco-chan, did something happen?》

《These people seem to have a connection with our master. Be careful not to slip up and say anything unnecessary.》

《With Master!? Got it. I’ll be careful. Thanks for telling me.》

The moment our master came up, Cicely’s drawn-out tone disappeared.

The strongest emotion Cicely holds toward our master is ‘awe’, and it seems that whenever he is mentioned, she loses all composure.

Two days after departing the Brown Wall Kingdom, things had gone smoothly up to that point.

As she said, Princess Strawberry did not complain even when staying at relatively cheap inns.

I am curious what exactly happened to her, but I have no intention of prying. A veteran adventurer once told me that not asking unnecessary questions is the secret to a long life.

According to Mio-san, there is even a proverb in our master’s world: ‘Curiosity killed the cat’.

Incidentally, since I am a dog beastman, I am not particularly curious.

However, after passing more than halfway through the Atto Confederation, and just as the Crimson Empire was about to come into view, a problem arose.

Or rather, it would be more accurate to say that a problem was about to arise.

Thanks to the map given to us by our master, we can grasp situations beyond our visual range.

However, we cannot reveal information that we should not be able to know in front of those who are unaware.

As a result, even when we know a problem will occur, we sometimes have to pretend ignorance and proceed, which can be frustrating.

After moving forward for a while, the ‘problem’ finally became visible.

I signaled Cicely, and we brought the Lesser Wind Dragons to a hovering stop.

“Did something happen?”

“Yes. There is a bird-type monster ahead.”

The familiar monster is called a ‘Bright Falcon’.

It is an A-rank monster, and to defeat it without casualties would require at least ten A-rank adventurers, assuming they have effective anti-air attacks.

“What kind of monster is it?”

“It is an A-rank monster called a Bright Falcon. It does not seem to have noticed us yet, so if we make a wide detour, we can avoid it.”

Since it is a glowing monster, it is easy to notice it before it notices us.

“Is it better to avoid it, then?”

“No. Defeating it would be easy, so we will follow Your Highness’s instructions. Please choose whether to prioritize speed and defeat it, or prioritize safety and detour.”

“Your Highness, we should detour!”

From atop Cicely’s Lesser Wind Dragon, Milfy urged a detour, but Princess Strawberry shook her head.

“I am sorry, but could you defeat that monster?”

“Your Highness!? It is an A-rank monster! That is dangerous!”

Milfy cried out at Princess Strawberry’s request.

“However, there is an A-rank monster present, and S-rank adventurers capable of dealing with it are here. I believe it would be a waste not to take advantage of this situation. Considering the location, there is a chance it could head toward the Crimson Empire. It would be best to deal with it before it causes damage somewhere.”

It seems she was not ‘prioritizing speed’, but rather the safety of her own country and surrounding nations.

To be honest, this helps.

The Bright Falcon actively attacks living creatures, so it should be exterminated on sight.

However, since the purpose of this request is escort duty, I cannot say that I want to go out of my way to defeat it.

If we chose to detour here, I would have had to arrange behind-the-scenes work to ask other adventurers or mercenaries to handle it.

“But no matter how skilled Lesser Wind Dragons are at aerial combat, fighting an A-rank monster while carrying us would be reckless!”

“Please rest assured. You will not be exposed to any danger.”

“”Huh?””

I have no intention of engaging in aerial combat while carrying the escort targets on the Lesser Wind Dragon.

“Could you please hold the reins for a moment?”

“Y-yes…”

Princess Strawberry took the reins without fully understanding.

“Cicely, I’m leaving the protection of the two of them to you.”

“Okaay. Do your best.”

As I was activating several skills, I leapt off the Lesser Wind Dragon.

“”Whaaat!?””

I am capable of flying and engaging in aerial combat without the \<Flight> skill.

While it is possible to fly using high-level \<Wind Magic>, it is difficult to control on its own, does not allow for quick movement, consumes a great deal of mana, and is unsuitable for prolonged combat.

Moreover, while flying, other \<Wind Magic> cannot be used, making aerial combat extremely difficult for mages.

In my case, other skills and magic tools compensate for high-speed movement, allowing me to fight in the air without issue.

Additionally, my high stats and large mana pool allow for long-duration flight, and since my main style is close combat, I am not troubled even if I cannot use \<Wind Magic>.

“Hah!”

Before the Bright Falcon noticed me, I closed in and severed its head with a longsword.

My main weapon is a dagger, but as a high-ranking adventurer, I have learned how to handle most basic weapons. I used a longsword because it was convenient for finishing off a large monster in a single blow.

I stored the Bright Falcon’s corpse in ‘Storage’.

Leaving monster corpses unattended can cause problems.

“Thank you for waiting.”

“”…””

When I returned to the Lesser Wind Dragon, both of them were staring blankly.

“Do all S-rank adventurers fly through the air…?”

“No. At the very least, I do not know of any S-rank adventurers capable of solo aerial combat.”

Our master does not count, as he is not an S-rank adventurer.

Our companions can fly if they are in a state of ‘Spiritization’, but that would not be ‘solo’, so they do not count either.

“Coco-chan is amazing, you know.”

“That much was obvious just from watching the battle… And I now understand why the Advance Trading Company calls you the highest-level adventurer.”

“Thank you…”

I am happy to be praised, but there is no end if I look upward, so I must not get carried away.

After the encounter with the Bright Falcon, we encountered no further problems and arrived safely at the Crimson Empire.

At the border, when we completed the entry procedures, Princess Strawberry said it would be fine to stop there, but we adhered to the original request and escorted her all the way to the imperial capital.

More precisely, we escorted her to the grounds of the Advance Trading Company in the capital.

“Thank you very much.”

“Thank you.”

The two of them, now dressed in a dress and a maid outfit prepared by the company, bowed deeply.

The maid outfit was not one used by our master’s subordinates, but rather a type commonly used in this country.

Just as we were about to leave, considering the request complete, hurried footsteps echoed.

“You two, welcome back. I was shocked when I heard you had gotten lost.”

The one who appeared was His Majesty Scarlet Crimson, Emperor of the Crimson Empire.

Huh? Weren’t we supposed to call soldiers to escort them to the castle? Why is the head of the nation here?

“I have returned safely, Father.”

He had said ‘you two’, but only Princess Strawberry replied, while Milfy knelt on the spot.

Milfy is also His Majesty’s daughter, but she is the child of a concubine and has no right of succession (this is not public information).

Not getting involved in royal family matters is the secret to a long life.

“So, you two are the rumored S-rank adventurers?”

“Yes. This is Coco-san and Cicely-san.”

“I see… That bastard Jin can mass-produce people of this level, huh.”

Just as we had heard, His Majesty Scarlet is aware of our master’s situation to some extent.

He likely realizes that our strength originates from our master, even if our master himself did not say so.

“Coco, Cicely, I thank you for escorting the two of them.”

Should we kneel as well?

We had completely missed the timing…

“If you wish, I could host you at the castle. What do you say?”

“We are very grateful for the offer, but it would be excessive compensation, so we must respectfully decline.”

“I see. Well, if you’re related to Jin, that’s the answer I expected. It’s a pain how you never let me repay the favor in a simple way…”

His Majesty Scarlet let out a sigh.

As an aside, this request came from the Advance Trading Company, and the Crimson Empire was not involved at all.

That means the full reward was paid by the Advance Trading Company.

Apparently, since we are associates of our master and expected to become valued clients, they provided extra service.

Just before we left, His Majesty Scarlet asked us this question.

“Hey, if you know a way to repay my debt to Jin, could you tell me?”

That is exactly what I want to know the most.

---

**Characters**

Name: Coco

Gender: Female

Age: 12 (at first appearance)

Race: Beastman (Dog)

Title: Jin’s Slave, S-rank Adventurer

Notes: One of Castal’s adventurer slave group. Her strongest emotion toward Jin is ‘loyalty’. Simply put, she is a loyal dog. By combining \<Wind Magic> with numerous skills, she has raised aerial combat to a practical level. This is because Jin flies as a matter of course, and she believed that to be useful to him, she needed to fly independently. Though it is not obvious, most of her motivations revolve around Jin.

Name: Cicely

Gender: Female

Age: 11 (at first appearance)

Race: Human

Title: Jin’s Slave, S-rank Adventurer

Notes: One of Castal’s adventurer slave group. Her strongest emotion toward Jin is ‘awe’. She is often described by others as gentle and easygoing, but that composure disappears only in front of Jin, leading Jin to think she is always serious. She often acts together with Coco and frequently supports Coco’s more flashy actions.

After returning home, she stops making demands regarding food, clothing, and shelter.

## **Interlude 6**

**AN:**

・Shindo Rin’s Interactions: The Followers Arc

・Chief Labyrinth Guardian Caro: Labyrinth Tour

Background settings.

---

Shindo Rin’s Interactions: The Followers Arc

Perspective: Author

Timeframe: After Volume 13

In the northern reaches of the Kingdom of Sanokia, which lies near the Kingdom of Castal, there are currently seventeen Heroes affiliated with the country.

In truth, since all of them (every last one a woman) have already lost the qualifications required to be Heroes, it would be more accurate to call them former Heroes. However, because few people know that fact, they are still treated as Heroes in the public eye.

Ironically, because the real Heroes have been largely ineffectual, and these women have produced better results, they are widely known as the most outstanding Heroes of all.

The Kingdom of Sanokia has provided these exceptional women with a large mansion.

From the kingdom’s standpoint, it would have been acceptable to grant each of them a house of her own, but because all seventeen wished to live together in a single residence, the result was not merely a ‘large house’, but a ‘large mansion’.

Beyond the fact that they are former Heroes, the seventeen women share another common trait.

All of them were saved by Shindo Jin, and later became his followers.

Their greatest objective is ‘to be of use to Jin’, and because they are comrades who share that same purpose, the strength of their bond is extraordinary.

Their current goal is the ‘Defeat of the Demon King’.

This is not a duty imposed upon them as Heroes, but an order given by Jin himself.

As a result, all seventeen Heroes are constantly active. Despite having been given such a fine mansion, it is usually rather empty.

However, on that particular day, they were unusually gathered in the reception room to welcome a single guest.

The guest’s name was Shindo Rin, the younger sister of the man they revered, Shindo Jin.

“Let me be blunt. How many people do you know who would answer my brother’s call and choose to be transferred to this world?”

It was a question Jin himself would never ask.

And the one who answered it was Shippouin Kanna, the de facto leader of the seventeen former Heroes.

“To confirm, you mean people who would be willing to abandon everything in their original world for the sake of Shindo-sama. Is that correct?”

“Yes, that understanding is correct.”

The World Tree in the Elven village possesses a function that allows the summoning of people from other worlds. Rin herself came to this world because Jin used that function to summon her.

Those who are summoned are given the choice of whether or not to transfer to the other world. If they choose to do so, they must be prepared to abandon everything in their original world on the spot.

What Rin was asking was how many people would accept if Jin summoned them.

In other words, she was asking about the number of followers who were not present here.

“According to the information we have gathered, seventy-three women and thirty-two men meet that criteria. Of those, nineteen have such significant influence in their original world that their disappearance would almost certainly cause a degree of social upheaval.”

Even if the person themselves wished to be summoned, it would be impossible for there to be no impact on those left behind.

Among Jin’s followers were a considerable number of people who wielded great influence.

“Then how many people are there whose transfer would have almost no impact on their original world?”

“There would never be zero impact, but there are twenty-six individuals whose sphere of influence is extremely limited. All of them are women in their teens or twenties.”

An overwhelming female ratio.

“May I ask a question? Did Shindo-sama say that he intended to perform a summoning?”

“No. My brother hasn’t said anything of the sort. He seems to have no intention of using the summoning function in general. He said that even summoning me was not something he did of his own initiative.”

The circumstances were that, after relentless pressure from Mio, Jin ended up summoning Rin.

“Then why are you asking us something like this?”

“To persuade my brother, and have him summon followers from another world.”

“…You do not intend to act against Shindo-sama’s wishes, correct?”

For Shippouin, that was the most important point of all.

“Of course not. In this case, my brother’s stance is ‘on hold’. Since I exist as a precedent, it should not be an outright refusal. Honestly, I have nothing but gratitude for Mio-san.”

Once Jin has rejected something, he almost never changes his mind.

When Jin first said ‘shelved’, if Mio had not stopped him and urged him to proceed with the summoning, the likelihood of it ever happening would have dropped dramatically.

“If the people summoned would have little impact on their original world, I think my brother would at least consider it.”

“What benefit does summoning people from another world bring to you, Rin-san? To be frank, I do not understand why you would be so proactive in encouraging it.”

If the idea had come from a fellow follower, that would be one thing, but Shippouin could not grasp why Rin herself wanted the summoning.

“There are two reasons. The biggest one is that I want to increase my brother’s ‘allies’. People who are summoned are granted exclusive skills. If they are followers, I am certain they would become my brother’s ‘allies’ and use those skills for his sake.”

In their original world, the followers were neither poison nor medicine to Jin.

Although no one said it in front of Jin, one of his close friends, Asai, referred to them as an ‘unofficial underground fan club’.

Unless the target is a celebrity, there is very little that a fan club can actually do.

But in another world, things are different.

In a world far more dangerous than their original one, having absolute ‘allies’ carries immense meaning and value.

If those allies also possess special skills, that value increases even further.

“The twenty-six people I mentioned would, if summoned, unquestionably choose to become Shindo-sama’s subordinates. Unlike us, who attend the same school as Shindo-sama, those women outside the school are starved for points of contact with Jin-sama.”

Shippouin did not say it outright, but in a single phrase, those twenty-six could be described as ‘Jin’s stalkers’.

Blessed with enough wealth to live without working, they do not belong to any company or school, and devote all of their time and abilities solely to following Jin.

Their guiding principles are ‘do not let Jin notice us’ and ‘if Jin falls into danger, protect him with our lives’. Their cohesion rivals that of Shippouin and the others.

To be precise, since they operate as a team in their protective efforts, their teamwork is incredible.

As an aside, Jin has not noticed them (he cannot perceive those without hostile intent), but Asai has.

“The other reason is that, if there are people in the same position as me, I want to bring them here.”

“The same position means?”

“The people I mentioned at the beginning. Those who would choose to transfer to this world if my brother called them. I truly believe that coming to this world, where my brother is, was the right choice for me.”

According to Rin, ‘If I realized Jin was gone, I would go insane’.

Incidentally, the death of a middle school girl driven mad would cause a public uproar. Her classmates would be traumatized.

“What do you think would happen to those twenty-six followers if your brother were gone?”

“I do not even want to imagine it…”

Considering the worst-case scenario, Shippouin’s expression darkened.

Incidentally, the mass suicide of twenty-six women would also cause a public uproar.

The others, aside from those twenty-six, have strong connections beyond Jin, and would barely manage to endure.

“To put it simply, it is sharing happiness.”

It was a rather dangerous form of sharing.

“I understand. I will compile the detailed information on those twenty-six and provide it to you.”

From Shippouin’s perspective as well, there was nothing objectionable about strengthening Jin’s forces.

As an aside, the seventeen women led by Shippouin and the twenty-six stalkers envied one another.

The stalkers envied the fact that the seventeen could openly belong to the same organization as Jin, while the seventeen envied the stalkers’ ability to discard all other ties and devote all of their time solely to Jin.

As the saying goes, ‘the grass is always greener on the other side’.

“Thank you. I will begin persuading my brother as well.”

After this, she succeeded in obtaining permission under the condition, ‘We will continue summoning until there is a failure’.

---

**Characters**

Name: Shippouin Kanna

Gender: Female

Age: 17 (at time of first appearance)

Race: Human (Otherworlder)

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Transferee, Otherworld Hero

Notes: One of Jin’s followers from the original world. Among the seventeen who transferred to another world, she serves as the leader-like figure. A young lady from a distinguished family and an all-rounder type character. It is difficult to see just how versatile she is in the main story. Currently accumulating achievements against demonkind. As a supplement, she had already met Rin before this chapter. In their original world, they were aware of each other but had no interaction. It is a strange relationship in which they first truly spoke after coming to another world. Incidentally, they spoke of nothing but Jin.

Title: Chief Labyrinth Guardian Caro: Labyrinth Tour

Perspective: Caro

Timeframe: Around Volume 13

Today is the day of the labyrinth tour.

During the labyrinth tour, I, the Chief Labyrinth Guardian, explain the structure and functions of the labyrinth to those who have newly joined Jin-sama’s subordinates, particularly those who will be using the labyrinth.

“The Labyrinth of Estea is publicly said to have fifty floors, but in reality it extends to sixty. Explorers cannot proceed beyond the fifty-first floor. Everything beyond that is space for private use by the management side, that is, us. At present, up to the fifty-fourth floor is in use, and as you can see, the fifty-first floor serves as a residential area.”

A labyrinth is far easier to understand by seeing it than by explaining it with words.

Therefore, it is customary to guide people through the floors in order, starting from the fifty-first.

At first glance, the residential area on the fifty-first floor looks like an ordinary town, but it contains only facilities related to food, clothing, and shelter.

Specifically, there are ordinary houses, an orphanage, inns, grocery stores, eateries, clothing shops, a medical clinic, and parks.

Facilities unrelated to food, clothing, and shelter are, as a rule, placed on other floors.

“This residential area was originally prepared for the Labyrinth Guardians who manage the labyrinth, but since Jin-sama became the Labyrinth Ruler, it has also been used as housing for people who have no place outside the labyrinth.”

Among those participating in this tour, there are also people who live in this residential area.

According to Jin-sama’s explanation, they are people whose survival outside is unknown and who have no homes to return to.

“For example, orphans abandoned in the labyrinth, refugee elves whose settlements were destroyed, and…though they are not people, even tamed monsters live here.”

Put simply, it has become a place where those without any affiliation outside the labyrinth are gathered.

Conversely, it is precisely because the labyrinth exists that Jin-sama can freely increase the number of his subordinates.

Without the labyrinth, his forces would not have grown to their current extent.

This is my small point of pride.

“The gender ratio is about two to eight, overwhelmingly female.”

“Isn’t the fact that there are many women around my brother not limited to the labyrinth?”

The one who asked this question was Rin-sama, Jin-sama’s younger sister, who was participating in today’s briefing.

“If anything, this is a place with more men. Excluding the Labyrinth Guardians, the ratio changes to about four to six. The Labyrinth Guardians are all female.”

“Is that because of my brother’s instructions?”

“No. According to the rules of the labyrinth, a Labyrinth Guardian can only be of the opposite sex to the Labyrinth Ruler, meaning only women can become Guardians.”

Labyrinth Guardians are immortal beings.

In the sense that they have no place outside the labyrinth, one could say they are the same as the other residents.

As an aside, all of the Labyrinth Guardians besides myself were originally explorers.

When they were on the verge of death inside the labyrinth, I offered them a deal: I would save them in exchange for becoming Labyrinth Guardians.

“I see. So as far as the labyrinth is concerned, the high number of women is not my brother’s personal taste.”

It seems Rin-sama speaks her mind freely to Jin-sama.

Having finished the explanation of the fifty-first floor, we moved on to the fifty-second.

“The role of the fifty-second floor is food production. It contains pastures, fields, forests, groves, lakes, and rivers, all the land necessary for food production. Thanks to the labyrinth’s functions, we manage the environment, including temperature, allowing us to supply food stably.”

The reason there were no fields on the fifty-first floor is because everything has been consolidated onto the fifty-second.

Those who live within the labyrinth generally eat food produced on the fifty-second floor.

By dividing areas using the labyrinth’s functions, it is possible to cultivate plants and animals in environments optimized for them.

Recently, efforts have also been made to bring in flora and fauna from outside the labyrinth to improve quality.

As a result, even crops of the same type are of higher quality than those grown outside.

Some of it is sold outside the labyrinth, and sales are reportedly excellent.

This is also one of the floors that has been reinforced recently, as Jin-sama has a strong interest in ‘food’.

I am not very familiar with the details, but the previous Labyrinth Ruler, Akira-sama, had little interest in meals, and it seems the Labyrinth Guardians managed it on a minimal basis.

“Hey, just how big is this labyrinth, anyway? I’m supposed to be working on this floor…”

Earth-san, who would be becoming a new resident of the labyrinth, asked this question.

Because he and his family cannot return to their homeland, they chose to live in the labyrinth.

Earth-san will work as a fisherman in the lake on this floor.

Incidentally, in their case, they are simply unable to return home and are otherwise ordinary people, so they are permitted to leave the labyrinth as well.

“Each floor of the labyrinth has the same area as the territory of the Kingdom of Estea above ground. If you would like to know more, I can show you a map later. Would you like that?”

“No, I don’t need to see a map…That explains why he never hesitates to accept more people.”

That last mutter was likely referring to Jin-sama.

Being able to freely use floors fifty-one through sixty means, by simple calculation, that he possesses land equal to ten times the territory of the Kingdom of Estea.

One full floor, that is, land equivalent to one entire kingdom, is devoted solely to food production.

Moreover, because it is inside the labyrinth, there are no poor harvests, and even overproduction can be preserved using Jin-sama’s power.

To be honest, I cannot find any reason to leave the labyrinth.

Food, clothing, and shelter are all fully contained within it.

We proceeded further and moved on to the explanation of the fifty-third floor.

“On the fifty-third floor are facilities for processing. In addition to processing crops produced on the fifty-second floor, this is also where processing and creation unrelated to food take place. As with the fifty-second floor, the environment is adjusted according to purpose.”

The reason production and processing were separated into different floors is that mixing facilities with different purposes on a single floor would reduce expandability.

Such zoning is impossible outside the labyrinth, but inside, where teleportation is possible, it poses no problem.

“Those who live in the labyrinth will generally work on either the fifty-second or fifty-third floor. Jobs are assigned according to skill aptitude, but adjustments can be made if the individual has a preference.”

Because Jin-sama’s ability allows him to see a person’s aptitude, the basic approach is to have them work in a suitable job.

However, we have also been instructed to allow some flexibility if the person has a strong preference.

If someone has a preference but no aptitude at all, there are cases where they work in an apt job until they acquire skills appropriate to their desired role.

Basically, Jin-sama’s subordinates receive points according to their work.

By saving these points, they can exchange them for skills managed by Jin-sama.

Those who make their living through combat often exchange points for skills useful in battle, while those involved in production tend to exchange them for corresponding skills.

Incidentally, some people pour all their points into skills related to their hobbies. I have heard of cases where someone obtained \<Singing> because they love singing, or acquired a magic-type skill simply because they wanted to try it once.

The final floor, the fifty-fourth, is somewhat different in nature.

The fifty-fourth floor was added after Jin-sama became the Labyrinth Ruler.

“The fifty-fourth floor is a training floor. Among Jin-sama’s subordinates are those who make their living through combat, and those who need power for self-defense. On this floor, it is possible to conduct training that cannot be done above ground, as well as training that recreates above-ground environments.”

The fifty-first through fifty-third floors are self-contained within the labyrinth.

In contrast, the fifty-fourth floor is designed with use by people from outside the labyrinth in mind.

I believe this is largely because Jin-sama’s activities are primarily focused outside the labyrinth.

On the fifty-fourth floor, its vast land can be used for a variety of training.

One-on-one sparring, combat training against monsters generated by the labyrinth’s functions, and outdoor training in altered terrains are commonly used.

It has also been used to test-fire area-of-effect attack magic and overly conspicuous skills that cannot be used above ground.

We are currently in the easiest-to-understand area, the one-on-one combat training zone.

Explorer Cynthia-san and the vampire Latina-san are fighting at full skill output. Their non-skill status values appear to have been adjusted to roughly the same level.

It would not be an exaggeration to say this is a combination you could never see above ground.

Since most of the participants are amateurs when it comes to combat, they are watching the unfolding battle with wide eyes.

Incidentally, both of them are regulars on the fifty-fourth floor.

Those who love fighting tend to spend time here whenever it does not interfere with their assigned duties.

“I want to fight!”

The one saying this with sparkling eyes is Asuka-san, an oni-girl.

She is apparently also a \<Hero>, like Maria-san and Cynthia-san. Do all \<Heroes> enjoy fighting so much…?

“Um, the explanation for this floor is finished, so could you wait just a little longer?”

“Okay!”

It seems likely that another regular will be added soon.

After seeing off all the participants, today’s labyrinth tour came to an end.

“Haa…No matter how much time passes, I never get used to speaking in front of people.”

Until Jin-sama became the Labyrinth Ruler, I managed the labyrinth alone for a very long time, and my experience dealing with people is not exactly abundant…No, to be frank, it is insufficient.

Given my years of experience and position, it was unavoidable that I became the Chief Labyrinth Guardian, but the abilities required to manage a labyrinth and the abilities required to stand above people are entirely different things.

An ordinary Labyrinth Guardian only needs to manage their assigned area, but the Chief Labyrinth Guardian has no assigned area. I must manage the Labyrinth Guardians themselves, and also serve as an explanatory guide like today.

For someone as inexperienced as me, it was a rather high-difficulty task.

“Still, it is better than managing a labyrinth without a Labyrinth Ruler…”

Without a Labyrinth Ruler, it is not possible to increase the number of Labyrinth Guardians. I was the only Labyrinth Guardian for a very long time.

It was lonely, and more importantly, it was impossible for one person to manage everything in the labyrinth. I had no choice but to leave much of it to automatic processing, and compared to when Akira-sama was present, I was dissatisfied with the lower quality of management I could provide.

Now, I no longer feel lonely, and the number of Labyrinth Guardians has increased, allowing for high-quality management, which satisfies me.

The atmosphere is quite different from when Akira-sama was here, but this is likely closer to the form of the labyrinth I had hoped for.

“And thanks to Jin-sama becoming the Labyrinth Ruler, I even gained the perk of being able to eat sweets from all over the world.”

In truth, I have a weakness for sweet foods.

Unfortunately, before Jin-sama arrived, the labyrinth’s sweets situation was not very good.

Because there was only one Labyrinth Guardian, I could not go out to eat above ground.

However, now Jin-sama travels the world, and ingredients and dishes from various regions gather in this labyrinth.

As a result, at the eateries on the fifty-first floor, sweets from all over the world can be eaten to one’s heart’s content.

“I talked a lot today, so I will have some fruit jelly that seems gentle on the throat. Apparently, there were new fruits in the countries of the people who attended the briefing today, so it looks like the number of new desserts will increase.”

Labyrinth Guardians are immortal beings.

As long as the labyrinth exists, their bodies are maintained in optimal condition. In other words, no matter how much they eat, they do not gain weight. In this one respect, many women are glad they became Labyrinth Guardians.

---

**Characters**

Name: Caro

Gender: Female

Age: 68 (at time of first appearance)

Race: Beastkin (Rabbit)

Titles: Labyrinth Guardian, Jin’s Property

Because Labyrinth Guardians are treated like fixtures of the labyrinth, the title is ‘Property’ rather than ‘Slave’. By the previous ruler’s orders, she adds ‘pyon’ to the end of her sentences when speaking in front of Jin. She often forgets. When Jin is not present, she does not add it. She neither likes nor dislikes carrots.

Initially a reckless combat maniac, she has now calmed down to being an ordinary combat maniac. Her final combat style is pure close-quarters combat using gauntlets. She uses no magic or projectiles whatsoever. She wastes nearly all the advantages of the \<Hero> skill, yet is strong.

When she is not on the fifty-fourth floor, she works as a maid.

Like Latina, she is a seeker-type, and has safely become a regular on the fifty-fourth floor. In terms of the catalog specifications of her initial skills, she is among the strongest of the local Heroes. She looks like an adult, but has the mind of a child, making her dangerous in various ways.

**AN:** Jin is a dense-type protagonist who is insensitive to affection.

He is sensitive to hostility and malice, but cannot notice stalking that originates from affection.

His poor compatibility with Orihara stems from that very reason.

I had wanted to include details about the labyrinth situation somewhere, but the timing never worked out. It is late, but I have included it here.

## **The Death Mage Who Doesn’t Want a Fourth Time**

## **383 : The beginning before winter**

《The Levels of the ‘Transcendant Strength,’ ‘Constant Super Mana Recovery,’ ‘Extreme Strengthen Subordinates,’ ‘Divine Venom Secretion (Claws, Fangs, Tongue),’ ‘Enlarged Attack Power while Unarmed,’ ‘Super Strengthened Body Part: Hair Claws, Tongue, Fangs,’ ‘Demon Thread Refining,’ ‘Super Increased Mana Recovery Rate,’ ‘Enlarged Vitality,’ ‘Augmented Attribute Values: Reigning,’ ‘Augmented Attribute Values: Worshiped,’ ‘Strengthened Attribute Values: Demon Empire of Vidal,’ ‘Self-Strengthening: Cannibalism,’ ‘Augmented Attribute Values: Cannibalism,’ ‘Murder Healing,’ ‘Self-Strengthening: Murder,’ ‘Augmented Magical Power while equipped with a Staff,’ ‘Strengthened Attribute Values: Guide,’ ‘Blood Rule,’ ‘Roar of Destruction,’ ‘Golem Genesis,’ ‘Hollow World God Magic,’ ‘Precise Mana Control,’ ‘Divine Alchemy,’ ‘Group Coordination,’ ‘Group Commander,’ ‘Death Thread Reeling,’ ‘Dark Scream,’ ‘True Demon King Artillery Technique,’ ‘Demon World Binding Technique,’ ‘Transcend Limits: Fragments,’ ‘Whip Technique,’ ‘Staff Technique,’ ‘High-speed Flight,’ ‘Musical Instrument Performance,’ ‘Dancing,’ ‘Muscle Technique,’ ‘Magic Fighting Technique,’ and ‘Labyrinth Domination’ Skills have increased!》

《The ‘Augmented Attribute Values while Enveloped in a Soul’ Skill has awakened to ‘Enlarged Attribute Values while Enveloped in a Soul,’ and the ‘Augmented All Attribute Values’ Skill has awakened to ‘Enlarged All Attribute Values!’》

The intensive training of Borkus and the others against the Demon King Familiars had great effects on Vandalieu as well. Because Demon King Familiars were split entities of Vandalieu, the experience they gained was reflected in his Status as his own.

It turned out that battles against opponents who had Skills at a high Level, something that monsters did not possess, were effective for Vandalieu as well.

And most importantly, he had gained Experience Points.

Because Demon King Familiars were split entities of Vandalieu, he had thought that the training would boost Borkus and the others’ Skill Levels, but not their Job Levels. After all, even if they defeated the Demon King Familiars, they only destroyed split entities of Vandalieu… a part of him. They didn’t actually kill anything.

But it turned out that Borkus and the others gained Experience Points from defeating the Demon King Familiars.

When Vandalieu and the others consulted Luciliano about this, he had responded with, “I do not understand the specifics of it, but the fact alone would be worth writing multiple theses about.”

According to Luciliano, there had been numerous theories in this world regarding Experience Points.

The theory that one absorbed some energy-like substance from the things that they defeated.

The theory that the gods evaluated and scored people’s feats, and people received that in the form of Experience Points.

The theory that Experience Points were not an extrinsic factor but an intrinsic one… that one’s soul was trained by their feats and the energy produced by that process was what people called Experience Points.

There were other theories out there, but these three were the most prominent. And most scholars and theorists believed that the first was the most likely. They believed that the Experience Points gained by those with non-combat-related Jobs were absorbed from the faint quantities of energy present in the materials and resources they worked with.

And those other than scholars and theorists did not think too deeply about Experience Points. One can breathe even if they don’t know exactly what air is made of, and one’s heart beats steadily even if they don’t understand how their heart and blood vessels are structured. In the same way, one’s Level increases even if they don’t understand how Experience Points work.

Vandalieu had never thought very deeply about Experience Points, either. And that was no different now.

He knew that they were a phenomenon that could not be explained by any proven theory, but this did not cause him any convenience, so he had left the matter alone.

“Leaving that aside, it’s time for a Job Change,” Vandalieu said to himself as he touched the crystal ball.

《Jobs that can be selected: Creator, Tartarus, Wild Spirit, Dark Battery Cannoneer, Dark Beast User, Hollow Shadow Caster, Balor, Apollyon, Demogorgon, Soul Devourer, God Devourer, Nergal, Ravana, Shaitan, Chi You, Ouroboros, Rudra, Blood Ruler, Demon Electricity User, Juggernaut, Berserk Muscle User, Apophis, Azathoth, Taotie, Hollow World God Mage, God Spirit Alterer》

He had recently reached Level 100 with ‘Fallen Warrior’ and ‘Insect Ninja,’ and he was here to change Jobs again now because he had just reached Level 100 with ‘Eclipse Cursecaster.’

‘Fallen Warrior’ had been a Job that provided bonuses to all martial-combat-related Skills. It was indeed a literal ‘Warrior’ Job in that it was excellent for every kind of physical combat technique… Perhaps the ‘Fallen’ part was why it had provided bonuses to his venom-related Skills as well.

‘Insect Ninja’ was a scout-type Job that made it easier to handle bugs as followers… though unfortunately, it had provided less-than-ideal bonuses to his Skills, as he had not put much effort into improving his scouting techniques.

And as for ‘Eclipse Cursecaster,’ it was a Job that allowed him to curse or implant seeds and microbes in those who he touched with his hands, feet, tongue, nose, tentacles, or blood.

It was a Job that was useful for inflicting continuous damage over time against an enemy in combat, for distributing seeds over a wide area of farmland, and for cultivating mushrooms.

“Now then, my next Job… I select ‘Nergal.’”

Nergal was an unusual mythological figure. In Mesopotamian mythology, he was the god of the underworld, and at the same time, the god of the sun – though he symbolized the sun as bringing drought and withering, rather than blessings and warmth.

It could be considered a fitting Job for Vandalieu, the ‘Eclipse Emperor’ who ruled with Talosheim as his capital.

《The Levels of the ‘Transcendant Strength,’ ‘Underworld God Magic,’ ‘Constant Super Mana Recovery,’ ‘Super Increased Mana Recovery Rate,’ ‘Enlarged Vitality,’ ‘Augmented Attribute Values: Ruling,’ ‘Augmented Attribute Values: Worshiped,’ and ‘Staff Technique’ Skills have increased!》

《The ‘Self-Strengthening: Murder’ Skill has awakened into ‘Super Self-Strengthening: Murder,’ and the ‘Murder Healing’ Skill has awakened into ‘Super Murder Healing!’》

Name: Vandalieu Ark HIllwillow Solder Zakkart

Race: Dhampir (Mother: Goddess)

Age: 13 years old

Title: Ghoul Emperor, Eclipse Emperor, Guardian of the Cultivation Villages, Holy Son of Vida, Scaled Emperor, Tentacle Emperor, Champion, Demon King, Oni Emperor, Trial Conqueror, Transgressor, Black Blood Emperor, Elder Dragon Emperor, Food Cart King, Genius Tamer, True Ruler of the Red-light District, Patron Saint of Transformation Equipment, Liberator of Goddesses, Colossus Emperor, Savior, Demon King Slayer, Self-proclaimed Human

Job: Nergal

Level: 0
